25b5: yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams mngon par 'byung ba dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras chos nyid kyis kyang / byang chub sems dpa' srid pa'i tham pa ni gdon myi za bar mngon par
25b6: 'byung ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gis phyir mngon par 'byung ba yongs su ston pa dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag na
25b7: byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dka' ba spyod pa'i sbyor ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar dma' ba la mos pa'i sems can gi khams yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams dka' ba/
25b8: spyod pa ston pa dang / lta ba'i rnam pa la gnas pa'i sems can rnams gyen du bskyod pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams dka' ba spyod pa ston pa dang / las dang bya bas 'khyams par gyur pa'i

26a1: sems can rnams la las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon sum du bstan pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams dka' ba spyod pa sten pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams
26a2: 'byam klas par chos nyid rjes su 'brang bar bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams dka' ba spyod pa ston pa dang / bdag gi dub pa nye bar zhi zhing mthu dang ldan pa yongs su bstan pa'i phyir byang chub sems
26a3: dpa' rnams dka' ba spyod pa ston pa dang / ma yid ni chos la chags pa rnams kyi don tu byang chub sems dpa' rnams dka' ba spyod pa ston pa dang / 'dod pa'i bde ba dang / phrad par brtson zhing rang gi bde
26a4: ba lha len pa'i sems can rnams skyo bar bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i rnams dka' ba spyod pa'i ston pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa brtsams pa'i khyad par yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/
26a5: byang chub sems dpa' rnams dka' ba spyod pa ston pa dang / skye bo phyi ma rnams brtson 'grus rtsom pa la yang dag par sbyar ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams dka' ba spyod pa ston pa dang / ma yin
26a6: na dbang po yongs su ma smin pa'i lha dang mi rnams yongs su smin par bya ba'i dus bsdad pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i rnams dka' ba spyod pa ston pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang
26a7: chub sems dpa' rnams sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gi phyir dka' ba spyod pa'i sbyor ba yongs su ston pa dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po byang chub tu 'gro
26a8: ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub tu 'dod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rab tu bskyod pa'i phyir

26b1: byang chub sepas dpa' rnams snying po byang chub tu 'dod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du bdag gi lus rnam par phye ba yongs su bstan pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub du
26b2: 'dod pa dang / sngon ldan cig du spyod spyod pa'i grogs kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnams bskul ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub tu 'dod pa dang / snying po byang chub kyi rgyun rnam par bye ba
26b3: yongs su bstan pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub du 'dod pa dang / sems can ji ltar mos pa rnams la lus dang spyod lam dang / byang chub sems kyi shing gi rgyan rnam par phye ba yongs su bstan
26b4: pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub tu 'dod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon du lta ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams
26b5: snying po byang chub tu 'dod pa dang / gom pa dor ba dang / 'dag pa thams cad du ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo la snyoms par 'jug cing / skad cig sad cig du rnam par 'tshang rgya ba las mi 'da' ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems
26b6: dpa' rnams snying po byang chub du 'dod pa dang / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ba yin dang nam mkha' lding dang pa'ab ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi bgon po thams
26b7: cad kyi mchod pa blang ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub tu 'dod pa dang / chags pa med pa'i ye shes chen pos rnam par bye ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams
26b8: c ad rnam par blta ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yid la byed cing phyogs thams cad du rnam par phye ba'i mngon par rdzogs pa'i byang chub yongs su bstan pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub

27a1: du 'dod pa'o/ / kye rgyal sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po byang chub tu 'gro ba thams cad 'dul ba'i dbang gi phyir yongs su bstan padag go//
27a2: sangs rgyas rmad gcad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// bam po gsum pa// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying po byang chub la 'dug
27a3: pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rab tu spyod cing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub la 'khod do// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sdang bar byed cing / byang chub sem
27a4: dpa' rnams snying po byang chub la 'khod do/ / ngan song thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed cing byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub la 'khod do// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rdo rje'i rang bzhin du byin gyis
27a5: rlob cing byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub la 'khod do/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gang na seng ge'i khril rnam par lta zhing byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub la 'khor do/ yid nam
27a6: ma nga nyam pal rnam par mirtog cing byang chub sems das nyid kyang rgyal 'ad de ga na 'i sras da pyod la yo su ston cing byang chub sems dpa' rnams seng po byang chub la 'khod do/ / rdo rje'i snying po'i ting
27a7: 'dzin rjes su rtogs par byed cing byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub la 'khod do/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs rnam par dag pa'i gnas yang dag par len cing byang chub sems
27a8: dpa' rnams snying po byang chub la 'khod do/ / dag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i mthus 'gro ba thams cad byin gyis rlob cing byang chub sems dpa' rnams snying po byang chub la 'khod do// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub

27b1: sems dpa' rnams sa byang rnaba' 'dus pa / rgyal pa'i thas byang chu mamamada' rnam gad pabyung chub pa ga' sa nanas kya yang du na dbyung sa pan sa/ na
27b2: r gyal ba'i sras de la nying po byang chub mchog pa 'khod pa 'byang chub sems dpa' rnams pa 'jig tan gyi khams thams cad na pazhugs pa di bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs nas
27b3: zhal mngon par bstan te/ phyag g.yas pa brgyang shing / kye ded dpon chen po rgyal bar gyur cig/ rgyal bar gyur cig ces gsung rjod de 'di ni ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos dang po'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras snying po byang chub mtshas
27b4: la 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad dgongs pa dang / byin gyis rlob pa yang dag par mdzad de 'di ni ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos gnyis pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras snying
27b5: po byang chub mchog la 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la sngon lhan cig du spyod spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams 'ongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la dun nas bskor cing mchod pa'i las rnam par
27b6: phye ba rnam pa sna tshogs mngon par sgrub ste/ 'di ni ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos gsum pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras snying po byang chub mchog la 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
27b7: kyi rtswa dang gal ba dang / sdong po dang nags tshal thams cad kyang bsam pa yod go lnga ste/ snying po byang chub gang la ba der 'dug cing phyag 'tshal te/ 'di ni ngo satshar rmad du byung ba'i chos bzhi pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i
27b8: spyod pa thams cad las yang dag par 'da' ba'i tshe yang chos kyi dbyings rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin mngon du gyur te/ ting nge 'dzin de thog ma thag tu byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad las yang

28a1: dag par 'da' bar 'gyur te/ 'di ni ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos lnga pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras rgya mtsho mchog gi dam pa dri ma med cing kun nas snang la 'od gsal ba'i sa'i snying po la 'khod pa'i byang chub
28a2: sems dpa' rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi sprin chen pos kun nas yog par 'gyur te/ 'di ni ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos drag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras snying po byang chub kyi mchog la
28a3: 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mthas de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pa dang / rim grong bya ba shin tu rgya chen po rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod pa'i las kyi phyir 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa
28a4: thams cad du 'byung ste/ 'di ni ngo mtshar zad du byung ba'i chos bdun pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras snying po byang chub mchog la 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la ye shes mchog gis sems can thams cad kyi
28a5: bsam pa dang / dbang po dang spyod pa mngon du 'gyur te/ 'di ni ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos brgyad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras snying po byang chub mchog la 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la blo shin tu rnam par
28a6: dag pa zhes bya ba ting nge 'dzin mngon du 'gyur te/ ting nge 'dzin de thob ma thag tu nam mkha'i dbyings tshad med pa dang / dus gsum rgyas par 'gengs pa'i lus kun nas gnas par 'gyur te/ 'di ni ro
28a7: mtshar zad du byung ba'i chos dgu pa'o/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras snying po byang chub mchog la 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus kyi las dus thams cad la yang dag par gzhol zhing ye shes chen po chags
28a8: pa med pa rdul dang bral ba'i snang ba dang ldan par 'gyur te/ 'di ni ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i

28b1: chos rnams te/ byang chub sems dpa' snying po byang chub mchog la gnas pa rnams la 'byung bar 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras don rnam pa bcu po 'di dag gi dbang yang dag par mthong nas snying po byang chub mchog la 'dug pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
28b2: ba dang 'dul ba ston teg gang zhe na 'di ltar kun nas nyon mongs pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa na thab mo dang / g.yul la mos pa'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i stobs kyi cha ba nyid yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir byang chub ses
28b3: dpa' bdud 'dul ba ston to/ / yid gnyis dang the tsom du gyur pa'i mi dang lha rnams kyi yid gnyis dang the tsam gcod pa'i phyir bdud 'dul bston to// bdud kyi sde yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir bdud 'dul ba ston to// zab mo dang g.yul la
28b4: mos pa'i lha dang mi rnams kun nas bsdu ba dang / kun nas 'dus pa'i lha dang mi rnams 'dul ba'i dbang gi phyir bdud 'dul ba ston to// byang chub semasad pa'i mthul thub pa med pa yongs su bstan pa'i phyir bdud 'dul ba ston to//
28b5: sems can gzhan mos shing so bar bya ba'i phyir bdud 'dul ba ston to// phyi ma'i skye bo rnams la snying rje ba'i phyir bdud bdul ba ston to// snying po byang chub la 'dug gi bar gyi bdud kyi las yongs su bstan pa dang / byang chub sems
28b6: dpa' bdud kyi las thams cad las 'das pa yongs su bstan pa'i phyir bdud 'dul ba ston to/ / nyon mongs pa'i stobs kyis nyi ma smad cing stobs med par byas pa yongs su bstan pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba brjod pa dang /
28b7: byams pa'i stobs yang dag par bstan pa'i phyi bdud 'dul bston to kun nas nyon mongs pa'i 'jig rten gyi 'ams 'byam klas pa dag du chos nyid rjes su 'brang ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' bdud 'dul ba ston te// kye rgyal ba'i sras don
28b8: bcu po de dag gi dbang mthong nas ni byang chub sems dpa' bdud 'dul ba ston to/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa ste/

29a1: bcu gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams bdud dang las dang nyon mongs pa thams cad las 'das shing byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa yin
29a2: byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo thams cad la rnam par rtse ba yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam gtan 'byam klas pa thams cad dang ldan pa yin/ chos dkar po'i tshogs thams cad yang dag par
29a3: bstsags pa yin/ chos snang ba rnam par dpyad par bya ba thams cad shin tu rnam par phye ba yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du khyab pa'i lus dang ldan pa yin/ sems can thams cad la snyoms pa'i
29a4: sems dang dbyangs su ldan pa yin/ byin gyi rlabs thams cad kyis rab tu chog par byin gyis brlabs pa yin/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs
29a5: rnam par mi rtog pa thob pa yin/ skad cig gcig gis dus gsum rnam par 'tshang rgya ba yin/ shin tu rnam par sangs rgyas pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang rab tu thob pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs
29a6: dang ldan pa yin te/ 'di ltar gnas dang gnas ma yin pa'i stobs dang ldan pa yin/ zag pa zad pa shes pa'i bar gyi stobs dang ldan pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams
29a7: kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa ste/ stobs bcu po de dag dang ldan pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro'o// kye rgyal ba'i
29a8: sras de ltar mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ni chos kyi 'khor lo chen po bcur bskor te/ rnam pa bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar ma 'jigs pas

29b1: shin tu sbyangs pa'i ye she sa dang ldan pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi sgra rjes su bsgrags pa dang / bden pa bzhi'i tshul gyis shin tu rtogs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa bsgribs pa med pa'i rjes su
29b2: song ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi sems dga' bar 'gyur ba dang / thogs pa med cing blta bar dka' la yo ba med cing sdug bsngal gyi gsal shing 'byin pa dang / sngon gyi snying rje chen po'i byin gyis brlabs
29b3: ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du grag pa dang / bskal pa grangs med par chos ston pa rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / dbang po dang stobs dang byang chub kyi yan lag dang / bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa dang /
29b4: ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa dang / legs par spyod pas bskor ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras sgo rnam pa bcu po de dag la sogs pa rnam pa tshad med par de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi 'khor lo skor ro// kye rgyal
29b5: ba'i sras de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo de ni sems can gzhan gyi rgyud la chos dkar po'i rnam pa bcus thogs pa med pa dang / mngon par
29b6: med par 'byung bar 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar smon lam thams cad kyi stobs kyi shugs dang / snying rje chen po'i byin rlabs dang // sems can gyi khams thams cad mi gtong ba dang / ye shes kyi rnam
29b7: par 'phrul pa bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa dang / dus la bab par thob par byed pa dang / rigs pa'i tshul bzhin du mi 'khrul pa dang / dus gsum shes par bya ba rab tu rtogs pa dang / lus kyi dbang zil
29b8: kyis mi non pa dang / tshig gi dbang dmigs par dka' ba dang / ye shes kyi dbang tshig bzhin du khong du chud par byed pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras chos dkar po'i rnam pa bcu po de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa dgra

30a1: bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo sems can gzhan gyi sems kyi rgyud la thogs pa med pa dang / mngon pa med par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs
30a2: rgyas kyi phrin las rdzogs par mdzad zin pa'ide bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ni don bcu'i dbang gzigs nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po ston te/ bcu ga
30a3: na/ 'di ltar yang dag pa'i lta ba bzhin du 'du byed mi rtag pa yongs su ston pa dang / 'dus byas thams cad yid brtan du mi rung bar bstan pa dang / mya ngan las 'da' ba'i phyogs bde bar 'gro bas 'jigs pa dang /
30a4: bag tsha ba thams cad dang bral ba yang dag par bstan pa dang / gzugs kyi lus la zhen pa'i lha dang mi rnams la gzugs kyi lus mi rtag pa nyid du yang dag par bstan pa dang / chos kyi sku la yang dag par
30a5: sbyar ba dang / rnam par 'gyur ba'i mthu phyir mi zlog par yongs su bstan pa dang / 'du byed thams cad 'dod pa dgur mi rung zhing dbang bsgyur du med pa yongasu bstan pa dang / sa gsum gyi 'khor ba thams cad sgyu ma'i rnam
30a6: pa lta bur yongs su bstan pa dang / mya ngan las 'das pa ni snying po dam pa ste/ mi 'jigs pa'i chos nyid du yang dag par bstan pa dang / kun 'byung zhing 'jigs par 'bral bar 'gyur ba'i yongs su bstan pa
30a7: dang / / kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi chos nyid kyis kyang de bzhin te/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las thams cad rdzogs par mdzad de/ dgongs pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs
30a8: shing chos kyi 'khor lo shin tu bskor te/ 'dul ba thams cad shin tu dul nas byang chub sems dpa' thams cad shin tu lung bstan par 'gyur te//

30b1: mnyam pa med pa'i go 'phar yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba chen por yongs su mya ngan las 'da'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras don bcu po de dag yang dag par gzigs nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
30b2: par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mnyam pa med pa'i go 'phang yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po yongs su ston to/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa yongs su spyod pa zhes
30b3: bya ba'i chos kyi sgo ste/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mang pos gsungs pa'o// don tshad med pa khong du chud par 'gyur ba'o// mkhas pa'i skye bo dga' bar byed pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' thams
30b4: cad kyi spyod pa dang / smon lam chen po rgyun mi 'chad par byed pa'o// sems can gang gis 'di thos par gyur te/ thos nas kyang mos par byed pa dang / mos par gyur nas kyang nan tan gyis yang dag par
30b5: bsgrub pa de dag thams cad myur du bla ni med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su mngon par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro/ / kye rgyal ba'i sras de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub ni byang chub sems dpa' nan tan lhung
30b6: byed pa rnams kyis 'grub pa'o/ / nan tan dang mi ldan pa rnams kyis ma yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras de lta bas na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nan tan la gnas pas 'jig rten las 'das
30b7: ba'i chos kyi sgo'i le'u byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / yon tan gyi 'byung gnas don rnam par gdan mi za ba'i me tog chos kyi sgo thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba/ ye shes kyi sgo la 'jug pa'i
30b8: 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yang dag por 'das pa nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi lam 'phel ba 'gro ba thams cad dang thun mong ma yid pa/ chos thams cad kyi sgo snang bar byed pa/

31a1: 'gro ba thams cad kyi 'jig rten dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par 'brel bar byed pa/ 'di rim grong byaste// mnyan par bya'o/ blang bar byag/ yongs su gzung bar byag/ yongs su ga rdza
31a2: nas kyang nges par rtogs pa'i sgo yongs su snang ba dang / smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa la brtson par bya'o// bya rgyal ba'i sras de ltar brtson pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la ni blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
31a3: byang chub dkon pa ma yin no/ / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi sgo'i le'u chos thams cad kyi sgor yang dag par gzhol ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bstan pa'i tshe// sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / chos kyi rnam grangs la
31a4: chos nyid thob pas phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med grangs med pa rnams rab tu g.yos par gyur to/ / 'jig rten gyi khams g.yos par gyur pa de dag thams cad kyang snang ba chen pos rgyas shing gsal bar
31a5: gyur to/ / phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyang dgyes par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la zhal bstan nas gsung brjod pa/ kye rgyal ba'i bu legs so legs so// ji ltar khyod
31a6: kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams la/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi sgo'i le'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / yon tan gyi 'byung gnas don rnam par gdon mi za ba'i// me tog nas kyi
31a7: thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba ye shes kyi sgol 'jug pa'i 'jig tan gyi lam thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa dang / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi lam dang bral ba/ 'thob thams cad dang
31a8: d gas da na da gzha na bya pa da@#

31b1: pas shin tu byang ba ste/ rgyal ba'i bu khyod kyis chos kyi byin gyi rlabs dang mthus/ mos pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di legs par bshad de nged kyis kyang mngon par bsngags so// de bzhin du nga bzhin gshegs pa tham
31b2: cad kyis kyang mngon par bsngags so/ / kye rgyal ba'i bu khyod kyis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di da ltar dang ma 'ongs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ma thos pa'i chos thos par bya ba'i phyir nged kyis kyang byin gyis
31b3: brlabs pa mdzad do/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po'i sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur bltas te/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la bltas nas/ chos kyi
31b4: dbyings thams cad du bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// // gang rnams de dag bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig stong du brtul zhugs dka' spyad pa// gang rnams de dag sangs rgyas bye ba khrag
31b5: khrig stong las byung ba'i chos kyi sras/ / gang rnams de dag sems can bye ba khrag khrig stong rnams byang chub rab 'god pa// dpe bla med pa de dag rnams kyi spyod de bshad kyis rtsa gcig mnyan par byos/ nga ga sangs rgyas
31b6: khrag khrigamatha' yas mchod kyang bdag ni sangs rgyas mi rnams pa/ / gang dag nyon mongs bcings pa'i 'gro bzar byed sems can 'du shes mi gnas dang // gang rnams de dag sangs rgyas yon tan rtag tu
31b7: chol yang yon tan mi gnas pa/ / de dag 'jig rten rab tu dga' bar byed pa'i mchod mchog mdzes pa brjod par byed// gang rnams de dang srid gsum las dang nyon mongs bdud kyi dbang song snang // gang rnams de dag
31b8: 'phags pa'i yon tan ldan zhing khyu mchog spyod pa ston pa po/ / gang rnams de dag gti mug nyon mongs nyes bral bsam pa zhi zhing rab zhi pa// 'gro ba rnams la spyod pa'i rim pa ston pa de dag yon tan brjod par

32a1: bya/ / gang rnams de dag bdud gas 'gro ba kun las rgal ta thams cad dbang byed pa// 'gro ba thams cad bdag la sprul pasna tshogs tha da mtha' yas rab tu ston// sems bskyed gyur ma thag
32a2: gnas dang 'jig pa'i bya ba thams cad stan byed pa/ / de dag yon tan sna tshogs mdzes pa sems can dga' bar byed pa brjod par bya// sid pa'i rgyud na sems can sdug bsngal nyen cing skye dang za/ bas gzir ba
32a3: dang / / 'chi dang mya ngan dag gis gtses shing gnod byas nyon mongs kun tu gzir mthong nas// de dag thar par bya phyir snying rje rgya cher bskyed nas ye shes mchog dgod pa// de dag yon tan shin tu dge ba
32a4: phyogs tsam bshad kyis rtse gcig mnyan par byos/ / sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod pa brtson 'grus dga' bar bsam gtan la'ang rnam par rtsen// shes rab thabs kyi pha rol phyin cing byams dang snying rje
32a5: lhag pa'i bsam pa dang / / dga' ba'i chos la brtson zhing btang snyoms dga' bas bskal pa brgyar yang spyod spyad pa// de dag spyod ldan yon tan ldan pa rnams kyi yon tan bstan gyis de dag nyon// gang rnams
32a6: de dag byang chub gnyer phyir bye ba khrag khrig stong gi lus skems pa/ / gang rnams byang chub zhi ba tshol phyir srog la lta ba med par gyur pa dang // gang rnams ded/ ga sems can phan phyir rtag brtson bdag gi bde
32a7: ba mi tshol ba/ / byams dang snying rje'i sems ldan thub pa de dag kun gyi spyod mchog brjod par bya// rgya mtsho'i chu thigs 'grangs pa re res thams cad zad par bya bar rung srid kyi// de dag yon tan bskal pa
32a8: bye ba khrag khrig du ma stong du brjod byas kyang / / dpe tsam bya bar mi nus legs par brjod cing bstan par mi nus 'on kyang go/ sems can pa'i don tu sangs rgyas yul rnams bstan par bya ba mnyan

32b1: par byos/ / gang dag 'gro ba rnams kyi don phyir dag pa kun 'dzin dkar po 'phel byed kyang // mtho bar mi sems dma' bar sems med mi dma'i chos tshol ngoms par yongs par gyur// 'gro ba kun nas
32b2: don gnyer chu klung ye shes mtsho chen shes rab shing sdong ste/ / ston pa'i mkhas pa de dag rnams ni sa ltar 'gro ba thams cad 'tsho ba yin// byams pas rlan zhing snying rje rtsa ba dga' ba snying po brtan pa sdom pa
32b3: ste/ / ze ba ye shes dri na tshul khrims bzang po'i lo ma me tog yon tan can// sangs rgyas 'od kyis rab tu turgyas byas blo gros ldan pa sems can dga' byed pa// de dang de dag pad mo lta bur 'dus byas mgos
32b4: 'gro ba rnams la snang / / sa bon mos pa sa gzhi bsam pa byams pa snying rje dag gi rtsa ba ste// sdong po shes rab thabs na yal ga lcug ma dag ni pha rol byin rab lnga// bsam gtan shes rab mngon shes
32b5: me tog rgyas pa kun mkhyen ye shes 'bras bu ste/ / chos kyi shing mchog rdzu 'phrul bya ba 'khod de des ni 'jig rten gsum po khebs// rims kyis dkar yangs yongs su spel ba lus yin dben
32b6: pa rnams ni rkang pa ste/ / dran pa mgrin pa spyod mchog shes rab mgo yin ral pa rnam par grol ba dge/ stong pa don dam sul dang phug yin byams dang snying rje dag ni mig gnyis ste/ de dag
32b7: song gi lta bur bdag med sgra 'byin bdud snga rab tu skrag par byed/ / 'gro ba ma lus rnams ni 'khor ba'i 'brog dgon nyon mongs mi zad 'khyams 'gyur te// bdud kyi bya ma rta dang rkun por bcas pas zin gyis
32b8: gti mug mdongs gyur pa/ / lam ni rab ston mi mkhas sems can mthong nas ded dpon mkhas pa de dag ni lam gyi mthar khrid 'jig pa med pa'i grong khyer dam pa mchog la rab tu dgod// 'gro ba dag ni 'dod chags zhe sdang gi

33a1: mug pa nyon mongs pa tshogs nad btab cing / / yun ring nas ni 'dus byas sdug bsngal dag la gzhol zhing sdug bsngal rab 'bar ba// sems can mthong nas snying rje bskyed de nyon mongs pa'i nad
33a2: pa kun gso zhing / / nad rnams zhi bar byed pa stong phrag brgyad cu rtsa bzhi dam pa dag kyang ston// rgyal po lta bu de dang de dag 'khor rnams dga' byed 'gro la chos kyang ston// sdig pa spongs la dge la bsnyen
33a3: cing sangs rgyas yon tan rnams kyang tshol cig ces/ / rkang gnyis dbang po'i chos kyi yul la kun mkhyen ye shes dbang po dbang bskur ba// rgya chen byang chub yan lag rin chen 'byung gnas de dag
33a4: ba'i 'phags pa'i nor/ / tshul khrims lte ba ting nge 'dzin mu khyud brgyan pa'i ye shes 'od dang shes rab mtshan// ye shes rna ba'i gzhu can nyon mongs 'dom zhing bdud kyi sde rnams dkrug byed pa// chos
33a5: kyi sgron mche 'byin mchog rnams de dang de dag sangs rgyas bskor ba'i/ / 'khor lo mchog rnams skor zhing pha rol rgol ba dag dang mu stegs thams cad 'joms// ye shes chun zab cing mi zad shin tu rgya chen
33a6: chos kyi ro dang ldan byang chub yan lag de bzhin bsam gtan rin cen gang ba 'gro kun shes par dka'/ / thams cad mkhyen pa'i gnas kyi mtha' rlabs mtha' yas yul rnams dag cing lhag bsam dge/ de dang
33a7: de dag ye shes rgya mtsho mtshungs med bstan pas zad par mi 'gyur ro/ / 'jig rten rab 'phags rtag tu yul gyis mi gos 'gro ba rnams kyang gnas gyur pa// bsam gtan mngon shes rab 'phel ye shes rtse//
33a8: mo lhag pa'i bsam pa mi skul pa/ gang dag de dag nyer phrad shes rab ye shes mchog gis rab tu 'dra bar 'gyur// de dang de dag yon tan ri rab shes rab rab brtan 'gro ba kun gyis bltas// lhag pa'i bsam pa

33b1: mchag sa rdo rje mtshungs shing 'dra ste brtul zhugs thams cad brtan/ sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun thams cad mkhyen pa'i spyod pas bsam pam byed // bdud dang sems can nyon mongs 'angag rten rlung
33b2: dag gis mi'i skyer rab brtan pa/ / de dang de dag 'jig rten dam pa nyan mongs 'bar bdag las bzlog par byed// byams pa'i sprin rnams kun 'dus seng po sdug pa dag pa'i glog can rgyu rdzog pa// bra sa
33b3: rnams ni rdzu 'phrul gnas bzhi dbyangs kyi 'brug sgra 'byin cing rab tu sgrog/ so so yang dag rig dang tshul khrims yan lag brgyad ldan chu'i char 'bebs pa// de dang de dag sprin chen nyon mongs zhi byed sems
33b4: can don phyir mngon par 'phags/ / shes rab rab tu dga' dang khrel ba dag ni thobs te chos kyi rgyal mtshan bsgreng // ye shes shing thabs yin te thar pa'i sgo bye dran pa de dag sgo ba yin// bden pa rnams ni
33b5: lamachen bzhi ste shin tu dge ba'i rdzu 'phrul rab brgyan pa/ / srid pa gsum na bdud sde dag gis mi thul grong khyer chos nyid dag du ston// thams cad mkhyen gyi sems mchog shing la rab 'dug rngu
33b6: 'phrul rkang pa'i brtan/ / gshog pa thabs kyi stobs te pha rol non mthu byams dang snying rje mig gnyis yin// ston pa de dag 'gro kun thub med mkha' lding dbang po 'dreg shul 'dra// srid ba'i mtshonas
33b7: 'don cing lha rnams mya ngan 'da' ba'i mchog la 'god/ / tshul khrims dang dkyil 'khor rdzu 'phrul rkang pa'i shugs ldan ye shes 'od gzer 'phreng ba mdzes// 'od snang kun 'char nyon mongs 'joms zhing
33b8: srid pa'i rgya mtsho rab tu skam par byed/ / stobs dang dbang po dge ba'i sman 'phel sems can pad mo yongs su rgyas byed de// de dang de dag snang byed chos kyi nyi ma'i khyu mchog 'gro ba kun tu 'byung // chos dbyings

34a1: rnam par dag pa dkyil 'khor 'gro ba kun byas bltan mdzes pa ste/ / nyan thos rang rgyal rnams kyi tshogs mang skar ma 'dra ba dag ni zil gyis mnan// sems kyi rgyung rnams mthong nas sring
34a2: pa gsum du 'phel dang 'grib pa rnam par ston/ / de dang de dag ye shes zla ba 'gro la 'char zhing mkhas pa nam mkha' mtha'// chos kyi dbang po 'gro ba kun la dbang byed gzugs dang yon tan dag gis brgyan
34a3: ye shes rdo rje tha' ba thabs ni mig ste chos la dbang chen bsgyur gnas pa/ / lus dang mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs kun gyis blta ba'i dbang po ste// chos kyis 'gro ba kun las rgyal ba de dang de dag
34a4: chos kyi dbang po yin/ / srid pa gsum na 'dod pa'i 'dam dang nyon mongs las las rab 'das kun dbang po// byams pa snang dang thugs rje bsam gtan dga' dang btang snyoms rnams la mas// srid pa
34a5: gsum po kun tu tha dad lus ston chos kyi sgras kyang go byed pa/ / de dang de dag tshangs pa lta bur rnam dag mos shing lta ba'i rnam par sel// 'khor las rab tu 'das shing rnam dag yul dang ldan pa bdag
34a6: bo chos kyi dbang / / phyir ldog mi 'gyur blo gros che 'chad gang rnams theg pa dma' dang tha dad la// chos kyi dbang por dbang bsgru 'jig rten dam pa ye shes phyir ldog mi 'gyur ba// thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan dbang phyug
34a7: grags chen de dang de dag 'jig rten dbang / / nam mkha'i mkha' dbyings lta bur dngos dang rnam bral dmigs pa thams cad rnam bskul pa// 'gro ba kun tu bya ba nyams len khyu mchog ci la'ang gnas pa med pa
34a8: ste/ 'gro ba kun tu spyod pa dkar zhugs mkhas pa de dag rab tu mi gnas pa// de dang de dag ye shes dge zhing dag pas shes rab nam mkha'i dbyings dang 'dra// de dang de dag shin tu rgya chen thabs ldan pa ltar

34b1: 'gro ba kun gyis gsol/ / chu 'dra dang de dag byams dang snying rje nyon mongs rnams ni rab tu sel// de dang de dag ye shes mas ni nyon mongs sreg cing bag chags bcas pa bstsal// ston pa de dag mi gnas rlung da
34b2: 'dra bar srid pa gsum na rab tu rgyu/ / de dang de dag rin chen 'dra ste shin tu dkon zhing 'gro ba 'bul yang sel// de dang de dag rdo rje lta bur srid pa gsum na lta ba kun tu 'jom// de dang de dag yon tan kun gyi 'phral ba sna tshogs
34b3: 'jig rten gsum mdzes byed/ / ston pa de dag nor bu rin chen mtshungs 'dra spyod pa kun gyi gtsug tu phyin// de dang de dag me tog lta bur yon tan rab brgyas byang chub yan lag rtse// phreng ba lta bur de dang de dag smon
34b4: lam bcings shing 'jig rten mgon laganas/ / de dang de dag tshul khrims ma nyabs skyon med rnam dag dri ni drar bzhi ma// de dang de dag 'jig rten gsum na chos dang ye shes kyis ni bag chags dag/ gdugs 'dra
34b5: de dang de dag stobs kyi bla res nyon mongs rdul las skyob par byed/ / ye shes rgyal mtshan bsgreng ba'i thugs mnga' de dang de dag nga rgyal rgyal mtshan snyol// de dang de dag spyod pa'i ba ran sna tshogs yid 'ong ye shes kun tu 'phadra/
34b6: kos 'dra de dang de dag rdzu 'phrul yon tan 'gro ba kun la khebs par byed// theg pa 'dra ba khyu mchog mtha' yas de dang de dag 'jig rten gsum las 'byin// de dang de dag rab dul glang po lta bur yid kyis rtag tu dul la gnas/
34b7: de dang de dag rdzu 'phrul tas ni khal cher khyer zhing 'jig rten gsum las 'da'// klu'i gling po lta bu de dang de dag sems kyi yul la chos char 'bebs// de dag 'gro ba kun la me tog ud dum par mtshungs 'dra shinaH
34b8: dkon/ dpa' bo lta bu de dang de dag nyon mongs 'joms zhing bdud kyi sde rnams 'khrug/ mi ldog 'khor lo lta bu de dang de dag 'dren pa rnams kyis rab tu bcud// de dang de dag sgron ma lta bur man pa sel cing sems

35a1: can lam yang ston/ / de dang de dag chu klung lta bur yon tan der cing lam rgan rjes su 'gro// de dang de dag zam pa lta bur ngal ba med par rtag tu 'gro ba sgrol// gru dang grwa chen lta bur smon lam rtag btab ye shes/
35a2: gang chen mtsho thob byed// de dang de dag mnyan pa lta bur 'gro ba ye shes thang chen mchog la 'god// de dag bskyed mos tshal gyi dga' la rtse zhing 'gro la yang dag spyod pa stan/ de dag ces kyi rnam tha ma dgas matag le gas gas
35a3: med khang dag pa/ / mkhas pa de dang de dag sman ltar nang zhi byed cing nyon mongs rab tu sel// sman gyis rgyas pa'i gang ri lta bur de dang de dag ye shes 'byung gnas sa// de dag sangs rgyas lta bur ye shes kyis ni 'gro ba
35a4: gnyid log mun pa sel/ / yang dag sangs rgyas lta bur gzhan min yid kyis 'gro ba yang dag rtogs par byed// de dang de dag rgyal ba ci 'dri de ltar 'ongs te mkhas pa de nyid gnas// ro dang de dag thams cad mkhyen pa lta bur
35a5: ye shes 'byung gnas kun nam sgor yang zhugs/ / zhi ba bskyed pa de dang de dag ston pas rab bsngags 'gro ba kun la ston// de dang de dag rang gi ye shes yul dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i spyod yul shes// de dang de dag
35a6: tshad med dpung dang 'dra bar gro ba kun na thub pa med/ / de dag ye shes mi 'jigs blo gros 'chang ba thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos kyang shes// gang na gang dag 'gro ba kun gyi gzugs dang mi rnams ji snyed snang yod pa//
35a7: kun tu gzugs snyoms gzugs kyi rjes su song zhing ming dbyangs rjes su song ba yin// gzugs rnams kun las 'das shing ming dang rnam par bral yang bya ba thams cad ston// de dag mthun 'gro ba rnams
35a8: kyis rnam pa kun tu brjod par mi nas so/ / gang dag 'di 'dra'i yon tan thob cing dngos bral dngos po med pa'i chos gnas shing // yod dang med pa'i mdud pa thams cad bral ba mkhas pa ye shes mngon sum can/

35b1: thams cad shes kyang ye shes rten pa ma yin ye shes de la gnas pa med// de dag spyod la 'jug pa'i yid 'ong 'jig rten dga' bar byed pa bshad par bya// chos kyi na lan sgyu ma rang bzhin dngas pa pa pas
35b2: rab rtogs nas/ / mkhas pa sangs rgyas byin gyi rlabs kyis smon lam thabs dang snying rje dag kyang byed// skal pa'i ye shes sgo dang ldan pas khwa mchog bya ba sna tshogs rab sten pa'i// byang chub sems dpa'
35b3: yid can rtse gcig mnyam pa med pa legs par grag/ lus cig la ni mtha' yas lus dang rgya chen lus rnams tha dang rab tu ston// sems med yid med sems kyi yul med 'on kyang 'gro ba kun tu de dag stor/
35b4: khyu mchog brjod pa'i pha ro lta phyin pa de dag dbyangs cig rnam par brjod byed kyang // 'gro ba dag ni sgra skad ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad rab tu brjod// nyon mongs rgyud byung lus dang bral yang sems can rnams
35b5: kyi lus la dbang sgyur te/ / brjod du med pa'i tshul gyis zhi ba rtogs shing sgra rnams thams cad rab tu ston// de dag sems kyi rang bzhin zhi zhing 'od gsal nam mkha'i mtshungs par yang dag shes// 'gro ba kun
35b6: mabya ba rnam pas rdzogs skan sa 'jig rten sna tshogs snyan/ / de dag lus rnams gang la'ang gnas pa med de lus kyang de dang de dag san pa byung// 'gro ba thams cad byen sto bdag dang rgyum thu gnas par sgru
35b7: thams cad kAn tre skye ba'i las dang ldan par skye ba dag la gnas pa med/ / rang gi lus la mkha' 'dra dngas bral sems can sems la sna chags rnam pa ste// mkhas pa kun la dbang sbyar de ga lus
35b8: mtha' yas kun tu ston byed cing / / me tog dri dang byug pa phye ma sel snyan gdugs dang ba dan dang // rgyal mtshan rnams dang thams cad mkhyen pa mchod pas rkang gnyis gtso bo 'jig rten mchog la mchod

36a1: byad kyang / mkhas pa bsam pa zag pas mas kyis 'du byung bar dub ma ba kun tusan// mkhas pa da ga zul ba lanabs drung shang rgyal bathams cad // khang rnams thadad dra na/
36a2: marung ba med de dag zla bkun kyang thub byed// chos kyi dam papas nas ting 'dzinar rim pa'i las ste ldan pa bgyur cing // thogros ldan par byed nam par ldan parnya parjod kyang ba bad/
36a3: bur rtogs nas shes rab ye shes thabs kyis pha rol phyin// sgyu ma lta bu'i chos dang gzugs spobs mtha' yas dang pa 'gro ba kun la ston// sna tshogs gzugs dang sgra rnams mtha' yas shin tu
36a4: sems kyang rab tu ston/ / 'gro ba thams cad la ni 'du shes dra ba 'jug pa ston kyang gnas pa med// 'gro don rjes 'gro dag la lar thog ma'i sems su 'gro la ston// la lar 'gro ba kun la byang chub
36a5: spyod pa mtha' yas rgya chen dag kyang ston/ / la lar spyan dang tshul khrims bzod pa brtson 'grus brtan dang shes rab rnams// la lar tshangs pa'i lam sdud kha cig du ni spyod pa mchog kyang rab tu ston/
36a6: mkhas pa rtog med de dag la lar spyod pa rdzogs shing bzod pa thob pa ston// la lar skye ba gcig gis thogs par nges shing la las rgyal bar dbang bskur ba// la lar nyan thos gzugs su gyur cing la
36a7: la dag du rang rgyal gzugs su g+hAr/ / bye ba khrag khrig mang po'i shing du mya ngan 'da' yang spyod lam ldog pa meng // de dag la lar lta bang brgya byin rlu bcas pa la lar tshangs par 'gyur// de dag las
36a8: 'i bum brnyes pan la lang gcig bu spyod par ston/ / la lang dge slong rab tu zhe zhing yod zhi la lang rgyal ba dbang phyug 'gyur// la lang chos kyi dra bar 'jug pa'i ye shes thu ma tshag gzugs kyang

36b1: rab tu ston/ / la lar bud med sgra rtsal ba rol rab byin la la dka' thub can du gyur// la lar 'dod pa'i longs spyod rgya chen ston cing la lar bsam gtan thub pa med// la lar mya ngan 'da' dang tshe'i sa dang la
36b2: lar rgan dang byis par ston/ / de dge spyod pa bsams na skye bo mos par 'gyur te yid gnyis rnyed par 'gyur// la la ra l-I dang 'grogs shing la lang shi 'phol lang mngar 'gro gnas par ston// la lar mngal
36b3: zhugs la lar rnam par sangs rgyas la lar 'khor lo rab tu skor/ / la lar skye ba la lar mya ngan las 'das pa la las bzo yang rab tu slob// la lar bud med tshogs kyi dpung nas la lar ting nge 'dzin la lar
36b4: mngon par 'byung / / la lar khyu mchog byang chub dam par sangs rgyas byang chub shing dbang drung na bzhugs// la lar 'khor lo rab tu bskor zhing la lar sna tshogs chos rnams yongs su tshol// la lang sangs
36b5: rgyas gyur cing shing rnams bye ba brgyar khyab 'gro bar ston byed kyang / / byang chub don tu spyod pa de dag tshogs rnams las kyang phyir ldog ma yin no// bskal pa'i grangs pa 'jug pa'i pha ral byin pas bskal pa bye ba
36b6: breg brgya dag/ khyam chag sems gcig dang ston sems gcig bskal pa brgyar yang de bzhin ston pa byed// 'gro ba thams cad la'ang tog dang mi rtog pa'i yul rnams thams cad ston// stegs pa med cing phyogs
36b7: laganas med pyod pa de dag kun kyang rab tu ston/ / gang phyir rgyal ba nyes rgyas de dag nyi ma'i phyogs med kun na bzhugs pas na// 'gro ba kun gyi rgyal baji snyed pa dag thams cad rngub cig snying du mthong // sangs rgya
36b8: zhing rnams bsgrub dang sems can yul dang chos kyi rgyu tshul rnams kyang mthong / / de ltar brtson pas bskal pa khrag khrig brtson byed 'on kyang cha shas zad mi 'gyur// de ltar 'gro ba kun gyi sems can tshul rnams

37a1: mtha' yas rgya chen rab tu shes/ / sems can gcig la mtha' yas lus dang rgyu dang bye ba khrag khrig yod pa'i rnams// de dag 'gro ba gcig dang ma lus thams cad dag la rnam pa kun tu stor ba byed/
37a2: bslab pa 'di'i phyogs la pha rol byin te ma bslabs rnams ni ston pa byed// dbang po rnon po 'bring dang gang dag dbang po rtul ba'ang rab shes nas// 'gro ba skal pa yod dang bskal pa med pa'i dbang po'i 'khor lo ska
37a3: bar byed/ / dbang po re re la yang dbang po thams cad rnam par phan tshun gnas pa dang // dbang po'i dngos po phra ba'i tshul dang gang dag dbang po brtan pa'ang rab tu shes// de ltar khams dang mos dang bsam pa spyod dang
37a4: nyon mongs bag chags rnams kyang shes/ / sngon gyi mtha' dang phye ma'i mtha'i sems spyod de ltar byung ba'ang de bzhin te// sems can kun gyi spyod pa'i pha rol tu phyin kyang 'ongs dang 'gro ba yod ma yin// ma nor
37a5: spyod pa shes nas 'gro la chos kyi dam pa ston pa byed/ / de ltar sems kyi sems spyod sna tshogs kun nas nyon mongs med pa dag/ sems gcig la ni khong du chud nas byang chub mchog tu kun mkhyen rnam sangs rgyas//
37a6: sems kyi skad cig gcig gis 'gro ba rnams bye rang gi shes pas rtogs gyur nas// sems kyi tshul shes sems med rab tu gzhol ba'i ye shes mchog la kun kyang 'god// rdzu 'phrul mchog thob ye shes
37a7: khyu mchog mngon par shes pa kun gyis chab tu 'phags/ / sems skyed gcig gis khrag khrig mtha' yas zhing dang phyogs rnams thams cad du yang 'gro// de ltar ye shes dbang sgyur 'gro zhing bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig
37a8: zad byed kyang / / sgra rgyud shin du phra ba gcig la zhugs par gnas las gar yang 'pho ba byed// 'tsho ba'i don tu sgyu mkhan gzugs rnams sna tshogs 'gro ba kun la stan byed kyang // sgyu ma kun btsal gzugs su mi

37b1: dmigs gzugs yod ma yin par yang dmigs pa med/ / de ltar mkhas pa ye shes thabs dang shes rab rgya chen sgyu mar zhugs pa rnams// sprul pa phun sum tshags pas 'jig rten phal chen khyab par byas shis
37b2: rab tu ston/ / nyi ma zla ba rgyu zhing mdzes la shin tu 'phags pa'i rnams// ma rnyogs chu rnams ji snyed dag du snang yang de ni chu dang 'dres ma yin// de ltar chos nyid dag pa'i dkyil 'khor mchog la shes pas shin tu
37b3: 'phags pa'i rnams/ / 'gro ba dag pa'i sems kyi yul la snang yang 'gro ba dag dang mdzes ma yin// la la gnyid log rmi lam dag na bya ba rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad byed// lo ni bye ba khrag khrig mang po zad par bris
37b4: kyang mtshan mo de mthong / / de ltar chos nyid dang bzhin mtshungs par rjes rtogs bya ba sna tshogs kun ston cing // skad cig gcig la bskal pa bye ba zad byed de dag ye shes zad mi 'gyur// ri'i dbang po'i ri sul
37b5: gnas pa 'jig rten dag dang mnyam du thos pa'i sgra/ / kun las sgra brnyan de dang 'dra bar brjod kyang rtag cing g.yo ba med// de bzhin chos kyi rang bzhin shes pa'i khyu mchog byang chub sems dpa' mkhas pa dag
37b6: rtog pa med par sems can sgra rnams ji snyed par na chos dang spyad pa ston/ / dpyid zla dag gi smig rgyu g.yos pa ji ltar sems can chung ni 'du shes nas// de nas chu rnyed mi 'gyur btung du med cing rdebs je skom
37b7: rnam par 'phel/ / de ltar mkhas pa thar la zhugs pa sems can dag ginyen mongs g.yo ba rnams// shes pas rtog pas sems can 'du shes bya med phyir zhing bya ba rnam par 'phel// gzugs ni dbu ba
37b8: lta bur khyu mchog ston te tshor ba'i chu bur 'dra/ / 'du shes thams cad smig rgyu lta bur rag las 'dus byas chu skyes shing dang 'dra/ sems ni sgra 'dra ba sgrub bya skyed byed de bzhin bya ba sna tshogs rab tu ston//

38a1: brang pa dgang pa stan sa dbang bsgyur dgan de la gnas pa med// byas dbang chen dang bzhin dbang mad 'khrul 'bar bya ba kun tu byin byed dang // khams rnams kyi dbyangs matangs dngas po gang /
38a2: bral bar 'gro ba rnams la ston// dam pa' don tshul zhi ba las ni bden pa sna tshags rnams kyang rab tu ston// de ltar de dag chos tshul nas par 'god pa ston pa byed kyang gnas pa mang // 'ang ba med cing blugs su 'gro/
38a3: ba med la rgyun du gnas pa med pa'i// nyon mongs rgyu las byung ba'i las dang las las sdug bsngal de ltar lam gsum 'dra// rkyen las rag las 'byung ba rnams dang yod dang med las rab tu 'das pa'i// yang dag
38a4: don dam bu ma'i lam ni dngos po med la gnas pa rab tu ston/ / skad gcig cig la dus gsum khong du chud kyang skad cig sna tshogs rnams kyang ston// 'dod dang gzugs dang gzugs med khams kyi yul dang bya ba sna tshogs/
38a5: ston pa byed// sdom pa gsum gyi spyod dang rab tu ldan zhing thar pa gsum yang rab tu ston// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du gcig la theg pa gsum du rnam par dgod pa de bzhin ston// gnas dang gnas ma yin pa rab tu dab par
38a6: chos dang dbang po pha rol phyin/ / khams dang mas pa dag dang nyon mongs rnam 'byed kun tu 'gro ba thob gyur pa// mig gi yul gyur sngon gyi gnas pa 'dran zhing nyon mongs zhi bar mkhas pa dag/ sangs rgyas stobs bcu dag gis
38a7: ye shes shin tu 'das kyang stobs la dmigs pa med/ / sangs rgyas thams cad rjes su dpog stod 'gro ba kun tu mngon par chos bzhed de// nyon mongs zag pa lhan cig skyes pa mi mnga' brang ba'ang brnyes par gyur pa med//
38a8: 'byung ba thugs su chud pa'i ye shes rgya chen des ni 'gro ba 'don pa mdzad// 'di'i gnas la rgyal sras 'jigs pa med cing 'on kyang zhi bar spyod pa med// 'khrul pa mi mnga' lam las g.yo ba 'ang mi mnga' gengs pa nyams pa

38b1: 'ang mi mnga' ste/ / mos dang brtson 'grus ting 'dzin shes rab rnam par 'byed pa ye shes gang du nyams pa med// thams cad mkhyen mdzad sdom pa gsum mdzad dus gsum kun la mngon sum mkhyen mnga' ba// 'gro ba kun
38b2: gyis mtho ba byams pa'i chos nyid ma 'phrogs chags pa med rnyes pa/ / chos sgo gang dag gis na spyod pa 'di dag rab tu thob pa smra ba'i mchog/ de dag yon tan mang po don gyis brgyan pa'i phyogs btsam bdag gis
38b3: brjod par bya/ / de dag spyod pa bskal pa khrag khrig dag tu brjod kyang zad par mi nus te// 'on kyang ji ltar sa'i rdul 'dra ye shes spyod pa phyogs tsam brjod par bya// sangs rgyas ye shes tan ldan bsam pa thob pas
38b4: mtshar 'du shes gnas pa'i rnams/ / spyod pa mchog dang ldan zhing byams pa'i rjes song brtson 'grus brtan pas rnam gnon cing // tshul khrims mi g.yo dbugs byin de dag 'gro ba thams cad yongs su smin par byed/
38b5: lus bstan rab tu thob nas rgyal sras rnams kyi spyod pa tshul bzhin thob par byed// sangs rgyas yon tan dag la zhugs kyang sems can sems dang zhing la sems pa byed// bskal pa'i dus la 'jug pas ye shes ldan zhing
38b6: mkhas pa skyo ba'i 'du shes med/ / gzungs kyi tshul dang yang dag tha dad stobs rnams thob cang yang dag don gyis rgal// bstan pa mtshungs med sems kyis mkhas pa byang chub zhi ba rnam par 'tshang yang rgya// sems kyi spyod
38b7: pa thams cad bzang po'i yon tan spyod pa'i mchog tu smon pa byed/ / snying rje'i rkyen dang byams pa mchog sten byang chub dam pa spyod par byed dang ldan// brtson pas pha rol phyin rtogs rab tu mkhas shing lte ba'i pha rol
38b8: byin gyur pas/ / khyu mchog mos dang rab tu rtogs pa'i stobs thob byang chub dam pa mngon 'tshang rgya// mnyam pa nyid kyis mnyam pa thob cing ye shes tshul gyis chos mchog ston byed pa// yon tan thob byed spobs dang

39a1: ldan pa de dag ches kyi dbang phyug mchog tu 'gyur/ / dbang la gnas kyang gnas pa med pas mnyam pa med pa'i sems kyi 'brug sna sgrog/ ye shes mchog dang de bzhin sprul pa bsgrub cing byang chub nye bar 'gro/
39a2: mkhas pa de dag bskal pa 'byam klas byin rlabs shes par dbugs byin rab tu 'thob// zab la gnas pas brtan par 'gro na gnas shing nem nur bstsal bas mkhas pa'i rnams// ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab chos kyi dgongs
39a3: pa mkhas shing rnam phye pha rol phyin/ / snyoms par 'jug pa'i ye shes yul la zhugs nas thams cad mkhyen par 'tshang yang rgya// ye shes rnam thar kun gyi pha rol phyin cing mngon par shes pas rnam par brtson// rig pa'i
39a4: snang ldan rnam grol nyon mongs bral bas 'gro la bskyed mos tshal dang 'dra/ / gang la dkar ba'i spyod pa'i gzhal med khang mdzes sna tshogs spyod pa ston pa po 'gro ba kun la rgyan rnams du ma rab tu ston kyang sems las g.yo
39a5: ba med/ bsam pa shin tu shes pas brtan pa rab tu mkhas shing pha rol phyin gyur pas// mkhas pa dag ni dag cing sbyangs pa'i ye shes kyis// 'gro ba dag dang mi mtshungs zhum med khyu mchog lhag pa'i bsam pa'i
39a6: rapo 'dra/ / ye shes rgya mtsho 'dra dang yon tan mi zad don tu spyod pa chen po spyong// de dag rin chen 'dra ba'i gnas la rdo rje lta bu'i go ca bgos pas gnas// shin tu rgya chen rtsom la rab tu mkhas shing 'gro ba kun na
39a7: thob med pa/ / byang chub mchog tu lung bstan skyon med khong du chud pa'i rgya chen sems la gnas// sangs rgyas gter mchog mi zad thob nas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'tshang rgya'o// rtag tu kun rdzob shes pas dbang
39a8: 'gyur rnam par 'phrul pa rnams la mkhas pas na/ / zhing rnams kun dang chos kyi yul la rnam par 'phrul pa'i ye shes rgyud la gnas// gnas dang smon lam spyod yul ye shes rnam par 'phrul pa'ang de bzhin te// 'gro

39b1: bdag la rnam par rtsa ba khrag khrag du mang dbang po stan/ / mngon par shes pa'i rdzu 'phrul stobs kyis rnam par 'phrul zhing nges par rnam par rtsa// khyu mchog de dag sangs rgyas yul la stobs thob 'gro ba kun gyis thub pa
39b2: med/ / mkhas pa 'jigs pa med dang bag tsha med dang pa 'dres rnams kyis shin tu brgyan// sangs rgyas sram dag las rnams thams cad byed cang shin tu mdzes pa'i lus dang ldan// de dag lus kyi las kyi dngos po shin tu
39b3: rgya che dag kyang dag cing dge/ de'ang 'byin pa'i tshe na rgyal bas byin gyis brlabs shing las ni mchog kyang byed// dam pa de dag sems bskyed gcig la sems rgyas byed pa'i sems kyang rab tu ston// rgyal ba'i sas
39b4: po thob pas rtag tu dbang po'i ting nge 'dzin dbang la rab tu gnas/ / bsam pa dag cing g.yo sgyu rnams dang bral te lhag pa'i bsam pa mngon sum gyur// mos pa'i 'jug pa rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad 'gro ba dag la
39b5: rab tu ston/ / bag chags thams cad spangs nas spyod pa dam pa rab tu 'dzin// nan tan bya ba 'grub pa'i ye shes mkhas pas thams cad mkhyen pa 'tshang yang rgya// bsam pa rnam par spangs nas de dag skyon mang
39b6: gnas pa zhi ba'i mchog kyang 'thob/ / mkhas pa 'od la shin tu bslabs pa de dag ming ni yon tan sgo nas grags// mtha' yas sems kyi yul ldan gnas pa med par lam rnams yang du sgom pa byed// ye shes
39b7: tshul la gnas shing 'gro ba rnams la lam gyi rgyan rnams shin tu ston/ / spyod pa lag pa lta bu dga' dang ldan pa khrag khrig shin tu phra ba rdul byas lag gis brdus khyer zhing // zhing rnams khrag khrig bye ma snyed du 'dor
39b8: zhing cig tu gnyis kyang gzhog par byed/ / zhing rnams de dag rdul du byas te de bzhin gzhan dang rnam par 'jig byed de// de 'dra'i rjes su dpag pa zad par gyur kyang 'jug pa de dag po zad ngo // 'jig rten kun

40a1: kye nyi ma zla ba skar ma gang dag stong rnams ji snyed dang / / gang yang nor bu'i 'ang dang me'a'ang dang gang na gar rnams lha dbang 'ad// mang ba de dag rab tu 'das pa'i 'od gzer khrag khrig spa gcig khung nas 'gyed/
40a2: 'jig rten kun gyi ngan song sdug bsngal zhi bar byed cing chos kyi dam pa ston// 'gro ba ma lus sgra'i rnam pa sna tshogs skad rnams thams cad ji snyed pa// khyu mchog de dag tshig cig rab du brjod pas sgra rnams thams
40a3: cad tshang bar rjod/ / srog chags bye ba rnams kyis yid du 'ong ba'i sgra thos dga' zhing mgu bar 'gyur// rgyal bas bstan pa'i chos kyi rnam pa ji snyed thams cad de las thos par 'gyur// gang yang ji snyed 'das
40a4: pa'i skal pa yod pa de dag ma 'ongs bskal par ston/ / gang yang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba ji snyed de dag 'das par ston// khyu mchog dag ni zhing rnams 'tshig dang gnas pa rnam pa tha dad ston par byed// 'gro ba
40a5: ji snyed thams cad mkhas pa de dag sgra rtsa gcig la rab tu dgod/ / 'das dang ma byon pa dang phyogs bcu kun na bzhugs pa'i rgyal ba ji snyed pa/ de dag thams cad rang gi lus las ma nor dbang sgyur rnam par 'phrul
40a6: pa ston/ / sprul pa'i byin gyi rlabs la shes pa'i mkhas pa de dag 'gro ba ji snyed sems// de snyed lus rnams rdul dang bral ba ston kyang lus la gnas pa gang yang med// lam yang drug po gang rnams ji snyed yod
40a7: pa'i 'gro ba kun gyis lus bsdus shing / / brgya byin tshangs pa'i 'jig rten mgon po rnams dang de bzhin lha dang mi'i rnams// gang yang nyan thos rang rgyal rnams la dad cing sangs rgyas skul mos pa la/
40a8: sangs rgyas byang chub 'grub pa'i spyod pa dag dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i spyod pa ston// 'gro ba kun gyi 'du shes dra bar pa dang 'bring dang tha mar 'jug pa'i rnams// thams cad shes shing byin rlob byang chub

40b1: 'chang rgya zhing rnams kun kyang rab tu stor/ / 'du shes dra ba rda ba slab pa zla ldan 'dzag rten 'du shes rnams la dbang skar ba// bya ba dang dak+Shar brdamed pa dang kun ma rtag byang chub spyad pa man// de dag da dang rnam par 'phrul
40b2: pa shin tu rgya chen dam pa gzhan yang ston/ / de dag gang la 'jig rten sa phan pa dang yul bin de dag bya ba ston// ston kyang lta ba lhur len ma yin gzhan yang byer zhing gong du ston pa byed// de dag sems can rnams kyi bsapa
40b3: pa ji bzhin spyod pa de bzhin yang dag 'jug/ lus ni rnam bakha' lta bu dag dang yid la chags med 'jig rten gsum gyi gtso// tshul khrims spos kyi byug pa rab tu zhi bge pa yin yon tan sna tshogs brgyan// chos
40b4: go 'phang skyon med thob cing thams cad mkhyen pa yid bzhin nor bu ste/ / bad gshegs kun gyis ye shes dbang skar thams cad mkhyen pa'i rgyal po'i thabs la gnas// pha rol byin pa rtag 'byung 'khor lo yin te blang
40b5: po mngon par shre ba mchog/ ye shes rdzu 'phrul rta ste chags pa med 'gro shes rab nor bu dam pa yin// spyod pa btsun mo bzang mo bsdu ba rnam pa bzhi po khyime bdag dam pa'o// thabs la shin tu mkhrab blon po yin te
40b6: mkhas pa de dag 'khor los bsgyur/ / stong pa lho yin seng po ye shes mchog/ snyed ni rdo rje lta bu snying rje'i bgo bgos ye shes gang ba pa'i mtshon ca yin// shes rab mgo sde chos rtog meg yin byang chub spyod pa yang ni
40b7: rna ba yin/ / tshul khrims dag cing nyon mongs med la gtsang ste mun bzhi byed sna yin te// spobs pa lce yin lus ni rig pa yin te sems ni ye shes dam pa yin// spyod pa rgyab yin te byang chub shing gnas seng ge'i
40b8: khre ni 'dug pa yin/ / tshangs pa'i lam rnams bdag ni mal yin stong pa chags med dam pa spyod yul lo// gang gis de dag snang bar 'gyur ba'i snang ba bde bar gshegs kyi ye shes yul// sems can spyod la rnam par

41a1: lta ba ye shes mchog ste rnam pa sna tshogs bsgyings/ / sems can dben zhing chags dang bral ba'i sbyin pa bsnyems pa med pa'i tshul khrims dang // bzod pa mi 'khrugs brtson 'grus mi ldog dbang bsgyur ba ni
41a2: bsam gtan dam pa yin/ / chub med cing nam mkha' 'dra ba shes rab byams pa sems can rnam par 'dren// skyon med snying rje na ma dag chos ni dga' ba nyon mongs gnas las btang yang snyoms// don ni zhib chos kyi yul la
41a3: nye bar 'gro ba bsod nams 'gro la bsngos/ / ye shes tshogs ni ral gri rnon po lta bu snang ba chen po'i rig pa ste// 'gro ba rnams la thos pa ston pas mi ngoms bskal par 'dren kyang 'jigs pa med// nan tan byed la gnas te bdud
41a4: rnams btul nas bdud kyi lam yang rab tu bcad/ / rgyal ba rnams kyi 'phrin las gang yin ye shes spyod dang lhag pa'i bsam pas 'dzin// nga rgyal las rnams rnam par spongs te rtag tu ye shes kyi'ang bya ba byed/
41a5: bdud rnams byin gyi rlabs bcom mkhas pa de dag sangs rgyas byin gyi rlabs kyis 'phags// chos kyi byin gyi brlabs thob blo gros chen po 'chang ba lha'i gnas su 'dod// lha rnams byas te 'chi 'phos song nas mchog na
41a6: mngal ni shin tu phra bar 'gro/ / skye ba mchog ni nye bar bstan nas mchog gi gom pa bdun ni 'dor ba byed// mkhas pa de dag sems can kun la bzo dang spyod dang btsun mo'i 'khor kyang ston// chags pa med par mngon par
41a7: byung nas byang chub shing drung chos kyi rgyan kyang byed/ / stong pa'i bstan las 'od gzer dra ba yangs pa bkye zhing yang dag skul ba byed// bdud rnams btul te byang chub go 'phang sangs rgyas chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu skor// sangs
41a8: rgyas sa yang rab tu bstan nas 'dren pa de dag mtshungs pa med par bzhud/ / gang gis mkhas pa bskal pa bye bar rnam par rtse zhing yang dag byung gyur nas// sems can bye ba khrag khrig stong phrag du ma sangs rgyas yon tan

41b1: 'god kyang / / rnam pa kun tu sems can mi gnas chos lam yin spyod lam ma yin pa'i// de dag gi ni spyod pa 'di 'dra mtha' yas shin tu rgya chen 'dor bstan to// de 'dra'i spyod dang ldan pa'i ye shes khyu mchog rdzu 'phrul
41b2: dag gis rnam par rtse/ / zhing rnams bye ba stong yang sra rtse gcig la bskal pa khrag khrig brgyar 'dzin te// lag tu khyer te zhing rnams bye bar 'gro yang lus la dal dub gang yang med// mkhas pas khyer nas ji lta'i
41b3: gnas su bkod kyang 'gro ba dag la gnod pa med/ / 'jig rten mkhyen pa'i zhing gi rgyan rnams ji snyed rnam pa tha dad bstan pa dag/ kun kyang ba spu'i gcig gi bu gar khyu mchog de dag rab tu ston// mkhas pa baspu'i
41b4: bu gar rgya mtsho'i chu rnams ma lus khongs chud rab ston kyang / 'phel zhing 'grib med 'gro ba dag la gnod par 'gyur med bya ba de yang ston// khor yug khyim ste ting 'dzin grong khyer mchog yan byams dang snying rje go ca'o//
41b5: shes rab ral gri yin te dran pa gzhu mdzes dbang po rno ba mda' yang yin// 'jig rten mkhyen pa rnams kyi byin gyi rlabs ni gdugs te ye shes rgyal mtshan bsgreng // de dang de dag bzod pa'i stobs kyis bdud kyi
41b6: dpung dang sde rnams 'dus pa 'jom/ / gzungs ni sa ste byang chub spyod pa chu klung ye shes lum shes rab shing // me tog byang chub yan lag ting nge 'dzin ni rta ste rdzu 'phrul rgyal mtshan brgyan// stong pa rnam thar brgyan
41b7: pa rdzing bu yin te rnam par dpyod pa bzang mo btsun mo ya ni/ / thar pa bdud rtsi bza' ba yin te chos ni btung ba theg pa gsum gyis rtse// de dag spyod pa de 'dra yid 'ong khyad par 'phags te de bas gong du mang // ga
41b8: gis bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig stong du skyob yongs su mi skye bar/ ston pa mchod cing rnam dag zhing la brtson pas 'gro ba ye shes mchog la 'god// kha na ma tho kun med ye shes rab gnas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid

42a1: rgyus byed/ / zhang rnams rdul gyi 'brur blags rer nas kyang bgrang zhing brtsa bar nus gyur la// bar snang ma'a' chan 'ad yang sra'as gzhal te zad par bya bar nus srad te// skang cig gcag la 'grab rnams
42a2: kyi sems ni bgrang tshul shes par nus srad kye/ / sangs rgyas sras rnams spyod pa dag ni bsal pa brgyar brjod zad par mi nus so// gang zhig yon tan nam dag 'di dag thob par 'dod cing gong du gzhan 'dod dang /
42a3: gang zhig sdug bsngal rnams las 'gro ba thar byas bde la 'god pa 'dod pa dang // gang zhig bde bar gshegs pa'i sku gsung thugs dang mnyam du 'gyur bar 'dod pa dag/ des ni rdo rje lta bur brtan pa'i sems su byas
42a4: te yon tan bslab par byos/ / / shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las// 'jig rten las 'das pa'i le'u ste// // bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi pa'o// /
42a5: sangs rgyas rmang gcad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// bam po bzhi pa// bcom ldan 'das mnyan du yod pa'i 'dze ta'i tshal skyabs med pazas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba'i nang po brang brtsegs
42a6: pargyan chen po car/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po dang / 'jam dpal la sogs pa 'di lta ste// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab dam pa'i ye shes rab dam pa'i ye shes dang / brtan pa pa
42a7: pa'i ye shes dang / chags med dam pa'i ye shes dang / me tog dam pa'i ye shes dang / nyi ma dam pa'i ye shes dang zla ba dam pa'i ye shes dang / dri med dam pa'i ye shes dang / rdo rje dam pa'i ye shes dang / rdul med dang /
42a8: pa'i ye shes dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang ba dam pa'i ye shes dang / byang chub sems dpa' skar ma'i rgyal mtshan dang / ri rab rgyal mtshan dang / rin chen rgyal mtshan dang / chags med rgyal mtshan dang /

42b1: me tog rgyal mtshan dang / dri med rgyal mtshan dang / nyi ma'i rgyal mtshan dang mdzes pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / rdul med rgyal mtshan dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang ba'i rgyal mtshan dang // byang chub sems
42b2: dpa' rin chen gzi brjid dang / blo gros chen po'i gzi brjid dang / ye shes rdo rje'i gzi brjid dang / dri ma med pa'i gzi brjid dang / chos kyi nyi ma'i gzi brjid dang / bsod nams ri bo'i gzi brjid dang / ye shes
42b3: snang ba'i gzi brjid dang / kun nas dpal gzi brjid dang / kun nas 'od dpal gzi brjid dang / byang chub sems dpa' phyogs bcu snang bas rgyas par 'gengs pa'i gzi brjid dang / byang chub sems dpa' sa sbed pa
42b4: dang / nam mkha'i snying po dang / pad mo'i snying po dang / rin po che'i snying po dang / nyi ma'i snying po dang / yon tan rnam dag snying po dang / chos rgya ba po'i snying po dang / rnam par snang ba'i snying po dang / gtsug gisang ba
42b5: dang / byang chub sems dpa' pad mo dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' bzang po'i mig dang / rnam par dag pa'i mig dang / dri ma med pa'i mige dang / chags pa med pa'i mig dang / kun nas lta ba'i lag dang /
42b6: shin tu rnam par dag pa'i mig dang / ud pa la'i mig dang / rdo rje'i mig dang / rin po che'i mig dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnam mkha'i mig dang // byang chub sems dpa' lha'i cod pan dang / chos kyi dbyings snang
42b7: pa'i blo gros cod pan dang / byang chub dam pa'i cod pan dang / phyogs rnam par snang ba'i cod pan dang / sangs rgyas thams cad yang dag par 'byung ba'i snying po cod pan dang / 'jig rten thams cad las mngod
42b8: par 'phags pa'i cod pan dang / kun nas rnam par snang ba'i cod pan dang / zil gyis non pa med pa'i cod pan dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi seng ge'i khri 'dzin pa'i cod pan dang / byang chub sems dpa'

43a1: chos dbyings nam mkha' kun nas snang ba'i cod pan dang / byang chub sems dpa' tshangs pa'i dbang po'i gtsug pud dang / klu'i dbang po'i gtsug pud dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sprul pa snang ba'i gtsug
43a2: bud dang / byang chub dam pa'i gtsug pud dang / smon lam rgya mtsho'i thams cad rab tu sgrog pa'i rin chen rgyal po'i gtsug pud dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu 'gyed pa'i nor bu rin
43a3: po che 'brug sgra'i gtsug pung dang / nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad tha mi dad par rnam par dmigs pa'i rin chen rgyal pos brgyan pa'i gtsug pud dang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rnam par 'phrul pa snang ba'i
43a4: rgyal mtshan dang / rin po che'i dra bas kun nas yog pa'i rgyal po'i gtsug pud dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo sgrog pa'i gtsug pud dang / byang chub sems dpa' dus gsum gyi ming thams
43a5: cad rab tu sgrog pa'i gtsug pud dang / byang chub sems dpa' rgya chen po'i 'od dang / gzi brjid dri ma med pa'i 'od dang / rin po che'i 'od dang / rdul dang bral ba'i 'od dang / skar ma'i 'od dang / chos kyi 'od dang / zhi
43a6: ba'i 'od dang / nyi ma'i 'od dang / rnam par 'phrul pa'i 'od dang / byang chub sems dpa' lha'i 'od dang / byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams dpal dang / ye shes dpal dang / chos dpal dang / mngon par shes pa'i
43a7: dpal dang / 'od kyi dpal dang / me tog dpal dang / rin po che'i dpal dang / byang chub kyi dpal dang / tshangs pa'i dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun nas snang ba'i dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' mangs par
43a8: dbyangs dang / rgya mtsho'i dbyangs dang / sa sgra'i dbyangs dang / 'jig rten dbang po'i dbyangs dang / ri dbang rgyal po'i 'thab pa'i dbyangs dang / chos kyi dbyings kun tu rgyas pa'i dbyangs dang / chos rgya mtsho thams cad

43b1: rab tu sgeg pa'i dbyangs dang / bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rab tu 'dul ba'i dbyangs dang / snying rje chen po'i tshul gyi sprin rab tu sgrog pa'i dbyangs dang / byang chub sems dpa' 'gro ba thams cad sdug bsngal
43b2: tu zhi bar byed pa dbugs 'byin pa'i dbyangs dang / byang chub sems dpa' chos kyis 'phags pa dang / khyad par gyis 'phags pa dang / ye shes kyis 'phags pa dang / bsod nams ripes 'phags pa dang / yon
43b3: tan gyi tshogs kyis 'phags pa dang / grags pas 'phags pa dang / kun tu snang bas 'phags pa dang / byams pa chen pos 'phags pa dang / ye shes rgya mtshos 'phags pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i de bzhin
43b4: gshegs pa'i rgyud kyi gdung gis 'phags pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' 'od kyi dpal dang / mchog gi dpal dang / kun tu 'phags pa'i dpal dang / rnam par snang ba'i dpal dang / chos kyi dpal dang / zla ba
43b5: dpal dang / nami mkha'i dpal dang / rin po che'i dpal dang / dpal gyi dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' ye shes kyi dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' ri'i dbang po'i rgyal po dang / chos kyi dbang po'i rjem po da
43b6: 'gro ba'i dbang po'i rgyal po dang / tshangs pa'i dbang po'i rgyal po dang / tshogs kyi dbang po'i rgyal po dang / lha'i dbang po'i rgyal po dang / zhi ba'i dbang po'i rgyal po dang / mi g.yo ba'i dbang po'i rgyal po dang /
43b7: mchog gi dbang pa rgyal po dang / byang chub sems dpa' mchog gi dbang po'i rgyal po dang / byang chub sems dpa' rab tu zhi ba'i sgra dang / chags pa'i mad pa'i sgra dang / sa'i dbyangs kyi sgra dang / rgya ma
43b8: 'brug gi sgra dang / sprin gyi dbyangs kyi sgra dang / chos snang ba'i rgyal po'i sgra dang // nam mkha' dbyings kyi sgra dang / sems can kun gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rab tu sgrog pa'i sgra dang / sngon gyi smon lam yongs su skul

44a1: pa'i sgra dang / byang chub sems dpa' bdud kyi dkyil 'khor bcom pa med pa byed pa'i sgra dang / byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'i blo dang / ye shes ri bo'i blo dang / nam mkha'i blo dang / dri ma med pa'i blo
44a2: dang / chags pa med pa'i blo dang / rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i blo dang / dus gsum snang ba'i blo dang / yangs pa'i blo dang / kun tu snang ba'i blo dang / byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyings su snang ba'i blo dang / de dag la sogs
44a3: pa'i byang chub sems dpa' lnga stong tsam ste/ / kun kyang byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang / smon lam gyis byung ba sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pas/ chags pa med pa'i spyor
44a4: yul can de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs su 'gyur/ drang du 'dod pas lus mtha' yas pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i yongs su bstan pa rnam par 'phrul pa yongs
44a5: su bstan pa rnam par dmigs pa bya ba la bsgrub pa med pa'i mig gi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i tshe// nye bar 'dod pa'i rgyun mi gcod pas/ tshad med
44a6: par byon pa/ ches rgya mtsho'i tshul thams cad la ye shes snang ba/ rab tu thob pas snang ba mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa/ so sa yang dag par rig pa rnam par dag pas bskal pa mtha' yas par shin tu ston pa ma
44a7: zad pa/ 'gro ba'i bas ma pa ji lta ba bzhin du gzugs kyi lus yongs su ston pas nam mkha'i dbyings kyis klas pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul rnam par dag cing mi gnas pa/ sems can gyi khams sems
44a8: can med pa dang / srog med pa yongs su shes pas rab rib med pa/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du 'od gzer gyi dra bas rgyas par 'gengs pas nam mkha' dang mnyam pa sha stag dang thabs gcig tu bzhags

44b1: so/ / nyan thos rdzu 'phrul chen po dang ldan pa lnga brgya ste/ thams cad kyang bden pa'i tshul gyi rang bzhin mngon par khong du chud pa/ yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon gsum du gyur pa/ chos kyi rang bzhin la zhugs pa/
44b2: sred pa'i rgya mtsho las gyen du 'phags pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs su 'gyur ba'i spyod yul can kun nas sbyor ba dang / bag la nyal ba dang bcings pa rnam par bzlog pa/ chags pa med pa'i gnas la
44b3: brtan pa/ nam mkha' ltar zhi ba la rnam par spyod pa/ sangs rgyas la the tsom dang nem nur dang / yid gnyis yongs su chad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rgya mtsho la mos pa'i lam du zhugs pa sha stag dang / 'jig
44b4: rten gi dbang po sngon gyi rgyal ba la bya ba byas pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la phan pa dang / bde ba'i don du zhugs pa/ gsol pa ma btab par dge ba'i bshes nyen du gyur pa/ sems can gzhan bsrung ba la zhugs pa/
44b5: 'jig tan thams cad las 'phags pa'i khyad par dang ldan pa'i ye shes kyi sgo la zhugs pa/ sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bstan pa'i spyod yu
44b6: las byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa yongs su bsrung ba la zhugs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs yang dag par bzung ba'i smon lam gyis yang dag par skyes pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung gi rgyun tu
44b7: 'byung ba/ mngon du gyur pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la mngon par mos pa sha stag dang yang thabs gcig go/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'khor dang bcas pa de dag dang / nyan thos rdzu 'phrul man
44b8: dang ldan pa/ de dag dang 'jig rten gyi dbang po 'khor dang bcas pa de dag 'di snyam du gyur te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi yul dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi

45a1: rlabs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi bsnyengs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par spyod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
45a2: pa'i mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes la ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mthu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi
45a3: smon lam dang / / sngon legs pa spyod pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi skyabs dang / dad pa'i mig yongs su dag pa dang / rgya chen po la mos pa'i sdang ba rab tu thob pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lhag
45a4: pa'i bsam par rnam par dag pa dang / bsam pa tha ga pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su smon cing yang dag par zhugs pa/ ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis 'jug pa 'am/ khong du chud
45a5: pa'am yid ces pa'am/ yongs su shes pa 'am/ rnam par rtog pa'am/ bzung ba'am rnam par dpyod pa 'am/ rnam par bsgom pa'am/ rnam par dbye ba 'am/ rnam par dgrol ba'am/ rab tu brjod pa 'am/
45a6: sems can pha rol gyi rgyud du phyin par bya bar ni mi nus na/ bcom ldan 'das nyid kyis bdag cag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bsam pa'i tshul ji lta ba dang / sems can bsam pa rnam pa tha dad pa dang /
45a7: mos pasna tshogs dang / shes pa sna tshogs kyi tshig dang / brdasna tshogs su gyur pa/ dbang sgyur ba'i sa gzhan dang / gzhan la gnas pa dbang po sna tshogs su rnam par dag pa/ bsam pa dang sbyor ba rnam pa gzhan
45a8: gzhan can/ sems dang bsam pa'i yul la gzhan dang gzhan can de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan gzhan dang gzhan la gnas pa/ chos bstan pa gzhan dang gzhan la mos pa dag la sngon thams cad mkhyen pa nyid

45b1: drazug yang yang dag par bstan thar/ na byang chub sems dpa' sman las mngon par bsgrubs pa lta'ang yang dag par brtan zang / na gyi byung chubs pas dpa' sa rdzun padang byam /
45b2: su dag pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang / sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i sa yongs su dag pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa lta'ang yang dag par stan grang // sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor mngon
45b3: par bsgrub pa yongs su rdzogs par mdzad pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang / sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i tshul mngon par bslab pa rnam par phye ba'i snang ba lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang / sngon byang
45b4: chub sems dpa'i lam gyi rgyan yongs su dag par mdzad pa lta'ang yang dag par stan grang / sngon byang chub sems dpa'i 'byung ba'i tshul rgya mtsho mngon par bsgrub pa/ lta 'ang yang dag par bstan grang /
45b5: sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i yang dag par bsgrub pa dang / rnam par 'phrul par rgyan phun sum tshogs pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang / byang chub sems dpa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho lta'ang yang dag par
45b6: bstan grang / mngon par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi sgos rnam par 'phrul pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / khyu mchog gi
45b7: mthu lta 'ang yang dag par bstan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par/ rnam par 'phrul pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan brang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sems can gyi khams
45b8: 'dul ba'i thabs kyi sgo lta yang yang dag par bstan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid chos kyi grong khyer la mnga' mdzad pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa sems

46a1: can thams cad kyilas bangs da palta'ang yang dag par ga/ thAng/ de na/ gshegs pa sems ca thams ca gag gshegs gang rnam pa 'phrul ba na
46a2: 'ang yang dag par bstan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi yon bzhes mdzad pa lta'ang yang dag par ba stan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi bsod nams
46a3: dang yon ston pa'i cho 'phrul mdzad pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi tshul la sangs rgyas kyi gzugs brnyan dmigs pa mdzad pa sa'ang yang dag
46a4: par stan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad la rnam par 'phrul pa'i tshe'i phrul mdzad pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad la yongs su bstan
46a5: dang / rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul mdzad pa lta yang yang dag par bstan grang / de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams cad la sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul bsam gyis mi khyab pas nas
46a6: 'phrul pa mdzad pa lta'ang yang dag par bstan grang snyam pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' di dag gi sems kyi yongs su tog pa thugs kyis mkhyen nas/ seng ge nam par bgyi
46a7: bzhis bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin nam mkha' dang mnyam pas dpe med pa 'gro ba thams cad du rnam par snang ba'i brgyan dang ldan pa/ thugs de chen po'i sgo bzhin can/ thugs rje chen pa sgo dang ldan pa/ zugs
46a8: rje chen po sngon du 'gro ba/ / thugs rje chen po'i chos can la mnyam par bzhag go/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de ltar mnyam par bzhag ma thag tu bo grang brtsegs pa brgyan chen po can yang mtha' dang dpas

46b1: mdapar yangs shing rdo rje thub pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis sa'i zhi rab tu bkod pa dang / nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po thams cad kyi dra ba kun tu bkram pa/ rin po che du ma'i me togs lams chal bar gang
46b2: gnor bu rin po ched ma pa mdzes par bkram pa dang / bai dUr+ya'i kabs mdzes par byas pa/ rin po che'i rgyal po 'gro ba rnam par snang bas rgyan shin tu rnam par bye ba dang / rin po che bzang po mang po dang ldan
46b3: nor bu rin po che 'dzam bu'i chu klung gi phung pos shin tu brgyan pa dang / rin po che thams cad las sgo gang dang / rta babs dang / pu shu dang / skar khur byas shing khri 'phar grangs med pa rnam pa dag pas brgyan pa
46b4: dang / 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad dang 'dra ba'i nor bu rin po che rgyan dang ldan pa dang / 'gro ba rgya mtsho dang nor bu rin po che rnam par phye ba dang / nor bu rin po che thams cad kyi dra bas kun nas yog pa'i
46b5: gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan rab tu bsgreng ba dang / sgro dang rta babs thams cad las 'od gzer chos kyi dbyings su rgyas par 'gengs pa rab tu 'byung bas rnam par mdzes par byas pa dang / phyi rol gi 'khor
46b6: kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sa'i gzhi stegs bu brjod du med pas brgyan pa dang / phyogs kun nas them skas kyi phreng ba nor bu rin po ches brtsegs shing shin tu rnam par bye bas rab tu mdzes par kun nas gnas
46b7: par gyur to/ / 'dze ta'i tshal thams cad dang chu zheng gab par shin tu yangs shing rgya che bar kun nas gnas par gyur te/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
46b8: sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang chu zhe kun tu rgya che zhing yangs pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyi rgyan sna tshogs dang ldan zhing / sa'i gzhi nor bu rin po che sna tshogs brjod du med pas kun nas grub pa

47a1: dang / / nor bu rin po che grangs med pa'i rabs kun nas bskor ba dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi shing ta la'i 'phreng bas mdzes par brgyan par kun nas gnas par gyur to// sangs rgyas kyi/
47a2: zhing de dag na spos kyi chu klung tshad med pa glong mtha' yas pas 'khyil pa'i spos kyi chus yongs su gdab/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi me tog mang po dang 'dres par gyur la g.yas phyogs su 'khyil cing 'bab pa/
47a3: sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dbyangs su sgrog pas rab tu brgyan pa dag kyang kun nas gnas par gyur to// rin po che'i me tog pun 'da' ri ka'i phreng ba dang / rin po che'i shing gam yo'i rin po che thams
47a4: cad kyi pad mo rab tu rgyas shing / shin tu 'phags pas mdzes par brgyan pa dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi khang pa brtsegs pa'i phreng ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa nor bu rin po che thams cad kyi dra bas
47a5: kun nas yog pa nor bu rin po che grangs med pa dra bas kun nas snang bas rgyan cing mdzes pa dang / nor bu rin po che'i gzhal med khang nor bu rin po che thams cad kyis brgyan pa grangs med pa smos
47a6: thams cad kyi ngang kun nas 'byung ba spos kyi sprin gyi rgyan dang ldan pa dag kyang kun nas gnas par gyur to/ / rin po che'i rgyal mtshan grangs med pa dang / gos kyi rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan gyi rgyal mtshan
47a7: dang / / rin po che snam bu'i rgyal mtshan dang / me tog gi rgyal mtshan dang / rgyal mtshan dang / phreng ba'i rgyal mtshan dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi dril bu'i rgyal mtshan dang / rin po che'i rgyal ba'i gdugs
47a8: kyi rgyal mtshan dang / nor bu rin po che snang bas kun tu rgyas par 'gengs pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo'i dbyangs rab tu sgrog pa'i

47b1: mamadu dang / brgyan rna ma pa dung ba'i rnam sacan dang / 'ardzun papa'i rnas pa zhin gshegs pa thams cad star bya snang ba ba tu ga pa rna
47b2: mthas da rnal 'dang / rnam pa sa rgya ra bye na / sa
47b3: ta'i tshal gyi nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad kyang lha'i gnas med khang gi sbyin bsam myos mi khyab pas brgyan par kun nas gnas par gyur to/ / 'jo nya'i tsha la nyid kyang spos sde tshogs kyi shing grangs med pa
47b4: sprin kyis kun nas yog cing brgyan pa dang / brjod du med pa'i rgyan sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i ri rab kyis kun nas 'khor cing brgyan pa dang / rol mo brdud pa dang dkrol ba brjod du med pa'i sprin las de bzhin
47b5: gshegs pa thams cad la bstod pa'i dbyangs ro snyan pa 'byung bas kun nas brgyan pa dang / rin po che'i pad mo brjod du med pa'i sprin gyis kun nas yog cing brgyan pa dang / rin po che'i seng ge'i khri brjod du
47b6: med pa'i steng lnga rdzas kyi rin po che'i stan bting pal/ byang chub sems dpa' 'a'od cing de bzhin gshegs pa la bskyed pa'i sgra byang mi snyan pa'i byin pa'i sprin gyis kun nam brgyan pa dang / lha dbar
47b7: rlub pa'i ga gas da bang da par 'byung ba nor dran po ma 'gyu'i sbyin kyis ku nas brgyan pa dang / bu tig / po dru ba'i srin parjod dume pas kun nas brgyad pa dang / mu ti ga mang pa'a'ang pa brtsegs
47b8: sri brjod dri mdapas kun cas yog cing brgyan pa dang / rdo rje la bu sra pa'i mu tig gi sprin brjod du med pa'i char mngon par bab pas rab tu brgyan par kun nas gnas par gyur to// de ci'i phyir zhen/

48a1: de bzhin gshegs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos dkar po'i tshogs bsam gyis myi khyab pa'i phyir ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi
48a2: mthu dang / byin gyis rlabs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs pa rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i
48a3: phyir ro/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gcig tu zhugs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par phye ba thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba'i byin gyi rlabs yongs su ston pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i
48a4: phyir ro/ / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams rdul shin tu pra ba cig la chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan rnam par dmigs par yongs su ston pa mdzad pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir ro// de bzhin
48a5: bzhin gshegs pa rnams pa spu'i bu gcig tu sngon gyi mtha'i de bzhin gshegs pa gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa yongs su ston pa mdzad pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir ro/ / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi
48a6: 'od gzer gyi sgo nas 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa snang bar 'gyur ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir ro/ / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams pa spu'i rtse mo gcig las sprul pa'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams thams
48a7: cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir ro bzhin gshegs pa rnams pa spu'i sgo gcig nas 'jig rten gyi khams 'dra ba dang / 'jig pa'i
48a8: bskal po yongs su ston pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir ro/ / ji ltar 'dze ta'i tshal de lta bu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pas yongs su dag par kun nas gnas par gyur pa de bzhin du phyogs bcur

48b1: 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha' mthas gtugs pa thams cad kyang yongs su dag par kun nas gnas shing rab tu brgyan pa dang / shin tu spyad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku
48b2: yongs su rgyas pa dang / 'dze ti tshal du yang dag par gzhol ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' yongs su rgyas pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho shin tu rnam par gnas pa dang /
48b3: rgyan thams cad kyi rgyan gyi char mngon par 'bab pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od kyis rab tu snang ba dang / rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab pas brgyan pa dang / zhing thams cad kyi rgyan
48b4: sprin gyis kun nas yog par brgyan pa dang / lha rdzas kyi lus thams cad kyi sprin gyi char rab tu 'bab pas brgyan pa dang / me tog sna tshogs thams cad kyi sprin shin tu rgyas pa'i lhun gyis kun tu rgyas shing brgyan pa
48b5: gos thams cad kyi shing gi sprin gyi mdzod nas gos kha dog sna tshogs su mdzes pa'i char rab tu 'bab pas brgyan pa dang / phreng ba dang lnga ldi dang se mo de'i rgyan thams cad kyi sprin gyi cher rgyun mi chad par mngon par
48b6: 'bab pas brgyan pa dang / spos sna tshogs kyi bdug spos phyogs kun nas 'thul pa'i sprin dang na bun gyi char thams cad kyi dbyibs lter mngon par 'bab pas rgyan pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyi me tog gi
48b7: dra ba'i sprin las rin po che'i rgyal po'i phye ma zhib bu'i char rgyun mi chad par rab tu 'bab pa dang / rin po thams cad kyi rgyal mtshan dang ba dan gyi sprin lha'i bu mo'i lag na khyer ba nam mkha'i dbyings kun tu rga
48b8: zhing 'khor bar brgyan pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyi pad ma rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'dab ma'i dkyil 'khor can chub mthon po dang ldan pa'i ze ba la rol mo bkod pa kun nas sgra 'byin cing dbyangs snyan par

49a1: sgrog pas brgyan pa dang / rin po che'i 'bru sna tshogs kyi dra ba dang / rin po che seng ge'i dra ba sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pa'i phreng ba dang / se mo dos brgyan par kun nas gnas shing snang bar gyur to//
49a2: de ltar bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin chen po seng ge'i rnam par bsgyings pa de la mnyam par bzhag ma thag du/ de'i tshe shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho sangs rgyas
