49a3: k yi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol gyi 'jig rten gyi khams gser gyi sprin sgron ma'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad dpal gyi gzi brjid rgyal po sangs
49a4: rgyas kyi zhing nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang ba'i smon lam gyi gtsug gi 'od gzer snang ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / ldan
49a5: cig du bcom ldan 'das des gnang nas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho de dag 'phags te/ nam mkha'i dbyings rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa dang / lha rdzas kyi me tog gi sprin gyi char mngon par 'bab
49a6: pa dang / lha rdzas kyi spos kyi sprin gyi char rab tu dbye ba dang / lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i pad mo'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab pa dang / lha rdzas kyi phreng ba'i sprin gyi char rab tu btang ba dang / lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i sprin gyi chang

49b1: brlab pa dang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi rgyan yid du 'ong bas nam mkha'i dbyings rgyas par 'gengs pa byed cing / mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang na ba der lhags nas bcom ldan 'das ga
49b2: la ba der dong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas shar phyogs su brtan te/ khang partsegs pa rgyan kun dang ldan zhing nor bu rin po che'i dra bas kun nas khyab pa dang / seng
49b3: g e'i khri nor bu rin po che phyogs rab tu sdang ba'i pad mo'i snying po can dag mngon par sprul nas nor bu rin po che yid bzhin gyi rgyal po'i dra ba'i rgyan gyis kun nas brgyan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lus
49b4: su byin gyis brlabs nas skyil mo krung bcas te 'khod do/ / lho phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du byed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol gyi 'jig rten gyi khams rdo rje rgyal
49b5: m tshan gyi snying po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa dpal gyi snying po kun nas snang ba'i rgyal po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po brtson 'grus kyi shugs thub par
49b6: d ka' ba'i rgyal po zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig du bcom ldan 'das des gnas nas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mdzod nas
49b7: 'phags te/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad spos kyi lnga ldi dang dra bas kun tra 'brel bar byin gyis brlab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad rin po che sna tshogs kyi lnga'i
49b8: dang / dra ba chen pos kun tu 'brel bar byin gyis brlab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyud thams cad me tog thams cad kyi lda ldi dang / phreng ba'i dra bas kun 'brel bar byin gyis brlab pa dang

50a1: sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi 'khor thams cad 'phreng ba dang lnga ldi dang / se mo do'i dra bas kun nas 'brel bar byin gyis brlab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi dkyil 'khor thams cad 'og gi 'jig
50a2: rten rdo rje thams cad kyi phreng bas yongs su bzung bar byin gyis brlab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi tshul thams cad nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi dra ba kun nas 'brel bar byin gyis brlab pa dang / 'jig rten
50a3: gyi khams thams cad gos sna tshogs kyi lda ldis kun nas yongs su blangs shing bzung bar byin gyis brlab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rin po che sna tshogs kyi lus kyi phreng ba dang lda ldi mang po'i dra
50a4: bas kun nas 'brel par mngon par bsgrub pa dang / zhing thams cad nor bu rin po che dpal gyi 'od gzer gyi lda ldi dang / phreng ba'i dra bas kun nas 'brel bar byin gyi brlab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad
50a5: rin po che rnam par snang ba'i lda ldi dang / dra bas kun tu 'brel bar byin gyis brlab pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gzhi nor bu rin po che seng ge yid du 'ong ba'i phreng ba dang / lnga ldi'i dra bas yongs
50a6: su bzung bar byin gyis brlab pa byed cing / mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang na ba der lhags nas bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der dong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/
50a7: lho phyogs su brtan te/ nor bu rin po che 'gro ba la rnam par snang ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa dang / seng ge'i khri nor bu rin po che phyogs kun tu rnam par snang ba'i pad mo'i snying po can dag mngon par sprul te/ rin po
50a8: che thams cad kyi me tog gi dra ba'i rgyan gyis kun nas brgyan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lus su byin gyis brlabs nas skyil mo krung bcas te 'khod do/ / nub phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho sangs

50b1: rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol gyi 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che'i ri rab rnam par snang ba'i rgyal mtshan mar ma zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbyings kyi migo/ sgron ma'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas byang chub sems dpa' dpal kun nas 'phags pa'i gzing dri ma bya byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho brjod du pad pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang /

50b4: sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rgyan par gang ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad spos kha dog sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med
50b5: pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rgyas par gang ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad bdug spos kha dog dang dri du ma dang ldan pa'i ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba
50b6: snyed kyis rgyas par gang ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad spos kha dog sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rgyas par gang ba dang /
50b7: chos gyi dbyings thams cad nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po mdangs 'byung bas thams cad kyi rdul gyi kha dog dang 'dra ba'i ri rab kyi snyid sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba stod kyis rgyas par ga
50b8: ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad nor bu rin po che skar ma'i rgyal mtshan 'od kyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs kyi rgyan dang ldan pa'i ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra bsnyed kyis

51a1: rgyas par gang ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad rin po che'i rgyal po rdo rje'i snying po kha dog snga tshogs can/ rgyan rnam pa tha dad pa'i yul dang ldan pa'i ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du
51a2: med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis brgyas par gang ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad nor bu rin po che 'dzam bu'i rin po che 'dzam bu'i chu klung 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du snang ba'i yul dang ldan pa'i
51a3: ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi nang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rgyas par gang ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad nor bu rin po che'i rgyal ba chos kyi dbyings thams cad rab tu snang ba'o /
51a4: rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nas khyab par byin gyis brlab pa dang / sems can gyi khams kyi yul thams cad nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs
51a5: pa thams cad kyi mtshan rab tu snang ba'i ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rgyas par gang ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi nam mkha' rin po che'i rgyal po
51a6: bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi sbyor ba rab tu snang ba yongs su ston cing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i sgra 'byin pa'i ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
51a7: kyis rgyas par gang ba dang / phyogs bcu thams cad rin po che'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po byang chub pa'i 'od dang ldan pa'i ri rab kyi sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul
51a8: shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rgyas par 'gengs pa byed cing / mi mdzod kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang na ba der lhags nas bcom ldan 'das ga na ba der dong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das la phyag

51b1: 'tshal nas/ nub phyogs su brtan te/ khang pa brtsegs pa spos kyi rgyal po thams cad kyi lhun dang ldan pa/ mu tig gi dra bas kun nas khyab pa dang / seng ge'i khri'i nor bu rin po che lha'i dbang po lab tu sna
51b2: ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi pad mo'i snying po can dag mngon par sprul nas/ rin po che gser gyi dra bas kun nas brgyan pa dang / yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che cod pan bcings pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i
51b3: lus su byin kyis brlab nas/ / sbrul mo krung bcas te 'khod do// byang phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol gyi
51b4: ' jig rten gyi khams rin pa ra gis yongs su snang ba zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbyings nam mkha'i dpal rnam par snang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi 'ang nas byang chub sems dpa'
51b5: c hags pa med pa'i dpal gyi rgyal po zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig du bcom ldan 'das des gnang nas
51b6: 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mchod nas 'phags te/ nam mkha'i dbyings rin po che'i snam bu'i sprin gyi rgyan gyis brgyan par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyangs rin po che'i gos kha dog ser po dang /
51b7: mdog ser po'i sprin gyi rgyan gyis rgyan par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyangs rin po che'i gos spos sna tshogs kyi dri zhim por bya ba'i sprin gyi char rab tu 'bab brgyan gyis brgyan par
51b8: byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings rin po che'i nyi ma'i rgyal mtshan gyi sprin gyi rgyan gyis brgyan par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings nor bu rin po cho gsar gyi mdog shin tu 'bar

52a1: ba'i sprin gyi rgyan gyis brgyan par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha' dbyings nor bu'i rgyal po rin po che 'bar ba'i gos kyi sprin gyi rgyan gyis brgyan par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha'i
52a2: dbyings nor bu rin po che skar ma thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan gyis sna tshogs su gyur pa'i gos kyi sprin gyi rgyan gyis brgyan par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings phyogs bcu kun nas nor bu rin
52a3: pa che'i snam bu khro bo'i rdo ltar snang ba'i sprin gyis yongs su rgyas par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha' dbyings phyogs bcu kun nas rin po che'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba'i dpal rab tu 'bar ba /
52a4: dang ldan pa'i gos kyi sprin gyis yongs su rgyas par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings phyogs bcu kun nas nor bu'i rgyal po snang ba shin tu gsal bas phyogs kyi dbyings rnam par snang ba'i
52a5: gos kyi sprin gyis yongs su rgyas par byin gyis brlab pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings rin po che'i rgyal po rgya mtsho'i rgyan gyi gos kyi sprin gyis kun nas yog par byin gyis brlab par byed cing / mi mdzod
52a6: kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang na ba der lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der dong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ byang phyogs su brtan te/ rin po che'i rgyal po

52b1: r gya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol gi 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che thams cad du mdzes pa'i rin po che 'od gzer gyi dra ba rab tu 'gyed pa zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs

52b7: rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad rin po che'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin gyis kun nas khebs par byin gyis brlab pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad rdo rje'i khang pa brtsegs
52b8: pa'i sprin gyis kun nas khebs par byin gyis brlab pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad gser gyi khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin gyis kun nas khebs par byin gyis brlab pa dang /

53a1: 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad gos kyi khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin kyis kun nas khebs par byin gyis brlab pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'byab klas pa thams cad pang
53a2: mo'i brtsegs pa'i sprin gyis kun nas khebs pa dbyin gyis brlab pa byed cing / mi mdzod kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang na ba der lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der dong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas bcom
53a3: ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas byang dang shar gyi phyogs mtshams su brten te/ nor bu rin po che'i khang pa brtsegs pa sgo chos kyi dbyings thams cad la mngon par lta ba dang / seng ge'i khri rin po che'i rgyal
53a4: po spos mtshungs pa med pa'i pad mo'i snying po can dag mngon par sprul nas rin po che'i khang pa'i me tog gi dra ba yongs su brgyan pa dang / rin po che'i rgyal po mdzod sna tshogs kyi dra ba'i cong pan bcings
53a5: pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lus su byin kyis brlabs nas skyil mo krung bcas te 'khod do/ / shar dang lho phyogs mtshams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med
53a6: p a'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol gyi 'jig rten gyi khams spos kyi sprin gyis brgyan pa'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa klu dbang gi rgyal po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas byang chub sems
53a7: d pa'i chos kyi 'od 'gro dang ldan pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig du bcom ldan 'das des gnang nas
53a8: 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho de nas 'phags te/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gser gyi kha dog lta bu'i sprin gyis kun tu khyab pa bya ba dang /

53b1: nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad rin po che mtha' yas pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin gyis kun tu khyab par bya ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i mdzod spu'i kha dog gi
53b2: 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin gyis kun tu khyab par bya ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad ni rin po che sna tshogs kyi kha dog lta bu'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin kyis kun tu khyab par bya ba dang / nam
53b3: mkha'i dbyings thams cad pa ra'i snying po'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin gyis kun tu khyab par bya ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad nor bu'i rgyal po rin po che'i shing g.yal ga'i dkyil 'khor la
53b4: ba'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin gyis kun tu khyab pa bya ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug tor lta bu'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyis kun tu khyab par bya ba dang / nam
53b5: mkha'i dbyings thams cad 'jam bu'i chuklu ge gsar gyi 'dog lta ba'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin gyis kun tukhyab thub dang / rnamama'a'i dbyings thams cad nyi ma'i khadag / bu bod kyi dkyil
53b6: 'khor gyi sprin gyis kun tu khyab par bya ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad zla ba dang / skar ma'i tshogs kyi kha dog lta bu'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin gyis kun tu khyab par byed cing / mi mdzad kyi 'jig
53b7: rten gyi khams gang na bder lhags nas bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der dong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ shar dang lho'i phyogs mtshams su brtan te/ rin po
53b8: tshe rdul dang bral zhing rnam par snang ba phun sum tshogs pa'i me tog gi khang pa brtsegs pa dang / seng ge'i khri rin po che'i seng ge'i rdo rje'i pad mo'i snying po can dag mngon par sprul nas nor bu'i rgyal po rin

54a1: po che'i 'od gzer rab tu 'bar ba'i dra bas yongs su brgyan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lus su byin gyis rlabs nas skyil mo bkrung bcas te 'khod do/ / lho dang nub kyi phyogs mtshams kyi 'jig
54a2: r ten gyi khams rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol gyi 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che'i nyi mi rab tu snang ba'i snying po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi 'khor lo'i
54a3: y e shes kun tu sdang ba'i rgyal po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas byang chub sems dpa' bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par 'thor ba'i ye shes rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi
54a4: khams rgya mtsho brjod pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu bcom ldan 'das des gnang nas/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho de nas 'phags te/ ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas me tog 'od 'phro ba'i
54a5: sprin nam mkha'i dbyangs ltar yangs pa rab tu dgye ba dang / ba spu'i bug thams cad nas rol mo'i 'od 'phro ba'i sprin nam mkha'i ltar yangs pa rab tu dgye ba dang / ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas nor bu rin po che'i 'od
54a6: 'phro ba'i sprin nam mkha'i dbyings ltar yangs pa rab tu dgye ba dang / ba spu'i bug thams cad nas rin po che'i gos 'od 'phro ba spos dang / bdug spos sna tshogs kyis rnam par bdugs pa'i sprin nam mkha
54a7: dbyings ltar yangs pa rab tu dgye ba dang / ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas klus rnam par sprul pa'i glog 'od 'phro ba'i nam mkha'i dbyings ltar yangs pa rab tu dgye ba dang / ba spu'i bug thams cad nas nor bu
54a8: rin po che rnam par sdang ba'i 'od gzer bkye ba'i sprid nam mkha'i dbyings ltar yangs pa rab tu dgye ba dang / ba spu'i bug thams cad nas nor bu rin po che gser rab tu 'bar ba 'od 'phro ba'i sprin nam mkha'i dbyings ltar yangs pa

54b1: rab tu dgye ba dang / ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas rin pa che'i rgyal po dpal gyi snying po 'bar ba 'od 'phro ba'i sprin nam mkha'i dbyings ltar yangs pa rab tu dgye ba dang / ba spu'i brag thams cad nas na

54b3: rten gyi khams gang na ba der lhags nas bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der dong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams su brtan te/ nor bu rin po che

55a1: gnang nas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho de nas 'phags te/ mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po thams cad dang / ba spu'i sgo thams cad dang / lus thams cad nas dus gsum du de bzhin gshegs pa//
55a2: de thams cad kyi sku gzugs brnyan gyi sprin kun tu dgye ba dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po thams cad dang pa spu'i sgo thams cad dang / lus thams cad nas dus gsum du gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku
55a3: gzugs brnyan gyi sprin kun tu dbye ba dang / mtshan dang dpe' byad bzang po thams cad dang / ba spu'i sgo thams cad dang / lus thams cad nas dus gsum du zung bas byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi las kyi
55a4: gzugs brnyan gyi sprid kun tu dgye ba dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po thams cad dang / ba spu'i sgo thams cad dang / lus thams cad nas dus gsum du gshegs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams
55a5: cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi lus kyi gzugs brnyan gyi sprin kun tu dgye ba dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po thams cad dang / ba spu'i sgo thams cad dang / lus thams cad nas dus gsum

56a1: gyi/ 'jig rten gyi khams de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes nam mkha' lta bur chags pa med pa'i dpal rgyal
56a2: m tshan rgyal po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas byang chub sems dpa' bsgrib pa thams cad rnam par 'thor ba'i ye shes kyis rnam par rol pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho brjod du med

56a4: nges pa'i tshig mngon par bsgrub pa rgya mtsho rab tu brjod pa dang / dus gsum gyi byang chub sems dpa' thams cad 'byung ba'i tshul rgya mtsho'i sprin gyi 'brug sgra rab tu bsgrag pa dang / byang chub sems
56a5: dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i dbyangs rab tu bsgrag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i tshul rgya mtsho'i
56a6: sprin gyi sgra rab tu bsgrag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor zhing thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i dbyings rab tu bsgrag pa dang /
56a7: byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi yang dag par bsgrub pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i dbyangs rab tu bsgrag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad snying po byang chub tu gshegs pa

56b1: 'khor lo skor ba dang / mdo sde'i tshul nad ming rgya mtsho'i dbyangs kyi sprin gyi 'brug sgra bsgrag pa dang / 'gro ba 'dug pa thams cad ngas la bab pa'i 'khor los 'dul ba'i chos kyi tshul dang thabs kyi sgrarab tu
56b2: bslab pa dang / ye shes thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir smon lam ji ltar btab pa dang / dge ba'i khyad par dang dus dang thabs dang / chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho'i dbyangs rab tu bsgrag par byed cing / mi
56b3: mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang na bder lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der dong ste/ 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ 'og gi phyogs su brtan te/ de bzhin
56b4: gshegs pa thams cad kyi gzhal med 'ang gzugs brnyan rab tu snang ba rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi mdzod khang pa brtsegs pa dang / seng ge'i khri rin po che thams cad kyi gzugs kyi

57a1: nas/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtshad nas 'phags te/ mtshan dang dpe pyad bzang pa thams cad dang / bslal sa thams cadang / lus thams cad dang / yan la ga shing lag thams
57a2: dang / tshig gi lam thams cad dang / gos dang slad yogs thams cad nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor thams cad dang / bdag dang bcom ldan 'das rnam par sngang mdzad dang / sngon gi mtha'i myang thug pa

57a4: kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad na bzhugs pa rnams kyi sngon gyi sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa mdzad pa dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho dang / len pa dang sbyin pa'i dngos po thams cad kyi gzugs

57a6: dang / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho dag kyang rab tu snang bar yongs su bstan pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa'i yan lag dang nying
57a7: lag thams cad 'thub pa rab tu bstan pa dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar gyur pa yongs su bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi brtson 'grus dang drag shul
57a8: dang rnam par gnon pa dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar gyur pa yongs su bstan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bsam gtan rgya mtsho yongs su tshol zhing rab tu

57b1: bsgrub pa dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar gyur pa yongs su bstan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshul yongs su bsgrub cing / chos yongs su
57b2: tshore ba dang / ldan pa dang / bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong zhing shin tu zhe non pa'i lus dang po'i gzugs brnyan rnam par dmigs par bya bas sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar gyur pa yongs
57b3: su bstan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mthong zhing dga' ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi lam la 'gro ba thams cad mngon par mos par byed pa dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rtsam
57b4: rab tu snang bar gyur pa yongs su bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam rgya mtsho mngon par bsgrub pa'i sgo yongs su dag pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar
57b5: gyur pa yongs su bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rab tu grub pa dang / rnam par dman pa dang / rnam par dag par byas pa dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor brgya
57b6: mtsho rab tu snang bar gyur pa yongs su bstan pa dang / chos kyi dbyings rgya chen po rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad kyi sprin gyis rgyas par bkang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dkyil
57b7: 'khor dang ldan pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar gyur pa yongs su bstan par byed cing / mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang na ba der lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga na ba der dong ste/
57b8: 'khor dang bcas pas bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ steng gi phyogs su brtan te/ rdo rje'i dbang po sna tshogs thams cad kyis rgyan gyi snying po can gyi khang pa brtsegs pa dang / seng ga'i khri rdo rje dang

58a1: i n dra ni la'i pad mo'i snying po can dag mngon par sprul nas sa nor bu'i rgyal po rin po che thams cad rab tu 'bar ba'i dra bas kun rdzas brgyan pa dang rin po che'i rgyal po dus gsum du de bzhin gshes
58a2: pa'i mtshan dbyangs su sgrog pa'i phreng ba rab tu 'phyang ba dang / mgo la rin po che'i cod pan thogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' lus su byin gyis brlabs nas skyil mo krung bcas te 'khod do//
58a3: sangs rgyas rbang gcad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// bam po lnga pa/ byang chub sems dpa' nga dag thams cad kyang 'khor dang bcas par byang chub sems dpa' kun du bzang
58a4: po'i spyod pa dang smon lam gyis byed pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi zhabs kyi drung nas zhal de la pa/ ye shes yongs su dag pa'i mig dang ldan pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor
58a5: lo dang / mdo sde'i tshul gyi gsung rgya mtsho la rna ba yongs su gzhol ba byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dbang bab tu thob par bya ba la dam pa'i pha rol tu bgrong bar phyin pa'i mchog/ thob pa/ de bzhin
58a6: gshegs pa thams cad kyi drung du 'dong pa/ skad cig skad cig du yongs su bstan par rnam par 'phrul pas byung ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad lus gcig gis rgyas par dgang pa'i yul dang ldan pa/
58a7: de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du lus mngon par 'byung zhing rnam par snang ba/ rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad khams gcig du snang zhing khongs
58a8: su chud par yang dag par ston pa'i lus dang ldan pa 'gro ba thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'dul ba'i dus la sdod par gzhol ba/ de bzhin ga sheg pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i sprin gyi

58b1: 'brug sgra bsku'i bu ga thams cad nas rab tu sgrog pa'i yul dang ldan pa/ sems can gyi khams thams cad sgyu ma lta bur yongs su shes pa rab tu thob pa// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
58b2: kyi mig yor lta bur khong du chud pa/ srid pa'i rgyung du skye ba thams cad rmi lam lta bus shes pas byung ba las dang rnam par smin pa thams cad gzugs brnyan lta bur shes pas rnam par dag pa/
58b3: shes mngon par grub pa thams cad smig d+hA ba lta bur mngon par shes pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam blas pa thams cad sprul pa lta bur khong du chud pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang ya
58b4: shes kyi snang ba rab tu thob pa/ mi 'jigs pa'i khyu mchog dang / seng ge'i nga ros rnam par gnon pa/ so so yang dag par rig pa mi zad pa'i rgya mtshor zhugs pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi skad rgya mtshor
58b5: zhugs pa/ chos kyi nges pa'i tshig gi ye shes rab tu thob pa/ chos kyi dbyings dang nam mkha' ltar chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul dang ldan pa/ chos thams cad la bsgribs pa myed pa'i ye
58b6: shes rab tu thob pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi mngon par shes pa la ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par dkrug pa'i brtson 'grus dang ldan
58b7: pa dus gsum thams cad shes pa'i stobs la rab tu gnas pa/ chos thams cad la ye shes pa sgribs pa med pa rab tu thob pa/ gnas med pas nam mkha'i spyod yul dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen
58b8: pa'i sa len pa myed pa/ nam mkha' la bu'i brtson 'grus dang ldan pa/ srid pa thams cad mi dmigs pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul can/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi tshul rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/

59a1: 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad tha mi dad pa'i ye shes kyi sgor zhugs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad gcig nas gcig tu gzung ba'i rnam par 'phrul pas byung ba dang 'jig
59a2: rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad du skyes pa'i lus yongs su ston pa/ / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi dbyibs phra ba dang / rgya che ba dang yangs dang / dog pa sna tshogs rab tu rtogs pa
59a3: shin tu phra bar zhing rgya chen po yang dag par gzung ba'i ye shes khong du chud pa/ dmigs pa rgya chen po shin tu phra bar shes pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang sems kyi skad cig la
59a4: 'grogs pa rab tu thob pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi ye shes kyi lus dang ldan pa/ phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad du mgo rmongs pa med pa'i ye shes rab tu thob pa'i//
59a5: sems kyi skad cig gis phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad du rnam par 'phrul pas rgyas par 'gengs pa sha stag ste// de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi brlabs kyis de lta bu'i yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan
59a6: pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sha stag gis 'dze ta'i chal thams cad yongs su rgyas par gyur kyang / nyan thos chen po sha ri'i bu dang / me'u 'gal gyi bu dang 'od srung chen po dang / nam 'gru dang rab 'byor
59a7: dang / 'gag med dang / mos pa dang / ka ta'i bu dang / byams gang gi bul stsogs pas 'dze ta'i tshal na 'khong bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa de dag ma mthong ngo // sangs rgyas kyi bko/
59a8: pa de dag dang / sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par rol pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul dang / sangs rgyas kyi mda' chen po dang / sangs rgyas spyod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang /

59b1: sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa yang ma mthong ngo // byang chub sems dpa' yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa de dag dang / byang chub sems
59b2: dpa' kun nas 'ongs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun nas 'dus pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun nas tshogs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' nye bar 'ongs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnam par
59b3: 'phrul ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshe 'phrul dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang / byang chub sems dpa'i phyogs su 'khod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i seng ge'i the bkod pa dang /
59b4: byang chub sems dpa'i khang pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par brtse ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par lta ba dang / byang chub sems
59b5: dpa'i rnam par bsgyings pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par gnon pa dang / byang chub sems dpa di bzhin gshegs pa mchod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lung bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yongs
59b6: su smin par gyur pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sngon du 'dor ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi lus rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi lus yongs su rdzogs pa dang / byang chub sems
59b7: dpa'i sngon lam gyi lus rnam par dmigs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs kyi lus yongs su grub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i mtshan phun sum tshogs pa yongs su dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i
59b8: 'od kyi dkyil 'khor kha dog mtha' yas pa'i bkod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'od gzer gyi de ba rab tu 'gyed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sprul pa'i sprin kun tu 'gyed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i phyogs

60a1: kyi dra ba rgyas par 'gengs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor rnam par sprul pa yang ma mthong ngo // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ dge ba'i rtsa ba myi mtshungs pa'i phyir te/ de dag gis ni sngon
60a2: sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa mthong ba'i rgyur 'gyur ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bstsags so/ / de dag la ni sngon sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams su gtogs pa'i
60a3: sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi yon tan dang / bkod pa yongs su dag pa yang dag par bstan pa mdzad do// de dag la ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag
60a4: par brjod pa ma mdzad do/ / de dag gis ni sngon 'khor ba 'khor ba'i tshe sems can rnams bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par bskul ba ma byas so// de dag gis ni gzhan gyi sems kyi
60a5: rgyud la byang chub tu sems bskyed pa rab tu bzhag pa ma byas so/ / de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung rgyud mi gcad pa'i phyir zhugs pa ma yin no// de dag ni sems can thams cad yongs su bsdu ba'i phyir
60a6: brtson pa ma yin no/ / de dag gis ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par bskul ba mi byas so// de dag gis ni sran 'khor bar 'khor ba'i tshe/ 'gro ba thams cad las khyad par du 'phags
60a7: pa'i ye shes kyi sa la dmigs pa ma byas so/ / de dag gis ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'gyur ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba nye bar bstsags pa ma byas so// de dag gis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'jig rten las 'das
60a8: pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su ma bsgrubs so/ / de dag gis ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa thams cad du rnam par 'phrul pa'i mngon par shes pa khong du ma chud do// de dag gis ni byang chub sems dpa' mig

60b1: gal ma gyis rnam par dmigs par bya ba 'jig rten las 'das pa thun mong ma yin pa'i byang chub du dmigs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam chen po las byung ba khong du ma chud do/ / nyan thos
60b2: dang rang sangs rgyas kun gyis ni byang chub sems dpa'i 'du shes sna tshogs yongs su 'dzin lags kyis/ rnam par dmigs pa thun mong ma yin pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs las blang ba'i/
60b3: ma'i rnam pa'i chos nyid kyis grub pa/ byang chub sems dpa' 'du shes sna tshogs yongs su 'dzin pa byin gyis rlob pa/ byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i shugs chen po rnam par 'phel bar byed pa khong du ma chung
60b4: do/ / de bas na nyan thos chen po mchog gi zung dang / bzang po'i gzung la stsogs pa de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa de me mthong myi mos so// mi shes so// bong du mi chung ngo // mi rtogs so//
60b5: rig go/ yid myi ches so// me sems so// rnam par mi lta'o// rtogs par mi lta'o// nges par mi sems so// nye bar mi sems so// de ci'i 'phyir zhe na/ don sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul te nyan thos kyi
60b6: spyod yul ma yin no/ / de bas na nyan thos chen po de dag 'dze ta'i cha la de nyid na 'khod kyang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa de dag pa mthong ngo // de dag la de dang 'thun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba med do//
60b7: de dag gis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa de dag mthong du de la bu'i ye shes kyi mig rnam par mi dag go/ dmyigs pa chud dul rgya chen po 'byin gyi rlabs kyis 'jug tu ting nge 'dzin de lta bu med do//
60b8: de dag shes pa dang / khong du chud par bya ba 'am/ rtogs par bya ba'am/ rgyas par dgar bar bya ba 'am/ 'jug par bya ba 'am/ rnam par lta ba'apa/ nyams su mod par bya ba 'am/ gnan pa 'am/ rnam par

61a1: gnan pa 'am/ gzhan gyis thos par bya ba 'am/ bstan par bya ba 'am/ smos par bya ba 'am/ yang dag par bstan par bya ba 'am/ bstabs par bya ba 'am/ sbyin par bya ba 'am/ de la
61a2: sems can rnams yongs su bskul bar bya ba 'am/ sbyar bar bya ba 'am/ rab tu 'god par bya ba 'am/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i chos nyid la sems can dgod par byar yang de dag la de lta bu'i rnam/
61a3: par thar pa med do/ de lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul med do// de lta bu'i khyu mchog gi mthu med do// de lta bu'i stobs med do// de lta bu'i gnas med do// de lta bu'i 'du shes med do// de lta bu'i mig gi mthu med do
61a4: de lta bu'i ye shes med de/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de dag ni de ltar nyan thos kyi thag pa las byung ba nyan thos kyi lam gyis yongs su grub pa/ nyan thos kyi spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs pa
61a5: nyan thos kyi 'bras bu la gnas pa/ bden pa snang ba shes pas nges par rtog pa/ yang dag pa'i mtha' la gnas pa/ shin tu zhi ba'i mthar thug pa/ snying rje chen po'i bsam pa med// 'jig rten thams
61a6: cad la mi lta mi sdod pa/ rang gi don grub pa dag ste/ de dag ni 'dze ta'i tshal de nyid du kun nas 'dus te 'khod la/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan snga dang g.yas g.yos dang / snam na bcom ldan 'das la
61a7: mngon tu lta bar gnas kyang / 'dze ti'i tshal dar sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa de dag mthong bar ma gyur to// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yang dag par ma bsgrubs pa dang /
61a8: thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yang dag par ma bsdus pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la yang dag par ma zhugs pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la smon lam yang dag par ma/

61b1: btang ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mngon par ma bsgrub pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su ma bsgoms pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes ma sbyangs pa de dag gis ni
61b2: de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam par 'phrul pa de la 'jug cing rtogs par bya ba 'am/ blta zhing khong du chud par bya bar mi nus so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs dang
61b3: ldan pa rnams kyi mig gi lam gyis blta ba yin gyi/ nyan thos kyi mig gis blta ba ma yin no// de bas na nyan thos chen po de dag 'dze ta'i tshal de nyid ni 'khod kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par
61b4: 'phrul pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i kun nas 'dus pa yang mthong bar ma gyur to// de'ang 'di lta ste dper na/ gang gA'i
61b5: chu klung chen po'i ngogs pha rol chu rol du yi dgas bkres pa dang / skom pas rab tu mnan pa gcer pa/ gos med pa/ lus kyi mdog dang / kha dog tshig cing 'tshungs pa/ rlung dang nyi mas bskams
61b6: pa/ bya rog mang pos gtse pa/ spyang ku dang / was mtho ba tsam pa/ brgya stong mang po kun nas 'dus kyang / 'ga' 'ga'i chu klung chen po mi mthong ste/ sgrib pa'i las kyis bsgribs pa'i phyir la las ni
61b7: bskams te chu med par mthong ngo / / la las ni thal bas yongs su gang bar mthong ngo // de bzhin du nyan thos chen po gnas brtan de dag 'dze ta'i tshal de nyid na 'khod kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
61b8: dang mi 'thun pa'i phyogs ma rig pa'i ling thog gis mig kun nas kheb pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i mthus yongs su ma bzung ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam

62a1: par 'phrul de dag ma mthong ma shes so/ / 'di lta ste dper na 'dun ma chen po 'dus pa'i skye bo mang po'i dbus su mi la la zhig gnyid kyis myos te/ log par gyur nas/ de gnyid kyis
62a2: log pa'i mi lam du gnas te de nyid na lha'i gong rdal brgya byin gyi gnas bltan mdzes pa dang / ri rab kyi steng shing dang bcas pa/ bza' shing gi ra ba'i 'khor dang bcas pa/ lha'i bu mo bye ba
62a3: khrag khrig brgya stong gis gang ba/ lha'i bu khrag khrig brgya phrag stong snyed gnas pa na lha'i me tog sna tshogs kyis yongs su gang ba dang / yid bzhin gyi shing lha rdzas kyi gos dang mu tig gi phreng ba dang / rin po
62a4: che'i rgyan dang / se mo do sna tshogs mang po 'byin pa dang / lha rdzas kyi sil snyan rnam pa sna tshogs rlung gis yongs su bskyod cing sgra dbyangs yid du 'ong la snyam pa 'byin pa'i sil snyan gyi shing mang po dang / dga' ba'i
62a5: rtsed mo bkod pa rnam pa sna tshogs mthong bar gyur la/ lha'i bu mo mang pos glu blangs pa dang / lha rdzas kyi rol mo byas pa'i sgra yid du 'ong zhing snyan pa thos par gyur to// bdag nyid kyang de na 'dug pa snyam byed la
62a6: lha rdzas kyi bkod pas klubs pa'i gnas de dag thams cad mthong bar gyur gyi na za tshogs mang po de dag gis gnas de nyid na 'khod bzhin du mi mthong / ye shes khang du mi chung ngo // de ci 'byor zhe na/ den skyes
62a7: brag nyid kyis log pa de nyid kyi rmi lam gyis blta ba yin gyi/ gnas de nyid na 'khor kyang skye bo mang po de dag gis blta ba ma yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / 'jig rten gyi dbang po byang chub
62a8: la mngon par mos pa de dag sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs rgya chen po dang / rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs ma nor bar shin tu bsags pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du smon las shin tu mngon par bsgrubs pa dang

62b1: de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan thams cad la shin tu zhugs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam bkod pa chen po dang ldan pa la shin tu gnas pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi chos nyid dang / yan lag
62b2: rnam pa thams cad du shin tu rdzogs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams cad kyi
62b3: ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su gnon pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par spyod pa thams cad la rnam par rtse ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul thams cad la
62b4: chags pa med par rnam par spyod pas bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba ded dag dang / / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par rol pa de dag mthong zhing khong du chud pa nyams su myong bar gyur
62b5: kyang nyan thos chen po mtshan gau zung dang / bzang ba'i bzung las sogs pa de dag la byang chub sems dpa' mig med pas mthong bar 'gyur/ shes par mgyur to// 'dis ste dper na/ re'i rgyal po la ba can
62b6: sman kye 'brang gnas kyis gang ba la bsngags dang / rig sngags dang / sman gyi tshul dang / blang ba'i rgyus shes shing rigs sngags grub pa'i skyes bu gnas pa/ sman gyi cho ga thams cad shes pa sman blang ba'i las
62b7: byed kyang ri ba'i dbang po de nyid la gnas pa'i phyugs dang / ba lang dang ra lug 'tsho ba dang / rngon pa dang de ma yin pa'i mi sman gyi tshul mi shes pa gzhan dag gyis/ sman de dag gi cho ga dang / sman gyi
62b8: ro dang mthu dang yon tan dang byin dang / thabs dang 'phrad pa mi shes so// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi yul la zhugs pa byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i

63a1: sum gyis byung ba/ de dgags de bzhin gshegs pa'i tang mdzin gyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i yul de dag ma tha yang nyanams can pa mchog gi zung dang / bzang po'i zung bsags par dag cas/
63a2: lamatshim par gyur pa/ gzhan gyi dgas pa lal bar gzhags/ btang byams can de dga' tshos de nyid na gnas kyang / tshe 'di la bde bar spyod pas 'di shing dga' bar gnas pa/ zhus par de bzhin
63a3: gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i yul de dag khong du mi chud do/ / 'di lta ste dper na/ sa chen po rin po che thams cad kyi 'byung gnas pun supa tshogs pa/ gter brgya stong du mas gang
63a4: rin po che sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pas yongs su gang ba 'di la'ang rin po che'i 'byung gnas dang / gter gyi rgyus la mkhas shing bya ba' mi rin po che brtag pa'i gtsug lag gi ma blo shin tu byang
63a5: ba gter gyi gtsug lag dang / rgyus dang / don rtags kyi nom par lobs pa/ bsod nams rgya chen po'i stobs kyis brtan pa de dag de las rin po che ci 'dod par blangs shing / bdag kyang yongs su
63a6: tshim par byed pa dang / ma la legs par rim gror byed/ bu po smos kyang legs par gso bar byed cing / de ma yin pa'i sems can rgan pa dang / na ba dang / dbul ba dang / nyam nyes pa dang / kha zas
63a7: dang / / gos kyis mi 'byor pa rnams la sdud cing khyab par mgo ba sha byed la/ nor gyi dga' ba sna tshogs nyams su myong bar byed kyang / sems can rin po che'i 'byung gnas dang / gter gyi rgyus mi shes pa
63a8: bsod nams ma byas pa/ rin po che la shes pa'i mig yongs su ma dag pa/ de dag de nyid na 'khod kyang / rin po che'i 'thung gnas dang / rin po che'i gter de dag khong du mi chud mi shes pas rin po che'ang blang du

63b1: mad do/ / rin po che'i don kyang byar med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa la zhugs pa la ye shes kyi mig shin tu rnam par dag pa de bzhin gshegs
63b2: pa'i ye shes kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa la zhugs pa/ de dag 'dze ta'i tshal na 'khod cing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa de dag mthong la chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug cing / ting nge 'dzin gyi phyag rgya
63b3: yongs su sgrub ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa mchod pa dang / rim grol brtson zhing dam pa'i chos yongs su bzung ba la mngon par brtson te/ bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhis sems can de dag yongs su sdud kyang nyan thos
63b4: chen po de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs chen po kun nas 'dus pa de lta bu'ang ma mthong ma shes so// 'di lta ste dper na/ skyes bu la la zhig
63b5: mig gnyis gos kyis bkab ste/ rin po che'i gling du phyin par gyur na/ des rin po che'i gling der phan tshun 'gro ba dang / 'greng ba dang 'dug pa dang nyal ba byas kyang rin po che'i 'byung gnas de mi mthong ngo //
63b6: rin po che'i shing dang gos kyi rin po che dang / spos rin po che dang / rin po che thams cad kyang mi mthong la/ rin po che de dag gi spyod yul lam/ rin thad dam/ yongs su spyod pa'i rgyus kyang mi shes pas
63b7: de ni rin po che de dag len kyang mi len la/ rin po che'i don kyang nyams su myong bar mi byed do// gang gi mig la bsgribs pa med pa de dag gis ni de dag thams cad mthong zhing shes so// de bzhin du byang
63b8: chub sems dpa' chos rin po che'i gling chen por phyin pa de dag gis bla na med pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rin po che'i 'jig rten thams cad kyi rgyan tu gyur pa mngon tu gyur te/ 'dze ta'i tshal na

64a1: b zhugs shing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i yongs su ston pa mthong yang nyan thos chen po de dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs kyi drung de nyid na gnas shing
64a2: spyod kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi yul rnam par 'phrul pa'i cho 'phrul de dag ma mthong ngo // byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs mang po de lta bu'i rin po che'i 'byung gnas chen po yang mthong bar
64a3: ma gyur to/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / cho 'phrul pa'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa de dag ltar thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mi 'thun pa'i phyogs
64a4: kyi ma rig pa'i gos kyis ye shes kyi mig bkab pa de dag la byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi mig yongs su dag pa de lta bu med do/ / de dag gri chos kyi dbyings gci ga nas gcig tu rgyud pa la 'jug pa de lta
64a5: bu khong du mi chud do/ / 'di lta ste dper na/ mig yongs su dag pa rdul dang bral bas rab tu snang ba dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i rab rib dang / mun pa thams cad dang mi 'grogs pa yod de de mi la la zhig gis thob
64a6: par gyur na/ de rdul dang bral bas rab tu snang ba dang / ldan pa'i mig yongs su dag pa dang ldan pas mtshan mo mun pa'i mun nag shin tu gnag par gyur pa'i nang na sems can bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong kun
64a7: nas 'dus pa dang / cho ga dang spyod lam rnam pa sna tshogs dang ldan zhing mun pa'i rab rib kyis mig yongs su 'khrugs par gyur pa'i mi'i khrod na 'dug cing rnam par rgyu la phan tshun 'gro ba dang / 'greng
64a8: ba dang spyod lam rnam pa sna tshogs kyis spyod kyang ma de dag gis skyes bu spyod lam sna tshogs kyis spyod pa de mi mthong mi shes so/ / skyes bu des ni 'gro ba'i tshogs chen po spyod lam dang cho ga sna tshogs

64b1: kyis rnam par spyod pa/ phyogs tha dad du mngon par bltas pa/ dbyibs kyi rnam pa tha dad pa kha dog gi rnam pa tha dad pa dmigs pa'i tshul tha dad pa thams cad kyang mi mthong ba med do// de bzhin du de
64b2: bzhin gshegs pa byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyi 'khor mnga' ba/ rnam par dag cing chags pa mi mnga' ba'i spyan dang ldan pas 'jig rten thams cad mkhyen cing gzigs te/ sangs rgyas kyi ting nge
64b3: 'dzin gyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul chen po bstan pa mdzad kyang nyan thos chen po de dag gi de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes dang ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par sprul pa'i cho 'phrul chen po de
64b4: dag mthong bar ma gyur to/ / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i tshogs chen po de lta bu yang mthong bar ma gyur to// 'di lta ste dper na/ dge slong la la zhig skye bo mang po'i tshogs kyi dbus su sas
64b5: khyab pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs pa 'am/ chus byab pa 'am/ mes khyab pa 'am/ rlung gis khyab pa 'am/ sngon pos khyab pa 'am/ ser pos khyab pa 'am/ dmar pos khyab pa dang / dkar pos
64b6: khyab pa 'am/ lhas khyab pa 'am/ sems can sna tshogs kyi lus kyis khyab pa 'am/ sgra dbyangs kun gyis khyab pa'am/ dmigs pa thams cad kyis khyab pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na 'gro ba
64b7: mang po'i tshogs de dag gis chu'i phung po de mi mthong ngo / / me'i snang ba de yang mi mthong ngo // sems can sna tshogs kyi lus kyis khyab pa dang / dmigs pa thams cad kyis khyab pa'i bar du yang mi mthong ste/ ting nge
64b8: 'dzin de la snyoms par zhugs shing rnam par spyod pa rnams ni ma gtogs so/ / de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pas sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi yul gyi rnam par sprul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa de dag yongs

65a1: su bstan pa mdzad na nyan thos chen po de dag gis mthang zhing shes par mgyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' da bzhin gshegs pa'i lam la zhugs pa de dag gas na bzhin gshegs pa
65a2: yul de dag mthong ngo / / khong du chud do// 'di lta ste dper na/ slu ba grub pa'i mi ni mig gnyis bskus ma thag tu/ skye bo mang po thams cad kyis lus mi mthong ngo // des ni 'gro 'am 'dug gam/ 'greng yang
65a3: rung ste/ 'gro ba mang po thams cad mthong ngo // de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten las 'das par 'gro ba thams cad kyi yul las yongs su 'das pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul du
65a4: zhugs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi mig gis shes par bya ba des 'gro ba thams cad gzigs kyang nyan thos chen po de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa de dag ma mthong ngo // /
65a5: 'di lta ste dper na/ mi'i tsher 'grogs pa'i lha rtag tu rjes su 'brang ba ni/ des mi de mthong yang mis lha de mi mthong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul la zhugs pa/
65a6: byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kun nas 'dus pa chen po'i dbus su sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po yongs su bstan pa mdzad kyang / nyan thos chen po de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam
65a7: par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi 'khor gyi rnam par 'phrul pa de dag kyang ma mthong ngo // ma shes so// 'di lta dper na/ dge slong sems thams cad la dbang
65a8: dam pa'i pha rol tu bgrod par phyin pa'i 'du shes dang / tshor ba 'gog pa la snyoms par zhugs pa ni shes pa med la tshor ba med pas dbang po drug gis kyang bya ba gang yang nyams su mi myong ste/

65b1: mya ngan las 'das pa'ang ma yin la/ 'jig rten gyi tha snyad thams cad gnas de yod kyang snyoms par zhugs pa de nyid kyi byin gyi rlabs dang mthus des mi shes mi mthong ngo // de bzhin du nyan thos chen po
65b2: dag 'jo ta'i tshal de na'ang rnam par spyod la dbang po drug kyang yod de/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang / rnam par 'phrul pa dang / khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / cho 'phrul pa de dag mthong bar ma gyur/
65b3: khong du chud par ma gyur/ shes par ma gyur to// byang chub sems dpa'i cho 'phrul chen po de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa de dag kyang khong du ma chung ma mthong ma shes so// de ci'i
65b4: phyir zhe na/ sangs rgyas kyi yul ni zab cing yangs la tshad med de/ blta bar dka' zhing rtogs par dka' ste/ khong du chud par dka' la 'jig rten thams cad las yongs su 'das pa'o// sangs rgyas
65b5: kyi yul ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ nyan thos dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyis mi 'dus pa'o// de bas na nyan thos chen po de dag 'dze ta'i tshal de nyid na 'khod cing bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs kyi drung
65b6: na spyod kyang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa de dag dang byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs chen po de dag kyang ma mthong ngo // 'dze ta'i tshal 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa
65b7: rnam par dag pa'i yon tan dang / rgyan yongs su 'dus pa de'angam mthong ma shes so// de ni sngon du ma gyur pa'i phyir ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang mdzad kyi smon lam gyi gtsug gi/
65b8: 'od gzer rab tu snang bas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad 'di dag smras so// ltos shig sems can dam pa'i// sangs rgyas byang chub bsam mi khyab// rgyal bas sangs rgyas

66a2: tshangasas/ / cas kyi rgyal bar cha 'phral // cad lda pams kyis mapa// na sa babyu na// des 'jig ta sa// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dag sang/ na
66a3: tu rnam par klubs/ / yang dag sangs rgyas skyed pa yi// chos rab de dag mtshan nyid med// nam 'phrul mtha' dang dbus med pa// tshig gi lam gyis rjod dka' ba'i// nam 'phrul shin tu zab pa dag/
66a4: rgyal bas 'dzi ta'i tshal du bstan// rgyal sras bdag nyid che ba'i rnams// zhing rnams bsam yas bye ba nas// rgyal ba'i zhal ltar mos dga' ste// kun nas 'dus pa'i tshogs la ltos// sman lam
66a5: yongs su phun sum tshogs/ / smon lam spyod pa chags med pa// de dag bsam pa shes par ni// 'jig rten kun gyis mi nus so// de dag sems dang spyad yul dang // snod pa dag kyang nyan zas dang /
66a6: rang rgyal thams cad yongs kyis kyang // rnam pa kun tu shes mi nus// rgyal sras shes rab chen po'i rnams// gzhan gyis thub dka' pham med la// dpa' ba'i rgyal mtshan ma 'dres shing // ye shes
66a7: sa la gzhol gyur pa/ / ting 'dzin dpag tu tshad med la// grangs chen mnyam par bzhag pa'i rnams// chos dbyings thams cad rgyas bkang zhing // rnam par 'phrul pa kun kyang ston// de nas byang chub
66a8: sems dpa' thub par dka' ba'i brtson 'grus kyi shugs kyi rgyal pos sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas nas/ / de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so//

66b1: bsod nams snying po shes rab che// byang chub spyod pa'i tshul rtogs shing // 'jig rten kun la bde byed pa'i// bde gshegs sku las skyes pa ltos// yid gzhungs blo gros mtha' yas shing // shin tu
66b2: mnyam bzhag sems ldan pa/ / mtha' dang dbus me zab pa'o// ye shes rgya cheg spyod yul can// rgyan rab mang pos mdzes byas pa'i// 'jo to' nags tshul rgya che ba// byang chub sems dpas kun
66b3: rgyas shing / / bde gshegs bzhugs pa'i gnas gyur pa// gnas med mi gnas gyur pa'i rnams// phyogs rnams bcu nas kun 'dus te// pad mo'i stan la 'khad pa dag/ rgya mtsho mang la hA/
66b4: bgyis// gnas med len pa med pa'i rnams// spros pa med cing mi rten la// rdul bral chags pa'i sems med pa// chos kyi dbyings la gzhol ba dang // ye shes rgya chen rab dpa' ba// rdo rje'i sems
66b5: ni mi g.yo zhing / / grub pa med pa'i chos rnams la// mya ngan 'da' bar gang ston pa// phyogs bcu'i zhing mang bye ba'i rnams// grangs kyis mi chod kun nas 'dus// yang dag sangs rgyas drung du lhags//
66b6: gnyis kyi 'du shes rnam par spangs// rang 'byung shig kya seng ge'i// rnam par 'phrul pa 'di dag mthong // de'i byin rlabs dam pa yi// byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag lhags// sangs rgyas chos la byed
66b7: pa med/ / chos dbyings gzhi la 'ang de bzhin te// tha snyad tsam du yongs 'byed pa'i// pha rol phyin pa'i rgyal ba'i sras// chos kyi dbyings la dbyer med pa'i// mtha' la thug ma de dag gnas// tshig rnams
66b8: yongs su zad med pas/ / chos la dbye ba'ang rab tu 'byed// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun nas 'phags pa'i gzi brjid rgyal pos/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par

67a1: bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// ltos shig sems can dam pa'i// ye shes dkyil 'khor shin tu yangs// dus dang dus min mkhyen mdzad cing // sems can
67a2: rnams la chos kyang ston/ / mu stegs ldan pa tshogs 'dus pa'i// rgol ba thams cad rab tu 'jom// sems can bsam pa ji bzhin du// rnam par 'phrul pa yongs su ston// phyogs na mi bzhugs
67a3: bde gshegs rnams/ / sangs rgyas yul gyi rjes su bzhud// tshad med pa dang tshad yod pas// thub pa chen po 'das pa min// nyi ma mkha' las 'gro ba ni// nyin par 'grengs pa sa ba med// de
67a4: bzhin mkhyen pas mkhas ston pa/ / dus gsum chags pa med pas brjod// zla ba nya ba'i mtshan mo la// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor 'phags par snang // de bzhin chos dkar yongs rdzogs pa'i/
67a5: mgon po rnams kyang mthong ba yi// bar snang nam mkha'i dbyings 'di las// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor rgyu ba ni// gar yang thogs pa med par 'gro// sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul de bzhin no// ji ltar nam
67a6: mkha'i phyogs rnams kyi/ / zhing rnams kun la mi gnas pa// de bzhin 'jig rten sgron ma'i// sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul shes par bya// ji ltar sa ni 'jig rten na// lus can kun gyi gnas yin pa/
67a7: 'jig rten sgron ma'i 'jig rten na// chos kyi 'khor lo de ltar gnas// ji ltar rlung ni chags med par// mkhas las mgyogs par rab zla ba// de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyid kyang // 'jig rten
67a8: khams su rab tu rgyu/ / ji ltar chu'i phung po la// zhing rnams 'grangs pa kun gnas pa// de bzhin dus gsum sangs rgyas kyang // ye shes tshogs la rab tu gnas// de nas byang chub sems dpa'

67b1: dpal gyi snying po chags pa med pa'i rgyal pos/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i'atshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// ji ltar rdo rje ri dang brag/
67b2: g.yag shin tu mtho yang ba// ji ltar 'jig rten kun skyob pa'o// sangs rgyas mngon par 'phags pas mtho// ji ltar rgya mtsho'i chu chen dang // tshad med rnyog pa med pa ltar// sangs rgyas mthong ba
67b3: 'ang de bzhin te/ / 'jig rten kun gyi skom pa gcod// rgya mtsho chu las 'phags pa yi// ri bo ri rab ci 'dra ba// de bzhin 'jig rten sgron ma yang // chos kyi 'tsho las mngon par 'phags// rin
67b4: chen kun gyi 'byung gnas kyis/ / rgya mtsho rgyas pa ji bzhin du// rang byung ye shes de bzhin te// mi zad skad cig rab mkhyen pa// mgon po'i ye shes shin tu zab// tshad med de bzhin bgrang du med//
67b5: de bas sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul pa// bsam gyis mi khyab tshad med ston// sgyu ma'i mtshan nyid ston pa'i// sgra mkhan mkhas pa ji lta ba// da ltar sangs rgyas mkhyen dbang yang // rnam par 'phrul pa
67b6: rab tu ston/ / yid bzhin nor bu rnam dag pa// bsamangon rdzogs byed ji lta ba// de bzhin bsam pa dag pa la// rgyal ba smon lam rdzogs pa mdzad// 'od snang gsal ba byed pa'i// rin chen
67b7: nam snang ji lta ba/ / de ltar thams cad mkhyen dag pa// 'gro ba'i bsam pa gsal bar mdzad// ji ltar phyogs la mngon lta'o// rin chen zur brgyad rab gnas pa// de bzhin chags med smonas
67b8: yang/ chos dbyings rab tu snang ba mdzad// chu dang rin chen 'od gsal ba// ji ltar dri med chu 'dar byed// de bzhin sangs rgyas mthong bas kyang // 'gro ba'i dbang po dag par 'gyur// de nas byang

68a1: chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyings su smon las rab tu 'phrul pa'i zla ba'i rgyal pos/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ da'atsha tshigs su
68a2: bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ / phyogs 'di oMn dran la yis// kha dog mdog cing byas pa ltar// sangs rgyas mthong bas skye dgu rnams// de bzhin byang chub mdog du 'gyur// sangs rgyas
68a3: rdul phran re re la/ / rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs rnams// tshad med gzhal du med pa ston// byang chub sems dpa' rnam dag mdzad// de ni rmad byung shin tu zab// mtha' yas bsgrub par
68a4: dka' ba ste/ / blo ldan ye shes yul de la// 'jig rten rnams ni 'bab mi nus// byang chub sems dpa' bsgrub don du// rgyan rnams phun sum tshogs pa dang // sangs rgyas tshul gyis rnam
68a5: sbyangs pa'o/ / chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa ston// sangs rgyas zhing rnams mtha' yas pa// blo ldan bskor ba'i sangs rgyas kyis// kun nas gang bar gyur pa yang // rgyal ba de la ston pa mdzad//
68a6: chos kun mda' skyar ston pa ste// shag kya'i khyu mchog skyes par gyur// de'i mtsho 'phrul tshad med pa// 'di dag rtag tu byung ba yin// brtan pa'i spyod pa sna tshogs rnams// tshad med rnam par
68a7: gzigs kun nas/ / rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' yas pa// tshad med gzi can ston pa mdzad// 'jig rten mgon po rgyal sras rnams// chos kyi dbyings la slob pa mdzad// chos rnams thams
68a8: cad yongs la yang / / chags med ye shes spyod yul 'gyur// skyes bu dbang po'i byin brlabs kyis// cho 'phrul brgya dang rab ldan zhing // 'jig rten thams cad rnam spyod pa'i// chos kyi

68b1: 'khor lo rab tu 'khor/ / sems can gtso bo'i yul la yang // ye shes dkyil 'khor yongs sbyangs shing // shes rab chen po'i klu chen rnams// 'jig rten thams cad 'grel par 'gyur/
68b2: de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi don gyi blo gros gzi brjid rgyal pos/ bcom ldan 'das kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag
68b3: smras so/ / drang srong dam pa'i mchog rnams kyi// dus gsum nyan thos gang byung ba// de dag kun gyis bde gshegs kyis// gshegs thabs 'jog 'dig mi shes so// dus gsum sa
68b4: lus thams cad kyi/ / ma nor rang rgyal gang byung ba// de dag gis kyang mgon po'i// gshegs thabs 'jog 'deg mi rig go/ ma rig mun pas bsgribs pa rnams// khyi ltar ltung la rgyus
68b5: pa'i/ / sems can de 'dra kun gyis ni// mgon po mi shes smos mi dgos// rgyal ba tshad mas gzhal ba min// de ni shes par myi nus te// sangs rgyas chags med ye shes can// tshig gi
68b6: lam las shin tu 'das/ / zla ba nya rgyas 'od mnga' ba// brtan pa mtshan gyis rnam par bris// de ni bskal pa dpag yas par// rnam 'phrul thogs med spyod pa mdzad// tshul sgo re res sangs rgyas la//

68b8: kyang / sangs rgyas chos ni bsam mi khyab// gang zhig de la smon byed cing // gang zhig yid kyis dga' mos pa// de dag kun gyi de 'dra ba'i// spyod yul blta dka' 'thob par 'gyur/

69a1: bsod nams ye shes mtha' yas dang // tshogs cen yangs pas rnam gnon la// dri med blo ldan sems gnas pa// de dag 'a dze ta'i tshal la 'jug/ de dag smon lam rgya che bas/

69a4: med de khas ma yas ye shes sku mngar bas/ / de dag bsam pas mi nus so// phrin las dkar po bsam yas pas// sangs rgyas su rab bsgrub pa'i phyir// de la 'jig rten gsum gyi mgon/

69a6: thams cad rnam spangs pas/ / rdul med spros pa mi mnga'o// ye shes 'od gzer rab 'gyed pas// 'jig rten kun tu nyi ma 'dra// khams gsum thams cad rnam spyod pas// srid pa'i 'jigs
69a7: pas rnam par gcod/ / byang chub sems dpa' bsgrub pa mdzad// byang chub 'byung gnas de bzhin no// kha dog mtha' yas ston mdzad kyang // kha don kun la gnas pa med// sems can kun gyis
69a8: bsam yas pa'i/ / kha dog tshad med yongs su ston// skad cig gcig la sangs rgyas kyi// byang chub bsam yas sbyangs pas na// de'i ye shes mthar phyin par// rtag par sus kyang mi nus

69b1: ga bstan pa pa sngags/ / rang ba rnam par 'gyur ba meng // du la dus gsu rgyal bkun// nga cagagazugags badzad// ga pa sag/ ma sa sa/ /
69b2: byang chub don gnyer bas// sems la sems shes bya ba yang // de la sams skye med par bsam// gang gis sangs rgyas bskyed pa'i// sangs rgyas chos rnams bsam mi khyab// de dag brjod pa'i yul
69b3: ma yin/ shin tu zab pas tshig lam spangs// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang mdzad kyi// smon lam dpal gyi rgyal mtshan gyis// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par
69b4: bltas ste/ / de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// dran pa rmongs med dag pa'i rnams// chos 'dzin shin tu nges rtogs shing // blo gros bsam gyis mi khyab pa// byang chub rgya mtsho mi zad pa/
69b5: de dag yid ni 'di la des// de dag spyod pa'i spyod yul yin// de dag shes pa 'dir mi g.yo// de dag 'di la the tsom 'chad// de dag skyo bar mi 'gyur te// de dag yid kyang zhum mi 'gyur// sangs rgyas
69b6: chos la rab gzhol bar/ / de dag sems kyang rab tu 'byung // de dag dad pa rting tshugs shing // yang dag 'phags pa rab tu skyed// dmigs med gnas pa med pa'i// ye shes 'di la de dag dga'//
69b7: bskal pa bye bar bsags pa'i// yongs su rdzogs pa'i dge ba'i chos// ye shes 'di 'dod mtshungs pa med// de dag thams cad yongs su sngo// 'khod pa'i nang na rgyab yang // 'khong ba dag la
69b8: gnas pa min/ / sangs rgyas chos rnams rab rtogs pas// sangs rgyas yul la rab tu rtse// sems can khams na ji snyed du// 'jig rten phun sum tshogs rgyu ba// de dag thams cad brtan pas

70a1: spangs/ / sangs rgyas phun sum tshogs la gnas// sangs rgyas rtag tu 'byung gyur kyang // 'jig rten don mad rab tu gnas// chags med spyod pa de dag ni// rtag tu sems can don la
70a2: gnas/ / de dag spyod pa mtshungs med de// lus can kun kyis bsam mi khyab// 'jig rten bde ba kun sems pas// de dag sdug bsngal rnam par bzlog/ 'jig rten kun la snying rje rtse zhing // byang chub
70a3: ye shes rnam dag pas/ / de dag 'jig rten snang bar gyur// 'jig rten thams cad rab tu 'grol// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ba sgrib pa thams cad rnam par grol ba'i rgyal pos/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi
70a4: rlabs kyis/ / phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te// de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// bskal pa bye ba phrag brgyar yang // sangs rgyas sgra ni rab bkod na// the tsom thams cad gcod pa'i// dam pa'i
70a5: mthong ba ci zhig spros/ / chos kun thugs su chud rtogs pa// 'jig rten gsum po'i bsod nams stegs// sems can thams cad rnam spyod pa'i// 'jig rten sgron ma mthong gis dka'// sems can
70a6: gtso bo ma smad pa'o/ / gzugs kyi sku ni mthong gyur na// bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig tu// ngoms shing tshim pa skyer mi btub// mi'i dbang po sku gzugs la// rgyal sras rnams lta lta zhing // rang gi dge ba'i/
70a7: chags med pa// gzhan don brtson po byang chub sngo// thub pa chen po'i gzugs kyi sku// de las so so yang dag rig/ chags med ye shes 'byung gyur pas// de ni sangs rgyas byang chub sngo// sems can
70a8: bsam yas tshad med pa/ / rnam par mdzad de theg chen la// btsun nas thub pa med pa'i mchog/ byang chub dam par lung yang bstan// bsod nams chen po'i rang bzhin zhing // ye shes dkyil 'khor shang

70b1: cing byung / / 'jig rten chad med kun tu snang // bsod nams phung po rnam 'phel mdzad// sdug bsngal dra ba rab tu gcad// ye shes phung po rnam par spyong // gang gis rgyal ba bsnyen bkur ba// de dag ngan song
70b2: 'jigs pa med/ / rkang gnyis dam pa mthong gyur na// shin tu yangs pa'i sems skye ste// 'di snang gsal ba'i shes rab mthu// grangs med de bzhin skye bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas skyes bu'i mchog
70b3: mthong zhing / / byang chub dam par nges par 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur bya zhes// de dag kun kyang nges par sems// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyings kyi smon lam gyi gzhi
70b4: rab tu rtogs pas/ / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// yon tan mtha' yas 'phun ldan pa// shag kya'i khyu mchog thub mthong nas// yongs su bsngo ba byed pa'i sems
70b5: theg pa che la rnam par dag/ sems can kun gyi don gyi phyir// thugs rje che mnga'a'i brtan pa rnams// chos kyi 'khor lo bskor mdzad pa// de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung bar 'gyur// bskal
70b6: pa khrag khrig phrag brgyar yang / / sems can don la brtson mdzad pa'i// sangs rgyas rnams la lus can rnams// kun gyis lan glan cing kyang nus// ngan song gsum pa me zad par// bskal pa bye bar
70b7: bcos bla'i/ / chags pa thams cad bzlog mdzad pa'i// ston pa mi mthong ma ma yin no// sems can kun gyi rgyud rnams na// sdug bsngal phung po rnga yod pa// ma lus nyams su bzod nus kyi// sangs
70b8: rgyas mi mthong ma yin no/ / 'jig rten 'di dag thams cad na// tha dad ngan song rgyud yod pa// de dag yun ring gnas bla'i// sangs rgyas mi mthong ma yin no// sems can dmyal ba re re yang // bskal pa

71a1: tshad med gnas bri'i/ / mtha' yas rgyal bas brnyas pa'i// byang chub mchog las ring gnas min// ci zhig phyir ni ngan song du// yun ring gnas par 'dod chen na// rgyal ba'i dbang po mthong ban/
71a2: ye shes 'phel ba'i rgyur 'gyur phyir// rgyal ba'i 'jig rten mchog mthong na/ sdug bsngal thams cad 'chad par 'gyur// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas spyod yul gi/ ye shes khong du chud par 'byung // sangs rgyas
71a3: ma'amachog mthong shing / / sgrub pa thams cad zad par 'gyur// byang chub gang gis 'thob pa'i// bsod nams tshad med 'phel bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas mthong bar sems can rnams// the tsam yid gnyis
71a4: chad par 'gyur/ / 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten gyi// bsam pa yang yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang pos// byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs
71a5: thams cad la rnam par bltas te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin seng ge rnam par bsgyings pa 'di nyid de bas kyang rnam par dbye ba dang / rgya cher brjod pa dang / gsal bar bya ba dang / rab tu brjod pa dang /
71a6: yang dag par bstan pa dang / shin tu snang bar bya ba dang / rab tu gsal bar bya ba dang / man ngag bstan pa'i phyir// chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pas// dus gsum mnyam pa nyid
71a7: dang / sems can gyi khams mnyam pa nyid dang / 'jig rten thams cad mnyam pa nyid dang / las kyi rgyud thams cad mnyam pa dang / sems can gyi bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang / sems can gyi mos pa mnyam pa
71a8: dang / chos kyi snang ba mnyam pa nyid dang / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i dus mnyam pa nyid dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi dbang ba mnyam pa nyid kyis// de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin seng ge rnam par

71b1: bsgyings pa/ 'di nyid byang chub sems dpa' de dag la bstan pa'i tshul bcus yang dag par rab tu ston te// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos ltar chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gtogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul
71b2: shin tu phra ba rnams la/ sangs rgyas cig nas gcig du chud pa bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste nam mkha'i dbyings kyis klas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi shing thams cad du/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i skal par de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon
71b3: tan rje su brjod pa bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa yongs su skye ba dang / mtha' dang dbang med pa'i mngon par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi sgra rgya mtsha yongs su brjod cing bstan pa dang / 'ang
71b4: lta ste nam mkha'i dbyings kyis klas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyis dkyil 'khor gyi byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun snying po'i byang chub la mngon du gyur pa'i gnas dang / 'di lta ste dus
71b5: gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi sku dang 'dra bar sprul pa ba spu'i sgo thams cad nas sems skad gcig la rab tu bgyi zhing chos kyi dbyings rgyas par dgang ba bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste/ phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi zhing
71b6: rgya mtsho gzhi mnyam par byin gyis rlabs cing lus gcig gis rgyas par dgang ba bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste dmigs pa'i gzhi thams cad la sangs rgyas kyis rnam par sprul pa dus gsum thams cad yang dag par
71b7: gzhol bar 'gyur ba'i byin gyi rlabs yang dag par bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu zla ba rnams la/ dus gsum gyi zhing gcig nas gcig tu brgyad pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phral ba dang

72a1: bskal pa rgya mam yongs su bshad cing bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi smon lam rgya mtsho thams cad baspu'i sgo thams cad nas rab tu brjod pa/ phyi ma'i mtha' byin gyis
72a2: brlabs pas/ byang chub sems dpa' yang dag par 'byung ba bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam pa'i seng ge'i khri dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang / snying po byang chub kyi rgyan tha
72a3: mi dad pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo rnam pa tha mi dad par rab tu bskor ba/ phyi ma'i mthar byin gyis brlabs pa bstan pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ltar seng ge rnam par bsgyings pa/ ting nge 'dzin 'di la bstan pa
72a4: bcu po de dag la sogs pa shin tu bstan pa sangs rgyas kyi gang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod de/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul lo// / dmas
72a5: chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin chen po seng ge rnam par bsgyings pa'i 'di nyid kyi don gyi phyogs bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas byin gyis brlabs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i
72a6: zhal du lta zhing 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho thams cad la rnam par bltas nas sangs rgyas kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' dang dbus med pa la
72a7: rnam par bltas te/ 'jig rten gyi khams bsam gyis mi khyab par yang dag par gzhol ba la rnam par bltas nas/ ye shes bsam gyis ma khyab pa'i sna ma'i chos nyid la rnam par bltas te/ dus gsum gyi sangs
72a8: rgyas mnyam pa nyid bsam gyis ma khyab pa la rnam par bltas nas/ / mtha' dang dbus med pa'i dag gi las dang / nges pa'i tshig dang / chos kyi tshul thams cad la rnam par bltas te/ de'i mtshigs su bcad pa

72b1: 'di dag smras so/ / baspu'i gcig la rgya mtsho rgyal ba'i zheng // zhing kun shin tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam// de nas sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' 'khor// kun gyis yongs bskor sangs rgyas gdan la bzhugs//
72b2: skrag cig rtsel zhing mnga' rgya mtsho'i rnams// snying po byang chub pad ma'i gdan gnas pas// chos dbyings rgya chen yongs sa rgyas bkang zhing // shing drung dam pa kun na mgon po snang // shing rnams
72b3: kun gyi rdul phran rab mad rnyed/ / rgyal ba spu rtse gcig la yongs bzhugs pa// byang chub sems dpa' 'khor los yongs su bskor// kun kyang bzang po'i spyod pa ston pa mdzad// zhing mchog gcig na
72b4: rgyal ba bzhugs gyur kyang / / byang chub sems dpa'i sprin mang mi zad pa// de dag phyogs bcu ma lus thams cad nas// 'byam klas zhing kun bkang zhing kun kyang 'od// zhing rnams bye ba'i rdul
72b5: phran mnyam pa'i/ / byang chub sems dpa' yon tan rgya mtsho'i 'od// phyogs bcu'i chos dbyings rgyas pa kun bkang zhing // ston pa de la kun kyang 'khor nas ldang // shing rnams kun tu
72b6: gzugs brnyan rab tu ston/ / chos kyi rgyal po rgyal ba'i ye shes mtsha// de dag kun kyang bzang po'i spyod la gnas// sangs rgyas kun gyi 'khor du nye bar 'dod// 'byam klas zhing
72b7: rnams kun na 'khod spyod cing / / byang chub sems dpa'i dga' ba rab gnas te/ chos kyi sprin mnyam dpa' 'od dag ni// zhing gcig du yang bskal pa bye bar spyod// byang chub sems
72b8: dpa'i spyad pa spyod par byed/ / chos kyi gang chen mtsho spyod rnam par snang // smon lam rgya mtsho kun la rab tu 'jug/ de dag sangs rgyas sa'i spyod yul gnas// rgyal ba'i chos rnams gzhan dang

73a1: gzhan 'byung ba'o/ / dedag pan babang pa byung bags// sangs rgyas yon tan legs pargya mtsho dang // rnam par 'phrul ba rgya can yangs la 'phru// bde gshegs chos
73a2: dbyings kun tu rgyas bkang zhing / / zhing rnams kun gyi rdul phran ji snyed pa'i// sku'i sprin rnams rtag tu 'gyid mdzad cing // chos kyi char gyis byang chub rab la 'khod/
73a3: sangs rgyas mang gcad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas brtson bar do/ bas po drug pa/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin
73a4: seng ge rnam par bsgyings pa 'di nyid la de bas kyang bstan te/ 'god par 'dzad pa'i don du smin mtshams kyi mdzod spyi'i nang nas chos kyi dbyings so kun nas rnam par dmigs pas/ dus gsum
73a5: snang ba zhes bya ba 'od gzer chen po 'od ga zer gyi dkyil 'khor sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa 'jal shin tu zab sted dang ldan pa pakye ste/ / phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi 'ams rgyam tshe thams cad kyi sangs
73a6: rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad snang bar mdzad do/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'dzi ta'i tshal du tshogs pa de dag gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gtogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing nam mkha'i dbyings kyi
73a7: mthas klas pa thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra bi'i khong du chud pa'i sa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba dag la/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi ming du bya ba 'dog
73a8: sna tshogs dang / rnam pa sna tshogs su rnam par dag pa dang / zhing sna rogs dang / dbyibs sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing dag na/ byang chub sems dpa' snying po byang chub du phyin te/ seng ge'i khril 'dug pa 'jig

73b1: rten gyi dbang po thams cad kyis shin du mchod pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyis kun nas bskor ba/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ba mthong ste/ la
73b2: la ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa tsam du shin tu yangs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil na/ chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab pa'i dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor gyis chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba mthong ngo //
73b3: lal na ni lha'i gnas na 'dug/ la la na ni kwa'i gnas na 'dug/ la lan ni gnod sbyin gyi gnas na 'dug/ la lan ni lA ma yin gyi gnas na 'drag/ lal na ni nam mkha' lding gi gnas
73b4: 'dug/ la la na ni pi 'am ci'i gnas na 'dug/ la lan na lto 'phye chen po'i gnas na 'dug/ la lan ni mi'i dbang po'i nang na 'dug/ la lanan mi'i 'jig rten gyi grong dang grong khyer dang /
73b5: grong rdal dang / ljongs dang / khams dang / rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor dag na rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs dang / spyod lam sna tshogs dang / lus sna tshogs dang / ting nge 'dzin
73b6: gyi sgo rnam par dmigs pa sna tshogs dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi mngon par shes pa sna tshogs dang / rigs dang rgyang sna tshogs su byung ba dang / kha dog rnam par dmigs pa sna tshogs dang
73b7: 'od kyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs dang / 'od gzer gyi dra ba bkye ba sna tshogs dang / dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs dang / gtam gyi skyes bu'i gzhi sna tshogs dang / bstan pa'i

74a1: gzhi sna tshogs dang / tshig dang yi ge dang nges pa'i tshig sna tshogs kyis 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs na chos ston pa mthong bar gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' ji snyed kyis
74a2: 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyi saklas pa nam mkha'i mthas gtugs pa phyogs bcun rnam par gnas pa/ / phyogs kyi rgyud mtha' yas par 'dus pa/ phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad du
74a3: gtogs pa/ chos sna tshogs kyi sgo dang ldan pa/ phyogs kyi ming du bya ba sna tshogs su gtogs pa/ phyogs sna tshogs kun tu gzhol ba phyogs charnam pa tha dad par gtogs pa
74a4: phyogs sna tshogs kyi rjes su song ba/ phyogs rgya mtsho sna tshogs su gtogs pa 'di lta ste/ shar phyogs dang lho phyogs dang nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang / byang dang shar
74a5: gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar dang lho phyogs mtshams dang / lho dang nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub dang byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og dang steng gi phyogs kyi zheng
74a6: gi lhun gyi phyogs dang / sems can gyi lus kyi phyogs dang / sems can gyi ming du bya ba'i phyogs dang / sngon gyi mtha'i mur thug pa'i phyogs dang / phyogs bcu 'ad ltar
74a7: byung ba'i phyogs dang / nam mkha'i khongs thams cad du skra'i rtse mo shin tu phra ba dgod pas dmigs pa'i phyogs dang / zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba gcig nas gcig tu

74b1: brgyud pa'i phyogs la 'jug pa khong du chud par bya ba'i phyogs dang / las kyi 'du byed sna tshogs kyis yongs su grub pa de phyogs dang / skra'i rtse mo gcig la mtha' dang dbus med pa'i nam mkha'i
74b2: dbyings kyi mang du bya bar gtogs pa'i phyogs kyi khongs su chud pa'i dus gsum gyi dbyings mnyam pa nyid du gzhol bas/ kun tu gtogs pa'i 'gro ba thams cad tha mi dad pas/ sems can
74b3: t hams cad kyi 'du shes kyi rnam pa la mnyam pa'i sgra dbyangs su gyur pa'i 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems la gzugs brnyan rab tu snang bar gyur pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin
74b4: rnam par 'phrul pa/ sems can thams cad kyi lus la mngon par lta ba/ dmigs par bya bas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du 'gro ba'i tshul dang ldan pa/ bskal pa thams
74b5: cad la ye shes tha mi dad pa zhing thams cad la kun tu snyoms pas sems can gyi bsam pa ji lta ba de bzhin du gzugs mngon sum du bstan pa rnam par dmigs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
74b6: p a'i rnam par 'phrul pa sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par snyan pas sems can thams cad 'dul ba rgyan mi 'chad pa mthong bar gyur pa de dag thams cad ni sngon bcom ldan 'das rnam par
74b7: snang mdzad kyis dge ba'i spyod pa bskal pa mnyam pa dang / bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhis yongs su bsdus pa mthong ba dang mnyam pa dang / rjes su dran pa bsnyen bkur bas yongs su smin

75a1: par byas pa dag go/ / sngon bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du sems bskyed pa la bcud pa dag go/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dang de dag gi drung du gshegs
75a2: pa'i tshe dge ba'i rtsa bas yongs su bsdus pa dag ste/ de ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba skal pa mnyam pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su smin par 'gyur ba'i thabs kyis shin tu bzung
75a3: ba'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam par 'phrul pa chos kyi dbyings ltar yangs shing nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs par gyur pa dag kyang
75a4: mthong zhing khong du chud par gyur pa yin te/ la la ni chos kyi sku la 'jug go// la la ni gzugs kyi sku la 'jug go/ la la ni sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa' yongs su bsgrub pa la
75a5: 'jug go/ / la la ni pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pa la 'jug go/ la la ni spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su dag pa'i rgyan la 'jug go// la la ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa'i rnam par 'phrul
75a6: pa la 'jug go/ / la la ni mngon par byang chub pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa la 'jug go// la la ni sangs rgyas rnam par spyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin thami dad pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa la 'jug go/ la la ni de bzhin
75a7: gshegs pa'i stobs dang mi bsnyengs pa la 'jug go lal ni sangs rgyas kyi so mo yang dag par rig pa rgya mtsho la 'jug go/ de dag la sogs pa sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi

75b1: zhing brjod du med pa'i phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la 'jug ste/ mos pa sna tshogs dang / lam sna tshogs dang / sgo sna tshogs dang 'jug pa sna tshogs dang / 'bab pa sna tshogs dang / rnam pa
75b2: sna tshogs dang / rjes su 'brang ba sna tshogs dang / phyogs sna tshogs dang / snod sna tshogs dang / yul sna tshogs dang / 'jig rten sna tshogs dang / khong du chud pa sna tshogs dang / tshogs sna tshogs dang /
75b3: rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs dang / thabs sna tshogs dang / ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs kyis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rgya mtshod dag la 'jug go// ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs kyis 'jug pa 'di lta ste/ byang
75b4: chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos kyi dbyings kun nas brgyan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin dus gsum thams cad la thogs pa med par yul snang bar byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'
75b5: ting nge 'dzin chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi tha mi dad pa'i ye shes snang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul gyi dbyings la 'jug pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'
75b6: ting nge 'dzin nam mkha'i dbyings su snang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu 'thob pas rnam par 'byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i
75b7: ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas kyi bsnyengs pa mi mnga' ba'i rgyan gyis rnam par gnon cing rnam par bgyings pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul thams cad kyi klong gi snying po dang /

76a3: dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos kyi rgyal po'i thabs chags pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin dmigs pa thams cad la sangs rgyas rgya mtshornam par lta ba dang / byang chub sems dpa
76a4: ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyud thams cad du tha mi dad pa'i lus snang ba'i rgyal mtshan dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku tha dad pa'i yul la 'jug pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting
76a5: nge 'dzin 'jig rten thams cad kyi rgyud kyi rjes su 'jug pa snying rje chen po'i snying po can dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos thams cad kyi gnas la brten pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang / byang chub sems
76a6: dpa'i ting nge 'dzin shin tu zhi la rab tu zhi bas kun tu snang ba'i dkyil 'khor dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sprul pa bzang po dmigs su med pas/ kun tu 'phrul pa'i gzugs brnyan dang /
76a7: byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin zhing thams cad yongs su 'dra ba'i byin gyi rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin zhing thams cad du mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i rnam par bsgrub pa dang / byang/
