76b1: pa'i rnam par spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad skyed pa las byung ba'i byin gyi rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin yon tan rgya mtsho thams cad la
76b2: nan tan gyis 'jug pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin pa dmigs pa ma lus pa thams cad du rnam par 'phrul pa mngon par bsgrubs pas/ phyi ma'i mthar byin gyis rlob pa dang / byang chub sa ma
76b3: dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho la 'jug pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin phyi ma'i mthar de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs yang dag par 'dren
76b4: pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin bcu'i zhing rgya mtsho da ltar byung ba thams cad yongs su dag par mos pa'i byin gyi brlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin sems kyi
76b5: skad cig gcig la sangs rgyas thams cad dang rnam par spyod cing 'grogs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin dmigs pa thams cad la chags pa med pa'i mthar 'jug pa dang / byang chub sems
76b6: dpa'i ting nge 'dzin 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig tu byin gyis rlobs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad kyi skur 'phrul pa mngon par bsgrub pa
76b7: dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin dbang po rgya mtsho rdo rje'i dbang po lta bu thams cad khong du chud pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sku cig pa'i snying po'i
76b8: byin bye rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sems kyi skad cig gcig gi chal chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul thams cad khong du chud pas khom par gnas pa dang / byang

77a1: chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos kyi dbyings thams cad du zhing 'byam klas pa bsgrub pa yongs su ston pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin spri'u tshugs su gzhi la rnam par spyod pa'i byin
77a2: gyi brlabs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi sems can gyi lus tha mi dad par byin gyis rlobs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ye shes kyi klong thams/
77a3: cad la mngon sum du yang dag par gzhol ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin mtshan nyid yongs su shes pas rab tu 'byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin
77a4: dus gsum sems kyi skad gcig cig la tha mi dad pa'i dkyil 'khor dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sems kyi skad cig thams cad chos dbyings kyi tshul gyi rang bzhin dam pa dang / byang chub sems
77a5: dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i ye shes kyis rnam par gnon pa'i seng ge dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin dmigs pa thams cad chos kyi
77a6: dbyings su shes pa'i mig gi dkyil 'khor dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin stobs bcu'i rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pas yang dag par rtsom pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rmig

77a8: dpa'i ting nge 'dzin glong mi g.yo ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos gcig la chos thams cad yongs su 'du bar ston pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos gcig gi tshig gi/

77b1: lam langs pa'i dgags rab tu 'bred pas byang chub sems dpa' de dag bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mad kyis brgyas kyi 'phrul bas rnam par 'phrul ba rgyam nga dag larab tu 'jug go/ blang nabs ngas/
77b2: dpa' ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rgyal mtshan byin gyi rlabs kyis chos ston pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ngas gsum gyi mu lamathar thug pa med pa dang / byang chub sems pa'i ting
77b3: 'dzin bskal pa thams cad khong du chud pas tha me dad pa'i ye shes dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin tshul shin tha phra bas stobs bcu khong du chud pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin mi 'phrogs par
77b4: byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bskal pa thams cad du mngon par bslab pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin phyogs thams cad kun tu shugs kyis mngon du mthar pa'i sprin dang / byang chub sems dpa'i

77b7: sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa'i zla ba'i 'od nam mkha' ltar rdul dang bral ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge dzin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad nam mkhar byin gyis rlob pa dang / byang
77b8: chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos thams cad la dbang po'i rten rab tu snang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos thams cad kyi don rnam par 'byed pa'i sgron ma dang / byang chub sems dpa'

78a1: ting nge 'dzin stobs bcu'i dkyil 'khor snang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' ting ngange 'dzin dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas dpal gyi rgyal mtshan dang / byang chub sems dpa' tang nge 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad
78a2: gcig tu 'dres pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin skad cig skad cig la brtsams pa thams cad mthar phyin par byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin bsod nams mi zad pa'i
78a3: snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas mtha' yas pa mthong ba'i yul rab tu snang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting 'arjed chos thams
78a4: la rdo rje'i seng ge ltar rab tu gnas pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sprul pa yongs su ldan phra rabs kyis migs pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / byang chub sems
78a5: dpa'i ting nge 'dzin de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis mnyan pa'i nyi ma gnon pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin dus gsum gcig du skyed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos thams cad
78a6: rang bzhin gyis rab tu zhi bar sgra dbyangs kun tu sgrog pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba'i sa 'tshams 'dzin pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos kyi dbyings ma
78a7: lus pa thams cad dkyi gnas kyi pa ma tshal rab rgyas pa nga byung chub sems dpa'i/ / rang 'dzin panas med pa'i rnas kyi dbyings nam mkha' la rnam par ga ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin phyogs
78a8: cog tu phyogs bcu rgya mtsho yongs su sud pa'i klong dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi thams cad kyi sgong 'jug pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin chos rgya mtsha thams

78b1: bad dang ldan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin sems can thams cad la 'od rab tu 'gyed pas/ rab tu zhi ba'i lus su 'gyur ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' tang nga 'dzin sems kyis dag cag cag la

79a1: sa pa byan rdzas btub padang / byang chubasems dpa' nga 'dzin sems can thams cad pa byu sa rgya yan pa gnas par 'grub thams cad kyisbya yangasas 'byed pa rgyal man

79a4: kyi rnam par thar pa'i pho brang la rnam par lta bas seng ge rnam par bsgyings pa dang / de dag la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi lam la 'dug pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med
79a5: pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rgya mtsho de dag la rab tu 'jug go// sems kyi skad
79a6: cig re re la chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs par 'jug pa'i tshul gyis sngon bskal pa mnyam par spyad pa yang rjes su dran no/ / de ltar byang chub sems dpa' de dag 'jo
79a7: ta'i tshal du phyin cing bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngan 'khod pa/ seng ge'i khri rin po che sna tshogs kyi pad mo'i snying po can/ 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba
79a8: dang mnyam par yangs pa la 'khod pa ye shes dang mngon par shes pa chen po'i rnam par 'phrul pas byung ba/ / ye shes dang mngon par shes pa rno ba dang ldan pa'i sa rjes su thob pa/ ye shes

79b1: kyi kun tu rnam par dpyod pa/ shes rab kyi 'byung gnas kyi rigs su byung ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la mngon du gyur pa/ ye shes kyi mig rab rib med pa dang ldan pa/ sems can gyi kha lo
79b2: snang ba'i rang bzhin zab pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ba/ rtag tu rnam par rtog pa med par chos la spyod pa/ chos kyi dmigs pa thams cad rab tu
79b3: rtogs pa/ chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis zhi bar dmigs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad shin tu zhi bas/ gnas tha dad pa med pa la rab tu gzhol pa/ 'jig rten tha dad pa
79b4: thams cad du ba tu zhugs pa/ gnas med par zhing thams cad du 'dod pa/ chos kyi gnas thams cad la brten pa med par chos thams cad blag ba med pa'i gzhal med khang du phyin pa/
79b5: 'gro ba thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba la zhugs pa/ sems can thams cad la bde ba'i lam ston pa/ ye shes dang rnam par thar pa shin tu 'phags pa'i gnas kyi spyod
79b6: yul can/ 'dod chags dang bral ba'i mthar phyin pa'i ye shes kyi lus dang ldan pa/ srid pa'i rgya mtsho thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la yang dag pa'i mtha' rnam
79b7: bar ston pa/ chos rgya mtsho'i shes rab snang ba'i dkyil 'khor can/ ting nge 'dzin gang chen mtsho dang ldan pa'i dkyil shin tu mnyam par bzhag cing / snying rje chen po rab tu sems pa/ chos
79b8: kyi tshul sgyu ma'i rnam pa lta bu'i rab tu rtogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad la rmi lam lta bur zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba thams cad mig yor lta bur khong du chud pa sku

80a1: skad dang dbyangs thams cadasgra/ snyan lta bur rnam par rig pa/ chos thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes sprul pa lta bra rab tu rtogs pa/ khyad par du 'phags pa'i smon lam shin tu
80a2: bsags pa/ ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor kun nas rnam par dag pa'i mkhas pa dang ldan pa/ sems shin tu zhi shing rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa gzungs kyi rgyud thams cad kyi ye shes kyi yul dang ldan
80a3: pa/ ting nge 'dzin gyi stobs kyis ngogs pa med par kun nas rab tu gnon pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi gnas kyi mthar phyin pa'i mig dang ldan pa/ chos thams cad la dmigs pa med par rnam par spyod pa
80a4: rab tu thob pa/ shes rab rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa la rnam par spyod pa/ ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i pha rol tu song ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i stobs dang / shugs thob pa/
80a5: 'phrul gyi pha rol tu phyin pas 'gro ba thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ting nge 'dzin gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dbang du gyur pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi don mkhas pa la byin ci log med
80a6: pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa/ chos kyi mdzod dbye ba'i cho ga la mkhas pa/ nges pa'i tshig shes pa lam/ spro ba'i stobs dang / chos kyi sprin zad mi shes pa dang ldan pa/ mi 'jigs
80a7: pas khyu mchog dang seng ge'i ngado 'byin pa/ gnas med pa'i chos kyi dga' ba la dga' bar mos pa/ chos thams cad la rab rib med pa'i mig gis lta ba/ 'jig rten thams cad
80a8: 'byung ba dang / 'jig pa'i shes pa'i zla bar gyur pa/ shes rab kyi dkyil 'khor gyis bden pa'i tshul thams cad la rnam par spyod pa'i 'od gzer can/ ye shes kyi rdo rje bsod

80b1: nams kyi khor yug du gyur pa/ dper bya ba thams cad las shin tu 'das pa/ chos thams cad la dbang po dang ye shes kyi myu gu rab tu skyes pa/ dpa' ba'i rgyal mtshan dang ldan pa/ bdud
80b2: thams cad kyi rgyal mtshan rab tu stsol ba la dpa' ba ye shes mtha' yas pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi gzi brjid can/ 'gro ba thams cad las mngon par 'phags pa'i lus dang ldan pa/
80b3: chos thams cad la shes rab bsgrib pa med par zad pa dang / mi zad pa'i mtha'i ye shes kyis rnam par sangs rgyas pa/ yang dag pa'i mtha'i kun gyi mthar phyin pa la
80b4: gnas pa/ / mtshan ma med pa la rnam par lta bu'i ye shes kyi mig mngon sum can/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa'i rgyu la
80b5: mkhas pa/ mi gnyis pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul dang ldan pa 'jig rten rgyud thams cad la rnam par blta ba/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyud gnas med pa la thams cad du
80b6: gzugs brnyan snang bar gyur pa/ / chos thams cad la mun pa dang rnam par bral ba ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor mun pa med pa la rab tu zhugs pa/ phyogs kun tu chos kyi snang rab tu
80b7: bkye ba/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing mchog du gyur pa/ thos pa dang mthong ba dang / smon lam don yod pa'i zla ba/ bsod nams kyi ri rab 'jig rten thams cad la
80b8: mngon par 'phags pa/ phas kyi rgol ba'i tsho gas thams cad tshar gcod pa la shin tu dpa' ba/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du sgra skad dang dbyangs kyi nga ro 'byin pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi

81a1: su mthong bas mi dmas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sku'i gzugs brnyan gyi dbang sgyur ba dang ldan pa/ 'gro ba gdul ba dang 'thun pa'i lus su byin gyis rlob pa/ zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad du lus gcig
81a2: gis rgyas par 'gengs pa/ mngon par 'du bye ba med pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi dkyil 'khor yongs su dag pa/ thogs pa med par 'gro ba'i ye shes chen po'i theg pa gru dang ldan pa/ ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gyis chos
81a3: kyi dbyings thams cad du lus rab tu snang ba/ ye shes kyi nyi ma 'gro ba thams cad du shar ba/ 'gro ba thams cad bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du dga' ba'i kha dog dang ldan pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsam pa dang /
81a4: dbang po rab tu rtogs pa'i ye shes can/ chos thams cad bsgribs pa med pa'i yul khong du chud pa/ chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin skye ba med pa rnam par rig pa phro ba dang yangs pa phan tshun du yongs su bsdu
81a5: pa la dbang sgyur ba/ sangs rgyas kyis zab me'i tshul nges par rtogs pa/ don zab mo'i tshig dang / yi ge'i tha snyad la mkhas pa/ tshig dang yi ge dang don mi zad par rab tu brjod pa/ mdo sde rgya mtsho thams
81a6: cad tshig cig du chud par rab tu ston pa/ gzugs dang ye shes kyi lus rgya chen po byin gyis rlob pa/ bskal pa mtha' yas par yongs su 'dzin pa'i gzungs dang ldan pa'i byin gyi rlabs can/ sems kyi
81a7: skad cig gcig gis bskal pa brjod du med par gnas pa/ rab tu rtogs pa'i ye shes can/ sems kyi skad cig gcig gis dus gsum shes pas/ 'jig rten thams cad mngon par shes pas// chos
81a8: kyi gzungs kyis sangs rgyas kyi tshes rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa dran zhing spobs pa 'gro ba thams cad kyis shes par 'gyur ba'i thabs kyis chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba las phyir mi ldog pa/ sangs rgyas kyi

81b1: yul la ye shes snang ba rab tu thob pa/ gya nom par snang ba'i ting nge 'dzin la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag pa chags pa med pa'i mtha'i chos thams cad rab tu dbye ba'i ye shes la mngon par mkhas pa/
81b2: chos thams cad las khyad par du 'phags pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i yul la ye shes kyis rnam par rtse ba/ dmigs pa thams cad rgyan bzang po'i byin kyis rlob pa/ chos kyi dbyings myog
81b3: med pa la phyogs kyi rjes su 'brang bas rab tu zhugs pa phyogs thams cad rnam par dbye bas chos kyi dbyings la yang dag par gzhol ba shin tu phra ba ste/ yangs pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba la byang chub tu rnam
81b4: par 'tshang rgya ba/ rang bzhin kha dog med pa las kha dog thams cad yongs su ston pa/ phyogs gcig la yang dag par gzhol ba de lta bu'i yon tan dang ye shes mtha' yas pas yang dag par bskyed
81b5: de bsod nams dang ye shes kyi snying po dang ldan par gyur pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bstod pa bsngags pa bskur ba tshig dang yi ge mi zad pas yon tan dang legs pa brjod du med pa'i byang chub sem
81b6: dpa' 'dze ta'i tshal du 'dus te/ 'khod pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la 'jug pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od gzer gyis rab tu snang bar gyur pa/ de dag gi lus thams cad dang / khang pa
81b7: brtsegs pa de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa'i longs spyod de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa'i stan de dag dang / 'dze ti'i tshal thams cad nas kyang / dga' ba chen po'i shugs rab tu thob pa'i chos nyid
81b8: dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos snang ba bsam kyis mi khyab pa rab tu thob pas dga' ba'i shugs las byung ba'i rnam par 'phral pa chen po'i brgyan mngon par 'thon nas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad

82a1: rgyas pa khyab par gyur to/ / 'di lta ste sems kyi skad cig re re la 'od gzer gyi dra ba'i sbyin shin tu yangs pa/ 'gro ba thams cad yongs su tshim par byed pa mngon par 'thon te/ phyogs bcu rgyas pas
82a2: khyab par gyur to/ / rin po che sna tshogs kyi dril bu'i sprin mngon par 'thon te/ dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yon tan dang legs pa rab tu brjod pa'i sprin gyi nga ro rjes su bsgrags pas phyogs
82a3: bcu rgyas par khyab par gyur to/ / dmigs pa thams cad las 'gro ba thams cad rol mo'i sprin mngon par 'thon te/ sems can thams cad kyi las dang rnam par smin pha rol mo'i sgra snyan par blang bas rjes su
82a4: sgrog cing phyogs bcu rgyas pa khyab par 'gyur to/ / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa sna tshogs yang dag par ston pa'i tshul gyi sprin mang po mngon par 'thon nas/ byang
82a5: chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam gyi sgra dbyangs rab tu sgrog pas phyogs bcu rgyas par khyab par gyur to/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sprul pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa'i sprin mang po mngon par 'thon//
82a6: nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsungs gi dbyangs rjes su brjod cing phyogs bcu rgyas par khyab par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos rnam par brgyan pa'i sprin
82a7: mang po mngon par 'thon nas/ zhing thams cad du 'byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa rab tu brjod cing phyogs bcu rgyas pa khyab par gyur to// dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang
82a8: mnyam pa'i snying po byang chub kyi sprin mang po mngon par 'thon nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyan byung ba yongs su ston cing / phyogs bcu rgyas par khyab par gyur to// dmigs pa

82b1: thams cad las klu dbang po'i las kyi sprin mang po mngon par 'thon nas/ spos sna tshogs kyi char rab tu 'bebs shing phyogs bcu rgyas par khyab par gyur to// 'gro ba thams cad kyi dbang po lus dang 'dra ba'i
82b2: sbyin mang po mngon par 'thon nas/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa yongs su rjod pa byed cing phyogs bcu rgyas par khyab par gyur to// zhing yongs su dag pa rin po che thams cad kyi rang bzhin
82b3: yongs kyi gzugs brnyan gyi sprin mang po mngon par 'thon nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba mngon par ston cing / phyogs bcu rgyas par khyab par gyur to// de dag la sogs pa byang chub
82b4: sems dpa' de dag gi byin gyi rlabs dang / chos kyi sdang ba rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa rab tu thob pa'i chos nyid kyis rgyan chen po rnam par sprul pa'i sprin sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
82b5: byung bar gyur to/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal gyis sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis rnam par 'phrul pa de dag yongs su ston pa byed cing phyogs bcur rnam par bltas nas// de'i tshe tshigs su bca
82b6: pa 'di dag smras so/ / 'dze ta'i tshal du sangs rgyas byin gyis rlabs// mtha' yas rgya chen yongs su byung la ltos// dmigs pa kun las lus kyi sprin chen rnams// mngon par 'thon zhing phyogs rnams kun tu khyab/
82b7: bde gshegs mas po rnams kyis tshogs brgyan// kha dag mtha' yas rgya chen rnam dag pa// stan dang dmigs pa yongs su bcas pa la// de ga thams cad gzugs brnyan 'byung ba snang // ldan rnams
82b8: rin chen 'od 'phro'i sbyin/ / bde gshegs sras po rnams kyi spu rtse las// sangs rgyas gsung rnams rab tu sgrog byed cing // zhing rnams kun gyi dbyings su khyad par 'phro// tshangs pa'i dbang po'i gzugs 'dra

83a1: ba/ lus rnams dang // spyad lam rab tu'i bdag pa'i gzugs// zhing gi ma tog kun las mngon 'thon te// bsam gtan yan lag brjod cang kun tu 'dong // kun tu bzang po 'dra ba'i rgyal ba'i sras// mtshan /
83a2: dpe byung bzang pos brgyan po'i lus// grangs med bas ma yas bde gshegs pa snga las// sprul pa de 'dra thogs pa med par 'byung // bde ga shegs sras po dus gsum byung ba'i rnams// yon tan rgya mtsho'i les
83a3: pa brjod pa dag/ rgya mtsho tshe mnyam rgyan sprin de dag kun// 'dze ti 'tshal na gnas shing rab tu brjod// phyogs rnams kun gyi sems can yongs kyi las// rgya mtsho chen po sna tshogs ma lus par// 'dze ti'i tshal gyi shing
83a4: gi gzugs rnams kyi/ / gseb nas byung bar gyur pa kun tu grag/ dus gsum byung ba'i rgyal ba thams cad kyi// zhing rnams kun gyi ma lus rnam 'phrul pa// zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i rdul snyed de dag kyang // so so'i dmigs/
83a5: kyis dmigs par 'gyur ba snang // sangs rgyas phyogs kyi zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i sprin// spu rtse re rer sna tshogs rnam phye ba'i// sangs rgyas gnas rnams skad cig re rer yang // de dag la yang sangs rgyas sprin mang bzhug
83a6: 'gro dang mnyam par phyogs rnams kun bkang zhing / / sems can thabs kyis yongs su smin par byed// de dag 'od las spos kyi 'od 'phro dang // me tog phal chen rgya mtsho'i sprin kyang 'byung // mkha' ltar tshad med//
83a7: rin chen gzhal med khang // ma lus rgyan rab kun gyis rnam mdzes pa// de dag thams cad phyogs rnams kun khyab byed// zhing dang snying po byang chub de bzhin no// dus gsum byung ba'i rgyal ba'i sras rnams kyis/
83a8: kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i rnam tshul du// zhing rnams rgya mtsho rnam par dag byas shing // rgyan rab sna tshogs 'gro ltar tshad med pa// phyogs rnams dus gsum kun tu gang byung rnams// bskal pa rgya mtsho chen

83b1: por rnam sbyangs pa/ / de dag kun kyang 'dze ta'i nags tshal gyi// bar snang mkha' la gzugs brnyan tshul du snang // de nas byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin gyis// rgyang shin tu snang bar byas pa de
83b2: ngag las/ / byang chub sems dpa' re res kyang / snying rje chen po'i sgo sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du zhugs par gyur nas/ de dag de bas kyang 'gro ba thams cad la phan pa dang /
83b3: yongs su bsdu ba'i don du zhugs par gyur te/ de ltar mnyam par bzhag pa de dag gi ba spri'i sgo re re nas kyang / 'od gzer sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mngon par 'thon
83b4: par gyur te/ 'od gzer de dag gi sgo re re nas kyang byang chub sems dpa' 'phrul pa'i sprin 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad dang 'dra ba'i lus dang / 'gro ba thams cad la mngon par lta ba'i lus dang / sems
83b5: can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / / 'phrod pa'i lus dang ldan pa mngon par 'thon te/ mngon par 'thon nas kyang / phyogs thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings rgyas par bkad nas/ sems can thams
83b6: cad yang dag par skul zhing yongs su smin pa bya ba dang / gdul ba byed do// lha'i gnas na shi 'pho ba yongs su bstan pa'i sgo dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du skye ba yongs su bstan pa'i sgo dang /
83b7: byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su bstan pa'i sgo dang / rmi lam yongs su bstan pa'i sgo sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis sems can yongs su bskul ba
83b8: byed do/ / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam gyis 'byung ba'i sgo dang / 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su bskyod pa'i sgo dang / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyod pa yongs su bstan pa'i sgo dang / de bzhin

84a1: gshegs pa thams cad na tan bya ba / ra tu bsgrub pa dang / yan lag dang / gag ca pa' bzad pa'i bar la du phyin pa yangs smra sa pa'i sno byung chubasams dpa'i rnam
84a2: par 'phrul pa chen pos brtson 'grus kyi pha ral tu phyin pa yongs su bstan pa'i sgo dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bas ma gtan dang rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa thams cad
84a3: dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi lam gyi dkyil 'khor snang ba rab tu brdzud pa'i sgo dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su btsal ba'i phyir/ chos kyi chog dang yi ge re re'i phyir/ lus grangs med pa yongs
84a4: su bstan pa'i sgo dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi drung du 'gro zhing chos thams cad yongs su dring ba'i sgo dang / dus la ji ltar 'bab pa dang / bsam pa ji ltar 'bab pa dang / bsam pa ji la ba bzhin du
84a5: 'gro ba'i drung du 'gro zhing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su smin par 'gyur ba thob par bya ba'i tshul rgya mtsho snang ba'i rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i sgo dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bsod nams dang ye
84a6: shes kyi tshogs thams cad bdud dang phas kyis rgol bas mi tshugs pa'i stabs kyi rgyal mtshan yongs su bstan pa'i sgo dang / bzo thams cad shes shing mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i shes pa'i sa bon yongs
84a7: su bstan pa'i sgo dang / 'gro ba thams cad las khyad par du 'phags par shes shing mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i ye shes kyis yongs su bstan pa'i sgo dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa'i khyad par
84a8: shes shing mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i ye shes kyis yongs su bstan pa'i sgo dang / sems can thams cad kyi dbang po la 'jug pa'i dbang po nyon mongs pa dang / bag chags sna tshogs yang dag par gzhom

84b1: gas ga mas sa dngasas bdan pa' gyu / dgra 'azugs pasams rnarnams ngasas su par byab du dus pa sa da shA /
84b2: rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu zab med kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag sems can thams cad kyi gnas su phyin par snang ste/ la la ri lha gnas su phyin par snang // la la
84b3: gnas su phyin par snang ngo / / la la ni gnad sbyin gyi gnas su phyin par snang ngo // la la ni dri za'i gnas su phyin par snang ngo // la la ni lha ma yin gyi gnas su byin par snang ngo // la la nin ma mkha' ldangan
84b4: gnas su phyin par snang ngo / / la la ni mi 'am ci'i gnas su phyin par snang do// la la ni lto 'phye chen po'i gnas su phyin par snang ngo // la la ni tshangs pa'i dbang po'i gnas su phyin par snang ngo // la la ni mi
84b5: gnas su phyin par snang ngo / / la la ni gshin rje'i gnas su phyin par snang ngo // la la ni yi dgas kyi gnas su phyin par snang ngo // la la ni sems can dmyal ba'i 'jig rten thams cad du phyin par snang ngo //
84b6: la ni yi dgas kyi skye gnas kyi rgyud thams cad du phyin par snang ngo // mthong bas 'dul ba'i sems can dang / thos pas 'dul ba dang rjes su dran pas 'dul ba dang / dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor gyis 'dul ba dang /
84b7: ming gi chu klung gi sgras 'dral ba dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyis 'dul ba dang / 'od gzer gyi drabs rab tu 'gyed pa dang 'dul ba dang / sems can rnams kyi bsam pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su smin//
84b8: par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i phyir snying rje chen po tha mi dad pa dang / smon lam tha mi dad pa dang / ye shes tha mi dad pa dang / sems can yongs su bsdu ba tha mi dad pa'i tshul du byang chub sems dpa' de dag 'dzeta

85a1: tshal nas rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan rnam pa sna tshogs kyis 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad dang / sems can gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs par byed
85a2: par snang yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs kyi drung nas mi g.yo ste/ la la ni rang gi gnas dang khang pa brtsegs pa dang / stan dang 'khor dang bcas pas/ phyogs bcu rgyas par byed par snang yang / de bzhin gshegs
85a3: pa'i zhabs kyi drung nas mi g.yo'o/ / la la ni sprul pa'i sprin rab tu 'gyed par snang ngo // la la ni sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i don du gcig pa gnyis su med par 'gro bar snang yang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i
85a4: 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor nas mi g.yo'o/ / la la ni dge sbyong gi gzugs/ la la ni tshangs pa'i gzugs/ la la ni rtul zhugs can thams cad kyi cha byad dang / cho ga dang chu zheng gi gzugs/ la la ni sman pa'i gzugs
85a5: la la ni chod pa'i gzugs/ la la ni nyan pas 'tshe bo'i gzugs/ la la ni gar mkhan gyi gzugs/ la la ni lha khyer ba'i gzugs/ la la ni bzo thams cad dang ldan pa'i gzugs su grong dang grong khyer
85a6: dang / grong rdal dang / ljongs dang / khams dang / rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor du phyin par snang ste/ dus kyi dbang gis dus kyi rjes su 'brang zhing ming dang gzugs dang lus mngon par bsgrub pa tha dad pa dang / lus kyi
85a7: kha dog dang dbyibs tshul dang 'dra ba dang dbyangs rnam pa tha dad pa dang / skad rnam pa tha dad pa dang / spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa dang / gnas rnam pa tha dad pas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad
85a8: mig 'phrul lta bur shes pa dang / bzo'i 'khor thams cad rab tu brjod pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi shes pa brjod pas snang ba'i sgron ma dang / bde ba thams cad kyi byin kyi brlabs kyis brgyan pa dang /

85b1: las thams cad snang bar byed pa'i 'od dang ldan pa dang / phyogs thams cad theg pa la gnas pas rab tu spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa chos thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu snang ba la spyod cing / sems
85b2: can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i don du grong dang grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang ljongs dang khams dang / rgyal po'i gnas dag du phyin par snang ngo // de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa gnas pa med pa'i
85b3: khang pa brtsegs san 'dug 'dug pa las bskal pa 'thun pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / rtag tu phyi bzhin 'brar ba'i lag na rdo rje dag dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyi nyam blta ba la brtson zhing sangs rgyas
85b4: thams cad bsnyen bkur bar smon pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i lus kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha dag dang / sngon gyi smon lam gyis rjes su 'brad pa'i rkang gis 'gro ba'i ris su gtogs pa'i lha dag dang / chos mnyan pa
85b5: la mngon par mos pa'i sa'i lha dag dang / snying rje chen po la brtson pa'i lum dang / mtsho dang mtshe'u dang / rdzing bu dang khron pa dang / chu klung gi lha dag dang / shes rab kyi 'od snang bas rab tu gsal ba'i me'i lha dag dang /
85b6: rin po che'i gcod pan thogs pa'i rlung gi lha dag dang / chos kyi phyogs snang bar khong du chud pa'i phyogs kyi lha dag dang / ma rig pa'i mun pa gsal ba la brtson pa'i mtshan mo'i lha dag dang / de bzhin gshegs
85b7: pa'i nyi ma mngon par bsgrub pa la brtson pa'i nyi ma'i lha dag dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi nam mkha'i brgyan pa la brtson pa'i nam mkha'i lha dag dang / 'gro ba thams cad srid pa'i rgya mtsho las bsgral bar brtson
85b8: pa'i gang chen mtsho'i lha dag dang / / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du tshogs yang dag par bstsags pa la brtson zhing / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i spro mngon par 'phags pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i ri'i lha dang / 'gro ba thams cad

86a1: k ye lus brgyan par brtson zhing sangs rgyas thams cad kyi kha dog dang byin gyis brlabs la smon cing brtson pa'i chu klung gi lha dag dang 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems kyi grong rdal yongs su bskyed par
86a2: brtson pa'i grong gi lha dag dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos kyi grong khyer du smon cing mos pa'i klu'i dbang po dag dang / sems can thams cad yongs su srung ba la zhugs pa'i gnod sbyin gyi dpa
86a3: rag dang / sems can thams cad kyi dga' ba'i shugs rnam par 'phel bar bya ba la brtson pa'i dri bo'i dbang po dag dang / yi dgas kyi rgyu thams cad rnam par bzlog pa la btsun pa'i yul bum gyi dpa
86a4: dag dang / sems can thams cad srid pa'i rgya mtsho nas gdon pa'i smon lam gyis zhugs pa'i nam mkha'i lding gi dbang po dag dang / 'jig rten thams cad las 'phags pa'i de bzhin grashegs pa'i sku dang /
86a5: stobs yongs su sgrub par smon lam yongs su skyed pa'i lha ma yin gyi dbang po dag dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mthong bas dga' bar gyur cing / lus rab tu 'dud pa'i lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po dag dang / 'khor
86a6: ba las skyo ba'i yid dang ldan zhing dor blta ba'i lho'i dbang po dag dang / rim gro chen po rab tu byed cing lus rab tu 'dud pa'i tshangs pa'i dbang po dag dang / lhan cig du de dag gis rim gro chen pos mngon par stong
86a7: de mchod cing / de lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par gnon pa'i rgyan phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan par rang gi gnas nas byung ste/ bcom ldan 'das la g.yas phyogs su bskor ba lan brgya phrag du ma
86a8: zhig du byas nas/ mchod pa rnam pa du mas mchod de/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan snga nas phyir byung nas// lho phyogs logs su yul rgyu zhing song ngo // /

86b1: bab pa bdun pa/ de nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis/ cha dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ta'i bus 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa byang chub sems dpa' rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyad phun
86b2: sum tshogs pa de 'dra bas 'dze ta'i tshal nas byung ste/ lho phyogs logs su 'gro ba mthong nas/ de 'di snyam du gyur te/ bdag kyang 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang lhan cig du yul d+ha zhing 'gra
86b3: swam nas/ de dge slong drug bcu rtsa pa kyis bskor cing mdun du byas te/ rang gi gnas nas byung nas/ bcom ldan 'das gangan pa der song ste/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis lo skyabs phyag 'tshal
86b4: nas/ bcom ldan 'das la zhus te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gnang ba dang / bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum du bskor ba byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spu snga nas phyir byung ste/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur
86b5: pa gang na ba der dge slong lhan cig tu spyod pa rab tu byung nas ring po ma lon par gsar du zhugs pa sha stag ste/ 'di ltar dge slong rgya mtsho'i blo dang / legs par byin pa chen po dang / bsod nams kyi 'od dang /
86b6: chen po dang kun khyab sbyin pa dang / rnam dag spyod pa dang / lha'i dpal dbang po'i blo gros dang / tshangs pa'i dpa pa dang / dge slong zhi ba'i blo gros dang / de dag las stsogs pa'i dge slong drug bcu rtsam kun kyang /
86b7: sngon gyi rgyal ba la b+hA bzlas pa/ dge pa'i rtsab bstud pa/ mas pa zan mor gyur pa/ rang ba'i mig yongs su dag pa/ sems rgya chen pas yongs su stod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi phyogs kyi rnam par blta ba la
86b8: mthu yod pa/ chos kyi ngo bo nyid dang / rang bzhin nges par rtogs pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ gzhan la phan par gyur pa'i blo can/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan la mngon par mos pa/ 'jam dpal

87a1: gzhon nur gyur pa'i chos bstan pas 'dul ba sha stag dang 'grogs shing mdun du byas te sngon du bdang nas/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa gang na ba der dong ngo // de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa ti'i bus de ltar
87a2: lam du zhugs te/ 'dod pa'i tshe dge slong de dag kun la bltas nas/ dge slong rgya mtsho'i blo la smras pa/ rgya mtsho'i blo byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal gyi lus mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos rnam par brgyan
87a3: cing yongs su dag pa/ lha dang mir bcas pas bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su dag cing sems can tshad med pa'i dga' ba yongs su skyed pa dang / 'od gzer gyi dra ba'i rgyan sem
87a4: can dpag tu med pa'i sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar byed pa dang / 'khor phun sum tshogs pa sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa bas yongs su bzung ba dang / lam gyi rgyan 'gro ni lam mig mangs ris su gnas pa dang /
87a5: lam rnam par gnon pa'i rkyen phyogs kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la mngon par lta bas gnas pa dang / bsod nams phun sum tshogs pa'i rgyan g.yas g.yon nas gter chen por mngon par 'thon pa dang /
87a6: sngon gyi sangs rgyas la rim gro byas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang rgyu mthun pas/ shing gi gseb thams cad nas rgyan mang po 'byung ba dang / 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad la mchod pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par
87a7: 'bebs shing btud de phyag 'tshal ba dang / phyogs bcu nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis 'od gzer gyi dra ba'i dkyil 'khor mang po bkye ba/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rab tu sgrog cing sme bar
87a8: 'char ba la ltos shig ces/ de dag la stsogs pa tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bus/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la lam du zhugs pa'i yon tan gyi rgyan tshad med pa dag/ dge slong de dag yongs su bstan to/

87b1: brjod do// bshad do// smras so// bkrol lo// rab tu brjod do// rnam par bya'o// gsal bar byas so// de ltar gnas brtan shA ri'i bus 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i yon tan ci tsam du brjod pa de tsam du
87b2: dge slong de dag gi sems rnam par dag par gyur to/ / rab tu dad par gyur to// dga' ba'i shugs rnam par 'phel bar gyur to// mos par skyes par gyur to// de dag gi sems kyi rgyud lus su rung bar gyur to//
87b3: dbang po rab dang par gyur te// yid bde ba rnam par 'phel bar gyur to// yid mi bde ba rab tu byung bar gyur to// sems kyi skyon dang bral bar gyur to// sgrib pa thams cad rdzir ldog par gyur to// sangs rgyas
87b4: blta ba la mngon par mos par gyur to/ / sangs rgyas kyi chos la sems rab tu gzhol bar gyur to// byang chub sems dpa'i dbang po yongs su dag par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa'i dad pa'i shugs skye
87b5: bar gyur to/ / snying rje chen po 'byung bar gyur to// pha rol tu phyin pa'i dkyil 'khor gnon par gyur to// snying rje chen po yongs su skye bar gyur ro// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas rgya mtsho yongs su snang bar gyur to//
87b6: de ltar de dag thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du mos pa'i shugs thob par gyur nas 'di skad 'dzer to// mkhan po bdag cag kyang skyes bu dam pa de'i drung du phyin par mdzad du gsol zhes nas/ de nas tshe dang ldan pa
87b7: shA ri'i bu dge slong de dag 'grogs te/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa gang na ba der song nas 'di skad ces smras so// 'jam dpal dge slong 'di dag ni khyod la blta bar 'dod pa dag go/ de nas 'jam dpal
87b8: gzhon nur gyur pas/ dge slong de dag dang 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gi sa'i phyogs de tsam du bcas par glang po'i lta stangs kyis gzi dang ldan par khyab par bltas pa dang / de'i rjes su dge slong de dag gis

88a1: 'jas dpal gzhon nur gyur ba rkang pa gnyis la smra bas phyag 'tshal nas/ thal ba sbyar ta'adi skad ces smras so// skyes bu dam pa khyod mthong ba dang / khyod la phyag 'tshal ba 'dag pa'i rtsa
88a2: 'di dang / bdag cag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba gzhan khyod kyis mkhyen pa dang / mkhan pos thugs su chud pa dang / gang yang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shag kya thub pas mngon du gzigs pa'i dge ba'i
88a3: rtsa ba des/ khyod ci 'dra ba de 'dra bar gyur te/ rnam pa 'di 'dra ba'i lus thob par shog shig/ rnam pa 'di 'dra ba'i dbyangs dang / rnam pa 'di 'dra ba'i mtshan dang / 'di lta bu'i rnam par 'phrul pa dag kyang khyod
88a4: ji lta ba bzhin du thob par shog shig ces/ dge slong de dag gis de skad du smras pa dang / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas dge slong de dag la 'di skad ces smras so// dge slong dag yongs su ma skyo ba'i
88a5: sems bskyed pa bcu dang ldan pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo theg pa chen po la zhugs pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa lta smos kyang ci dgos kyi/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa yang gnon par 'gyur
88a6: ro/ / bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad blta ba dang / bsnyen bkur ba dang / mchod pa dang rim gro bya ba yongs su mi skyo ba'i sems bskyed pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad bstsa
88a7: pa las phyir mi ldog cing yongs su mi spro ba'i sems bskyed pa dang / chos thams cad brtsal ba la yongs su mi spro ba'i sems bskyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa thams
88a8: cad sbyor ba la yongs su mi skyo ba'i semos bskyed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin thams cad yongs su bsgrub pa la yongs su mi skyo ba'i sems bskyed pa dang / dus gcig nas

88b1: gcig tu brgyud pa thams cad du 'jug pa la yongs su ma skye ba'i sems bskyed pa dang / phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing rgya mtsho rgyas par dag zhing yongs su dag par bya ba la yongs su ma skyo ba
88b2: sems bskyed pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba la yongs su mi skyo ba'i sems bskyed pa dang / zhing dang bskal pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyong
88b3: pa mngon par bsgrub pa la yongs su mi skyo ba'i sems bskyed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sbyar bas sems can gcig yongs su smin par bya ba'i
88b4: tshul du sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya bas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs gcig yongs su bsgrub pa la yongs su mi skyo ba'i sems bskyed pa'o// dge slong dag yongs su mi skyo
88b5: pa'i sems bskyed pa bcu po 'di dag dang ldan pa'i rigs bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo dad pa dang ldan pa ni dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad la yongs su 'grub par 'gyur ro/ / 'khor ba'i rgyud thams cad las byar
88b6: ldog par 'gyur ro/ / 'jig rten gyi rgyud thams cad las gyen du 'phags par 'gyur ro// nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sa thams cad las phyir yongs su 'da' bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa
88b7: thams cad kyi rig spyi dang rgyud du 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam la yang dag par 'grub par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yon tan gyi nan tan
88b8: la rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la yongs su dag par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi stobs la yang dag par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// bdud dang /

89a1: pas kyis rgol ba thams cad rab tu 'dul bar 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i sa yongs su gnon par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa dang shin tu nye bar 'gyur ro// de nas dge slong
89a2: de dag gis chos kyi tshul 'di thos nas/ sangs rgyas thams cad rnam par mthong ba la chags pa med pa'i mig gi yul zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob par gyur to// de'i mthus phyogs bcu mtha' las
89a3: med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na bzhugs pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mthong bar gyur to/ / 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi 'gro ba'i rgyud du skyes pa'i sems can de dag kyang ma lus
89a4: pa mthong bar gyur to/ / 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can rnams kyang ma lus par mthong bar gyur to// 'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang rnam par bya ba sna tshogs su mthong bar gyur to// 'jig
89a5: chen gyi khams de dag na rdul shin tu phra ba ji snyed yod pa de dag kyang grang ba'i tshul gyis rab tu shes par gyur to/ / sems can de dag gi rin po'i'atsho'i gnas dang / longs spyod de dag kyang mthong bar gyur/
89a6: de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi dbyangs kyi yan lag rgya mtsho yang thos par gyur to// chos bstan pa de dag kyang tshig dang yi ge dang nges pa'i tshig dang skad dang ming dang brdas yongs su shes par gyur to// sems
89a7: can de dag gi sems dang dbang po dang / bsam pa la yang / me bar lta bar gyur to// sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha'i tshe rabs bcu yang rjes su dran par gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi chos kyi 'khor lo
89a8: bcu'i nges pa'i tshig mngon par bsgrubs pa la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur to/ / rdzu 'phrul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa mngon par bsgrub pa bcu la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur to// bstan pa'i tshul mngon par

89b1: bar bsgrub pa bcu la yang dag par rab tu zhugs par gyur to/ / rjes su bstan pa'i tshig mngon par bsrub pa bcu la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi so so yang dag par rig
89b2: pa'i tshul mngon par bslab pa bcu la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur to/ / ting nge 'dzin de thob ma thag tu/ byang chub kyi sems kyi yan lag stong phrag bcu yang yongs su rdzogs par gyur to// ting nge 'dzin stong phrag
89b3: bcu yang yongs su non par gyur to/ / pha rol tu phyin pa'i yan lag stong phrag bcu yang rnam par dag par 'gyur te/ sdang ba chen po rab tu thob cing shes rab chen po'i dkyil 'khor gyis snang bar gyur pa de dag
89b4: gis byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa bcu rab tu thob par gyur to/ / de ltar mngon par shes pa'i myu gu gzhon zhing shin tu phra ba thob ste/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa brtan pa la gnas pa de dag 'jam
89b5: dpal gzhon nur gyur pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la yang dag par bskul nas rab tu bkod do// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la rab tu gnas pa de dag
89b6: thon ma chen po'i rgya mtshol thugs shing / mngon par sgrub par gyur to// de ltar smon lam chen po'i rgya mchos mngon par sgrub pa'i sems rnam par dag pas yus yongs su dag par btu thob par gyur to// 2ma
89b7: rnam par dag pas lus yang ba rab tu thob par gyur to/ / da ltar lus rnam par dag pa dang / lus yang bas mngon par shes pa'i sgod de dag shin tu yangs par byed pas/ mi nyams shing rjes su 'brang ba'i mngon par
89b8: shes pa rab tu thob par gyur to/ / mngon par shes pa de thob pas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i rkang pa'i drung nas kyang mi g.yo la/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su bsgrub pa'i phyir phyogs bcur

90a1: gags shAg+sa/ ya sa nga ga tu yang na
90a2: chub tu gnapa/ mtha byas yul nA zhing lha phyogs logs su snying pa'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba'i grong rdal chen po gang na pa ra legs pa song / byin nam grong ngas chen po stong pa'i 'byung gnas kyi
90a3: phyogs logs na/ / nags tshal chen po rgyam sna chags kyi rgyal mtshan gyi mun ces bya ba rtson gyisangs rgyas bzhugs bzhugs pa'i mchod rten sems can smin par byed pa'i don du/ da bzhin gshegs pas
90a4: byin gyis brlabs pa zhing mtha' yas par ming gi sgra rjes su grags pa dang / sngon cang bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdzad pa'i tshe/ yongs su btang bar dka' ba dum yongs su gtang bste/
90a5: sa'i phyogs de na lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa rnams rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par mchod pa la brtson pa'i gnas

90a8: zung rnam par bzlog ste/ lha dang mir skye ba yongs su 'dzin par gyur nas/ der klu stong phrag bcu bla na med pa yang dag par rtogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par gyur to// chos bstan pa'i tshe/ sems

90b1: can gyi khams mtha' yas pa dang dpung med pa theg pa gsum gyis dus gzhan dang gzhan da rnam par 'dul bar gyur to/ / de nas skyid pa'i 'byung gnas kye ma rnams kyis/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur byur ba skyang sa/
90b2: 'byung gnas kyi grong rdal du phyin te/ sbrul sna tshogs kyi rgyan sna tshogs kyi mchod rten gyi gzhi 'di nyid na rnam par spyod do zhes thos nas/ dge bsnyen tshong dpon shes rab chen po la stsogs pa dge bsnyen par

90b7: moni/ dge bsnyen ma 'od bzang mo dang / lus bzang mo dang / dge ba yod pa dang / dge ba'i dpal dang / zla ba'i dpal dang / zla ba'i 'od dang / dpal gyi 'od dang / dpal bzang mo dang / dge bsnyen ma mig bzang

91a1: spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la lan gsum du bskor ba byas nas/ phyogs gcig tu 'kha do// dal tshong dpon gyi bran bzangs na/ tshong dpon gyi bu brtul

91a3: po dang / tshang dpon gyi bu nor 'od bzang po dang / de dag la stsogs pa tshong dpon gyi bu lnga brgyas bskor cing mdun du byas te/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa gang na ba der dong nas/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'o/

91a5: bzang po dang / yid du 'ong ba'i bzhin dang / brtan pa'i blo gros dang / dpal bzang mo dang / tshangs pas byin dang / dpal gyi 'od dang / bu mo 'od bzang mo la stsogs pa bu mo lnga brgyas bskor cing mdun du byas te/ 'jam
91a6: dpal gzhon nur gyur pa gang na ba der dong nas/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la lan gsum du bskor ba byas nas/ phyogs
91a7: gcig tu 'kho do/ / de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas snying pa'i 'byung gnas kyi grong rdal nas skyes pa dang / bud med dang khye'u dang bu mo de dag 'dus te 'khod par shes nas/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin
91a8: bstan pa'i byin gyis zil gyis mnan te/ byams pa chen po'i byin gyis tshim par byas nas/ snying rje chen po'i byin gyis chos bstan pa mngon par bsgrubs te/ ye shes kyi byin gyis sems dang bsam pa

91b1: rnam par phyin mams pa / / na pam tshas btsun par dag / dgran rgyan yangs la basmras sa// nga pan sa ban dgA sa shes byab coM b+h+ya g-is d+hash+tha
91b2: dwab nor bzangs shes bya ba de thog ma ma'i mngal du zhugs ma thag du khyim do'i 'khor kun nas rnam par phye ba'i rin po che sna bdun gyi sreng pa 'thon par gyur to/ / r-in po n+d+ha'i stong ba dadag gi 'gan
91b3: rin po che'i gter bdun yod de/ gser dang dngul dang / bai dUr+ya dang / shal dang mu tig dmar po dang / a sma gang ba dang / mu si ra gal ba dang / rin po che sde bdun gyi rin po che'i sdong po de dag kyang gter
91b4: de dag nas skyes te/ sa'i gzhi brtol nas mngon par mthon par gyur to// de yan lag dang nying lag thams cad yongs su rdzogs te/ zla ba bcu lon nas btsas pa dang / de'i tshe gter chen po bdun po de dag kyang
91b5: chu zheng dang rngams su khru bdun tsam du sa'i steng nas mngon par 'phags te/ snang bar gyur nas rnam par snang zhing mdzes par gyur te// khyim der rin po che sna tshogs kyi snod lnga brgya yang byung bar gyur te/ 'di/
91b6: ltar mar gyi snod dang / til mar gyi snod dang / sbrang rtsi'i snod dang / mar sar gyi snod dang / gzhan dag kyang so so nas yo byad sna tshogs thams cad kyis yongs su gang bdag ste/ 'di ltar rdo rje'i snod spros
91b7: sna tshogs kyis yongs su gang ba dang / spos kyi snod gos sna tshogs kyis yongs su gang ba dang / man shel gyi snod kha zas dang / spyan gzigs sna tshogs ro mchog du zhim pas yongs su gang ba dang / nor
91b8: bu'i snod rin po che sna tshogs kyis yongs su gang ba dang / gser gyi snod dngul sil mas yongs su gang ba dang / dngul gyi snod gser phyes gang ba dang / phra men gyi snod nor bu rin po che bai dUr+yas yongs su

92a2: tig dmar po'i snod a sma gar pas yongs su gang ba dang / nor bu rin po che skar ma rgyal mtshan gyi snod rin po che'i chu 'dang gis yongs su gang ba dang / nor bu rin po che chu 'angang gi snod nor bu rin po che skar ma'i
92a3: rgyal mtshan gyis yongs su gang ba dang / de dag la stsogs pa rin po che'i snod lnga brgya 'thon par gyur to// tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs de btsas ma thag du khyim dang ba 'dang / mdzod thams cad du nor dang 'brung

92a8: nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la bltas te/ dga' ba'i gtam byas nas de la 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas kyi chos

92b1: thams cad yang dag par bsdu zhing 'thon par bya ba las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas thams cad gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa thams cad/
92b2: shes par bya ba las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo dang sprul pa'i rkyen las kyang brtsams
92b3: sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnam par dag pa las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi sku'i yongs su grub pa las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas
92b4: thams cad kyi gsung rnam par phye ba las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan rnam par dag pa las kyang brtsams/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid las kyang
92b5: brtsams te/ chos kyang bstan par gyur to// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzang dang / skye bo'i tshogs chen po de dag chos dang 'thun pa'i gtam gyis
92b6: bstan te/ yang dag par bskul nas spro ba bskyed de/ dga' bar byas nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du sems bskyed du bcud de/ sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su dran par byas nas/ skyid pa'i
92b7: 'thung gnas kyi grong rdal de'i sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos bstan pas/ byin gyis rlabs te bde bar byas de de nas song ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis 'jam dpal gzhon
92b8: nur gyur pa las rnam pa de lta bu'i sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang / che ba nyid thos nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mos shing brtson pas phyi bzhin du 'brang ste/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la

93a1: tshigs su bcad de mngon par bstod do/ / blo gros chen po mtha' yas spyod yul can// khyod kyi mthus ni sems can sman slad du// bdag kyang byang chub mchog du zhugs par gyur// de la nges pa gang
93a2: mchis bdag las gson/ / dga' ba'i chu bkang 'obs kyis kun nas bskor// nga rgyal dregs pa'i rab mtho bar brtsegs// sems can lam rgyud sgo rnams btsud cing gdangs// de 'dri'i khyim ni srid gsum
93a3: ming ldan mo/ / de ni gti mug ma rig gzings pas khebs// 'dod chags zhe sdang me lces rab tu gdungs// rtag par bdud kyi dbang po'i dbang gyur pas// de la byis pa ma rig rten kyang 'chab// sred pa'i sgrog
93a4: dang zhags pa shin tu glags/ / g.yo dang sgra'i skyon gyis 'thobartsams shing // the tsom yid gnyis dag gis mig mdongs pa/ log pa phyin phyogs lam la rab tu zhugs// phrag dog ser sna'i theg pas btags
93a5: shing bcings/ / yi dgas byol song sems dmyal mi khom rgyu// rga shi nad dang skye bas rab tu mnar // mgo rmongs lam rgyud 'khor lo kun tu 'khor// de la khyod ni thugs rje rnam dag pa'i// dkyil 'khor ye shes 'od
93a6: gzer snang ba mdzad/ / nyon mongs rgya mtsho bsgom par shar ta 'phags// nyi ma 'dra bas bdag la snang ba mdzod// byams pa bsgoms pas dkyil 'khor rdzogs shing nya// bsod nams zla 'od bde ba'i gzer 'gyed pa
93a7: sems can kun gyi gnas su shar gyur gyis/ / zla ba nya ba lta bus bdag snang mdzad// dkar mthu thams cad yongs bsogs dkor mnga' zhing // chos dbyings mkha' la chags pa med mnga' ba// chos kyi 'khor lo
93a8: rin chen sngon 'dres pas/ / rgyal por gyur pas bdag la bstan du gsol// byang chub theg pa'i smon lam mthu mdanga' ste// bsod nams ye shes shin tu yang bsags shing // sems can kun la phan pa'i don

93b1: zhugs pa'o/ / ded dpon chen pos bdag kyang bskyang du gsol// bzod pa brtan zhing sra bi'i go mnabs te// ye shes spyan mang 'thugs rje'i phyag ring bas// bdud kyi zag dpung tshogs rnams mngon 'gyur ba // dpa' bo chen po
93b2: bdag gi bsel yang mdzad/ / chos kying rabaskal brtan bzugs shing // ting 'dzin mchog gi snga mos kun nas bkang // nyon mongs sgrag can la min 'dul mdzad pa// brgya byin byung pas bdag kyang gzigs su gsol/
93b3: kyis pa'i gnas snang khams gsum 'a pa na// 'on mongs las rnams rnam par bsal ba mkhyen// dz+ha'i sa dang la mchud 'khor tshangs par// me ma brlabs bdag kyang thal bstan gsol// ngan 'gro'i marnam
93b4: par bzlog mdzad cing / bde bar 'gro ba'i lam rnams rnam stong ba// 'jig rten can gyi lam gyi rgyung las 'das// bdag la'ang thar pa'i sngon bstan drugasol// rtag dang bdag dang ba bang 'du shes ldan// laga'
93b5: slonga'i skyabs kyis skyabs gyur gyis/ / bden pa'i ye shes spyan rnomachog mnga' bas// thar sgo bdag la'ang myung du dbye bar gsol// yang dag log pa'i lam la mkhas byar cing // lam gyis rgyas dang tshul la bas
93b6: mi mnga'/ lam rnams kun gyis 'dul ba thugs su chud/ bdag la byang chub shul ni bdag la bstan du gsaso//
93b7: yang dgas pa'isa'i thar la thugs// sangs rgyas can gyi yan tanam gyis babran// sangs rgyas tshas legs sa rtagacar 'babs pa// byang chub bralan bdagal bstan du gsol// la ba gang 'dus mtshan
93b8: rnams dang / / da ltar byung ba'i rgyal ba snang mdzad pa// sems can gtso bo legs par gshegs pa'i phyogs// de yang lam gron mdzad pa'i bdag bstan gsol// las kyi 'khrul 'khor tshul la mi bsnyengs pa//

94a1: chos theg shing rta'i 'khrul 'khor mkhyen gyur cing // ye shes theg pa'i tshul la rnam nges pa// byang chub theg pa bdag la bshad du gsol// mos shing smon pa'i 'khor lo'i mu khyud can// bzod pa rdo rje'i//
94a2: snying rje srog shing chen// dad pa'i gnya' shing rin chen lags sbas pa'i// byang chub theg la bdag kyang skyon du gsol// gzangs rnams kun gyis rnam dag dkyil 'khor can// byams pa brtsegs pa dga'
94a3: bas rab brgyan pa/ / so so yang dag rig pa'i dril 'breng can// theg mchog bzang pos bdag la bstan du gsol// tshangs pa'i spyod pa'i lam gyis mngon par brgyan// ting 'dzin bud med khrag khrig kun nas
94a4: rgyu/ chos kyi nga'i dbyangs chen chab sgrags pa// theg pa'i dam pas bdag la bstan du gsol// bsdu ba bzhi'i mi zad mdzod ldan pa// ye shes rin chen yon tan pr-ing gis brgyan// khrel yod dul ba'i
94a5: 'phreng bas mchog bsdams pa'i/ / theg pa dam pa bdag la bstan du gsol// sbyin pa'i 'od gzang dkyil 'khor bzang po can// tshul khrims tsan dan snying rje'i byug ldan zhing // bzod pa'i gzar kyis
94a6: mtshan rnams dam sbyang ba'o/ / thug pa'i mchog la myur du ba dag bzhag gsol// sems can thams cad 'dul las mi ldog pa// bsam gtan ting 'dzin grong khyer mthong ston cing // shes rab thatha/
94a7: gnyis 'byor 'thun 'gro rgya ba'i// chos kyi theg pa'i mchog la bdag bzhag gsol// smon lam 'khor los lam gyi 'khor spong ba// chos kyi gzungs dam mthu brtan tshe ldan zhing // ye shes
94a8: 'khrul 'khor legs sbyangs legs byas pa'i/ / chos kyi theg pa de la bdag skyon gsol// kun tu bzang po'i spyod pas rab sbyangs shing // sems can lta bas rgyu la thogs med pa// kun tu bzang po'i

94b1: spyod pas gnon gyur pa'i/ / ye shes theg pas bdag la btud tu gsol// de nas brtan pas rdo rje bzhin gnas pa// ye shes sgyu mas legs sbyangs legs byas shing / sgrib dang chags pa thams
94b2: tsad gcod pa'i/ / bzang po'i thag la bdag kyang skyon par gsol// 'gro mnyam dri med shin tu yangs gyur pas/ sems can thams cad skyob pas bde sgrub cing // chos dbyings shin tu rgya chen nam
94b3: snang ba'i/ byang chub theg la bdag kyang bskyon du gsol// sdug bsngal phung po rab 'byung gcod byed pa// nyon mongs las kyi rdul mang spyod sel cing // bdud dang phas kyi rgol ba kun 'jom pa'i// chos kyi
94b4: thag la ba dag kyang bskyon du gsol/ / phyogs rnams kun tu ye shes rab snang ba// chos dbyings nam mkha' rnam par grub byed cing // sems can kun gyi bsam pa rdzogs pa'i// chos kyi theg la bdag
94b5: kyang bston du gsol/ / rnam dag mkha' ltar tshad med mi zad pa// sred dang ma rig lta ba'i skyon med cing // sems can kun la phan par rab gnas pa'i// chos kyi theg la bdag kyang skyon du gsol// rlung can
94b6: langs pa'i shugs kyi shugs ldan pas/ / smon lam mthu yis 'jig rten kun 'dzin cing // zhi ba'i gnas rab kun sar skyel byed pa'i// chos kyi theg la bdag kyang bskyon du gsol/ sa chen bzhi'i stobs rnams dang ldan pa
94b7: snying rje'i mthu dang shugs kyis khrar khyer zhing / / ye shes lo thag 'gro ba nyer 'tsho ba'i// thag pa'i mchog la bdag kyang bskyon du gsol// nyi ma lta bur 'gro ba nyer 'tsha zhing // bsdu ba rab yangs 'a#
94b8: dkyil 'khor can/ / gzungs kyi stobs mchog dag pa'i 'od bzang ba'i// ye shes nyi ma bdag la bstan du gsol// bskal pa mang po du ma rab brlabs pas// rgyu'i tshul dang sa kun mkhas gyur pa// gang gis

95a1: 6/ / 'dus byas grong khyer gzhom 'gyur ba'i// shus btan rdo rje 'a phags pas bdag la bsngal du gsol// sangs rgyas legs kun bslab pa bran sum gyis// ye shes rgya mtsho yangs pa gang zhig la// tshad
95a2: med rgya mtsho'i blo mangs brlabs gyur pas/ / de legs mi 'dra 'phags pas bka' stsal gsol// gang na yang dag spyan mnga' khyod bzhugs shing // ye shes rgyal po'i cod pan legs brgyan te// chos kyi dbu
95a3: thod dam pas dbu bcings pa'i/ / chos kyi rgyal po'i pho brang bdag kyang ston// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur byas glang po'i lha lhangs kyis bltas te/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi
95a4: bu da ltar khyod kyis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed de/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rjes su 'brang zhing byang chub sems dpa'i lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba 'dod de/ byang chub sems
95a5: dpa' spyod pa yongs su dri bar bsam pa legs so/ / rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams la snyan cing bsten pa dang / rim gror bya ba 'di ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su grub par 'gyur
95a6: pa'i gzhi yin te/ 'di ni 'thun pa'i rgyu yin gyis/ rigs kyi bu de bas khyod kyis dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsnyen bkur bas yongs su ma skyo bar gyis shig/ nor bzangs kyis smras pa/ 'phags pa ji ltar byang
95a7: chub sems dpa'as byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi/ ji ltar nan tan du bgyi/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa brtsam par bgyi/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'as
95a8: byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad par bgyi/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'as byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su rdzogs par bgyi// ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'as byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs

95b1: swa sbyang bar brdzi/ ji ltang byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug par bgyi/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'as byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mngon par bsgrub par bgyi/ ji skang byang chub sems
95b2: dpo'i spyod pa'i rjes su 'brang bar bgyi/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'as byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa la lhag par dmigs par bgyi// ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyas par brgya/
95b3: ji ltar byang chub sems dpas kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba rgya cher bstan du gsol// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nu gyur pas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la
95b4: tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ / dag pa'i bsod nams gang chen mtsho// de ltar khyod na nga'i drung ngu nyer phyin te// snying rje snying rtse rgya chen gyi// yid ldan byang chub dam pa tshal ba lags// 'gro ba thams cad grol don
95b5: spyod pa mtshungs med don sngon lam rab 'dabs shing / / 'gro ba kun gyi skyabs 'gyur ba// byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa'i tshul 'di yin// byang chub sems dpa'i brtan pa rnams// 'khor ba'i nang na sum
95b6: yid kyis spyod cing gangadag kun du bzang po'o/ / spyod pa thub med chags med 'thob par 'gyur// bsod nams 'od can bsod nams dpal// de ltar khyod ni kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la// 'grol pa na phyir sngon
95b7: byeng ba/ bsod nams rgya mdzad ga zhing dag pa'i mtshan// mtha' dang dab med char med pa'o// phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten sangs rgyas kun kyang mthong bar 'gyur// dran pa'i mtha dang stobs kyis kyang // de dag
95b8: chos kyi sprin kyang yongs su 'dzin par 'gyur/ / de ltar khyod kyis phyogs bcu'i// sangs rgyas zhang rnams kun tu rgyal ba mthong nas kyang // byang chub spyod pa'i don gyi phyir// de dag kun la smon lam rgya mtsho dag

96a1: byang 'gyur/ / 'jig rten gcog la slob byed cang // gang rnams sangs rgyas sa la gnas na btsal byas shing // 'di tshul rgya mtshor zhugs gyur pa// de dag kun kyang thams cad gzigs par 'gyur// byang
96a2: ni 'byamaklas zhing kun tu/ / bskal mang zhing rdul snyed du kun tu bzang po'o// spyod pa'i dam pa spyod byas shing // byang chub dam pa zhi ba 'thob par 'gyur// zhing rnams mtha' dang dbus med pa// ma lus kun tu bskal pa rgya mtshor
96a3: spyad par gyis/ / kun tu bzang po'i spyod mchog phyir// smon lam rgya chen yongs su rdzogs par byos// khyod ni smon lam thos gyur nas// sems can khrag khrig dga' ba yongs su skyes gyur cing // kun tu bzang po'i ye
96a4: shes kyis/ / byang chub mchog tu smon pa byed la ltos// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas// tshigs su bcad pa de dag smras nas// tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la/ 'di skad ces sgo'o// rigs kyi bu de ltar
96a5: khyod bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed cing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su btsal bas sems dpa' legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu 'di ltar bla na med pa yang dag
96a6: par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa de lta bu'i sems can yang rab tu dkon te/ de bas kyang gang gis kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed nas/ byang chub sems dpa' spyod
96a7: pa yongs su tshol ba de lta bu'i sems can ni chos dkon no/ / rigs kyi bde bas na byang chub sems dpas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes thob par bya ba'i phyir/ yang dag pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen las gdon
96a8: mi za bar rtogs pa thob par gyis shig/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen yongs su btsal ba la yongs su skyo ba'i yid med par gyis shig/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen blta ba la ngoms pa med par gyis shig/ dge ba'i

96b1: bshes gnyen gyis bstan pa la 'thun par 'dzin par gyis shig/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis thabs mkhas pa'i spyod pa la khong khro ba med par gyis shig/ rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na/ yul ma mo/
96b2: nom mchog ces bya ba yod de/ de na mgul legs pa zhes bya ba'i ri zhig yod pa de la/ dge slong sprin gyi dpal zhes bya ba 'dug gis de'i gan du song la/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'/
96b3: spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan dbya ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa brtsam par bya ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa la
96b4: spyod par bya ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / ji ltar yongs su dag par bya ba dang / ji ltar 'dug par bya ba dang / ji ltar mngon par bsgrub par bya ba dang / ji ltar rjes
96b5: su 'brang bar bya ba dang / ji ltar dmigs par bya ba dang / ji ltar rgyas par bya ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sa kun tu bzang po spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba dris shig dang / dge ba'i ba
96b6: gnyen de khyod la kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor ston to/ / de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dga' rangs te/ mgu zhing nyams pa de la tshim zhing yid bde ba skyes nas/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i rkang
96b7: pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ lan brgya stong du ma bskor ba byas te/ lan brgya stong tu mang phyir bltas te/
96b8: dge ba'i bshes gnyen yid du 'ong ba'i sems dang ldan pas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen mi mthong mi bzod de/ gdong mchi mas gang bang du zhing 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i drung nas song ngo // de nas tshong

97a1: maud kyi bu nor bzangs mtha kyis yul mi mo gya nom mchog ces bya ba der song ste byin nas/ yul mi mgya no ma mchog nas rnam par bzlas te/ sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsabs byung zhing las
97a2: chen pos rkyen ces brlabs pa'i longs spyod yid du 'ong ba la yongs su spyod cing ri mgul legs pa gang na ba der byin nas/ mgul legs pa'i ri la 'dzegs te/ dge slong sprin gyi dpal tshol tshol zhing /
97a3: shar phyogs logs su byung ngo // de bzhin du lho dang nub dang byang dang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub byang gi phyogs mtshams su
97a4: yang byung ste/ bla 'og tu zhi zhing dge slong sprin gyi dpal tshol tshol ba las/ des zhag bdun lon pa dang / dge slong sprin gyi dpal ri rtse gcig gcig gi sman ljongs na 'chag cing 'dug pa mthong nas/
97a5: de dge slong sprin gyi dpal gang na ba der song ste/ dge slong sprin gyi dpal gyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ dge slong sprin gyi dpal la g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te/ mdun du
97a6: 'dug nas thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces smras so/ / 'phags pas thugs su chud par mdzad du gsol// bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na/ ji ltar byang chub
97a7: sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyor pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa brtsam pa dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la spyad par
97a8: bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su rdzogs par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar yongs su dag par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar 'jug par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar rjes su 'brang bar bgyi ba dang / ji ltar

97b1: mngon par bsgrub par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar lhag par dmigs par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar rgyas par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs
97b2: par 'gyur ba ma 'tshal te/ 'phags pa khyod ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams la gdam ngag dang / rjes su ston pa mdzad ces thos nas/ 'phags pa ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' bla na med pa yang
97b3: dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'byung bar 'gyur ba bdag la bstan du gsol/ / de skad ces smras pa dang / dge slong sprin gyi dpal gyis tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs
97b4: kyi bu de ltar khyod kyis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed cing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su 'dri ba legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ byang chub
97b5: sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su btsal ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul yongs su btsal ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'byung ba rnam par dag pa yongs su btsal ba dang / byang chub sem
97b6: dpa'i spyod pa rgya chen po'i rnam par dag pa yongs su btsal ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa bsgrub pa rnam par dag pa yongs su btsal ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam
97b7: par thar pa yongs su bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i snang ba'i snying rje'i rgyud yongs su bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'gro ba'i bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rjes su 'brang ba dang / byang
97b8: chub sems dpa' 'khor ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i sgo yongs su bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnams kyi 'dus byas dang / 'dus ma byas kyi skyon dang / 'jigs pas mi gos pa'i rgyud

98a1: yongs su btsal ba 'din dka'o/ / shin tu dga'o// rigs kyi bu kho bo na mos pa'i stobs kyis dbang gis mig gi blo gros dang / rang ba'i bag rnam par dag pas kun du mngon pa sa pa'i
98a2: shas kyi 'ang snang ba/ phyir phyogs med pa dang / yul kun la thogs pa med cing bsgrubs pa med pa thams cad dang bral ba'i lhag mthong la mkhas pa dang / mig gi yul kun nas yongs su dag pa'i
98a3: las rnam par dag pa dang / phyogs kyi rgyud 'byamaklas pa thams cad du mngon par 'dud pa'i lus kyis 'dud pa la mkhas pa dang / sang sa rgyas thams cad kyichos kyi sprin yongs sa 'dzin pa'i ga
98a4: sa stobs kyis phyogs kyi rgyud thams cad nas mngon du gzigs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mthong ste/ 'di ltar shar phyogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa gcig kyang mthong ngo // sangs rgyas
98a5: gnyis dang bcu dang / sangs rgyas brgya dang / sangs rgyas stong dang / sangs rgyas brgya phrag song dang / sangs rgyas bya ba dang / sangs rgyas bya ba brgya dang / sangs rgyas bye ba stong dang / sangs rgyas byeb brgya/
98a6: phrag stong dang / sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong nas de bzhin gshegs pa tshad med pa dang / dpag tu med pa/ grangs med pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa mtshungs pa med pa/ kun tu mtha' yas pas
98a7: mtshams med pa/ gzhal du med pa/ brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag kyang mthong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa 'jam bu gling gi rdul shin tra pra ba snyed kyang mthong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa/
98a8: gleng bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / stong dang stong gnyis pa dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing ga rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang mthong / de bzhin

98b1: gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang mthong ngo / / de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing steng gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
98b2: dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhang brgya phrag stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba phrag brgya'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / sangs rgyas

98b7: ba dang / dbyibs sna tshogs mnga' ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs mnga' ba dang / khyu mchog gi mthu dang rnam par rol pa sna tshogs mnga' ba dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan rnam pa tshogs mnga' ba dang /

99a1: dag nas pa na tshogs mnga' ba dang / 'thaba' bsam pa jil ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs par mdzad pa dang / mngan par 'amang rgyu ba rnam par dag pa' skas rnam par 'phrul pa rnam pa rnag

99b2: pa thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa mthong zhing rnam par dmigs pa mi 'bral bas/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa'i sgo bskal par btags pa rab tu thob pa dang / gang gis dus thams cad du de bshin

100a1: de bzhin gshegs pa re re skyil mo krung du bzhugs pas kyang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rgyas par khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sku rnam par 'jug pas/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa

100b1: dang nam mkha' kun tu snang bas/ gang gis sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa'i sgo nam mkha'i sgro btags pa rab tu thob pa/ de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon tan brjod par nus ra skan/ song rigs kyi bu lho phyogs
100b2: gyi rgyud 'di nyid na phyogs kyi ljongs rgya mtsho'i sgo zhes bya ba yod pa de na/ dge slong rgya mtsho'i sprin ces bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'as byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la
100b3: bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig dang / rig kyi ba dge pa'i bshes gnyen de khyod la dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs dang / rgyu yongs su ston par 'gyur ro// tshogs kyis rgya chen po yang 'dang chung

101a1: sangs rgyas rma ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// bam po brgyad pa'o// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi gdams ngag de bzhin rjes su

101a3: sems dpa' rgya mtsho'i tshul de lta ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dkyil 'khor de la mngon par mos pa dang / sangs rgyas blta ba'i phyogs de la mngon par spro bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas rgya mtsho de la rjes su

101a7: par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par zhugs te/ bla na med pa'i ye shes rgya mtsho la 'jug par 'tshal na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams 'jig rten gyi rgyud las phyir ldog cing de bzhin gshegs

101b1: de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su 'grub par 'gyur ba dang / 'khor ba'i rgyud las ldog par 'gyur zhing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rgyud du 'jug par 'gyur ba dang / 'khor rgya mtsho'i rmad kyi 'a2
101b2: los las phyir ldog cing byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / smon lam gyi 'khor lor 'jug par 'gyur ba dang / bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rab tu 'jom zhing sangs rgyas kyi dkyil 'khor 'byung ba

101b4: gcod cing / mtho ris dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i sgo 'byed pa dang / khams gsum gyi grong khyer gyi sgo rnam par gcod cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi pho brang gi sgo rnam par 'byed pa dang / yo byad tham/

102a1: dngos par 'dzin pa thams cad dang bral ba dang / 'thon man med pa'i sa ltar sems mnyam pa dang / rang bzhin gyis snying rje che zhing byams par sems pa dang ldan pa dang / srid pa'i lam gyi rgyud thams
