102b1: rin po che'i 'byung gnas du mas rnam par brlan pa dang / chu'i phung po tshad med pa dang / kha dog rnam pa tha dad pa yang zhing bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / 'brang ba mtha' yas pa'i gnas su gyur pa dang sreg
102b2: chags mang po sna tshogs kyi rten du gyur pa dang / sprin chen po'i char yongs su 'dzin pa dang / gang zhing 'bri bar 'gyur ba med pa la rjes su sems pa byed cing gnas te/ rigs kyi bu de la kho bos 'di
102b3: snyam du bsams so/ / 'jig rten gyi khams 'di ni rgya mtsho chen po 'di bas kyang 'bags par rgya tshal/ 'di pas kyang yangs shing 'debs kyang tshad med pa la/ 'di bas kyang ngo mtshar dang ldan pa la la
102b4: zhig yod dam snyam ste/ de ltar kho bos tshul bzhin du bsam pa yid la byed pa la brtson par gnas pa ste/ rgya mtsho chen po'i 'od kyi gzhi las pad mo chen po nor bu rin po che in dra ni la thub pa med
102b5: cing rdo rje lta bur sra ba'i chub can/ nor bu rin po che bai dUr+ya ngan pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser ltar dri ma med pa'i lo ma rgya chen po can/ dus dang 'thun pa'i tsan dan gyi snying po'i brgyan
102b6: kyis brgyan pa/ rin po che a sma gang ba'i ze ba can/ rgya mtsho tsam du yangs shing rgya che ba lha ma yin gyi dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus sdong po'i lhun nas bzung ba/ rin po che sna tshogs brgya phrag stong
102b7: gi dra bas kun nas g.yog pa/ klu'i dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus spos kyi chu'i char mngon par phab pa/ nam mkha' lding gi dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus dar dang / rin po che'i lda ldi dngas
102b8: m o do mang po bcus bzung zhing rab tu spangs pa mi 'am ci'i dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus phan pa'i sems kyis kun nas blta ba lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus 'khor

103a1: nas mngon par 'dud pa/ srin po'i dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus 'dud cing mngon par mchod pa/ dri za'i dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus rol mo dang klu sna tshogs snyad pas bstod cing mchod pa/
103a2: lha'i dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus lha rdzas kyi me tog dang / spos dang phreng ba dang / bdug spos dang / byug pa dang phye ma dang / gos dang gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / lha'i dbang po sprin gyi char mngon par bab pa/
103a3: tshangs pa'i dbang po brgya stong phrag bcus spyi bos nas btugs te/ phyag 'tshal zhing mchod pa/ gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha bcu stong phrag bcus thal mo sbyar cing byug bya ba/ mi'i dbang po 'khor lo
103a4: skur pa brgya stong phrag bcus rin po che bdun gyis bsu zhing mngon par mchod pa rgya mtsho'i lha brgya stong phrag bcus mngon par mthon cing phyag bya ba/ nor bu rin po che skar ma'i ngang tshul brgya stong phrag bcu'i
103a5: 'od gzer gyi rgyan gyis rab tu snang bar byas pa/ nor bu rin po che bsod nams kyis dge ba brgya stong phrag bcus mkhos su phebs par 'brel bas rab tu brgyan pa/ nor bu rin po che rnam par snang ba brgya stong
103a6: phrag bcus snying po rab tu gsal bar byas pa/ nor bu rin po che dpal gyi snying po brgya stong phrag bcus dpal chen po shin tu 'bar bar byas pa/ nor bu rin po che'i mdzod snang ba brgya stong phrag bcus mtha' yas
103a7: par snang bar byas pa/ nor bu rin po che 'dzam bu'i chu klung brgya stong phrag bcus yongs su ston par gnas pas rab tu brgyan pa/ nor bu rin po che rdo rje seng ge brgya stong phrag bcus thub pa med par brgyan pa/ nor bu
103a8: rin po che nyi ma'i snying po brgya stong phrag bcus rgya cher gsal bar bsgrubs pa/ nor bu rin po che 'bar ba brgya stong phrag bcus kha dog sna tshogs su brgyan pa/ nor bu rin po che yid bzhin gyi rgyal po brgya stong

103b1: phrag bcus mi zad pa'i brgyan pa 'od 'bar bar byas pa byung ste/ padam chen po de ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba las byung ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pas yongs su
103b2: brtan pa'o/ / phyogs thams cad du mngon par dmigs su yod pa'o// sgyu ma'i rnam pa chos kyi byung ba'o// rjen pa'i dri ma med pa'i las byung ba'o// nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos kyi tshul gyis brgyan pa'o// rmi lam
103b3: lta bu'i chos nyid kyis yongs su byung ba'o/ / mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i tshul gyis rgyas btab pa'o// chags pa med pa'i chos kyi tshul dang ldan pa'o// phyogs kyi khams kun tu chos kyi dbyings rgyas par
103b4: 'gengs pa'o/ / sangs rgyas kyi yul brjod pa dang 'thun pa ste/ de'i rnam pa dang yon tan dang dbyibs dang / kha dog dang rgyan gyis mthar phyin par ni bskal pa brgya stong grangs med par yang khong du chud par mi
103b5: nus te/ pad mar da de bzhin gshegs pa'i saskyil drung du bzhugs pas khyab cang yongs su rgyas par mthong // de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku de yang 'di nas bzung ba nas med pa'i rtse mo bar gyis pa
103b6: rmas par mthong ngo / / de bzhin gshegs pa de'i gdan gyi rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang mthong / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab
103b7: pa dang / mtshan phun sun tshogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis
103b8: mi khyab pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i mdog rnam par dag pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / spyi gtsug bltar mi mthong ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / ljags yangs pasam gyis mi khyab pa yang

104a1: mthong ngo / / sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor bsam gyis mi khyab pa thos so// stobs tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / mi bsnyengs pa'i
104a2: brgyan rnam par dag pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa'i stobs mngon par bsgrubs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang rjes su shes so// sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yang dag
104a3: par bsgrubs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang rjes su dran no/ / mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang mthong ngo // chos kyi sprin gyi 'brug sgra mngon par bsgrags
104a4: pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang / yongs su bstan pa rnam par dmigs pa'i gnas dang / rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'ang thos so// g.yas phyogs kyi sku'i rnam pa tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang /
104a5: sems can gyi don dang / dgos pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongs su grub par 'gyur ba'ang mthong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa des kyang phyag g.yas brkyang zhing kho bo'i mgo la byugs nas chos kyi rnam
104a6: grangs kun nas mig ces bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa rab tu brjod pa chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi dang rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad rab tu snang ba/ chos thams
104a7: cad kyi dkyil 'khor la yang dag par gzhol zhing snang bar byed pa/ zhing gi dkyil 'khor dang / rnam par dag pas yongs su sdang ba/ zas kyi rgol ba'i dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par 'thor ba/ bdud kyi
104a8: bkrugs ma'i dkyil 'khor thams cad rab tu 'jom pa/ sems can gyi khams thams cad shin tu tshim par byed pa/ sems can thams cad kyi thibs po rab tu snang bar byed pa/ sems can thams

104b1: cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dbang po'i 'khor lo'i rgyud dang / mthu sdang ba'i byeng pa yang dag par bstan te/ kho bos yang kun nas mig gi chos kyi rnam
104b2: grangs de blangs so/ / bzung ngo spel to// bsams so// de ltar bzung ba de la'ang brin ni sdug tsha rgya mtsho chen po'i phung po tsam dang / smyu gu'i phung po ra rab ri'i rgyal po tsam zad par gyur kyang chos kyi rnam grangs de las
104b3: le'u re re dang sgo ngadadang chos kyi tshul re re dang chos kyi tshig rnam par phye ba ri re las kyang zad pa'am 'grib pa 'am/ 'byam pa'am/ mthar thug pa'am/ mtha' zad par 'gyur ba dmigs par mi rung ngo // rigs kyi bude
104b4: ltar bdag gi lo bcu gnyis tshang bar chos kyi rnam grangs kun nas mig ces bya ba 'di la nyi ma gcig ci yang thos pa 'dzin pa'i gzungs kyi 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pa zhig khong du chud do/ / zhi ba'i sgo'i
104b5: gzungs kyi 'od snang ba le'u grangs pa zhig la zhugs so/ / glong mtha' yas pa'i gzungs kyi 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pa zhig la yang dag par 'jug go// sa la rnam par dpyod cing rjes su rtogs par byed
104b6: pa'i gzungs kyi 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pas zhig rnam par bsgoms te rnam par dbye ba byas so/ / gzi brjid dang ldan pas gzungs kyi 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pa zhig yongs su blangs so// pad mo'i rgyan
104b7: gyi gzungs kyi 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pa zhig mngon par bsgrubs so/ / dbyangs kyi tshul gyi gzungs kyi 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pa zhig yang dag par bshad do// nam mkha'i snying po'i gzungs kyi
104b8: 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pa zhig rab tu phye'o/ / skar ma brtsegs pa'i gzungs 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pa zhig shin tu rgyas par byas so// rgya mtsho snying po'i gzungs kyi 'od snang bas le'u grangs med pa

105a1: zhig yongs su bkod do/ / kho bo'i drung du shar phyogs logs nas lha dang mi'i dbang po 'am/ klu dang klu'i dbang po 'am/ gnod sbyin dang / gnod sbyin gyi dbang po 'ab/ dri za dang dri za'i dbang po dang / lA ma
105a2: yin dang lha ma yin gyi dbang po 'am/ nam mkha' lding dang nam mkha' lding gi dbang po 'am/ mi 'am tsi dang ma 'am ci'i dbang po 'am/ lto 'phye chen po 'am lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po 'am/ mi dang mi'i dbang po
105a3: 'am/ tshangs pa'am tshangs pa'i dbang po 'am/ sems can gang su 'ongs kyang rung ste/ de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa sdang ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs kun nas mig
105a4: ces bya ba 'di nyid la rab tu bkod cing btsud de/ de dag kun kyang kun nas mig gi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di nyid la mos pas byas so// rtag tu btsud do// yongs su bsten to// yang dag par brjod do// yongs su
105a5: bsal bar byas so/ / rnam par bye'o rgyas par byas so// mngon par bstan to// rnam par dkrol lo// rab tu phye'o// shin tu snang bar byas so// de ltar shar phyogs la ji lta ba de bzhin du lho phyogs dang / nub phyogs
105a6: dang / byang phyogs dang / byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og dang bla'i phyogs nas sems can gang su
105a7: 'das kyang rung ste/ kun la yang snga ma bzhin no// rigs kyi bu de lta kho bos ni chos kyi rnam grangs cig gcig shes par zad na/ byang chub sems dpa'i sman lam yongs su dag pa dang ldan pas byed
105a8: chub sems dpa' spyod pa rgyam tshe thams cad la zhugs pa dang / skal pa thams cad du gnas pargyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir smon las rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa dang / stobs bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin

105b1: du rjes su 'brang bar bya ba'i phyir sems can rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa dang / stobs bcu'i ye shes chags pa med pa'i sdang ba yongs su bskyed pa'i phyir 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems rgya mtsho la zhum
105b2: pa dang / yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i dus la mi 'da' bar bya ba'i phyir sems can thams cad kyi dbang po rgya mtsho la zhugs pa dang / zhing thams cad rnam par dag par bya ba'i smon lam mngon par
105b3: bsgrubs so/ / zhing rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod cing rim gro byed pa'i stobs kyi sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa dang / ye shes rnam par dag
105b4: pas chos rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa dang / nan tan dang ldan pas yon tan rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa dang / brjod pa thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba mngon par bslabapa
105b5: pa'i phyir/ 'gro ba'i skad rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa rnams kyi spor ba shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skar/ dang srong rigs kyi bu 'di nas dpag tshad drug bcu 'das pa'i lho phyogs kyi gnas
105b6: 'di nyid na/ lang ka'i gnas rgya mtsho'i ngogs shes bya ba yod de/ de ni dge slong shin tu brtan pa zhes bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su spang bar
105b7: bya ba dris shig/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis/ dge slong rgya mtsho'i sprin gyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ dge slong rgya mtsho'i sprin la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su
105b8: skor ba byas nas yang dang yang bltas te/ dge slong rgya mtsho'i sprin gyi drung nas song ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi gdam ngag de dang / kun nas mig gi chos kyi rnam

106a1: grangs de yang rjes su dran par byed cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa de yang rjes su bsam pa dang / chos kyi tshig dang yi ge'i sprin de dag kyang yongs su bzung ba dang / chos kyi sku
106a2: mtsho'i tshul de dag la'ang 'jug par bya ba dang / chos kyi tshul de la'ang rnam par blta ba dang / chos kyi le'u dang glong gi tshul de dag la 'jug par bya ba dang / chos kyi nam mkha' nga la yang dag par gzhol bar
106a3: bya ba dang chos kyi dkyil 'khor de yang rjes su snang bar bya ba dang / chos rin po che'i gling du yang rjes su sems shing mthar gyis lang ka'i gnas rgya mtsho'i dogs shes bya ba gang na ba der phyin nas/ dge slong shin tu
106a4: brtan pa mthong bar dga' zhing shar phyogs su bltas so/ / de bzhin du lho phyogs dang nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi

106a7: me tog sil ma'i sprin gyis yog pa dang / lha rdzas kyi rol mo'i sprin gyi sgra dang / dar gyi padan grangs med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan par mthong ngo // klu'i dbang po rnams kyis nam mkha' de la a ga ru nag po'i

106b1: rol mo brdung ba dang / dkrol ba dang klung blang ba'i dbyangs thams cad sbyar cing blangs pa thos par gyur to// lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po rnams kyis nam mkha' de la gos shin tu phra zhing mdog bzang ba'i sprin bsam gyis ma

106b3: khyab pa byin gyis brlabs te/ yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan sdang ba dang ldan par snang bar byas so// mthong ngo // ma mkha' lding gi dbang po mang po yang mi'i gzugs dang dog dang byibs bu 'khor

107a4: par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpas sangs rgyas kyi chos bsgom par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sa sangs rgyas kyi chos rjes su 'brang bar bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems
107a5: dpa'as sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su brtul bar bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpas sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su bsgom par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpas sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam

107b1: dang / tshul gcig tu 'gyur ba'i slad du/ byang chub sems dpa' mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / ye shes rtogs par 'gyur ba'i slad du sangs rgyas kyi chos dang mi 'bral ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams

108a1: bos blangs te/ sangs su bcags/ rjes su thang shing rnam par bye ba dang / rnam par byad pa dang / rnam par bta/ bdag / snang bar bya ba dang / rab tu snang bar byab pas thugs pa ma pa' mtha' zhes bya/

108b1: do/ / sdang bar byung ngo // du ba 'thul bar byed do// me lce 'bar bar byed do// gcig tu gnas shing mang por skyur po mang por byas shing gcig tu bsgyur ro// snang ba dang mi snang ba'ang nyams su myong bar byed do// rtsig pa la/
108b2: 'ang thags thogs pa dang / rab la'ang thags thogs med par 'gro ste/ dper na nam mkha' la bya ba bzhin no// nam mkha' la skyil mo krung gis 'gro ste/ dper na mdab chags bya bzhin no// sa la yang bye'u

108b4: nos yang yongs su g.yo bar byed do// nyi ma dang zla ba 'di gnyis de ltar rdzu 'phrul che zhing de ltar mthu che la/ de ltar gzi brjid che ba yang lag pas kun nas yongs su nyug go/ tshangs pa'i 'jig rten gyi 'khor dag

108b7: ltar shar phyogs su 'gro'o/ / lho phyogs dang nub phyogs dang byang phyogs dang / byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og
108b8: dang bla'i phyogs su yang 'gro'o/ / sems kyi skad cig re re zhing yang shar phyogs logs su 'jig rten gyi khams gcig kyang 'da'o// 'jig rten gyi khams gnyis dang bcu yang 'da'o// 'jig rten gyi khams brgya dang

109a1: 'jig rten gyi khams snang dang/ 'ag tan gyi khams brgya phrag stong dang / 'jig rten gyi khams bya ba dang / 'jig tan gyi khams bya ba zag brgya dang / 'dag rten gyi khams bye ba phrag stong dang / 'jig nanaHkham
109a2: b+ha ba brgya zag dang / 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag thigasas phragastong dang / 'jig rten gyi khams cad med pa dang / 'ag rten gyi khams dpag tu med pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams grangs me pa dang / 'jig/ na/

109a8: khams kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de dang de dag na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ji snyed cig chos ston pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa de dag las de bzhin gshegs pa re re zhing yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha'

109b1: yas pa'i rdul shin tu pra ba snyed kyi lus sna tshogs dang / lus re re zhing yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha' yas pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi mchod pa'i sprin gyi char 'bebs shing / spyi dang 'gro'o// de dag tu phyin nas kyang me
109b2: tog thams cad dang / spos thams cad dang / phreng ba thams cad dang / bye ma thams cad dang / b+hag pa thams cad dang / na bza' thams cad dang / rgyal mtshan thams cad dang / lha'i ba dan thams cad dang / bla re thams cad
109b3: dang / dra ba thams cad dang / gzugs thams cad kyi mchod pa rgyun mi chad par byed do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis gang ji snyed du gsungs pa dang / bstan pa dang / brjod pa dang / yang dag par bshad pa
109b4: dang / yang dag par smos pa dang / yongs su brjod pa dang / man ngag du gsungs pa dang / shin tu bstan pa dang / rab tu brjod pa de dag thams cad kyang shes shing 'dzin to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi sa
109b5: rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa ji snyed pa de dag thams cad kyang rjes su dran no/ / shar phyogs su ji lta ba bzhin du lho phyogs dang / nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang / byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i
109b6: phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og dang steng gi phyogs su yang 'jig rten gyi khams kyang 'da'o// 'jig rten gyi khams gnyis dang bcu yang 'da'o//
109b7: 'jig rten gyi khams brgya nas 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang 'da'o// 'jig rten gyi khams de dag na sangs rgyas bcom ldan
109b8: 'das ji snyed cig bzhugs shing 'tsho ba zhes la/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsha dang de dag dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dag pa de dang de dag nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de

110a1: dang de ngaganams snyan pa dadag kun kyang mthang / / de bzhin gshegs pa de dag la'ang ma tog thams cad nas gzugs thams cad kyi bar gyis mchod pa byed // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dang ga
110a2: gis gang ji snyed du gsungs pa nas/ rab tu brjod pa'i ba de dag thams cad kyang yongs su shes shing 'dzin to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa gang ji snyed pa de dag
110a3: thams cad kyang rjes su dran no/ / sems can gang gis kho bo mthong bar gyur pa dang / gang dang gang 'grogs par gyur pa de dag kun kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu nges par 'gyur ro//
110a4: sems can phra mo 'am/ rags pa 'am/ ngan pa 'am/ bzang ba'am/ bde ba 'am mi bde ba gang ji snyed cig kho bos mthong bar gyur pa de dag kun la yang yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'dul ba'i dus la
110a5: mi 'da' bar bya ba'i phyir/ khong tu de dag gi lus kyi tshad dang mnyam par lus byin gyis rlob bo// sems can ji snyed cig kho bo'i drung du 'ong ba de dag thams cad kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam
110a6: par thar pa kun du 'gro ba 'di dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa rnam par gnon pa don yod pa la rab tu gzhog go// rigs kyi bu kho bos ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa thogs pa med pa'i
110a7: sngo kun tu 'gro ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod pa dang / rim thor btu sbyor gA/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'thun pa 'di shes par zad na// kho bos byang chub sems dpa'i
110a8: rjechen po dang tshul can/ theg pa chen po'i ngang tshul can/ byang chub sems dpa'i lam dang mi 'bral ba'i ngang tshul can/ thogs pa med pa'i ngang tshul can/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa'i snying po chu mi gzin

110b1: pa'i dang tshul can/ byang chub kyis mas yang sum gtang ba'i dang rdul can/ sangs rgyas kyangs la lhag par dmigs pa dang tshul can/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid meng la bya ba dang ma 'bral ba nga rdul na/
110b2: nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i ngang tshul can/ 'jig rten thams cad la mi gnas pa'i ngang tshul can/ chud mi brtson pa'i ngang tshul can/ ma nyams pa'i ngang tshul can/ mgod pa'i ngang tshul can/ glags med pa'i
110b3: ngang tshul can/ ma 'dres pa'i dang tshul can rnyog pa med pa'i nga tshul can/ 'grod pa med pa'i dang tshul can/ rnam par dag pa'i dang tshul can/ byang chub sems dpa'i rdul bral ba dag gi spyang pa gas
110b4: 'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan/ song rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na/ dbyi'i la'i grong rdal rdo rje re kro dbyer cing bya ba yod de/ de na dra byi la'i sprin ces bya ba 'dug gis de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang
110b5: chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du dris shig/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis dge slong rab tu brtan pa'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag
110b6: 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te/ yang dag yang bltas nas dge slong shin tu brtan pa'i drung nas song ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs chos kyi dad pa'i shugs dang / byin
110b7: gyis gnon pa/ sangs rgyas yid la bya ba'i 'du shes dang ldan pa/ dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung mi 'chad pa la rab tu brtson pa/ dus gsum snang bas sems snang bar gyur pa/ smon lam chen po yid la byed
110b8: pa dang ldan pa sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su bskyab pa'i thabs la zhugs pa/ 'dus byas kyi dga' ba thams cad la mi gnas pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin nges

111a1: bar rtogs par bya ba la brtson pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yongs su snang ba'i smon lam las ma g.yog/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na gnas pa med par gnas/
111a2: pa chos kyi sang ba de rjes su dran par bya ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen rjes su dran par byi ba dang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i rigs yongs su brjod pa byed cing / mthar gyis dbyila'i grong rdal rdo rje grong
111a3: tubyin nas/ drabyi la'i sprin yongs su tshol tshul ba las/ grong khyer gyi khyams shig na chos snyan pa'i don tu seng ge'i khrel 'dug cing / srog chags stong bcu rtsa ba zhig la chos kyi rnam grangs yi ge'i 'khong
111a4: lo'i rgyud kyi rgyan ces bya ba yongs su ston cing 'dug pa mthong ngo / / de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis dbyi la'i sprin gyi rkang pa gnyis la skye bos phyag 'tshal te/ dbyi la'i sprin la lan brgya stong dupar
111a5: g.yas phyogs su skor ba byas nas mdun du 'dug ste thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so/ / 'phags pa bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpas
111a6: byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i byang chub kyi sems srid pa'i lam rgyud thams cad du cha ba mi 'tshal ba dang / ji ltar yongs su
111a7: skyob ma mchis shing / bsam pa gtan par 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar thub pa ma mchis shing lhag pa'i bsam pa yongs su skyo ba ma mchis shing zhing blon po'i stobs yang dag pa skye bar 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar sgo kun nad
111a8: rnam par dag cing gzungs kyi stobs gnon par 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar ma rig pa'i rab rib dang / sgrib pa rnam par 'thor zhing / shes rab kyi 'od chos thams cad la rab rib ma mchis pa'i snang ba skye bar 'gyur ba dang /

111b1: jiltar don dang chos dngangs pa'i tshig dang slobs pa la mkhas pa la dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs shig/ so so yang dag par rig pa'i stobs gnon par 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar sangs rgyas thams cad
111b2: 'khor lo tha mi dad pa yang dag par 'dzin cing dran pa'i stobs yongs su gnon par 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar chos thams cad kyi phyogs rig pa'i snang ba rjes su rtogs shing / rig par stobs rnam par dag par 'gyur ba dang
111b3: ji ltar byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi stobs chos thams cad kyi don rnam par gdon mi za bar rab tu dbye ba la brtson pas 'grub par 'gyur ba ma 'tshal to/ / de nas dbyi la'i sprin gyis byang chub sems dpa'
111b4: la rim gro bya ba'i phyir/ seng ge'i khri de la langs te thabs nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la lus thams cad kyis phyag byas nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la gser gyi me tog gi phung pos mngon par gtor
111b5: nor bu rin po che rin tang med pa mang po dang / tsan dan gyi phye ma dam pas mngon par gtor to// gos tshon sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pas kha dog bsgyur ba brgya stong phrag du mas kyang mngon par bkab po// spos
111b6: kyi me tog kha dog rnam pa tha dad cing yid du 'ong ba blta na sdug pa mang pos kyang mngon par gtor nas mchod pa'i rnam pa sna tshogs gzhan dag gis kyang / mchod pa dang rim gro dang / bkur bsti dang sti stang cher
111b7: byas te/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor brnangs la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu khyod kyis de ltar blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du sems bskyed pa legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu gang gis bla na
111b8: med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa de ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gdung mi gcad pa'i phyir zhugs pa yin/ 'dod chags dang bral ba'i rigs yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par rig

112a1: par bya ba la brtson pa yin/ zhing gi rgyud thams cad yongs su dag par bya ba la zhugs pa yin/ sems can gyi rigs thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba la stagan du gnas pa yin/ chos
112a2: rigs thams cad yang dag pa de lta ba bzhin brtag pa la brtson pa yin/ las kyi rigs thams cad dang mi 'gal bar gnas pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rigs thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa
112a3: ba la rab tu brtson pa yin/ smon lam thams cad rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir yang dag par zhugs pa yin/ dus gsum gyi rgyud thams cad ye shes kyis khong du chud par bya ba la zhugs pa yin/ mos pa'i rigs
112a4: shin tu brtan par bya ba'i phyir brtson pa yin te/ do na de bzhin gshegs pa mang po thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa yin/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis yang dag par dgongs pa yin/ byang chub sems
112a5: dpa' thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid du gyur pa yin/ 'phags pa thams cad kyis rjes su dgyes par bya ba yin/ tshangs pa'i dbang po thams cad kyis mngon par dga' bar byas pa yin/ lha'i dbang pa thams ca
112a6: kyis yang dag par mchod pa yin/ gnod sbyin gyi dbang po thams cad kyis yongs su bsrung ba yin/ srin po'i dbang po thams cad kyis rim gro byas pa yin/ klu'i dbang po thams cad kyis bas pa yin/ mi
112a7: 'am ci'i dbang po thams cad kyis mngon par bsod pa yin/ 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad kyis yang dag par bsngags pa yin/ des rnamams can gyi khams thams cad kyang ngan song gi la margyud
112a8: gsum po yongs su gcad pa dang ma khom pa dang / ngan 'gro'i lam thams cad bzlog pa dang / dbul ba'i lam thams cad las yang dag par bzla ba dang / lha dang mi'i phun sum tshogs pa thob par bye ba

112b1: dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya chen po nyan pa dang / 'bral bar mi 'gyur ba dang / byang chub kyi sems kyi yan lag yongs su dag par bya ba dang / byang chub kyis
112b2: 'byung ba'i rgyud yongs su bslab pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lam snang bar thob par byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa la gnas par bya bas dpagra
112b3: byin par byas pa yin/ rigs kyi bu de la bdag 'di snyam du sems// byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni dka' ba byed pa ste/ 'byung bar dka' zhing mthong bar dka' ba'o// byang chub sems dpa'
112b4: rnams ni sems can la bag dro bar byed pas pa dang ma lta bu'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi rgyan du gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sdug bsngal gyis mnar/
112b5: ba rnams la skyabs su gyur pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni 'gro ba thams cad yongs su bsrung ba'i phyir gnas su gyur pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni 'jigs pa sna tshogs kyis
112b6: bcas pa rnams la dpung gnyen du gyur pa'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni 'gro ba thams cad ngan song gsum du lhung ba las yongs su rton pa'i phyir rlung gi dkyil 'khor lta bu'o// byang chub
112b7: sems dpa' rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par 'phel bar byed pas sa lta bu'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni bsod nams rin po che'i mdzod mi zad pa'i gter dang ldan
112b8: pas rgya mtsho lta bu'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni ye shes kyi 'od kyis snang bar byed pa'i phyir nyi ma lta bu'o// byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa bas shin tu mtho bas ri rab lta bu'o// byang chub

113a1: sems dpa' rnams ni snying po byang chub tu ye shes kyi zla ba 'char bar 'gyur ba'i phyir zla ba lta bu'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni bdud kyi sde thams cad rab tu 'jom pas dpa' bor gyur pa'o// byang chub
113a2: sems dpa' rnams ni rang byung gi chos kyi grong khyer du phyin par byed pas rtul phong pa lta bu'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi bdag la byams pa'i rlan yongs su skems pas me lta
113a3: bu'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni chos kyi sprin rgya chen po'i char mngon par 'bebs pas sprin lta bu'o// byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sems can gyi dbang po dang po la stsogs pa'i myu gu rnam par 'phru
113a4: bar byed pas char pa lta bu'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni chos kyi rgya mtsho'i 'gram yongs su ston pas mnyam pa lta bu'o// byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sems can thams cad 'khor ba'i rgya
113a5: mtsho las yang dag par sgrol ba'i phyir zam pa lta bu'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sems can thams cad kyis mngon par bgrod par bya ba'i phyir mu stegs lta bu'o// de ltar dbyil sprin gyis//
113a6: tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyi mdun du 'dug ste/ tshig gi rgyud de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rnams la yongs su bsngags pa byas nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la legs so zhes bya ba bsngags
113a7: so/ / da ltar de nas byang chub sems dpa' yang dag par dga' bar bya ba'i phyir/ tshig brjod pa'i tshe/ kha'i sgo nas 'od 'phro ba'i phung po rnam pa 'di lta bu byung ste/ 'od 'phro ba'i phung po des stong gsum gyi
113a8: 'jig rten gyi khams rgyas par gang bar gyur nas/ lha dang lha rdzu 'phrul chen po'am/ klu dang klu rdzu 'phrul la chen po 'am/ gnod sbyin dang gnod sbyin rdzu 'phrul chen po 'am/ dri za dang dri za'i rdzu 'phrul chen

113b1: po'am/ lha ma yin dang lha ma yin rdzu 'phrul chen po 'am/ nam mkha' lding dang nam mkha' lding rdzu 'phrul chen po 'am/ mi 'am ci dang mi'am ci'i rdzu 'phrul chen po 'am/ lto 'phye chen po dang lto 'phye chen po
113b2: 'phrul chen po 'am/ mi dang mi rdzu 'phrul chen po 'am/ tshangs pa dang tshangs pa'i rdzu 'phrul chen po 'am/ sems can gang sus mthong yang rung ste snang ba des yongs su snang bar byas pa de dag drabye'i la sprin gyi
113b3: drung du 'ongs so/ / de nas de ltar dbyi la sprin kyis bsams pa byin gyis brlabs shing thal mo sbyar te/ gnas pa lus dang sems sim par gyur pa/ dga' ba rgya chen po skyes pa sri zhu chen po la gnas pa/
113b4: nga rgyal gyi rgyal mtshan bcom pa/ g.yo rgyu dang bral ba/ dbang po rnam par dad par gyur pa de dag la dri byi la sprin gyis/ chos kyi rnam grangs yi ge'i 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi rgyan ces bya ba de nyid rgya cher yang dag
113b5: par bstan te/ khong du chud pa dang / rtogs pa dang / shes pa dang rig par byas so// de thos nas kyang de dag thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir me ldog par gyur to// de
113b6: nas de'i phyir chos kyi stan kha 'dug nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu kho bos ni dbyangs dang ldan pa'i gzungs thob pa ste/ de'i mthas kho bos stong gsum
113b7: gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di lha rnams kyi lha'i skad kyang shes so/ / de bzhin du klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang me 'am nI dang / lto 'phye chen po dang
113b8: mi dang mi ma yin pa dang / tshangs pa rnams kyi tshangs pa'i skad sna tshogs kyang shes so// lha rnams kyi lha'i snying sna tshogs kyang shes so// de bzhin du klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang nam

114a1: mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa dang / tshangs pa rnams kyi tshangs pa'i skad sna tshogs kyang shes so// lha rnams kyi lha'i skad cig pa yang shes so// de bzhin du
114a2: klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa dang / tshangs pa rnams kyi tshangs pa'i skad cig pa yang shes so// lha rnams kyi
114a3: lha'i skad tha dad pa yang shes so/ / de bzhin du glu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dag mi dang mi ma yin pa dang / tshangs pa rnams kyi tshangs
114a4: pa'i skad thams cad kyang shes so/ / byol song gi skye gnas su skyes pa'i sems can rnams kyi brda' dang skad dang ming thams cad kyang shes so// sems can dmal ba'i sems can rnams kyi skad dang
114a5: ming rnams kyang shes so/ / gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sems can rnams kyi skad dang ming rnams kyang shes so// 'phags pa'i skad dang ming rnams kyang shes so// 'phags pa'i ma yin pa'i skad dang ming rnams kyang
114a6: shes so/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshig dang brda' dang nges pa'i ngag sems can gyi bsam pa bzhin du 'byung ba yang shes so// sems can gyi skad re re la yang dus gsum du gshegs pa'i de bzhin
114a7: gshegs pa rnams kyi dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / gsung rgya mtsho sems can thams cad kyi ming dang gtam gyi sgra dang / tshig du ldan pa yang rtogs shing khong du chud // ji ltar stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig
114a8: rten gyi khams 'di'i sems can rnams kyi brda' dang / des pa'i tshig dang skad dang ming rgya mtsho la 'jug cing shes pa de bzhin du shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag khrig brga stong tshad med// gan pa med pa

114b1: bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ mtshungs pa med pa/ kun tu mtha' yas pa mu med pa/ sa mtshams med pa gzhal du med pa/ brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dang / de bzhin du lho phyogs dang nub phyogs dang /
114b2: byang phyogs dang / byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og dang steng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba
114b3: khrag khrig brgya stong tshad med pa dang brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar gyi sems can rnams kyi brda' dang / nges pa'i tshig dang skad dang ming rgya mtsho thams cad la 'jug cing shes te/ 'di ltar lha rnams
114b4: kyi lha'i skad kyang shes so/ / tshangs pa rnams kyi tshangs pa'i skad kyi bar du'ang shes so// rigs kyi bu kho bos ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs snang ba dbyangs dang ldan pa'i 'di shes par zad na
114b5: kho bos byang chub sems dpa' 'gro ba sna tshogs kyi brda'i rnam pa rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang / 'gro ba sna tshogs kyi skad dang / ming rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang / 'tho ba sna tshogs kyi ming shin tu bstan
114b6: pa rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang 'gro ba sna tshogs kyis brjod pa rab tu bkod pa dang / rnam par spyod pa rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang / tshig thams cad kyi mtshams sbyor ba thams cad rgya mtsho la zhugs
114b7: pa de dag dang / tshig lhur blangs te bstan pa rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang / dus gsum gyi dmigs pa thams cad dmigs pa gcig tu rnam par spyod pa rgya mtsho gang chen mtshal zhugs pa de dag dang / tshig gi
114b8: brtsegs te bstan pa rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang / tshig gnyis nas brtsegs te bstan pa rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang / tshig rab tu bye ste bstan pa rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang chos thams cad

115a1: rab tu dbye bas 'dul ba'i tshul bstan pa rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi skad rgya mtsho la zhugs pa de dag dang / dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa'i rgyan thams cad la zhugs
115a2: pa de dag dang / yi ge'i 'khor lo'i mthar phyin par bya bas rab tu dbye ba la byung ba de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan/ sod rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na yul nags tshal
115a3: na gnas pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de na tshong dpon gtang brjod ces bya ba 'dug gis de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i phyogs la brtson par bya ba dang / ji ltar 'brang bar bya ba dang /
115a4: ji ltar sems par nges par bzhag par bya ba dris shig/ de nas tshod dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis/ dri byi la sprin gyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ chos kyi rim gro byas nas dad pa'i mtshan nyid rtsa ba
115a5: tshugs pa la rab tu rtogs pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen las 'os pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la yang dag par lta zhing gdong mchims gang ba ngus te/ dri byi la sprin la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas
115a6: phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ yang dang yang bltas te/ phyag 'tshal zhing dra byi la sprin gyi drung nas song ngo // sangs rgyas rmad gcad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo'//
115a7: bam po dgu pa// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs snang ba dbyangs dang ldan pa'i rgyan de nyid la rjes su bsam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i skad kyi tshul
115a8: rgya mtsho de nyid la 'jug par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshul phra mo la 'jug pa de nyid rjes su dran par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems rnam par byang bas/ rnam par dag pa de nyid kyi

115b1: rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i bag chags bsdu zhing bsgrub pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su smin par bya ba'i sgo de nyid rnam par byang ba dang / byang
115b2: chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems can bsdu ba'i ye shes de nyid shin tu byed par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa'i stobs rnam par bya ba de nyid brtan par bya ba dang / byang chub
115b3: sems dpa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa'i stobs de nyid nye bar brtan par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i mos pa'i rgyud de nyid yongs su sbyang bar bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sems de nyid gdon mi za bar dge bar
115b4: bsam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yid dam chen po de nyid mthar phyin par byed cing / tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs yi dam brtan zhing smon lam gyi sems kyis yongs su skyo ba med pa'i rgyud kyi rgyan dang ldan pa/
115b5: phyir mi ldog pas rnam par gnon pa'i brtson 'grus can/ yid kyis brtul ba las mi bzlogs pa/ dad pa mi 'phrogs pa'i stobs dang ldan pa/ rdo rje mthu bo ches mi phyed pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i bshes
115b6: gnyen thams cad kyi gdam ngag 'thun par len pa/ shes rab kham bab pa'i yul dang ldan pa/ sgo kun nas rnam par dag pa la mngon du gyur pa/ ye shes rnam par dag pa'i spyod yul thogs pa kun tu lta ba'i
115b7: shes kyi tshul snang ba dang ldan pa/ sa'i gzugs kun nas snang ba rab tu thob pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi'i bye brag la mngon sum du gyur pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ gzhi kun la brten pa'i rgyan rnam par
115b8: dag pa'i rang bzhin rnam par dmigs pa gnas med pa dang / bdag gi med pa dang / gnyis su med pa'i spyod yul la rab tu brtson pa/ 'du shes thams cad las 'da' bar byed pa'i ye shes

116a1: kyi sgo rnas par dag pa/ chos kyi phyogs dang gzhi tha dad pa'i phyogs la so sor rtogs pa med pa 'jig rten gyi gzhi dang phyogs kyi bye thag las phyir mi ldog pa/ chos kyi gzhu dang phyogs kyi bye brag las
116a2: phyir mi ldog pa/ sangs rgyas kyi phyogs dang ga'i tha dad pa mthong ba dang / rnam par rig par bya ba la gzhol ba dus kyi phyogs dang gzhi'i bye brag khong du chud pa'i ye shes can/ chos kyi 'khor lo yid du 'ong bas yang
116a3: dag par bsgrubs pa'i blo dang ldan pa/ ye shes kun nas snang ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam par snang bas/ sems gsal bar byas pa/ yod kyi yul lus kun dang / ldan pa'i sa la zhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
116a4: ye shes sdang bas/ rgyud shin tu snang bar byas pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du dad pa'i dpa' rlabs kyi shugs kyis rab tu rlob pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos la mos pa'i shugs dang 'bral bar med pa/ de bzhin gshes
116a5: pa'i'abyin gyi rlabs kyis byin du rlabs pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad rang gi sems kyi rgyud khong du chud pa'i 'od kyis snang bar gyur pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi dra ba thams cad rang gi lus kyis rgyas par dkang
116a6: ba'i smon lam dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad rang gi lus su yang dag par bsdu ba dang / mngon par bsgrub pa la brtson pa/ dmathar kyis sor song ste/ lo bcu gnyis kyis yul nags tshal na gnas par phyin
116a7: nas/ de nas tshong dpon btang brjod de btsal btsal te mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang lus thams cad kyis phab te/ phyag 'tshal nas mdun du 'dug ste/ thal mo sbyar nang 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa
116a8: bdag de ring dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang mjal bar gyur pa ni bdag gis 'thob par bgyi ba legs par thob po/ / de ci'i slad du zhe na/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams ni mthong bar dka'o// 'byung bar dka' ba'o/

116b1: mjal bar dka' ba'o// bgrod par dka' ba'o// bsnyen bkur bgyi bar dka' ba'o// mnyes par bgyi bar dka' ba'o// 'grogs par dka' ba'o// rim 'gro bkyi bar dka' ba'o// dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams ni
116b2: rjes su 'brang bar dka' ba lags na/ de lta bu'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang 'grogs pa de ring bdag gis thob par gyur to// 'phags pa bdag gis 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas thams cad bsnyen bkar ba dang / sangs
116b3: rgyas thams cad la rim gro bgyi ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi zhal blta ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad rnam par dmigs par bgyi ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam pa nyid thob par bgyi ba dang / sangs rgya
116b4: thams cad kyi smon lam khong du chud par bgyi ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi smon lam yongs su rdzogs par bgyi ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang dag par bsgrub pa'i ye shes snang bar bgyi ba dang / sa

116b6: gsum du rtogs par bgyi ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi stobs dang mi bsnyengs pa yongs su dag par bgyi ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos bstan pa mnyan pas mi ngoms par bgyi ba dang / sangs
116b7: rgyas thams cad kyi chos bstan pa mnyan cing blang bar bgyi ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos bstan par yang dag par gzung bar bgyi ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos bstan pa rnam par dbye ba ba
116b8: ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos bstan pa yongs su gzung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang tshul gcig tu 'gyur bar bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang skal pa

117a1: mnyam par bgyi pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi spyod pa yongs su dag par bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bgyi pa dang / byang chub sems
117a2: dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi mdzod rab tu thob par bgyi ba dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi chos kyi
117a3: gter dang mdzod mi zad pa'i ye shes snang ba thob par bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi gter dang mdzod khong du chud par bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi mdzod tshad
117a4: med pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi snying rje chen po'i gter dang mdzod sems can 'dul ba'i mthar phyin par bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi rnam par
117a5: 'phrul pa'i gter dang / mdzod rnam par dmigs par bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dbang gyi gter dang / mdzod rang gi sems kyi dbang du bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi rnam
117a6: pa dag pa'i gter dang / mdzod rnam pa thams cad du brgyan par bgyi ba'i slad du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tusems bskyed nas/ 'phags pa de lta bu'i sems kyis bdag 'dir mchisas
117a7: bsam pa de lta bu'i dang yid la smon pa de lta bu dang / mngon par dga' ba de lta bu dang / sems dpa' de lta bu dang / gdon mi 'tshal bar bsgrub par bsams pa de lta bu dang / spyod pa mngon du bgyi pa de lta bu dang /
117a8: tshul khong du chud par bgyi ba la bos pa de lta bu dang / rnam par dag pa la gzhol ba de lta bu dang / rnam par dpyad pa'i bsam pa de lta bu dang / rab tu gzhol ba'i sems de lta bu dang / dge ba'i sbyor ba de lta bu dang

117b1: mngon du 'gyur ba'i dbang po de lta bus bdag 'dir mchis te/ 'phags pa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams la gdam dag dang / rjes su ston pa mdzad cing tshul ni nye bar ston pa mdzad/ rtogs par bgyi ba ni snang
117b2: bar mdzad/ lam ni bstan pa mdzad/ mu stegs la ni 'jom par mdzad/ chos kyi sgron rnam par 'byed par mdzad/ the tsom ni yongs su gcod par mdzad/ nem nur ni sel bar mdzad/ yid gnyis kyi zug
117b3: rdzu ni 'byin par mdzad/ dogs pa'i dri ma 'ini sbyor bar mdzad/ sems kyi thibs po ni snang bar mdzad/ sems kyi dri ma ni yongs su sel bar mdzad/ sems kyi rgyud ni rab tu dang bar mdzad/ sems kyi
117b4: g.yo sgyu ni yongs su sel bar mdzad/ sems kyi gdung ba ni yongs su sim par mdzad/ 'khor ba las ni sems rnam par bzlog par mdzad/ mi dge ba'i las ni phyir bzlog pa mdzad/ sems
117b5: can dmyal ba las ni ldog par mdzad/ gnas dang ni bral bar mdzad/ mngon par zhen pa las ni gyen du skyong ba mdzad/ chags pa thams cad las ni yongs su 'grol ba mdzad/ thams cad mkhyen pa
117b6: nyid du ni bsgrub pa mdzad/ chos kyi grong rdal du 'jug par bgyi ba'i slad du ni mngon du gyur par mdzad/ snying rje chen po la ni rab tu bsgrub pa mdzad/ byams pa chen po la ni rab tu gzhog pa mdzad/
117b7: byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la ni rab tu sbyor bar mdzad/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo bsgom pa la ni mdzud pa mdzad/ rtogs par 'gyur ba'i sku la ni gnas par mdzad/ rang bzhin nges par rtogs pa la ni
117b8: gzhog par mdzad/ stobs dang ldan pas ni khyab par mdzad/ 'gro ba thams cad mnyam pa nyid du ni sems rnam par dbye ba mdzad do zhes thos na// 'phags pa ji ltar byang chub sems dpas

118a1: byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la btsun par ba rtsi/ ji ltar sbyang bar bgyi/ ji ltar brtson par bgyis// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor rnam par dag par 'gyur ba bdag la bsta/
118a2: dra gsol// de nas tshong dpon btang brjod kyis de'i tshe/ byang chub sems dpa'i ting nga 'dzin gyi sgo sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yang dag por 'du ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi sgo klong mtha' yas pa sngon du'
118a3: bal/ sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i shugs dang // de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas yang dag par bsams shing ye shes snang ba nye bar bsgrubs pas snyoms
118a4: par zhugs so/ / tshong dpon btang brjod de ltar snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu gzugs kyi lus yongs su dag pa 'di lta bur gnas par gyur te/ lus yongs su dag pa de'i mthus phyogs bcu'i sangs
118a5: rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa dang bcas/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang bcas/ 'od rnam par dag pa dang bcas/ sngon
118a6: gyi spyod pa la zhugs pa dang bcas/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas/ smon lam gyi tshogs dang bcas/ spyod pa dang 'byung ba'i rgyun rnam par dag pa dang bcas/ mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang
118a7: rgya ba yongs su ston pa dang bcas/ chos kyi 'khor lo shin tu ston pa dang bcas/ sems can yongs su smin par mdzad pa dang bcas/ chos kyi ma'i mthar thug pa dang bcas par kun kyang lus kyi khongs su chud
118a8: cing 'dus par snang ste/ de dag phan tshun ma 'dres pa dang / phan tshun mchod pa dang / phan tshun shin tu rnam par phye ba dang / phan tshun shin tu rnam par gnas pa dang / tshul sna tshogs su zhugs pa dang / yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin

118b1: du rnam par dmigs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing rgyan sna tshogs can mnga' ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs kyi rgyan dang ldan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs yongs su ston
118b2: par snang ngo / / theg pa sna tshogs rnam par dgod pa mdzad pa dang / smon lam gyi sgo sna tshogs yongs su rjod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams la lan ni dga' ldan gyi pho brang du skyes shing // sangs rgyas kyi phrin las thams cad mdzad
118b3: par snang ngo / / la lan ni dga' ldan gyi pho zad nas 'phro ba dang / la lan ni yum gyi sku na bzhugs shing rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs yongs su ston pa dang / la lan ni skye ba dang / la lan ni byis pa'i rtsed mo ston pa mdzad pa dang
118b4: lalan ni btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na bzhugs pa dang / la lan ni mngon par 'byung ba dang / la lan ni snying po byang chub tu gshegs te/ rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan chen pos bdud kyi sde pham par mdzad pa dang / la la na ni lha dang
118b5: kA dang gnod sbyin dang dri zas yongs su bskor cing tshangs pa'i dbang pos chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba gdab pa dang / la lan ni chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba mdzad pa dang / la la na ni sems can thams cad kyi gnas
118b6: na bzhugs pa dang / la lan ni yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar snang ngo // 'jig rten gyi khams la lan ni de bzhin gshegs pa mya ngan las 'das pa rnams kyi ring bsrel rnam par dgod par snang ngo // sangs rgyas kyi zhing la
118b7: lan ni lha dang mi rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten la rgyan gyis grub pa byed par snang ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis sems can gyi ris rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi 'jig rten rnam pa tha dad
118b8: pa dang / sems can gyi lam rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi skye gnas rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi tshogs rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rgyud rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi bsam

119a1: ba'i rgyud rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can cil mos pa'i rgyud rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi dbang po'i nad rnam pa tha dad pa dang / dus kyi chud rnapa dang padang / sems can gyi las kyi bye brag rnam pa
119a2: bdad pa dang / sems can gyi las mi 'thun pa rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi 'jig rten rnam par dbye ba rnam pa tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi tshul lam dang spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa la spyod pa dang / sems can rgya mtsho bas
119a3: padang / stor ba'i rnam pa thad pa dang / dbang po mi mthun pa sna tshogs rngum pa tha dad pa dang / nyon mongs pa dang / bag chags sna tshogs bag la nyal bar gyur ba'i sems can 'dum thus pa na pas la sangs rgyas kyirnam
119a4: par 'phrul pa rnams sna tshogs yongs su bstan pa dang / yul sna tshogs kyi nges pa'i tshi ga dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag dang gsung rnam pa sna tshogs su bsgrags pa dang / mdo sde'i sna tshogs kyi tshul rab tu brjod pa dang /
119a5: gzung kyi sgo rnam pa tha dad pa'i rgyud dang so so yang dag par rig pa'i tshul gyi gzhung sna tshogs dang / 'phags pa'i bden pa'i ming rgya mtsho'i rgyud rnam pa sna tshogs dang / sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog dang seng ge'i nga ro rab tu
119a6: bsgrag pa dang / sems can gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba sna tshogs bstan pa'i cho 'phrul yongs su bstan pa dang / dran pa'i sgo sna tshogs can shin tu bstan pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' lung bstan
119a7: pa'i seng ge'i nga ro sna tshogs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo'imathu byung ba rnam pa sna tshogs kyis 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mtha' dang thas med pa mtha' yas par rnam pa tha dad pa ban tshun mtshad
119a8: dang/ rnam par dag pa'i dkyil 'khor sna tshogs yangs pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor shin tu phra bar 'dus pa dang / dpag tshad gcig gi tshad tsam dang / dpag tshad bcu'i tshad tsam dang / dpag tshad brgya'i ched tsam nas/

119b1: 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi tshad tsam du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung dbyangs
119b2: kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro bas chos ji snyed du bstan pa de dag thams cad kyang / tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis thos so blangs so// yang dag par bzung ngo bsams so// sangs rgyas kyi rnam
119b3: par 'phrul pa de dag kyang mthong ngo / / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba de dag kyang mthong ngo // de nas tshong dpon btang brjod dran zhing shes bzhin du ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas/ tshong
119b4: dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so/ / rigs kyi bu kho bo ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par thar pa thogs pa med pa'i rgyan ces bya ba yongs su blangs shing 'dzin pa ste/ rigs kyi bu de ltar kho bo ni de
119b5: bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par thar pa thogs pa med pa'i rgyan de la rtog cing dpyod pa'i tshe/ shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'dzam bu chu klung gi mdog dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
119b6: dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas skar ma'i dbang phyug rgyal po zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang ba'i snying po la stsogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thabs cig tu bzhugs
119b7: pa'ang mig lam du snang ngo / / lho phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams stobs thams cad kyi shugs dang ldan pa na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas spos kun tu rnam par
119b8: yangs pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' bsam pa'i rgyal po la stsogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang thabs cig tu bzhugs pa'ang mig lam du snang ngo // nub

120a1: lcags kyi ga rten gyi khams smras thams cad kya' dang ldan pan/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra btsam pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ri rab mang ma'i rgyal ba zhes b+ha la/ byung
120a2: sa dpa' chags pa med pa'i sems la lhags pa zang chubasams dpalakha gyi kyil 'altar thams ca dang thags pa ng+gA gas pa yang bgal sa du swA gA/ shA
120a3: k hams drang skrag rgyal mtshan na de bzhin ga shegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangasaHsa rdo rje rab tu 'dul bzhis babyang chubasems da dzi gas pas pa na
120a4: la sogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa yang mig laman snang ngo // byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams kyi 'jig rten gyi kha mas rin po che thams cad
120a5: rab tu 'bar ba na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mi dmigs pa'i spyan rnam par dmigs pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' dmigs pa med par shin tu sprul
120a6: pa la stsogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa yang mig lam du snang ngo // shar lho'i phyogs mtshams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams spos kyi 'od
120a7: gzer rab tu snang ba na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas spos kyi mar me zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi tha dad pa'i dpal gyi rgyal po la stsogs
120a8: pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa'ang mig lam du snang ngo // lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams nyi ma'i gzer ltar snang ba na/ de

120b1: b zhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas sgo kun nas ye shes rnam par snang ba'i dbyangs shes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' me tog gi 'od kun nas 'phro bar gtsug pud rab tu
120b2: 'byung ba la sngags pa/ byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa'ang mig lam du snang ngo // nub byang gi phyogs mtshams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams spos kyi rgyan
120b3: yid du 'ong ba'i dge ba'i snying po na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas yon tan rgya mtsho tshad med pa'i 'od ces bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyi 'od gzer thogs pa
120b4: med pa'i gzi brjid rgyal po blo gros la stsogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang / thabs gcig tu zhugs pa'ang mig lam du snang ngo // 'og gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi
120b5: khams ngan po che'i sang go'i snang zhing 'bar ba na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'od gzer chos kyi dbyings su spang ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' chos
120b6: kyi dbyings 'od 'phro zhing rnam par snang bar byung ba'i blo gros la stsogs pa byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa'ang mig lam du sdang ngo / / steng gi
120b7: phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams mtshan gyi 'di rnam par snang ba na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas yon tan grags pa thogs pa med pa'i rnam par thar
120b8: pa'i 'od kyi rgyal po zhes byang chub sems dpa' stobs dang / brtson 'grus thogs pa med pa'i brtson 'grus la sogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang thabs cig tu

121a1: bzhugs pa'ang mig lam du snang ngo / / rigs kyi bu de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa 'di dag la stsogs pa/ phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas//
121a2: sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mthong yang de bzhin gshegs pa de dag kyang 'dir mi byed/ kho bo yang der 'gro ba med de nam 'dod pa de na bde ba yod pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na/ de bzhin gshegs/
121a3: pa'od snang ba mtha' yas pa bzhugs pa'ang mthong ngo // tsan dan yod pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na de bzhin gshegs pa 'od snang rdo rje bzhugs pa'ang mthong ngo // spos ni yod pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na de bzhin
121a4: gshegs pa 'od snang rin chen bzhugs pa yang mthong ngo / / pad mo yod pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na de bzhin gshegs pa 'od snang rin chen pad mo bzhugs pa'ang mthong ngo // gser yod pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams
121a5: na de bzhin gshegs pa 'od snang zhi ba bzhugs pa'ang mthong ngo / / mngon par dga' ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams na de bzhin gshegs pa mi skul pa bzhugs pa'ang mthong ngo // shin tu brtan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams
121a6: nad de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge bzhugs pa'ang mthong ngo / / me long gi dkyil 'khor ltar snang ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams na de bzhin gshegs pa blo gros zla ba bzhugs pa yang mthong ngo // rin chen dpal gyi dad pas
121a7: brgyan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad bzhugs pa yang mthong ngo / / rigs kyi bu de ltar kho bos ni phyogs gang dang gang 'jig rten gyi khams gang dang gang gi de bzhin gshegs
121a8: pa gang dang gang mthong bar 'dod pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa de dang de dag kyang mthong ngo / / dus gang dang gang du dmigs par gang dang gang la sngon gyi spyod pa gang dang gang gis de bzhin gshegs pa mthong bar 'dod

121b1: pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa gang dang gang gi don dang / sems can 'dul ba gang dang gang gi don du de bzhin gshegs pa gang dang gang mthong bar 'dod pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa de dang de dag kyang mthong ste/ de bzhin
121b2: gshegs pa de dag kyang 'dir gshegs pa ma yin/ bdag kyang der phyin pa ma yin no// rigs kyi bu de ltar kho bos de bzhin gshegs pa rnams gang las kyang byon pa med par shes pa la rang gi rgyud las kyang gang
121b3: yang 'gro ba med par shes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams rnam par dmigs pa yang rmi lam lta bur shes la/ rang gi sems rnam par dmigs pa yang mi lam dang 'dra bar rgyu bar shes pa dang / de bzhin gshen
121b4: pa rnams rnam par dmigs pa yang gzugs brnyan lta bur shes la rang gi sems rnam par dmigs pa yang chu'i snod gsal ba lta bur shes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams rnam par dmigs pa
121b5: yang sgyu mas bya ba'i gzugs lta bur shes la rang gi sems rnam par dmigs pa yang sgyu ma lta bur shes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung yang sgra snyan ri'i brag ca lta bur brjod par shes la rang gi sems
121b6: r nam par dmigs pa yang sgra brnyan lta bur shes pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad ni rang gi sems kyi byin gyi rlabs las 'byung ngo zhes bya bar rjes su rtogs shing khong du chud
121b7: do/ / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa thams cad kyang rang gi sems kyi byin gyi rlabs so// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yang rang gi sems kyi byin gyi rlabs so// sems can thams cad yongs su smin par
121b8: bya ba dang / gdul ba yang rang gi sems kyi byin gyi rlabs so// byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa yang rang gi sems kyi byin gyis rlabs so// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi grong khyer du phyin

122a1: par bya ba yang rang gi sems kyi byin gyi rlabs so/ / rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas rnam par brtse ba yang rang gi sems kyi byin gyi rlabs so// sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par
122a2: 'tshang rgya ba yang rang gi sems kyi byid kyi brlabs so/ / chos kyi dbyings kun nas 'dus par khyu mchog gi mthu dbyung zhing rnam par 'phrul pa yang rang gi sems kyi byin kyi rlabs so// bskal pa thams cad
122a3: shin tu phra bar bsdu ba'i ye shes kyang rang gi sems kyi byin gyis rlabs so zhes bya bar khong du chud cing rjes su rtogs so/ / rigs kyi bu de la kho bo 'di snyam du sems te/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyis
122a4: ni rang gi sems nyid nye bar brtan par bya'o/ / chos kyi sprin gyis ni rang gi sems nyid yongs su brlab par bya'o// sgrib pa'i chos rnams las ni rang gi sems nyid yongs su spyang par bya'o// brtson 'grus kyis ni
122a5: rang gi sems nyid yongs su brtan par bya'o/ / bzod pas ni rang gi sems nyid mnyam par bya'o// ye shes khong du chud par bya bas ni rang gi sems gzhol bar bya'o// shes rab kyis ni rang gi sems nyid
122a6: yongs su sbyang bar bya'o/ / dbang rnams la ni rang gi sems nyid mngon par bsgrub par bya'o// sangs rgyas dang nyan thos mnyam pa nyid la ni rang gi sems nyid rgyas par bya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i
122a7: stobs bcus ni rang gi sems nyid snang bar bya'o snyam mo/ / rigs kyi bu kho bo de ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par thar pa thogs pa med pa'i rgyan 'di shes te/ blangs shing yongs su 'dzin par
122a8: mdzad na/ kho bos byang chub sems dpa' chags pa med pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ chags pa med par rnam pa'i spyod yul dang ldan pa/ da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad mngon sum du

122b1: zhugs pa'i ting nge 'dzin rab tu thob pa/ mya ngan las 'da' ba med pa'i mtha' la gnas pa rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi sgo'i ting nge 'dzin rab tu thob pa/ dus gsum mnyam pa nyid du gyur pa/ gzhi kun nas/
122b2: byed pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gyi tshul shes pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du lus rnam par bkram pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yul tha mi dad pa la rnam par spyod pa/ phyogs thams cad du mngon par
122b3: phyogs pa'i spyod yul dang ldan pa/ phyin phyogs med pa'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gyis rnam par lta ba de dag gi lus la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'jug cing 'dra bar snang yang de dag la bdag
122b4: dang 'jig rten gyi khams su gnyis kyi 'du shes med pa de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan/ song rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid kyi 'dzam bu'i gling gi/
122b5: mgo 'gebs pas rgyas par 'gengs pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de na dge slong rgya mtsho'i rgyal mtshan ces bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sa byang chub sems dpa'i
122b6: spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig/ de nas tshong dpon bu nor bzangs tshong dpon btang brjod kyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ tshong dpon btang brjod la lan brgya
122b7: kong du ma ngag yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ yang das yang bltas te/ tshong dpon btang brjod kyi yon tan grangs med pal snyan par brjod de brtag pa dang mos par bya ba dang / mi btang bar bya ba
122b8: sems shing rus te smre sngags gton nas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen sdug par sems shing dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rjes su 'brang ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la bsnyen bkur bar mos pa dang / na

123a1: pa'i bshes gnyen gyis bsgo ba dang / mi 'gal bar byed pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dge ba'i bshes gnyen la rag lus par rjes su blta ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la rjes su
123a2: bsam pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la g.yo rgyu med par spyod pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi sems kyi dbang du 'gro bar bya ba dang ldan pas de ba'i shes gnyen rnams gdon pa thams cad yongs su
123a3: spong bar byed pasam tsam du sems dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su skyid pas patsam du sems shing / tshong dpon btang brjod kyi drung nas song ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs tshong dpon btang brjod kyis bstan
123a4: pa de la rjes su sems shing / tshong dpon btang brjod kyi gdams ngag la nan tan du bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / byang chub
123a5: sems dpa'i ye shes snang ba bsam gyis me khyab pa rjes su dran par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings la 'jug cing 'bab pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa khong du chud par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams
123a6: kyi yongs su 'du bar bya ba'i tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa la 'dug par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rjes su blta bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing
123a7: yongs su bsdu ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mos par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi rgyan rjes su sbyang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin dang / rnam par thar pa'i rnam par dgod
123a8: pa dang / khyu mchog gi mthu byung ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa la yongs su brtag pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams tha dad pa la bsgrubs pa med pa/ bsas kyis mi khyab pa la 'jug pa la/ byang chub sems

123b1: ngapa'i las la bsam pa shin tu brtan pa de la nan tan du bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' las dang / smon lam gyi rgyud bsam gyis mi khyab pa de'i rjes su spyod cing mthar gyis 'jam bu'i gling gi mas//
123b2: 'gabs pas rgyas par 'gengs pa zhes bya ba gang na ba der byin nas/ dge slong rgya mtsho'i rgyal mtshan tshol tshal ba las/ 'chag pa'i gnas shig gi 'chag sa'i mthar thug ste/ ting nge 'dzin la
123b3: mnyam par bzhag nas dbugs kyi nang du rgyu ba med cing mi g.yol byed pa med cing lus drang por bsrang ste/ dran pa mngon du byas nas ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas rnam
123b4: par 'phrul zhing g.yas g.yon dang / steng logs su lus mtha' yas la tshad med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa spyi gtsug bltar mi mthong ba// kha dog du ma'i lus dang ldan pa sems kyi skad cig re re la kha
123b5: dog rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med pa yongs su ston pa de/ de de ltar mnyam par bzhag cing zab la zhi ste/ g.yo ba med cing dmigs pa med la dga' bas lus mtho bar gyur pa de'i baspu'i sgo thams cad nas/ byang
123b6: chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pas rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rab tu 'gyed pa byed cing 'dug pa mthong ngo / / rnam par thar pas rnam par 'phrul pa de'i mthus sems kyi skad cig
123b7: re re la sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchod pa snang ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongs su dag par bya ba dang / sems can
123b8: thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po rnam par bzlog pa dang / ngan song gi lam thams cad yongs su gcad pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bde ba'i lam gyi sgo 'byed pa dang / sems can thams cad

124a1: kyi nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba rab tu zhi bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi mi shes pa'i sgrib pa rnam par gtor ba dang / sems can thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la dgod pa'i phyir rnam par 'phrul
124a2: pa'i bye brag rnam pa sna tshogs mtha' yas pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs shing de'i rkang pa'i mthil gnyis nas/ tshong dpon gyi tshogs bkur sti dang / rim gro sna tshogs byed pa 'jig
124a3: rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i 'tshong dpon dang 'dra ba'i gzugs dang ldan pa lhag pa'i yul la spyod pa/ rgyan sna tshogs kyis lus shinaH klubs pa/ thor tshugs dang gtsug gi rin po che dang
124a4: cod pan sna tshogs thogs pa sangs rgyas kyi zheng grangs med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi bye ba byos pa'i 'khor dang ldan par byung ba mthong ngo / / bram ze dang khyim bdag mang po bza' btung rnam pa
124a5: mang po dang / ro'i yan lag sna tshogs su sbyar ba thams cad dang / rgyan thams cad dang gos thams cad dang / me tog thams cad dang / phreng ba thams cad dang / spos thams cad dang / byug pa thams cad
124a6: dang / 'dod pa'i yon tan thams cad dang / rin po che thams cad dang / gnas thams cad dang / snod rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad dang / yo byad rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad kyis/ sems can dbul po
124a7: rnams yongs su bsdud cing / 'gro ba sdug bsngal ba rnams dbugs dbyung ba dang / sems can gyi sems tshim par bya ba dang / sems can gyi bsam pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / sems can
124a8: rnams byang chub tu yongs su smin par byed cing phyogs bcu bkang ste/ 'dod pa mthong ngo // pus mo'i lha nga gnyis nas rgyal rigs mkhas pa'i gzugs dang / bram ze mkhas pa'i gzugs dang / 'jig

124b1: rten mkhas pa'i gzugs dang / bco sna tshogs la mkhas pa'i gzugs dang / mi'i 'gro ba'i rgyud na mkhas pa'i gzugs dang / 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i las kyi tshul dang / rgyas la
124b2: gsal zhing mkhas pa'i gzugs dang / 'jig rten gyis slob dpon du bya bar mkhas pa'i gzugs cha byad rnam pa du ma dang ldan pa/ dbyibs dang rgyan rnam pa du ma dang ldan pa/ yid du 'ong ba'i tshig mang po
124b3: brjod pas/ yid mi bde ba'i sems can rab tu dga' bar byed cing chos kyi nor gyis dbul ba'i sems can rnams la phan gdags pa dang / sdug bsngal ba'i sems can rnams bde bar bya ba dang / log par
124b4: ltung ba'i sems can rnams mngon par gdon pa dang / theg pa'i grul nyamanyes su gyur pa'i sems can rnams dbugs dpyang ba dang / 'jigs pa'i sems can rnams yongs su bskyab pa dang / dge ba'irtsa
124b5: ba'i sgo kun tu grag pa za bya ba dang / sdig pa'i las bzlog pa'i sgra yongs su bsgrag pa dang / dge ba'i chos yang dag par blang ba la sems can gzung ba dang / don spyod pa la sems can dgod pa dang / dga'
124b6: shugs yongs su bskyed pa dang / snyan par sla ba'i bsdu ba'i dngos po yongs su brjod pa dang / 'jig rten la don 'thun par bsgrub pa ston pa byed cing phyogs bcu rgyas par bkang ste/ 'dod pa mthong ngo //
124b7: lte ba'i dkyil 'khor nas drang srong mang po 'gro ba thams cad kyi lus kyi dbyibs su 'khod pa/ pags pa dang shun pa'i gos gyon pa/ ril pa thogs pa/ gzugs dang cha byad dang dbyibs sna tshogs can/
124b8: spyod lam rab tu zhi ba dag kyang byung nas/ steng dge bar snang las sangs rgyas kyi yon tan brjod pa byed cing / chos kyi sgra yongs su skrag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sgra brjod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge

125a1: 'dun yongs su bstan pa dang / tshungs pa'i spyod pa yongs su brjod pa dang / dbang po dben pa la sems can dgod pa dang / rang bzhin med pa'i don rab tu brtag pa dang / ye shes kyi don
125a2: 'jig rten rab tu dgod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi gtsug lagag rnam pa yongs su brjod pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi ye shes kyis 'brang ba'i lam sa tshul rab tu bstan pa dang / mthar kyis bya ba'i la
125a3: lasems can rab tu dgod pa pyad cing / phyogs bcu bka sa 'dod pa mthong // rgya ba logs gnyis nas/ kwa'i bu ma 'jig rten tu ba thams cad kyi grangs dang mnyam pa/ lus kyi dbyibs bsam
125a4: gyis me khyab pa du ma dang ldan pa byung ste/ klu'i rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis me khyab pa yongs su bstan pa dang / spos kyi sprin gyi rkyen bsam gyis mi khyab pa nam mkha'i dbyings la byin gyis brlab
125a5: pa dang / me tog gi sprin gyi brgyan bsam gyis me khyab pas nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad brgyan pa dang / phyeng ba'i sprin bsam gyis me khyab pa'i rgyan gyis nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad rnam par
125a6: grub pa dang / rin po che'i gdugs kyi sprin bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad yongs su khebs par bya ba dang / rin po che'i rgyal mtshan gyi sprin bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan
125a7: dang/ rin po che'i lha'i ba dan gyi sprin bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan dang / rin po che'i byang 'phrul sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / char bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan dang / nor bu rin po che dam pa'i sprin
125a8: gyi char 'bab pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan dang / rin po che'i se mo do sna tshogs dang / me tog gi sprin gyi char rab sam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan dang / rin po che'i khri la skyil mo krung du 'khod pa

125b1: mas da'i masas kyi srin kyi ma bas sa mas ma sgrub pa babs pa rgya dang / pacwa rgyan tshugs dang ldan pa'i bram ma mas kyi san kyi
125b2: smon gyi char 'babs pa bsam gyis sa khab pa dang / ngan po che pad ma thob ma tho bas tig gas dubs btsun pa/ rin papa tshal ba thams cad kyi 'dra'i smin gyi ma rnam par sha pa
125b3: me khyab pa'i chan dang / rin po che'i cod pan sa smi nor bu rin po che thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa/ 'odag zer gyi sprin mtha' yas pa'i char 'babs pa bsam thos mi khyab pa'i cha dang k+ta'i lus kyi
125b4: matog dang / phre ba dang / bdag pa dang / rgyan dang / lha'i bdan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan dang / lha'i bu mo mang po'i lus kyi sprin bal mo sbyar te/ gser gyi me tog snyim pas 'thor ba/ bzhin gshegs pa
125b5: la yon tan dang legs pa thams cad du bstod pa'i sprin gyi 'brug sgra 'byin pa'i char 'bebs pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyan rnam pa pa'i dbyings la byin gyis rlob cing / spos kyi phung po'i sprin na
125b6: po che thams cad kyi kha dog du 'dug pa dang / bdug spos kyi ni bran dang sprin shin tu rgya che bas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mngon par khebs par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi
125b7: khams 'byam klas pa thams cad rab tu brgyan pa dang / sems can thams cad rab tu dga' bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad mchod pas skad ceg skad cig du chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas
125b8: par 'gangs pa tshong dpon gyi bra nor bzangs kyis mthong ngo / / mthong ka'i dpal gyi be'u nas lha ma yin gyi dbang po sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste/ lha ma yin gyi sku

126a1: rnam par 'phrul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'arab tus na cing na 'jan can pa sangs su bsam pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams brgya gang rab tu bstod pa dang / ra' rgyal ba chen pa thams cad 'bab par bya ba dang /
126a2: lha'i gnas thams cad yongs su spyod pa dang / bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad zil gyis gnan pa dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad rab tu gdul ba dang / nga rgyal dang rlom pa dang dregs pa thams cad rab tu gzhom pa dang /
126a3: gnod par sems pa'i sems bzlog cing dga' bar bya ba dang / thob tsam pa'i sems phyir bzlog par bya ba dang / sems can rnams kyi mi dge ba'i chos rab tu zhi bar bya ba dang / nyon mongs pa'i ri rnam par gtor bang
126a4: nyon mongs pa'i thab mo shin tu zhi bar bya ba dang / lha ma yin gyi rgyus rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rnam par brtse ba sna tshogs kyis sems can rnams skyo bar bya ba dang / sdig pa las gyen du bskyod pa dang / 'khor bas 'jig
126a5: par bya ba dang / srid pa'i lam gyi rgyud thams cad nas gyen du bskyod de gnas med pa la rab tu gnas par bya ba dang / byang chub kyi sems la sems can rnams rab tu dgod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
126a6: byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu dgod par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa la rab tu bzung ba dang / byang chub sems
126a7: dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi tshul sdang ba yongs su bskyed pa dang / chos kyi tshul rnam par dgod pa sna tshogs kyi sems kyi skad cig rer na chos kyi dbyings rgyas par 'gengs par byed pa chod
126a8: dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis mthong ngo / / rgyab kyi gzhung nas nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas mang po sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung nas nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i

126b1: sems can bdag tu mngon par zhan pa rnams la bdag med pa dang / sems can med pa yongs su brjod pa byed cing rtag par mngon par zhen pa rnams la 'du byed thams cad mi rtag par yongs su

132a8: bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' dbang skur ba thos pa rnams la gzhi kun tu rten pa'i sprin ces bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / byang

132b1: chub sems dpa' chos chen po'i rgyal mtshan du dbang bskur ba rnams la sgo kun nas 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par 'bab pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' gzhon nur gyur pa/

132b3: chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' lhag pa'i bsam pa dag pa rnams la chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyi bye brag shes pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi cha
132b4: mngon par dbab pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sngon gyi sbyor ba dang ldan pa rnams la 'gro ba yongs su sdud pas kun nas brgyan pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang //
132b5: byang chub sems dpa' cher skyes pa rnams la dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor mngon sum du dmigs pa'i sprin ces bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang /

133a1: dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i smon lam gyis dga' bar byed pa'i mdzod ces bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / gzugs la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la gzhi kun tu mi zad pa'i
133a2: mdzod ces bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi chang mngon par dbab pa dang / tshangs pa'i res kyi lha rnams la tshul rgya mtsho tshad med pa'i 'brug sgra'i dbyangs shes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / dbang sgyur ba'i
133a3: lha rnams la stobs 'byung ba'i chos kyi yo byad mi zad pa'i mdzod ces bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / bdud kyi ris kyi lha rnams la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs rgyal mtshan sna tsha ba
133a4: tshegs can yang dag par bsgrub pa'i dbyangs shes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / 'phrul dga'i lha rnams la ye shes rin po che sna tshogs la brtson pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi dbyings kyi sprin gyi char

133a7: dga' ba'i shugs 'byung zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / gnod sbyin gyi dbang po'i gnas su chos kyi dbyings kyi nam mkha' la de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phral pas rgyas pa

133b1: dbab pa dang / lam yin byaganas su la gas sa rgyal darje' dkyis 'bang ces bya bar chas kyi sman mar mnapa dbab pa dang / nam mkha'i phreng ga dbang pa gnasas dpazhan gshegs pa thams

133b4: gnas su dga' ba'i rgya mtsho'i rnam par 'phel bar byed pa'i shugs shes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / mi'i gnas su 'gro ba thams cad las khyad par du 'phags pa'i ye shes rnam par 'byed
133b5: pa zhes bya ba chos kyi sprin gyi chang mngon par dbab pa dang / sems can dmyal ba'i 'jig rten du 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad rab tu na pa'i dbyangs dang / 'phags pa'i lam gyi tshig gi rgyud kyis brgyan
133b6: pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi chang mngon par dbab pa dang / byol song gi skye gnas su las kyi la mkhan ma tho ba med pa la nan tan du bya'i dbyangs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rdzas su dran pa'i sprin gyi dkyil
133b7: 'khor gyi ldan zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi pha rol du phyin pa bsgrags pa/ sems can thams cad

134a1: kyi nga ro zhes bya ba'i chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa mdzad cing chos kyi dbyings rgyas par 'gengs pa tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis mthong ngo / / ba spu'i bu ga thams cad las ba spu'i bu ga'i sgor

134b1: pathams cad kyang snying rnga chen pos dbang du byas pa'i phyir nyams su brjod par byas pa dang / bag la nyala'i bar byas pa dang / btang snyoms su bzhag pa'i byang nab sems dpa'i bzang ba'i snang bar
134b2: par 'phrul ba'i gzugs brnyan gyi gzugs des budag mthong ngo / / bkra'i bugazhi sgo'i 'dag par kyi dra ba dang / dkyil 'khod sa la las ni byang chubs mas dpa' thams da kyi brtson 'grus kyi pa rnamapa

134b6: len pa ji snyed pa dang / rigs su skye ba yongs su bzung ba ji snyed pa dang / gzugs kyi lus yongs su grub pa ji snyed pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi man ngag la nan tan tu bya ba'i gnas ji snyed pa dang /

135a1: snyed pa de dag thams cad kyang tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis mthong ngo / / ba spu'i sgo'i 'od gzer gyi dra ba dang / dkyil 'khor la la las ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyod pa la rnam par spyod cing / chos

135b1: cad kyis smon lam mngon par bsgrubs pa'i spyod pa dang / sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba'i smon lam mngon par bsgrubs pa'i spyod pa dang / zhing thams cad yongs su dag par bya

136a1: bar gnad panas shes dal rabacab ga pa dang / byung chub sems dpa' ba ga bas dasangasas bskyed pa byung chubs mas dang 'dran pas rgya pa sa pasu byung chub dung / byang chu smrab

136b1: dang / bsam gtan gyi yul gyi dga' ba nyams su myong bar bgyi ba dang / 'dus byas la spyod pa'i bde ba yongs su 'phel bar bgyi ba dang / khams gsum pa las 'byung ba'i sgo yongs su bstan pa la sta gon

137a1: ban skyong grangs mad pa thag banand pa 'ongs su 'brab par 'gyur / / smras pa 'phags pa ting lan 'da' phral der bsam pa dang / smras pa gas kyi bung dnge 'angan sa sa rnams par thug sa byam/

137b1: rgya ma thags pa med/ / sems can rgyam tha thams cad du 'dug cang yang du chud par bya ba la zags pa ma dang// sems can gyi dbang ba rgya mtshathams cad shes shing khong du chung pa la grags pa me /
