149a4: zhi bar bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snying rje'i sprin chen po kun nas 'du ba yin// rigs kyi bu mdor na/ de dag la stsogs pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i tshul dang / sgo grangs med pa brgya stong phrag
149a5: bcu dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis yongs su bsgrub par bya'o/ / rigs kyi bu gzhan yang 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa ni ye shes khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir chos thams cad la
149a6: yang dag par gzhol ba'o/ / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa ni yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir zhing thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba'o// rigs kyi bu de lta bas na/ kho mos ni bdag gi smon lam nam
149a7: mkha'i dbyings rnam par dag pa'i mtha' gang du thug pa de'i mthas klas par shog shig/ bdag gi smon lam 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dag pa'i mtha' gang du thug pa'i de'i mthas klas par shog shig/ bdag gi
149a8: sngon lam sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa dang / bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba dang / bag la nyal ba'i mtha' gang du thug pa de'i mthas klas par shog shig/ ces de ltar smon lam btab bo// smras

149b1: ba'i bags ma rnam par thar pa 'da' mang ci zhes bgyi/ smras pa rigs kyi burnam par thar pa 'dan nyon mongs pa med pa bde ba'i rgyal mngon ces bya ste/ rigs kyi bu khams kyang byang chub sems dpa'i rnam
149b2: par thar pa de gcig pu shes par zad na byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par 'dzin pa'i phyir/ sems rgya mtsho dang ldan pa lhag pa'i bsam pa brtan pa'i phyir ri rab dang 'dra ba/ sems
149b3: can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i nang rab tu ses par byed pa'i phyir sman gyi rgyal po mthong na legs pa lta bu/ sems can thams cad kyi ma rig pa'i mun pa sel ba'i phyir nyi mar gyur pa/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam
149b4: pa'i gnas su gyur pasas lta bu'i sems dang ldan pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi don byed pa'i phyir rlung du gyur pa/ sems can thams cad la ye shes kyi snang ba 'byin pa'i phyir mar mer gyur pa/ zhi ba'i sgras
149b5: sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'bebs pa'i sprin du gyur pas bsod nams kyi 'od gzer gyi de ba rab tu 'gyed pa'i phyir zla ba lta bur/ 'gro ba thams cad yongs su bsrung ba la zhugs pa'i
149b6: phyir/ brgya byin lta bu/ de dag gi spyod pa shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod pa 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa smyos pa 'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi rnam pa mtha'
149b7: dang dbus med par yongs su bstan par nus re skan/ / mong rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid kyi rgya mtsho rnam par rlob pa 'di nyid na yul chu bo gcad ma zhes bya ba yod de/ de na dang song 'jigs mchog dbyangs
149b8: shes bya ba 'dug gis de'i gan du song la dris shig dang / de rigs kyi bu khyod la byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa ston par 'gyur ro// de nas tshed dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis dge bsnyen ma yid bzhin gyi rkang da

150a1: gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ dge bsnyen ma yid bzhin la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ yang dang yang bltas te phyag 'tshal nas ngo mchi mas gang bar dus te/ byang
150a2: chub mchog tu dkon pa rjes su sems shing dge ba'i bshes gnyen rim gror bya ba dkon pa rjes su bsam pa dang / skyes bu dam pa 'phrad pa dkon pa rjes su bsam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dbang po 'thob pa
150a3: bya ba rjes su bsam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa yongs su dag pa dkon pa rjes su bsam pa dang / skal po mnyam pa'i bshes gnyen phrad pa dkon par rjes su bsam pa dang / byang chub tu yang dag pa
150a4: lta ba bzhin du mngon par mos shing sems nges par gzhog pa dkon pa rjes su bsam pa dang / mi mnyam pa med pa'i chos kyi tshul rjes su bstan pa'i sbyor ba dkon pa rjes su bsam pa dang / sems dri ma med cing
150a5: myi 'phrogs pa'i sbyor ba yang dag par bsgrub par dka' ba rjes su bsam pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du shugs drag po rnam par bskyed pa'i chos kyi snang ba dkon par rjes su bsam pa byed cing / dge bsnyen
150a6: ma yid bzhin gyi drung nas song ngo / / de nas tshod dpon gyi bu nor bzangs byang chub sems dpa'i gdams dag gi rjes su song ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su dag par bya ba dang /
150a7: rjes su song ba'i sems dang ldan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bsod nams kyi stobs rnam par 'phel bar bya ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas pa lta bu'i shugs drag pos rab tu snang bar bya ba'i sems
150a8: dang ldan pa/ chos kyi gter 'thob par bye ba la shugs drag po skyes pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub pa'i shugs drag po rab tu 'phel ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ chos thams

150b1: cad kyi phyogs la mngon du lta ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ chos kyi rang bzhin gyi 'od kyis snang bar byas pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ sgrib pa thams cad rnam par 'thor ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ chos kyi dbyings la mun pa/
150b2: med par rnam par lta ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ rdo rje rin po che mthu bo ches mi choms pa ltar dri ma med pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ bdud thams cad kyi dpudags brgal bar dka' zhing thub par dka' ba'i sems
150b3: dang ldan pa de mthar kyis/ yul chu bo gtsang ma gal ba der phyin nas/ drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs tshol tshol ba las/ de'i tshe drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs dge ba spyad pa'i gnas shing dang / shing phran
150b4: sna tshogs grangs med pa'i nags tshal mdangs dga' ba/ lo mas rgyas pa'i shing gis kun nas 'khrigs pa/ rtag tu me tog rgyas pa dang ldan pa'i shing sna tshogs can/ rtag tu shing shog mang po dang ldan pa'i shing thog
150b5: gi shing dang ldan pa/ nor bu rin po che sna tshogs shing drang nor bu rin po che'i spang leb kyis rtag tu bshigs pa dang ldan pa/ tsan dan dam pa'i shing kun nas bres pa/ a ga ru yid du 'ong ba'i shing las spos kyi dri
150b6: rtag tu 'byung bas rab tu brgyan pa/ phyogs bzhi nas shing pa ta la rnam par mdzes par skyes pa yongs su brgyan pa/ nya gro dro'i shing dbyangs yid du 'ong ba dang ldan pa/ 'dzem bu'i shing las rtag tu shing thog
150b7: smin pa 'bral ba/ me tog gi tshal pad mo dang / ud pa la gsar du skyes pas rab tu brgyan pa/ zhig na 'dug pa 'dug ste/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs/ drang srong stong
150b8: phrag bcus bskor cing / tsan dan gyi yal gshin tu 'brel ba'i byi sgribs shig na/ thor tshugs kyi cod pan dang / bags pa dang / rtsi 'gos gyon pa/ shing shun gyi smad yogs can rtsa'i stan la 'dug pa/

151a1: mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs ga la ba der song ste/ phyin nas yang dag pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang phrad pa'i bsam pas dge ba'i bshes gnyen ni yang dag pa'i
151a2: lam ston pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid 'byung ba'i sgo yin par yang dag par lta/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa la gzhog pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa de ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi gdams ngag la rag lus par
151a3: yang dag par lta/ stobs bcu'i ye shes rin po che'i gling du skyel bas/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi mnyan pa la rag lus par yang dag par ston/ stobs bcu'i ye shes snang ba
151a4: yang dag par skyed pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi sgron mas snang bar bya ba yin par yang dag par lta/ nyam nyes med par thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi grong du phyin par byed pas//
151a5: thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi lam ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen yin par yang dag par lta/ mnyam pa dang mi mnyam pa yongs su ston pas/
151a6: thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mar me ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen yin/ par yang dag par lta/ g.yang sa'i 'jigs pa thams cad med
151a7: par byed pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi stegs bu dge ba'i bshes gnyen yin par yang dag par lta/ byams pa chen po'i stobs kyis sim pa yongs su skyed pa'i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi gdug
151a8: ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen yin par yang dag par lta/ snying rje chen po yongs su bskyed pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shugs drag po ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen yin par yang dag par lta zhing chos kyi

151b1: rang bzhin gyi tshul rab tu snang bar byed pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid gsal bar mthong ba ni/ dge pa'i bshes gnyen lnga rag/ las par mthong nas/ lus thams cad kyis pab ste// phyag byas nas langs
151b2: te/ drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs la lan brgya stong du ma bskor ba byas nas mdun du 'dug ste/ bal mo sbyar nas yid du 'ong ba'i tshul gyisayid du 'ong ba'i tshig brjod de/ 'di
151b3: skad ces smras so/ / 'phags pa bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du sems bskyed na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang /
151b4: ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba ma 'tshal te/ 'phags pa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams la gdams dag dang / rjes su bstan pa mdzad do zhes thos nas/ 'phags pa ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' byang
151b5: chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba bdag la bshad du gsol// de nas drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyis bram ze'i byis pa stong phrag bcu po de dag
151b6: la bltas te 'di skad ces smras so/ / byis pa bdag rigs kyi bu 'dis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du sems bskyed de/ sems can thams cad 'jigs pa med pa la
151b7: 'gron du gnyer to/ / rigs kyi bu 'di ni sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i don du sta gon du gnas pa ste/ ye shes rgya mtsho la mngon du gyur pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos
151b8: kyi sprin gyi char btung bar 'dod pa'o/ / chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la 'jug par 'dod pa'o// ye shes kyi snang ba chen po la gnas par 'dod pa'o// snying rje chen po'i sbyin bsdu bar 'dod pa'o//

152a1: chos kyi char chen po mngon par 'dod pa'o// ye shes chen po'i zla ba 'jig rten du shar bar byas te/ nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba thams cad rab tu gzhil bar 'dod pa'o// sems can thams
152a2: cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par spel ba 'dod po'o/ / de nas bram ze'i byis pa stong phrag bcu po de dag gis me tog dri zhim la yi dang 'od zhang kha dog sna tshogs dang ldan pa mang pos tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la gtor
152a3: mngon par gtor to/ / rab tu gtor to// mngon par phyag 'tshal to// de ltar btud dbyug 'tshal nas/ g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te/ tshig 'di skad ces brjod do// 'di ni sems can thams cad yongs su
152a4: skyob par 'gyur ro/ / sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad rab tu zhi bar bgyid par 'gyur ro// byol song gi skye gnas kyi lam gyi rgyud thams cad rnam par gcod par 'gyur ro// gshin rje'i 'jig rten
152a5: kyi lam gyi rgyud thams cad rnam par bzlog par 'gyur ro/ / mi khom pa'i sgo thams cad gtsad par 'gyur ro// sred pa'i rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su skams par 'gyur ro// srid pa'i bcing ba gcod pa
152a6: 'gyur ro/ / sdug bsngal gyi phung po rnam par bzlog par 'gyur ro// ma rig pa'i mun pa sel bar 'gyur ro// bsod nams kyi 'khor yug gis 'jig rten yongs su skor bar 'gyur ro// ye shes rin po che'i
152a7: 'byung gnas su yongs su ston par 'gyur ro/ / ye shes kyi nyi ma'i tshor bar bgyid par 'gyur ro// chos kyi mig rnam par sbyong bar 'gyur ro// 'jig rten rnams la mnyam pa dang mi mnyam pa yang dag
152a8: par ston par 'gyur ro/ / de nas drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyis byis pa de dag la 'di skad ces smras so// byis pa gang gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa

152b1: de ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe/ sems can thams cad kyi bde ba rab tu bskyed de/ rim gyis thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang thob par 'gyur ro// byis pa dag rigs kyi bu 'dis ni bla na med pa yang
152b2: dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa ste/ de bas na 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thams cad kyis yongs su spong bar 'gyur ro// de nas drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyis/ tshong dpon gyi bu
152b3: nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so/ / rigs kyi bu kho bo ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa gzhan gyis mi thub pa'i rgyal mtshan thob pa'o// nor bzangs kyis smras pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam
152b4: par thar pa gzhan gyis mi thub pa 'di'i yul ji lta bu zhig mchis/ de nas drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyis lag pa g.yas pa brkyang ste// tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyi mgo la byugs nas lag pas
152b5: bzung ngo / / tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyis lag pa g.yas pas gzung ma thag tu/ de'i mod la tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis/ phyogs bcur sangs rgyas kyis zhing ba
152b6: stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu pra ba snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing mthong bar gyur te/ de dag gi de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi zhabs kyi drung na bdag
152b7: nyid 'dug par shes par gyur to/ / sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag kyang rnam pa grangs med par rnam par dag pa'i rgyan dang ldan par mthong ngo // de dag na'ang de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtshol
152b8: dog sna tshogs can rgyan rnam pa tha dad pa dang ldan pa dga'akhod par mthong ngo / / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho de dag na'ang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po 'bang bas brgyan pa dag

153a1: par mthong ngo / / de dag las kyang tshig dang yi ge gcig las kyang phyir phyogs pa med par ches bstan pa nyan te// de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo de dag kyang phan tshun du ma 'dres par yang dag
153a2: par 'dzin te/ / chos kyi sprin gyi char sems can bsam pa sna tshogs la 'bab pa de dag kyang yang dag par 'dzin to// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi sngon gyi smon lam mos pa sna tshogs kyi stobs kyis rnam par sbyangs
153a3: brgya mtsho la yang zhugs so/ / sangs rgyas kyi zhing dag par bsdu ba smon lam sna tshogs rgya mtshos rnam par dag pa rgya mtsho de dag la yang zhugs so// sangs rgyas kyi sku mdog sems can gyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin
153a4: du tshim par 'gyur ba'i rnam par dmigs pa de dag kyang mthong ngo / / sangs rgyas kyi 'od gzer gyi dra ba 'dod chags dang bral ba sna tshogs kyis rnam par dag pa'i rgyan gyi 'khor de dag kyang mthong ngo // sangs rgyas kyi
153a5: stobs de dag la'ang ye shes snang ba bsgribs pa med pa dang ldan pas zhugs so/ / de ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnam par thar pa gzhan gyis mi thub pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi ye shes kyi 'od kyis snang bar gyur pa/ tang nge
153a6: 'dzin rnam par snang mdzad kyi snying po snang ba rab tu thob pa/ ting nge 'dzin ye shes mi zad pa'i rnam par thar pa dang ldan pas/ gzungs kyi sgo snang ba phyogs kun gyi dra ba rab tu thob pa/ gzungs kyi sgo rdo rje'i snying pos
153a7: sems rab tu gsal bar byas pa/ ting nge 'dzin ye shes brtsegs pa rnam par 'phye ba'i yul la rnam par phye ba rab tu thob pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par spyod pa gzhi kun nas rnam par brgyan pa'i
153a8: snying po yul du gyur pa/ ting nge 'dzin gyi snang ba sangs rgyas nam mkha'i snying po'i dkyil 'khor la rab tu zhugs pa/ ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i mu khyud kyis sems rab tu

153b1: snang bar byas pa/ ting nge 'dzin gyi snang ba/ dus gsum gyi ye shes rin po che mi zad pa'i 'khor lo rab tu brtson pa des/ de bzhin gshegs pa la la'i zhabs kyi drung du ni nyin zhag gcig len par shes so//
153b2: la lar ni nyin zhag bdun lon pa snyam/ la lar ni zla ba phyed len pa snyam/ la lar ni zla ba gcig len pa snyam/ la lar ni lo gcig lon pa snyam/ la lar ni lo brgyar lon pa snyam/ la lar ni lo stong lon pa snyam/
153b3: la lar ni lo brgya phrag stong lon pa snyam/ la lar ni lo bye ba lon pa stam/ la lar ni lo bye ba brgya stong lon pa snum/ la lar ni lo bye ba stong lon pa snyam/ la lar ni le bye brgya phrag stong lon pa snyam/ la lar ni lo bye ba khrag khrig lon
153b4: pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa byed lon pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa gcig lon pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa brgya lon pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa stong lon pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa brgya phrag stong
153b5: lon pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa bye ba lon pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa bye ba phrag brgya lon pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa bye ba stong lon pa snyam/ la lar ni bskal pa bye ba brgya phrag stong lon pa snyam/
153b6: la lar ni bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong lon pa snyam/ byed pa nas de bzhin gshegs pa la la'i zhabs kyi drung du ni bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa snyed lon par gyur pa snyam byed de/ de
153b7: bzhin gshegs pa la la'i zhabs kyi drung du ni bskal pa 'dzam bu'i gling gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyad lon pa snyam byed pa nas/ bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul
153b8: shin du phra ba snyed lon pa snyam byed par gyur to/ / de nas drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyis/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs mthong ba dang / des yang bdag drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyi

154a1: mdun du 'dug par shes par gyur to/ / de la drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyis smras pa rigs kyi bu dran med// smras pa 'phags pa dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi byin gyi rlabs kyis dran do// blas
154a2: pa/ rigs kyi bu kho bos ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa gzhan gyis mi thub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'di shes par zad na/ byang chub sems dpa' 'gro ba thams cad las khyad par du 'phags
154a3: pa'i ye shes mngon par shes pa dang ldan pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob pa/ dus thams cad du 'khor lo bskor ba/ sangs rgyas kyi mtshan dang / ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa
154a4: byung ba'i nyi ma la rnam par dmigs pa'i rgyan rab tu thob pa/ dus gsum gyi yul skad gcig cig gi ye shes su yang dag par sdud pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du lus shin tu rnam par bkram pa
154a5: chos kyi dbyings thams cad la ye shes sdang ba'i rang bzhin dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa ji bzhin du mngon sum du mngon par langs pa/ sems can gyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du
154a6: spyod pas/ rnam par spyod pa dang 'thun pa'i tshul dang ldan pa 'dod pa bzhin du kun tu snang zhing dri ma med la 'od dang ldan pa'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa/ de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon
154a7: tan brjod pa'am/ smon lam gyi khyad par smras pa'am/ zhing gi mngon par 'du bya ba shes pa 'am/ ye shes kyi yul la 'jug par bya ba 'am/ ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gyi rjes su 'brang bar bya ba'am/
154a8: rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul pa la 'jug par bya ba 'am/ rnam par thar pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba 'am/ rnam par rtse ba'i rjes su 'brang bar bya ba 'am/ lus rnam par bye ba'i mtshan ma gzung bar bya

154b1: ba'am/ dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa brjod pa'am/ ye shes kyi snang ba rab tu stan par nus re skan// drang srong rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na yul yongs su tshol ba zhes bya ba yod de/ de
154b2: na bram ze rgyal po'i drod kyi skye mched ces bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba dris shig/ de nas
154b3: tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dga' rangs te/ mgu zhing nyams pade la tshim zhing yid bde ba skyes nas/ drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ drang srong 'jigs mchog
154b4: dbyangs la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ yang dang yang bltas te drang srong 'jigs mchog dbyangs kyi drung nas song ngo // sangs rgyas rmad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo'//
154b5: bam po bcu gnyis pa// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa gzhan gyis mi thub pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi ye shes kyis snang bar byas pa/
154b6: sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mngon sum du rnam par spyod pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mngon sum gyi ye shes kyis
154b7: mngon par shes pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i ye shes kyis sems snang bar gyur pa dus thams cad du yang dag par 'jug pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi snang ba rab tu 'thob
154b8: pa/ 'du shes kyi rnam pa thams cad la yang dag par 'jug pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi yul gyis snang bar gyur pa/ 'gro ba thams cad las khyad par du 'phags pa dang ldan pa'i ye shes snang ba thob pa/ thams cad

155a1: kyi rjes su song ba'i spyod yul la rnam par spyod pa mngon tu gyur pa/ gnyis su rnam par rtog pa med pas mnyam pa nyid du bstan pa'i ye shes lhur len pa/ dmigs pa thams cad la rab tu 'dral
155a2: ba'i ye shes snang ba dang ldan po/ mnyan pa thams cad la mngon du gyur ba'i bzod pa rnam par dag pa la mos pa'i mdzod la mkhas pa rang bzhin gyi chos la bzod pa khong du chud pa'i ye shes mngon par
155a3: shes pa dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rang bzhin bsgom pa dang mi 'bral ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shugs drag po las phyir mi ldog pa'i sems dang ldan pa/
155a4: stobs bcu'i ye shes snang ba'i 'od rab tu thob pa/ chos kyi dbyings brjod pa la mngon par mos pas/ ngoms pa med pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa/ nyid la rnam par spyod pa'i spyod
155a5: yul la 'jug pas/ khong du chud pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rgyun mtha' yas pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi dkyil
155a6: 'khor mtha' yas pa/ rnam par sbyangs pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi dra ba mi bzad pa/ khong du chud pa'i ye shes mtha' dang dbus med pa mngon du gyur pa'i sems dang ldan pa
155a7: sems can rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba la zhum pa med pa'i sems dang ldan pa des/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i yul mtha' yas pa la yang dag
155a8: par blta ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud rnam pa tha dad pa mtha' yas pa la yang dag par lta ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par phye ba sna tshogs mtha' yas pa la yang dag par blta ba

155b1: dang / 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas pa dmigs pa phra ba dang / yangs pa'i khongs su chud par bya ba la yang dag par blta ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi gzhi mtha' yas pa'i ming gi dra ba mchog
155b2: yang dag par blta ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams su rnam par spyad pa/ rnam par gdags pa mtha' yas pa'i kun rdzob rnam pa tha dad pa la yang dag par blta ba dang / sems can gyi mos pa sna tshogs
155b3: mtha' yas pa la yang dag par lta ba dang / sems can rnam par phye bo'i rnam pa tha dad pa/ mtha' yas pa la yang dag par blta ba dang / sems can mtha' yas pa la yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba
155b4: khong du chud par bya ba dang / yang dag par blta ba dang / sems can dang phyogs dang dus mtha' yas pa'i ming gi rnam pa sna tshogs la yang dag par blta ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen mngon du bya ba byed cing
155b5: mthar kyis yul tshol ba dang ldan pa gang na ba dang / bram ze rgyal ba'i drod kyi skye mched dag la bder phyin to// de'i tshe bram ze rgyal ba'i drod kyi skye mched thams cad bsgrub pa'i gzhir byas shing dka' thub drag po
155b6: la spyod do/ / de'i phyogs bzhi nas me'i phung po ri rab tsam du che ba bus pa dang / ri shin tu mtho pa'i sa'i lam gyi rgyud spu gri'i sos gshibs pas 'khor bar snang ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor
155b7: bzangs kyis/ bram ze'i rgyal ba'i drod kyi skye mched kyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ mdun du 'dug nas thal mo sbyar te/ 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa bdag gis bla na med pa yang
155b8: dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab pa dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba ma 'tshal te/ 'phags pa ni byang chub

156a1: sems dpa' rnams la gdams ngag dang / rjes su bstan pa mdzad do zhes bdag gis thos na/ 'phags pa ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang /
156a2: ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba bdag la bshad du gsol// des smras pa rigs kyi bu song la spu gri'i so dngar pa'i ri 'di la 'dzegs te/ me'i 'obs 'dir mchongs shig dang / des khyed kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod
156a3: pa yongs su dag par 'gyur ro zhes nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs 'di snyam du sems par gyur te/ mi khom pa brgyad las rnam par ldog pa yang shin tu dkon/ mir gyur te khom pa phun sum tshogs shing
156a4: rnam par dag pa yang shing rnam par dag pa yang shin tu dkon/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba yang shin tu dkon/ dbang po nyams pa med pa yang shin tu dkon/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thos pa yang shin tu dkon// skyes bu/
156a5: dam pa dang phrad pa yang shin tu dkon/ yang dag pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen yang shin tu dkon/ yang dag pa'i tshul rjes su bstan pas legs par sdud pa yang shin tu dkon/ yang dag par 'tsho bar bya ba yang
156a6: shin tu dkon/ mi'i 'jig rten na chos dang gnyer ba'i chos la nan tan byed pa yang shin tu dkon na/ de skad zer zhing bdag gi dge ba'i bar cad la zhugs pa de ltar bdag gi srog gcad par brtson pa 'di
156a7: bdud dam gcig ma yin nam/ bdud kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'am/ bdud kyi ris su gtogs pa 'am/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen ltar rdzus pa 'am/ byang chub sems dpa' la mi chags pa byed pa zhig
156a8: ma yin grang / / bdag gi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la bgegs byed par 'dod pa zhig ma yin gang / bdag la ma gol ba don par zhugs par 'dod pa zhig ma yin grang / bdag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos khong du

156b1: chud par bya ba'i chos kyi sgrol bgegs byed pa zhig ma yin grang / snyam nas/ de de ltar sems shing yid la byed pa'i tshe/ tshangs pa stong phrag bcu steng gi bar snang la gnas te/ 'di skad ces zer te/ rigs
156b2: kyi ba de lta bu'i sems mi brtan par ma byed cig/ rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di ni ting nge 'dzin rdo rje 'od 'gro ba'i snang ba rab tu thob pa ste/ brtson 'grus ldog pa med pa'o// brtsams pa chen
156b3: mtha' dang dbus med pa la zhugs pa'o/ / 'gro ba thams cad kyi sred pa'i rlan bskam pa la mngon par brtson pa'o// lte bu'i rnam pa dang dra ba thams cad gtub pa la brtson pa'o// nyon mongs pa'i
156b4: lcig lcig thams cad zad par bsreg pa la sta gon du gnas pa'o/ / mi khom mi shes pa 'bras mtha' dgon pa thams cad snang bar bya ba la brtson pa'o// sems can thams cad kyi rga shi 'ag yang
156b5: ma dang / 'jigs pa rnam par bzlog pa la yid dam brtan pa'o// dus gsum gyi mun pa bsngal pa la mngon par brtson pa'o// chos thams cad kyi 'od gzer bkye bzhugs pa'o// rigs kyi ba
156b6: 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ tshangs pa ji snyed cig mkhan po dang dbang sbyar ba dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyi gtso bor rang rang rlom zhing sems pa lta ba'i rnam pa sna
156b7: tshogs la mngon par zhen pa/ de dag thams cad 'phags pa 'di dka' thub dang / brtul zhugs kyi thugs dam gyi mthus rang rang gi gnas na bag dga' ba med cing de dag bsam gtan gyi ro dga' ba myong
156b8: ba med pas/ 'phags pa 'di'i drung du 'dod do// de dag byin pa dang / 'phags pa 'di'i rdzu 'phrul gyi sbyin pa dang / drag shul gyi dka' thub dang / brtul zhugs kyis zil gyis mnan te/ lta ba'i rnam pa

157a1: thams cad rnam par 'azlog pa dang / ngargyal dang rlom sems thams cad rab tu spang pa'i phyir chos ston to// 'gro ba thams cad la byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen pos bsam par bya ba dang / byang chub
157a2: kyi bsam pa brtan par bya ba dang / byang chub du sems bskyed pa shin tu yangs par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad yang dag par blta ba la mngon par brtson par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi dkyil
157a3: 'khor thob par bya ba yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / thams cad du grag pa'i sangs rgyas kyi dbyangs la thogs pa med cing bsgribs pa med par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// bdud stong phrag bcu'i yang steng gi
157a4: bar snang la 'khod nas lha rdzas kyi nor bu rin po ches mngon par gtor te/ 'di skad ces 'dzer to// rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas kyang so so'i gdung pa mdzad pa'i tshe/ 'od 'gro ba'i phung po
157a5: 'di las snang ba chen po byung zhing kho bo cig gi khyim dang / lus dang rgyan gyi longs spyod thams cad zil gyis gnon to// de'i phyir kho bos cag kyang so so'i gnas gnas na dga' ba med pas 'khor
157a6: dang bcas te 'phags pa 'di'i drung du 'dod do/ / kho bo cig 'di'i drung du phyin nas kyang 'phags pa 'di ni kho bo cig la ni ci nas rang rang gi sems so sor chud nas byang chub tu sems bskyed de/ bla na
157a7: med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ba de lta de ltar chos ston to/ / dbang sgyur gyi lha'i rgyal po stong phrag bcus kyang lha rdzas kyi me tog gis mngon par gtor to// 'a
157a8: skad ces 'dzer te/ rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lnga pa yongs su gdung bar byed pa'i tshe/ kho bo cig kyang rang rang gi gnas dag na dga' ba med do// de ltar bdag cag kyang rang rang gi sku

157b1: po'i 'khor dang bcas te 'di'i drung du 'dod do/ / bdag cag drung du phyin pa dang 'di ni bdag cag la rang rang gi sems la dbang sgyur ba 'thab par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// nyon mongs pa thams cad la dbang sgyur ba
157b2: thob par bya ba dang / bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du skye ba la dbang sgyur ba thob par bya ba dang / las kyi sgrib pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'i dbang rab tu thob par bya ba dang / snyoms par 'jug pa thams cad la dbang sgyur
157b3: ba thob par bya ba dang / yo byad la dbang ba'i rgyan yongs su dag par bya ba dang / bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du tshe la dbang sgyur ba thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// rab 'phrul dga'i lha'i rgyal po stong phrag bcu
157b4: yang steng gi bar snang la 'khod de/ lha rdzas kyi glu yang dag par sbyar ba'i nga ro snyan pa'i dbyangs bsgrags ste/ mchod pa byas nas 'di skad ces 'dzer to/ rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dga' thub lngas yongs su
157b5: gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ me'i phung po 'di las de dang 'dra ba'i 'od 'byung zhing des kho bos cig gi gizhal med khang 'di dag rnam par dag ste/ gsal ba dang 'od shin tu dang bar 'gyur ro// rgyan 'di dag dang lha'i
157b6: bu mo 'di dag kyang rnam par dag cing gsal la 'od shin tu dang bar 'gyur ro/ / de bas na bdag cag lha'i bu mo lha'i bu mo'i tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas par 'dod pa la dga' bar tshor ba med do// 'dod pa'i
157b7: bde ba la mngon par dga' ba med pas lus dang sems tshim par gyur nas/ 'phags pa 'di'i drung du 'dod pa yin te/ 'phags pa 'di ni bdag cag de ltar phyin pa rnams la sems cad rnam par dag par bya/
157b8: ba'i phyir chos ston to// sems can gyi 'od 'dod par bya ba dang / sems shin tu dag par bya ba dang / sems las su rung bar bya ba dang / sems kyi dga' ba yongs su bskyed pa dang / stobs bcu'i ye shes

158a1: thob pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / chos kyi shugs chen po rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku tshad med pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i phyir lus rnam par dag par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs
158a2: pa'i gsung thob par bya ba'i phyir rnam par dag par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid rab tu thob par bya ba'i sems/ rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// rab dga' ldan gyi lha'i rgyal po stong phrag
158a3: bcu lha'i bu dang / lha'i bu mo'i tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa dag kyang steng gi bar sdang la 'khod nas/ spos sna tshogs kyi phye ma'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab pas mchod pa byas te phyag 'tshal nas 'di
158a4: skad ces 'dzer to/ / rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dga' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ bdag cag kyang rang rang gi gnas na dga' ba med de/ de ltar dga' ba med pas 'di'i drung du 'dong ste/
158a5: bdag cag phyin pa rnams la 'phags pa 'di ni yul thams cad la ltos pa med par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// chog shes pa'i sems su bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par bskyed pa dang / byang chub tu
158a6: sems bskyed pa rab tu thob par bya ba nas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// rab mtshe ma'i lha'i rgyal po stong phrag bcu lha'i bu dang / lha'i bu mo'i tshogs
158a7: kyi 'khor dang bcas pa dag gis kyang lha rdzas kyi me tog ma na d+ha ra ba'i char mngon par phab ste/ 'di skad ces 'dzer to// rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/
158a8: bdag cag kyang lha rdzas kyi glu snyan pa la dga' ba med de/ de ltar dga' ba med pas/ 'phags pa 'di'i drung du 'dong ste// bdag cag phyin nas kyang 'phags pa 'di ni 'dod pa'i dga' ba thams cad rnam

158b1: par bzlog par bya ba nas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to/ / lha'i dbang po brgya byin stong phrag bcu so so nas nye ba'i dbang po sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang / lha'i bu dang lha'i bu
158b2: mo'i tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pas lha rdzas kyi gos dang / rin po che'i rgyan dang / me tog gi char mngon par bab ste/ 'di skad ces 'dzer to// rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba
158b3: mdzad pa'i tshe/ bdag cag kyang brgya byin gyi khang pa dang / bza' shing gi ra ba dang / rtse ba'i nags tshal dang / lha rdzas kyi rol mo brdung zhing dkrol ba dang / gam yon glu len pa'i longs spyod la dga' ba med de/ de
158b4: ltar bdag cag dga' ba med pas 'di'i drung du 'dong ngo / / bdag cag der phyin kyang 'phags pa 'di ni kho bo cag la 'dod pa'i dga' ba thams cad yongs su spang ba'i phyir chos ston to// 'di dag thams cad
158b5: rtag pa ma yin te/ mi brtan zhing 'jigs par 'gyur ba'i chos can no zhes bya ba'i tshig brjod do// dregs pa dang bag med pa thams cad yongs su gcad pa dang / bla na med pa'i byang chub tu spro ba bskyed pa'i
158b6: phyir chos ston to/ / rigs kyi bu gzhan yang 'dis bltas pa tsam gyis ri rab kyi rtse mo thams cad kyang g.yo bar 'gyur te/ des bdag cag gshegs pas sems skyo bar gyur nas/ thams cad mkhyen
158b7: pa'i sems brtan pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes su smon lam mngon par sgrub po// klu'i rgyal po shugs ldan dang / dga' bo dang bsnyen dga' bo la sogs pa/ klu brgya stong phrag bcu dag kyang
158b8: steng gi bar snang la gnas shing dus dang 'thun pa'i lha rdzas kyi can dan gyi sprin dang / klu'i bu mos klu blangs pa'i nga ro snyan pa'i dbyangs dang / lha rdzas kyi spos chu'i rgyun rab tu 'ab ba ba'i char mngon

159a1: par phab ste/ 'di skad ces 'dor to// rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba na dad pa'i tshe/ ma'i phung po chen po 'di las 'od chen po 'byung ste/ des kwa'i gnas pa tham
159a2: cad snang bar byas nas/ bye ma'i char dang / nam mkha' lding gi 'jigs pa yongs su sel to// khro ba 'byung ba yang zhi bar byas te/ lus sim par byas nas yid shin tu mos par byed do// de ltar sems shin tu
159a3: mos par gyur nas/ 'phags pa 'di ni bdag cag la chos ston te/ 'di ltar klu'i lam gyi rgyud don pa rnam par smad pa dang / sgrib pa'i las thams cad rab tu spang ba'i phyir nyes pa 'chags su bzung
159a4: cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed du bcud de thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la rab tu 'god do/ / gnod sbyin gyi dbang po stong phrag bcu yang nam mkha'i dbyings la 'khod //
159a5: mchod pa sna tshogs kyis bram ze'i rgyal ba'i drod kyi skye mched dang / tshed dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la mchod pa byas nas 'di skad ces 'dzer to// rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su
159a6: gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ kho bo cag gi 'khor kun kyang mi rnams la byams pa'i sems skye bar 'gyur te/ gnod sbyin dang srin po dang grul bum thams cad kyang byams pa'i sems dang ldan par 'gyur
159a7: ro/ / de dag byams pa'i sems dang ldan zhing 'che ba med pa la zhugs pa rnams kho bo cig gi drung du 'ong ngo // kho bo cig kyang de ltar byams pa'i dbang gis zil gyis gnod pas/ rang rang gi gnas de dang de
159a8: dag na dga' ba med de/ de ltar bdag cag kyang rang rang gi skye bo'i 'khor dang bcas te/ 'phags pa 'di'i drung du 'dod do// 'phags pa bdag cag de ltar 'ongs pa rnams la 'phags pa 'di'i sku las

159b1: masas thams ca snang ba byas gang / sa khyab pa yang dang / dashA ga nag sus da sams pa ga nas/ gas pazhanarnanas byu / gal
159b2: srin po dang grul bum dang / las srul po mang po byang chub tu sems skye bar 'gyur ba de ltar chos ston to// dri za'i dbang po stong phrag bcu dag kyang steng gi bar snang la 'khod nas 'di skad ces 'dzer to//
159b3: rigs kyi bu kho bo cig kyang rang rang gi gnas na 'khod pa'i tshe/ 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ me'i phung po 'di las 'od phyung ste/ bdag cag gi gnas snang bar gyur to//
159b4: de ltar bdag cag 'od des phog ste/ bde ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan par gyur pas/ 'phags pa 'di'i drung du 'dod ste/ bdag cag drung du phyin nas kyang 'phags pa 'di ni bdag cag ci nas kyang
159b5: bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir myi ldog par 'gyur ba de ltar chos ston to/ / lha ma yin gyi dbang po stong phrag bcu dag kyang rgya mtsho'i nang nas mngon par 'thon te/ nam mkha'
159b6: la bus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga btsugs te thal mo sbyar nas phyag 'tshal zhing 'di skad ces 'dzer to/ / rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ kho bo cig gi lham
159b7: yin 'jig rten tu mtsho dang ring bcas pa'i sachen po'i dkyil 'khor rab tu g.yo bar gyur te/ bdug cag kun gyi nga rgyal dang rlom sems dang / dregs pa thams cad brtul shugs dang / dkara' thub kyi zil
159b8: kyi non te/ 'phags pa 'di'i drung du 'dong ngo // der byin nas kyang 'phags pa 'di ni bdag cag la g.yo sgyu thams cad rab tu spang ba dang / chos zab mo'i bzod pa la gzung ba dang / mi g.yo ba'i chos nyid la

160a1: rab tu dgod pa dang / stobs bcu'i ye shes yongs su grub par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// nam mkha' lding gi dbang po shugs chen po 'dzin pa la stsogs pa nam mkha' lding gi dbang
160a2: stong phrag bcus kyang bram ze'i bu shin tu sdu gu'i gzugs su mngon par sprul te/ 'di skad ces mdzer to// rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ me'i
160a3: phung po 'di dag las 'od chen po byung ste/ bdag cag gi gnas snang bar byas nas/ yongs su g.yo bar byed do// des bdag cag kyang 'jigs shing skrag ste/ skye ba'i yid dang ldan par gyur nas 'phags pa 'das
160a4: drung du 'dong ngo / / 'phags pa 'di yang bdag cag la chos ston cing / byams pa chen po la yang dag par sbyar ba mdzad do// snying rje chen po la yang dag par dgod pa mdzad do// 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho
160a5: 'jug pa la yang yang dag par sbyor ba mdzad do/ / 'dod pa'i 'dam du bying ba'i sems can mngon par gdon par bya ba la'ang yongs su sbyor ba mdzad do// lhag pa'i bsam pa'i sgo rnam par dag par bya ba
160a6: la'ang rab tu sbyor ba mdzad do/ / shes rab dang thabs shin tu gsal ba la'ang yang dag par sbyor ba mdzad do// rnam pa ji lta bur yongs su smin par bya ba can rnams gdul bar bya ba'ang rab tu sbyor ba
160a7: mdzad do/ / mi 'am ci'i dbang po stong phrag bcu yang steng gi bar snang la 'khod de 'di skad ces 'dzer to// rigs kyi bu 'phags pa 'di dka' thub lngas yongs su gdung ba mdzad pa'i tshe/ kho bo cag gi
160a8: gnas na 'khod pa'i tshe/ ta la'i phreng ba las dril bu'i dra ba rin po che'i srang bus lnga ldir pa rgyus pa'i sil snyan dang / rol mo'i yo byad dang / rin po che'i rgyan dang / khyim gyi longs spyod thams cad las sangs

160b1: rgyas kyi sgra/ 'byung ngo // chos kyi sgra dang phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun gyi sgra dang / byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs pa'i smon lam gyi sgra 'byung ngo // 'jig rten gyi khams
160b2: kyi grangs su bya ba che ge mo zhig na ni byang chub sems dpa' ming dang 'di zhes bya ba zhig byang chub du smon lam 'debs so/ / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi grangs su bya ba zhig na ni byang chub sems dpa'i ming dang 'di
160b3: zhes bya ba zhig dka' ba yongs su gtong ba byed do/ / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi grangs su bya ba che ga mo zhig na ni byang chub sems dpa' ming dang 'di zhes bya ba zhig thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi ye shes

161a1: yang srid kyi de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi mtshan dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i phyang bar gang kho bo cag gi gnas

161b1: lha'i ris nyams su bde bar skyes so/ / de ltar bdag cag kyang 'phags pa 'dis mdzad pa la drin du gzo zhing mthong bas mi ngoms pas 'dod pa'i dga' ba thams cad yongs su spangs te/ 'phags

162a1: dpa'i ting nge 'dzin rab tu zhi ba'i bde ba mngon par shes pa zhes bya ba thob par gyur nas des 'di skad ces smras so/ / 'phags pa me'i phung po la de ltar reg na bde ba dang ri'i lam

162a3: ste/ rigs kyi bu kho bos na byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su mi zad pa 'di shes par zad na/ kho bos byang chub sems dpa' me'i phung po de lta bu 'gro ba

162b1: bya ba dris shig dang / de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis/ bram ze rgyal ba'i drod kyi skye mched kyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ bram ze'i rgyal ba'i drod kyi skye mched la lan

165b8: kyi rnam pa'i sgo dang / byang chub kyi sems 'byung ba'i rnam pa'i chos kyi sgo dang / byang chub kyi sems kyi tshogs kyi rnam pa'i sgo dang / smon lam gyi rnam pa'i sgo dang / spyod pa'i rnam pa'i sgo dang / mngon par shes

166a1: pa'i rnam pa'i sgo dang / 'byung ba'i rnam pa'i sgo dang / gzungs rnam par dag pa'i rnam pa'i sgo dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa'i rnam pa'i sgo dang / shes rab yongs su dag pa'i rnam pa'i sgo dang /

166a3: na/ kho mos byang chub sems dpa' sems nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa/ blo gros chos kyi dbyings ltar yangs pa/ d+hud bsod nams kyis tshogs kyis brtan pa/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam du zhugs pa/
166a4: 'jig rten gyi chos yongs su ma rgyu ba/ ye shes snang ba'i mig rab rib med pa rab tu thob pa/ chos kyi dbyangs thams cad mun pa med par khong du chud pa/ blo nam mkha' ltar tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ dmigs pa
166a5: thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i mig can/ chags pa med pa'i snang ba'i snying po dang ldan pa/ chos thams cad kyi don rab tu dbye ba la mkhas pa/ zil gyis gnon pa/ 'jig rten kun zil gyis gnon pa/ 'jig
166a6: rten gyi spyod pa'i tshul la rnam par spyod pa/ 'jig rten gyi lam gyi rlung thams cad kha na ma tho ba med pa/ 'jig rten gyi don byed pa la brtson pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi rten du gyur pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dgag tshul
166a7: dang rnam pa la mkhas pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du gnas pa'i bsam pa dang ldan pa/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs paston pa/ rus kyi 'khor lo thams cad la dbang sgyur ba de dag gi spyod pa shes pa'am/
166a8: yon tan brjod par nus re skar// drang srong rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na yul mig gsum pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de na dge slong ba lta na sdug pa zhes bya ba 'dug gis// de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub

166b1: sems dngas byang chubasams da' sdud pa la brlab par bya ba dang / ngagang na tan bya ba sa shig/ ngan pang dbar kyi bu nang bzangs kyis bu ma byams pa dang pa gas la skabs paga' ra la// bum byams pa dang
166b2: lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas yang dang yang bltas te/ bu mo byams ma'i drung nas song ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi rnam par spyod pa zab ma
166b3: rjes su bsam pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi zab mo khong du chud par bya ba la rjes su bsam pa dang / sems can gyi ye shes shin tu phra zhing zab pa rjes su bsam pa dang / 'jig rten gyi 'du shes kyi rnam pa zab mo
166b4: rjes su bsam pa dang / mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i dbyings zab mo rjes su bsam pa dang / sems kyi rgyun gyi dbyings zab mo rjes su bsam pa dang / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i dbyings zab mo rjes su bsam pa
166b5: dang / rang bzhin gyis dben pa'i dbyangs zab mo rjes su bas pa pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi rnam par dpyod pa'i dben pa'i dbyings zab mo rjes sra bas pa pa dang / chos kyi dbyings brdzun pa'i chan pa'i dbyings zab pa
166b6: rdzas su bsam pa dang / lus kyi 'khrul 'khor shugs kyis 'khor ba'i dbyings zab mo rjes su bsam pa dang / las kyis sna tshogs su gyur pa'i dbyings zab mo rjes su bsam pa byed cing mthar nas yul mig
166b7: gsum pa gang na ba der byin te/ yul gyi 'khor dang / grong khyer gyi 'khor dang / tshong dus kyi 'khor dang / zong rdal gyi 'khor dang / yul bu'i 'khor dang / lhas kyi 'khor dang / drang srong dge ba sbyong ba'i gnas kyilakho
166b8: dang / yul dang phyogs kyi 'khor dang / chu'i rgyud kyi 'khor dang / ri'i sul gyi 'khor dang / nags tshal chen po'i 'khor dag du dge slong blta na sdug pa yongs su tshol tshol ba las des dge slong blta na sdug pa nags

167a1: rgyal dug sha na/ gzhan 'ang dngal babapa/ gzugs mangs gang sdug la brtan yang dral ba/ sgra than tung gapas phyogs su 'byel ba dang ldan pa/ mig ga dgas par 'jug gagag du du
167a2: bo can/ bral ba yangs pa/ mig dkar nag 'byes shing ring la/ rdzim pa'i rje ma lte bur 'dug pa/ sA'i dbyibs legs shing bzang la/ ran par mdzes pa dang ldan pa/ mchu ma tshal ltar mdog bzang shing shin tu legs
167a3: pa dang ldan pa/ so mnyam zhing thogs bzang ba/ shin tu dkar ba bzhi bcu chang ba dang ldan pa/ 'gram pa'i lhang seng ge ltar 'dug pa/ mkhur ba shes gang zhing rgyas pa/ spen tshugs ga'u lang 'dug cing reng la/ shin tu
167a4: mdzes pa/ mdzad bu zla ba'i kha dog ltar 'dug pa'i thig le can/ rna shal ring zhing lhod par 'phyang ba/ zla ba nya ba ltar bzhin mdangs dang ldan zhing shin tu bzang pa/ mgul zlum zhing dung ltar mdzes pa/ snying ka
167a5: dpal gyi be'us brgyan pa/ ro stong seng ge'i stong ltar 'dug pa/ thal gong shin tu rgyas pa/ dpung mgo'i ldan legs shing zlum pa/ lag pa ring pa/ dra bas 'brel ba'i sor mo can/ galag 'khor los pa rgyan pa/
167a6: rka lag 'jam zhing gzhon la sha rgyas pa/ mdun shin tu mtho ba/ rked pa rdo rje ltar 'dug pa/ lus che zhing drang ba/ brla zlum pa/ pho mtshan gsang ba'i sbubs su 'dug pa/ byin pa ri dgas a ne ya'i byin pa ltar 'dug
167a7: pa/ sor mo ring pa/ rkang pi'i gting ba yangs pa/ 'od 'dom gang ba dang ldan pa/ mdog gser gyi kha dog ltar 'dug pa/ ba s+phu re re nas g.yas phyogs su gyen du 'khyil pa/ shing n+ya gro dA'i rgyal po ltar chu zhe dgab
167a8: pa/ lus mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos shin tu brgyan pa/ mig me 'gebs shing mi rgod pa/ dran pa nye bar gnas pa/ de'i rgyal po kha ba can lta d+ha dang / nags tshal dang / sman dang shing phran sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa/

167b1: blo shin tu yangs pa/ ye shes kyi spyod yul dang / yul la thub pa med pa/ dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyad sprin gyi sgra lta bu dang ldan pa/ g.yo ba dang rlom sems dang / g.yeng ba dang spros pa thams cad dang bral ba'i
167b2: sems dang ldan pa/ ye shes kyi spyod yul ma 'dres pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yul rgya chen po'i snang ba thob pa/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i bsam pa'i rgyun mi 'chad pa/ snying rje
167b3: chen po'i dkyil 'khor shin tu yangs pa skyes pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i thams cad kyi chos kyi tshul yongs su gzung ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi ye shes snang ba bskyed pa'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
167b4: tshul rjes su ngan zhing 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du 'chag pa la zhugs te/ drag dal med cing bad ral med la shin tu mdzes par 'chag pa/ gnas gtsang ma'i lha'i gos dang ldan pa/ lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang /
167b5: lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / me 'am ci dang / lce 'phye chen po dang / brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pas bskor cing 'dug pa mthong ngo // dge slong bltan mdzes
167b6: ba de 'chag sa'i tshe/ phyogs mngon du gyur pa'i phyogs kyi lha rnams/ phyogs kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su sgrub pa byed do// rkang gis 'gro ba'i lha rnams rin po che'i pad mos gom pa 'dor ba'i tshe/ yongs su blang ba byed do//
167b7: me'i lha snang ba'i dkyil 'khor zad mi shes pa rnams kyang / mun pa dang rab rib rnam par sel to// 'dzam bu rgyal mtshan gyi nags tshal gyi lha rnams kyang me tog mang po'i char mngon par babebs so// sa'i lha mi g.yo
167b8: ba'i snying po can rnams kyang rin po che'i 'byung gnas mang po ston to/ / nam mkha'i lha kun nas snang ba'i dpal dang ldan pa/ rnams kyang nam mkha'i dbyings yongs su brgyan pa byed do// mtshe'i lha dpal kun nas 'byung

168a1: ba rnams kyang rin po che dam pa mang pos mngon par 'thor te/ / ri rab kyi lha dri ma med pa'i snying po can rnams kyang thal mo sbyar cing phyag 'tshal lo// rlung gi lha thogs pa med pa'i stobs can rnams kyang /
168a2: spos dang bdug spos dang / me tog 'thor ba'i rlung rab tu 'gyid do// mtshan mo'i lha gnas par byed pa lus shin tu rgyan pa rnams kyang lus shin tu btud cing phyag 'tshal lo// nyin mo'i la rtag tu bsad par
168a3: byed pa'i dkyil 'khor can rnams kyang nor bu rin po che phyogs snang bar byed pa'i rgyal mtshan thogs shing / snang ba bskyed pa'i phyir nam mkha'i dbyings la 'khod do// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs/
168a4: dge slong blta na sdug pa gang na ba der phyin nas/ dge slong blta na sdug pa'i rkang pa'i bol gnyis la spyi bos btugs te phyag 'tshal nas/ dge slong blta na sdug pa'i rkang pa'i bol gnyis la bzhin sbyar te/
168a5: legs par byis nas mdun du 'dug ste/ thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa bdag ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod
168a6: pa yongs su tshol ba zhig lags te/ 'phags pa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams la gdams ngag dang / rjes su ston pa mdzad do zhes bdag gis thos na/ 'phags pa ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems
168a7: dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba bdag la bshad du gsol// des smras pa/ rigs kyi bu kho bo ni tshes btab na dar la bab pa rab tu byung bas btab na gsar du zhugs pa ste/ rigs
168a8: kyi bu kho bos ni tshe de 'dra ba gcig gis de bzhin gshegs pa gang 'ga' klung sum bcu rtsa brgyad kyi drung du tshangs pa'i spyod pa spyad de/ bdag gis de bzhin gshegs pa la la'i zham ring du ni nyin zhag gcig du tshangs pa'i

168b1: spyod pa spyad do/ / la lar na nyin zhag bdun du/ la lar na zla ba byed du/ la lar ni zla ba gcag du/ la la na lo gcig du/ la lar ni lo brkyang / la la na la stong du/ la la ngan la brgya phrag stong du/ la lar na
168b2: lo bya bar/ la lar ni lo bya ba khrag khrig du/ la lar ni lo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par/ la lar ni lo bskal pa bar ma// la lar ni bskal pa byed du/ la lar ni bskal par/ bdag gis de
168b3: bzhin gshegs pa la la'i nam ring du ni/ bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i tshangs pa'i spyod pa spyad de/ bskal pa bgrang ba'i tshul 'di nyid kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad las chos
168b4: bstan pa thos te/ gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa yang dag par blangs so// smon lam gyi rgyan yongs su sbyangs so// yang dag par bsgrub pa'i yul la zhugs so// spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyangs
168b5: so/ / pha rol tu phyin pa brgya mtshor yongs su rdzogs par byas so// mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa yongs su shes par byas so// de dag gis chos kyi 'khor lo 'khor ba phan tshun ma 'dres
168b6: pa dag kyang yongs su bzung ngo / / de dag gi spobs pa mnyam pa nyid kyang khong du chud par byas so// de dag gi bstan pa yang dam pa'i chos zad pa'i mthar thug gi bar du yongs su bzung ngo // kho bos de bzhin gshegs
168b7: p a de dag thams cad kyi sngon gyi smon lam rnams kyang smon lam gyi dkyil 'khor gyi ting nge 'dzin mngon par bsgrub pa'i stobs kyis rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir mngon par bsgrubs
168b8: so/ / kho bos de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyi sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rnams kyang spyod pa thams cad la 'jug pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob pa'i stobs kyis rang gi spyod pa yongs su dag par bya ba'i

169a1: phyir mngon par bsgrubs so/ / kha bos de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyi pha rol du phyin pa rnam par dag pa yang kun tu bzang po'i 'byung po'i stobs kyis mngon par bsgrubs so// gzhan yang rigs
169a2: kyi bu la po 'chags 'di na 'chag pa'i cha/ phyogs kyi rgyud kyi tha thams cad kyang shin tu rnam par la bi'i ye shes kyi sgos mngon du 'gyur ro// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rlung sde thams cad kyang sman lam chen po mdzan
169a3: par bsgrubs pa'i stobs kyis sems bskyed pa gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa 'da' zhing yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir rnam par 'grub par 'gyur ro/ / sems kyi skad cig gcig la sems can gyi
169a4: spyod pa'i tshul gyi sgo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag kyang byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang / smon lam mngon par bsgrubs pa'i stobs kyis stobs bcu'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs

169a6: par bsgrubs pa'i stobs kyis/ / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur ba dang / rim gror bya ba'i phyir mngon du 'gyur
169a7: ro/ / sems bskyed pa gcig la de bzhin gshegs pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i chos kyi sprin gyi char rnams kyang chos kyi 'khor lo yongs su 'dzin pa'i gzungs dang / smon lam mngon par bslabs pa'i
169a8: stobs kyis/ chos kyi tshul grangs med pa mngon par 'tshang rgya zhing khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir bsam pa la mngon par 'bad do// sems bskyed pa gcig la byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho brjod du med

169b1: p a'i yang brjod du med pa dag kyang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mig 'phrul lta bur yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i smon lam mngon par bsgrubs pa'i stobs kyis spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor thams cad yongs su dag par bya
169b2: ba'i phyir mngon du 'gyur ro/ / sems bskyed pa gcig la ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho brjod na med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag kyang ting de 'dzin gyi sgo gcig du ting 'dzin cig thams cad yang dag par 'dubyan
169b3: smon lam pa sbubs pa'i stobs kyis ting nge 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir mngon du 'gyur ro/ / sems bskyed pa gcig la dbang po rgya mtsha brjod du med pa'i yang ba
169b4: dra med pa dag kyang dran pa'i mthar phyin pa'i dbang po thob par bya ba'i smon lam mngon par bsgrubs pa'i stobs kyis dbang po'i 'khor lo dang / dus kyi 'khor lo thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang bar bya ba'i phyir mngon du
169b5: 'gyur ro/ / sems bskyed pa gcig la rus kyi 'khor lo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag kyang sems can zad mi shes pa zad par bya ba'i smon lam mngon par bsgrubs pa'i stobs kyis dus thams
169b6: cad du chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba'i phyir mngon du 'gyur ro/ / sems bskyed pa gcig la dus rgya mtsho brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa thams cad kyang dus gcig tu rnam par dgod pa'i tshul khong
169b7: du chud par ye shes snang ba'i smon lam mngon par bsgrubs pa'i stobs kyis/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi dus gsum rnam par dgod pa'i phyir mngon sum du gyur te/ rigs kyi bu kho bos ni
169b8: byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa shin tu zhi bar mi 'gyur ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba 'di shes par zad na/ kho bos byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa rdo rje lta bu dang ldan pa de bzhin gshegs pa

170a1: thams cad kyi rigs su rigs dang ldan par 'byung ba/ srog gi dbang po la rkun chad pa med pa/ ye shes kyi smon mazhi bar 'gyur ba med pa/ mi shigs pa mi byed pa'i lus dang ldan pa/ sgyu ma'i rnam pa
170a2: lta bu'i gzugs shin tu grub pa/ chu'i chos dang mnyam pa'i yan lag dang / nying lag du ldan pa'i lus can 'gro ba rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs par byed pa'i lus dang ldan pa
170a3: 'gro ba thams cad dang 'dra ba'i gzugs dang lus dang kha dog dang / dbyibs dang chu zheng yongs su ston pa/ me mdag dang me lce dang / dug dang mtshon gyis mi tshugs pa'i lus dang ldan pa'i/ rdo rje ltar sra
170a4: zhing 'khor yug ltar thug pa med pa'i lus can/ bdud dang pas kyis rgol ba thams cad kyi stobs kyi stobs med par byed pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi ri dang / 'dra bar 'gro ba kun las mngon par

170a6: cad kyi sprin gyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa/ phyogs kun tu rnam par snang ba/ sgrib pa'i ri thams cad rnam par gtor bas blta na mdzes pa mi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad shin tu 'jom pas shin tu dpa' bar snang
170a7: ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya chen po'i rgyu 'thun pa las byung bas bltan dga' ba 'byung bar shin tu dka' zhing kon pas me tog u dum 'bar ba lta bu de dag gi spyod pa shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan/

170b1: byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par gnon pa dang / nan tan rnam par dag
170b2: par bya ba la brtson pa/ byang chub sems dpa' stobs snang bas sems shin tu snang bar gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i brtan pa gzhan gyis mi thub cing brgal thag chad pa'i snying dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems
170b3: dpa'i smon lam gyi go cha bzang ngos sems zhum pa med pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa brtan pas kun tu gnas shing yongs su 'phel bar 'gyur ba la brtson pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyor pa'i sprin gyi
170b4: char yongs su 'dzin pa'i bsam pa dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi sprin gyi char gyis yongs su ngoms pa'i rgyun dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa' yon tan thams cad la 'jug pa'i smon

170b7: blta na sdug pa la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas yang dang yang bltas te/ dge slong blta na sdug pa'i drung nas song ngo //
170b8: sangs rgyas mad gcad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// bam po bcu gsum pa// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dge slong blta na sdug pa'i gdams ngag rjes su bzlog cing spel ba dang /

171a1: ud padang btud pab dang / bshad pa dang / mas rnam par than pa pa dang / med pa dang / yang dag par bstan pa dang / rnas sra bsas pa dang / yang na par 'jug par bya ba dang / bgrang bdang

177a1: dang / dri sna tshogs kyis tshim par byed de/ rigs kyi bu de ltar kho mo ni phru ba gcig po 'di las ci dga' ba'i kha zas kyis sems can brgya'ang yongs su tshim par byed do// sems can stong dang sems
177a2: can brgya phrag stong dang / sems can bye ba dang / sems can bye ba phrag brgya dang / sems can bye ba phrag stong dang / sems can bye ba brgya phrag stong dang / sems can bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong nas/
177a3: sems can brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa mos pa sna tshogs can rnams kyang ci la dga' ba'i kha zas kyis yongs su tshim par byed do// yongs su stobs par byed do// yongs su dga' bar byed do//
177a4: yongs su mgu bar byed do// yongs su spro bar byed do// shin tu tshim par byed do// yid bde bar byed do// 'on kyang 'phru ba 'di las 'god par 'gyur ro// 'grib pa med de dma' bar mi 'gyur ro// zad par mi
177a5: 'gyur ro/ / 'bri bar mi 'gyur ro// sa mtshams med par mi 'gyur ro// mthar thug par mi 'gyur ro// mung thug par mi 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu gzhung de dang 'dra bar sems can 'jam bu'i gling gi rdul shin tu pra
177a6: bsnyed dang / de bzhin du gling bzhi pa'i 'dog rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin sa za ba snyed dang / song gi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra bsnyed dang / stong gnyis kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu pra

177a8: rdul shin tu phra ba snyed cig 'ongs kyang / ci la dga' ba'i kha zas tshod ma sna tshogs dang / ro sna tshogs dang / kha dog sna tshogs dang / dri sna tshogs kyis yongs su tshim par byed do// yongs su dga' bar byed

177b8: kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gcig na ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams brgya dang / 'jig rten gyi khams stong dang / 'jig rten gyi khams brgya phrag stong dang / 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba dang / 'jig rten

178a1: gyi khams bye ba phrag brgya dang / 'jig tan gyi khams bye ba phrag stong dang / 'jig rten gyi khams brgya phrag song dang / 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong dang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'jam
178a2: bu'i gling gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / stong gi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang / stong gnyis kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul
178a3: shin tu phra ba snyed dang / song gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed nas/ de bzhin du shar phyogs kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra
178a4: bsnyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas sku'i tha ma 'dzin pa ji snyed cig bzhugs pa de dag thams cad kyang kho mo'i kha zas las gsol cing nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi 'bras bu
178a5: bsnyes par mdzad do/ / shar phyogs na bzhugs pa ji lba ba de bzhin du lce phyogs dang / nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang / byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs

178b2: 'ang rten gyi khams 'jam bu'i gling gi rdul gin thab snyed dang / gleng bzhi pa 'jig rten gyi khams kyang la shin tu za ba snyed dang / stong gi 'ag rten gyi khams kyi rdul gan zab rnyed dang / song
178b3: 'dig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu pa pa snyed dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu za ba spyad nas/ gang phyogs kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du zad pa' yang brjod pa

178b6: phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang / byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams dang / nub byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og ga phyogs dang / steng gi phyogs kyi
178b7: 'jig rten gyi khams gcig na/ byang chub sems dpa'i sku tshe gcig gis thogs pa ji snyed cig bzhugs pa de dag thams cad kyang kho mo'i kha zas las gsol cing snying po byang chub tu bzhugs te/ bdud rjedang
178b8: bcas pa rab tu pham par mdzad nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gcig na bzhugs pa ji lta ba de bzhin

179a1: du 'jig rten gyi khams brgya dang / 'jig rten gyi khams stong dang / 'jig rten gyi khams brgya phrag stong dang / 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba brgya dang / 'jig rten gyi khams

179a7: bu bud med 'di dag las sogs pa brgya stong grangs med pa phrag bcu kho mo dang bskal pa mnyam par spyod pa/ smon lam gcig pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba gcig pa/ 'byung ba'i rgyan cig pa/ mos pa'i lam rnam par dag

180a1: par spyod pa/ rnam par dag pa sha sta gcig kyang yod de/ rigs kyi bu zung med stong phrag bcu po 'di dag kyang skad cig gcig du 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sku tshe gcig gis thogs pa rnams
180a2: zhal zas yongs su dbul ba'i phyir phyogs bcu rgyas par 'dong ngo / / phru ba 'di nyid nas kha zas blangs shing / srid pa tha ma dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa rnams la bsod snyoms dbul ba'i rtsa
180a3: phyogs can rgyas par 'dod do/ / phru ba 'di nyid nas kha zas blangs shing phyogs bcu rgyas par bkang ste/ yi dgas kyi tshogs thams cad kha zas kyis yongs su tshim par byed do// rigs kyi bu de ltar kho mo grub
180a4: 'di nyid nas lha rnams ni lha'i kha zas kyis yongs su tsham par byed do/ / klu rnams ni klu'i kha zas kyis/ gnod sbyin rnams ni gnod sbyin gyi kha zas kyis/ dri za rnams ni dri za'i kha zas kyis/ lha ma yin rnams

180a6: mi'i kha zas kyis/ mi ma yin pa rnams ni mi ma yin pa'i kha zas kyis yongs su tshim par byed do// rigs kyi bu yud tsam zhig sdong dang de'i re mngon du 'gyur ro// dge bsnyen ma phul du byung ba des tshig de brjod/

180b1: te/ de lar 'ongs pa dedag dge bsnyen ma bral du byung bas/ stan de dag la bkod de/ so so nas ci la dga' ba'i kha zas tshad ma sna tshogs dang / ro sna tshogs dang / kha dogs chags dang / dri ska tshogs dang ldan
180b2: par yongs su tshim par byas so/ / yongs su bltabs par byas so// yongs su dga' ba byas so// yongs su mgu bar byas so// yongs su spro bar byas so// shin tu tshim par byas so// yid bde bar byas
