180b6: ni lha'i kha zas kyis yongs su tshim par byas so/ / klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto'i phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa rnams kyang mi ma yin/
180b7: pa'i kha zas kyis yongs su tshim par byas nas/ yid bde bar 'gyur bi'i bar drabyas so// 'on kyang phub de las 'god par 'gyur ba med/ 'gribs pa med/ dma' ba med/ zad par gyur pa meng/ sa mtshams
180b8: su gyur pa med/ mthar thug pa med/ mur thug pa med do// de nas dge bsnyen ma phul du byung ba des/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu kho mos ni byang chub sems dpa'i//

181a1: rnam par thar pa bsod nams kyi mdzod mi zad pa'i rgyan ces bya ba 'di shes par zad na/ byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams chen po'i rgya mtsho me zad pa'i bsod nams dang ldan pa/ bsod nams kyi tshogs
181a2: rgya chen po shin tu brtsegs pa/ nam mkha' lta bur gyur pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi smon lam yongs su rdzogs par byed pas/ nor bu rin po che yid bzhin gyi rgyal po lta bu/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsab
181a3: yongs su bsrung bas/ bsod nams chen po'i 'khor yug dang ldan pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du rin po che'i snyim pa nas char ltar 'thor ba bsod nams chen po'i sprin du gyur pa/ chos kyi grong khyer gyi sgo 'byed
181a4: pas/ bsod nams chen po'i mdzod la mngon sum lta ba/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi phongs pa'i mun pa sel bas bsod nams chen po'i sgron mar gyur pa/ chos kyi grong khyer shes pa 'am/ yon tan brjod par nus
181a5: reskan/ drang srong rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na grong khyer 'byung ba chen po zhes bya ba yod de/ de na khyim bdag mkhas pa zhes bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub
181a6: sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba dris shig/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dge bsnyen ma phul du byung ba'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ dge bsnyen ma
181a7: phul du byung ba la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ yang dang yang bltas te/ dge bsnyen ma phul du byung ba'i drung nas blta bas mi doms bzhin du song ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu
181a8: nor bzangs bsod nams kyi mdzod mi zad pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i rnam par thar pa'i snang ba rab tu thob pa de bsod nams rgya mtsho de la ni rjes su sems/ bsod nams nam mkha' de la ni kun tulta/

181b1: bsod nams kyi drang por ni yongs su 'dzin// bsod nams kyi ri bo lan mngon par 'dzeg/ bsod nams kyi tshogs de ni yang dag par sdud / bsod nams kyi chu bo de la ni 'bog/ bsod nams kyi tshogs kyi
181b2: mu stegs de las rab tu 'bab/ / bsod nams kyi dkyil 'khor de ni yongs su skyong// bsod nams kyi gter de la ni yang dag par lta/ bsod nams kyi tshul de ni rjes su dran par byed/ bsod nams kyi
181b3: tshogs de ni yongs su 'dzin/ bsod nams kyi rgyud de ni yongs su spyod pa byed cing / mthar kyis grong khyer 'byung ba chen po gangadan pa der phyin nas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'dod cing dge ba'i bshes gnyen la
181b4: blta bas bsgom pa'i sems kyi rgyud dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen kyis byin gyis brlab pa'i bsam pa can/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen la thogs pa med par spor ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la ri ma gror
181b5: bya bas skyo ba med pa'i brtson 'grus dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la rag lus pa dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis nges par gyur par bsod nams kyi tshogs thams cad dang / dge
181b6: ba'i bshes gnyen gyis rnam par spel ba'i thabs mkhas pa'i spyod pa dang / gzhan gyi drid mi 'jog par dge ba'i bshes gnyen rim gror bya ba la mkhas pa dang / rnam par 'phel ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams
181b7: cad dang / rnam par dag par 'gyur ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa dang / yang dag par 'phel ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i dbang po dang / yongs su smin par 'gyur ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba
181b8: thams cad dang / yang dag par 'phel ba'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub pa dang / shin tu yangs par gyur pa'i snying rje chen pos bdag nyid thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du nye bar gyur par yang dag par

182a1: mthong nas/ sangs rgyas thams cad las byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pas chos kyi snang ba yang dag par zad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu snang ba rnam par 'phel bar byed
182a2: cing khyim bdag mkhas pa yongs su tshel tshol ba las/ grong khyer gyi dbus lam gyi bzhi mdo zhig na rin po che sna bdun gyi stegs bu zhig la/ rin po che grangs med pa las byas pa'i khri nor bu rin po che'i rkang pa
182a3: rdo rje dang / in dri ni la sna tshogs kyis spras pa bkye ba/ gser gyi lcag pod kyi dra bas legs par blas pa/ nor bu rin po che dri ma med pa'i snying po can rin po che lnga brgya tsam gyis gzugs legs par brgyan pa
182a4: lha rdzas kyi stan sna tshogs bting pa/ ba gam yo nas lha rdzas kyi gos kyi rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan mang po bgreng ba/ rin po che du ma'i dra bas kun nas g.yog pa rin po che'i bla re chen po bres pa/ bla nas gser dang
182a5: rin po che'i me tog gi lda ldi mang po bkye ba zhig la 'dug cing / 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi gdugs yu ba med pa'i bai dur+ya las byas pa ni drung nas bsgreng bzhing bzung / g.yab rnga dri ma med pa'i rdul yab dang /
182a6: po'i rgyal po lta bus ni legs par g.yo ba/ spos kyi rim gro'i yo byad sna tshogs kyis ni gdugs shing bsangs/ rol mo brdud pa dang / dkrol ba lha rdzas kyi dbyangs las 'das par sgra 'byin pa lnga brgya tsam
182a7: gyis ni g.yags phyogs nas brdungs shing dkrol/ grong khyer 'byung ba chen po na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams shin tu dga' bar bya ba'i don du lha rdzas kyi me tog gi sprin gyi char ni kun nas 'bab par gyur pa/ g.yog/
182a8: sog chags stong phrag bcu tsam sngon dge ba'i rtsa ba bskal pa mnyam par spyod spyod pa/ dag nyan cing dga' bar byed pa/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rgyan gyis shin tu brgyan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa

182b1: yongs su grub pa/ lha dang mi'i gzugs las shin tu 'das pa sha stag gis kun nas bskor cing 'dug pa mthong nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs khyim bdag mkhas pa gang na ba der song ste/ byin nas khyim bdag mkhas
182b2: nga'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ khyim bdag mkhas pa la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas mdun du 'dug ste/ thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa bdag ni 'di
182b3: lta ste/ sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal zhi bar bgyi ba dang / sems can thams cad shin tu bde ba la 'god pa dang / sems can thams cad 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho nas mngon par gdon pa dang / sems
182b4: can thams cad chos rin po che'i gling du yang dag par bskal ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi sred pa'i brlan shin tu bskam pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi snying rje'i brlan yang dag par bskyed pa dang /
182b5: sems can thams cad kyi 'dod pa'i dga' ba dang / sred pa rnam par zlog pa dang / sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la mos shing bsgrub par bgyi ba dang / sems can thams cad 'khor ba'i
182b6: pas mtha' dgon pa las yang dag par bzla ba dang / sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang chos la dga' zhing mos pa yang dag par bskyed pa dang / sems can thams cad khams gsum gyi
182b7: grong rdal nas gdon pa dang / sems can thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa'i pho brang du gzung ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi don du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu zhugs kyis kyang /
182b8: ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba ma 'tshal te/ 'phags pa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams la gdams ngag dang / rjes

183a1: sra bstan pa mdzad do zhes bdag gis thos na/ 'phags pa ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems
183a2: can thams cad kyi rten du 'gyur ba bdag la bshad du gsol/ / de skad ces smras pa dang / khyim bdag mkhas pas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu de ltar khyod kyis bla
183a3: na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa legs so legs so/ / rigs kyi bu sems can gang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed cing / byang chub sems
183a4: dpa'i spyod pa yongs su tshol ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen blta bas mi ngoms pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi drung du mi 'gro bas mi ngoms pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la rim gro bya bas sgyid lug
183a5: pa med pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen btsal bas yid mi bde ba mi skyed pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen btsal ba las phyir mi ldog pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la mos shing dang ba'i yid las rnam par mi
183a6: ldog pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi dor blta ba las phyir mi zlogs pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi gdams ngag gi tshul la zhum pa med pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la rim gro dang bsnyen bkur bya bas
183a7: mi skyo ba de lta bu ni shin tu dkon no/ / rigs kyi bu khyod kyis kho ba'i 'khor 'di dag mthong ngam// smras pa 'phags pa mthong ngo // smras pa rigs kyi bu 'di dag kun kyang kho bos bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
183a8: byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dag ste/ / 'di dag kho bos de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su bskyed pa'o// 'di dag ni kho bos pha rol tu phyin pas bsdus te gsos pa'o// 'di dag ni kho bos chos dkar po

183b1: thams cad kyis bskyed pa'o/ / 'di dag ni kho bos de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la rnam par bskyed pa'o// 'di dag ni kho bos 'jig rten gyi rigs las gyen du bskyod pa'o// 'di dag ni kho bos de bzhin gshegs pa'i
183b2: rigs la bkod pa'o/ / 'di dag ni kho bos 'jig rten gyi lam gyi 'khor lo las bzlog pa'o// 'di dag ni kho bos chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba la btsud pa'o// 'di dag ni kho bos ngan song gsum gyi rgyung du ltung bas
183b3: yongs su bzung ba'o/ / 'di dag ni kho bos chos nyid khong du chud par bya ba la bskor ba ste/ rigs kyi bu de ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems can thams cad kyi skyabs su gyur pa yin no// rigs kyi bu lo
183b4: bos ni yid kyi mdzod nas byung ba'i bsod nams mang po thob pa ste/ de'i mthus kho bo ni zas 'dod pa rnams la zas kyi sbyin pa byed de/ btung ba 'dod pa rnams la btung ba dang / ro'i dam pa 'dod pa rnams la rol
183b5: dam pa dang / bza' ba 'dod pa rnams la bza' ba dang / bca' ba 'dod pa rnams la bca' ba dang / bldag pa 'dod pa rnams la bldag pa dang / mur ba 'dod pa rnams la mur ba dang / gos 'dod pa rnams la gos
183b6: dang / me tog 'dod pa rnams la me tog dang / phreng ba 'dod pa rnams la phreng ba dang / spos 'dod pa rnams la spos dang / bdug pa 'dod pa rnams la bdug pa dang / byug pa 'dod pa rnams la byug pa dang / bye ma 'dod
183b7: pa rnams la bye ma dang / rgyan dang lhab lbub 'dod pa rnams la rgyan dang lha ba lbub dang / rin po che 'dod pa rnams la rin po che dang / gser 'dod pa rnams la gser dang / dngul 'dod pa rnams la dngul dang /
183b8: tig 'dod pa rnams la mu tig dang / rten 'dod pa rnams la rten dang / stan 'dod pa rnams la stan dang / mal cha 'dod pa rnams la mal cha dang / na ba'i gsos sman dang / yo byad 'dod pa rnams lan pa'i

184a1: gsos sran dang yo byad dang / bzhon pa 'dod pa rnams la bzhon pa dang / dga' ba 'dod pa rnams la dga' ba dang / glang po dang rta dang / shing ha dang / ba lang dang / bong bu dang ma he dang / ra lug 'dod pa
184a2: rnams la glang po dang / rka dang shing rta dang ba lang dang / bong bu dang ma he dang / ra lug dang / rgyal mtshan dang / gdugs dang / ba dan 'dod pa rnams la rgyal mtshan dang / gdugs dang bdan dang / zan po dang bran
184a3: mo 'dod pa rnams la bran po dang bran mo dang 'khor gyi byis pa 'dod pa rnams la 'khor gyi byis pa dang / bud med 'dod pa rnams la bud med dang / bu mo gno nu 'dod pa rnams la bu mo gnonu dang / cod pan dang /
184a4: gtsug gi rin po che 'dod pa rnams la cod pan dang gtsug gi rin po che dang / thor dpag dang bcas pa'i gtsug gi rin po che 'dod pa rnams lathor dpag dang bcas pa'i gtsug gi rin po che dang / sgra mthon ting dri ma
184a5: med pa'i dkyil 'khor 'dod pa rnams la/ skra mthon ting dri ma med pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi sbyin pa byed pa nas/ yo byad sna tshog sa thams cad 'dod pa rnams la yang yo byad sna tshogs thams cad kyi sbyin pa
184a6: byed do/ / rigs kyi bu yud tsam zhig sdod dang / 'u re mngon sum du mthong bar 'gyur ro// de skad ces khyim bdag mkhas pagam/ tshig de brjod ma thag du de'i mod la sems can grangs med bzhis
184a7: khyim bdag mkhas pa 'di sngon gyi smon lam gyis bos pa'am/ phyogs tha dad pa dang / yul tha dad pa dang / gnas tha dad pa dang / grong dang / grong khyer tha dad pa dang / grong rdal tha dad pa dang / tshong 'dus
184a8: tha dad pa dang / ljongs tha dad pa dang / 'or gyi grong tha dad pa dang / khyim tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi rgyud tha dad pa dang / sems can gyi rigs tha dad pa dang / sems can rnam pa mi 'thun pa tha dad pa dang /

184b1: lam gyi rgyud tha dad pa dang / gnas kyi rnam pa dang / ming du bya ba tha dad pa nas/ sems can skye mched rnam par dag pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ kha zas sna tshogs don du gnyer ba kha zas sna tshogs 'dod pa/ bsam pa tha dang
184b2: pa bza' ba dang btung ba dang / gtsang ma 'dod pa dang / sha 'dod pa dang / kha zas rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs don du gnyer ba/ lam gyi rgyud rnam pa sna tshogs kyi khyad par du skyes pa'i skye mched la gnas shing 'di lta ste/
184b3: mi'i nang nas 'bras can dang / sran can dang // bu ra ba dang / skyo ma dang nya dang sha la sogs pa kham gyis bza' ba'i zas sna tshogs don du gnyer ba dang / mi'i nang nas ji lta ba bzhin du 'gro ba'i rgyud thams cad na rnam
184b4: par spyod pa dag las kyang / kha zas dang btung ba sna tshogs don du gnyer ba dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i mthu dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pa thogs pa med par gtong ba'i rnga'i sgra dang / byang chub sems
184b5: dpa'i sngon gyi sngon lam gyis bos pas kun kyang 'ongs par gyur te/ 'ongs nas kyang khyim bdag mkhas pa la slongs mo 'debs so// gdong du la'o// sdong do// gsol ba'i'adebs so// de nas khyim bdag mkhas
184b6: pas slong ba de dag kun nas 'dus par shes pas/ yud tsam du bsams te nam mkha' la bltas pa dang / nam mkha' dbyings nas/ kha zas dang btud pa rnam pa sna tshogs ro sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ kha dog
184b7: sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ dri sna tshogs dang ldan pa mang po 'thon te/ lag mthil du 'ong bar gyur to// des de dag yongs su blangs shing de ltar kun nas 'dus pa'i slongs mo pa mos pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa/
184b8: de dag ci 'dod pa'i zas dang / btung ba'i rnam pa dang / yo byad kyi khyad par thams cad kyis yongs su tshim par byas so// ci 'dod pa yongs su byin no// rab tu dga' bar byas so// shin tu tshim par byas so//

185a1: dga' ba shin tu skye bar byas so// nyams shin tu bde bar byas so// yang rab tu dga' bar byas so// de ltar de dag shin tu tshim par byas de des kyang mchog ste/ de'i 'og tu chos bstan pa 'di lta
185a2: ste/ ye shes kyi tshogs rgya chen po bsngags pa'i rgyu yongs su brjod do chos bston to// phongs pa thams cad 'byung ba mi srid pa'i rgyu yongs su brjod pa dang / skyed pa chen po yongs su 'grub par 'byung
185a3: ba'i rgyu yongs su brjod pa dang / chos kyi ye shes kyi tshul thob pa 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su brjod pa dang / bsod nams kyi tshogs rgya chen po bstsags pa'i rgyu yongs su brjod pa dang / dga' ba bza' ba'i zas
185a4: rab tu 'thob pa 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su brjod pa dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos shin tu brgyan pa'i lus thob pa 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su brjod pa dang / thub pa med pa'i stobs rnam par dag pa thob pa 'byung
185a5: ba'i rgyu yongs su brjod pa dang / bla na med pa'i kha zas yongs su shes pa'i thob pa 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su brjod pa dang / bdud kyi dpung thams cad rab tu 'jom pa'i bsod nams kyi stobs mi zad pa rab tu thob
185a6: pa 'byung ba'i rgyu yang yongs su brjod pa byas te chos ston to/ / des kha zas don du gnyer cing 'ongs pa rnams la nam mkha'i dbyings nas kha zas rnam pa sna tshogs blangs shing tshim par byas te/ de dag la tshe dang
185a7: mdog dang / stobs bde ba dang / spobs pa phun sum tshogs pa thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// des btung ba don du gnyer cing 'ongs pa rnams la btung ba mang po zhim pa kha na ma tho ba med pa/ yid shin tu dga'
185a8: bar byed pas dag gis tshim par byas nas/ de dag la 'khor bas skom zhing 'khor ba las dga' ba las rnam par bzlog pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos la dga' zhing sangs rgyas kyi chos la mos pa yongs su

185b1: bskyed pa'i phyir chos bstan to/ / ngas ro'i mchog don du gnyer cing 'ongs pa rnams la ro'i mchog sna tshogs dang ra ba dang / sbyar ba dang lan cha dang tsha ba dang / kha ba dang / bska pa dang / rnam pa tha dad pas
185b2: yongs su tshim par bas te/ de'i 'og du skyes bu chen po'i mtshan ro bro ba'i mchog thob par bya ba'i phyir chos bstan to// des bzhon pa don du gnyer cing phyogs kyi rgyud sna tshogs nas 'ongs pa rnams
185b3: la bzhon pa sna tshogs kyi sbyin pas yongs su bsdud de/ de dag theg pa chen po la gnas par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to// des gos don du gnyer cing phyogs sna tshogs nas 'ongs pa kun nas 'dus par shes
185b4: nas/ yud tsam du bsams te/ nam mkha'i dbyings la bltas pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings las gos sna tshogs sngon po dang ser po dang / dmar po dang dkar po dang / la' rgan dang / shel gyi kha
185b5: dog du 'dug pa kha dog sna tshogs can kha dog du mar rnam par dag pa dag 'thon cing lag pa'i mthil du 'ongs pas/ des de dag gis slongs mo pa de dag la yongs bsdad nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
185b6: ngo tsha shes pa dang / khrel yod pa bla na med pa dang / mdog gser gyi kha dog lta bu thob par 'gyur ba rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos bstan to// de bzhin du yo byad sna tshogs thams cad kyis ji ltar 'ongs
185b7: ba'i spongs mo pa rnams la bsdud pa byas nas/ ci rigs su chos bstan to// de ltar khyim bdag mkhas pas byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i yul bstan pa byas nas/
185b8: tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu kho bos ni yid kyi mdzod nas byung ba'i bsod nams kyi rnam par thar pa 'di shes par zad na/ kho bos byang chub sems dpa'i yo byad

186a1: la dbang thob pa rin po che'i lag pa thob par gyur pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad lag pas yongs su khebs par byas shing / sangs rgyas kyi mchod pa sna tshogs bsgrub pa'i phyir/ de bzhin
186a2: gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du rin po che kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi char rab tu 'bebs pa de bzhin du rgyan kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / cod pan kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / khang pa
186a3: brtsegs pa kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / na bza' kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / lha rdzas las rol mo brdung ba dang / dkrol ba dang / glu yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs snyan pa sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / me tog kha deg sA
186a4: tshogs kyi sprin dang / spos kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / bdug spos dang phreng ba dang byug pa dang / bye ma dang chos gos dang / gdugs spos dang rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan kha dog sna tshogs dang / rnam pa thams cad
186a5: du sangs rgyas thams cad mchod pa'i sprin dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang / sems can thams cad kyi gnas su sangs rgyas thams cad mchod cing bsnyen bkur ba dang / sems/
186a6: can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba'i phyir yo byad thams cad kyi char 'bebs pa de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon tan brjod pa'am/ rnam par 'phrul pa bstan pa nus re skan/
186a7: drang srong rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na grong khyer seng ge'i gzugs shes bya ba yod de/ de na chos kyi tshong dpon rin cen gtsug bud ces bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems
186a8: dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dga' rangs te/ mgu zhing nyams bde ba la tshim zhing yid bde ba skyes nas

186b1: khrim bdag mkhas pa la chos lnga rim gros slob ma'i tshul bstan te/ de'i byin gyi rlabs kyis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad thob par 'gyur bar yongs su lta zhing / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang de la rag lus
186b2: bar blta ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dben par sems dpa' rgyun mi 'chad par bstan pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi bka' shin tu nyan pa'i sems dang ldan par bstan pa dang / dge ba'i bshes
186b3: gnyen gyi dbang du 'gyur ba'i rjes su 'brang bar bya ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi gdams ngag dang / tshig mnyan par bya ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen las byung ba'i ngang ba'i dbang po la bsam/
186b4: pa byed cing / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis gtams te btang bas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsnye/ na cing bkur ba dang / rjes su 'brang bar bya ba'i sems kyis/ khyim bdag mkhas pa'i rkang pa
186b5: gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ khyim bdag mkhas pa la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ yang dang yang bltas te/ khyim bdag mkhas pa'i drung nas song ngo //
186b6: de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyi bsod nams kyi chu bo de la ni yid ches par sems/ bsod nams kyi zhing de la ni yang dag par blta/ bsod nams kyi ri bo de ni yongs su spyod/ bsod
186b7: nams kyi mu stegs de la ni yang dag par 'jog/ bsod nams kyi mdzod de ni rnam par 'byed/ bsod nams kyi gter de la ni shin tu lta// bsod nams kyi dkyil 'khor de ni yongs su spong /
186b8: bsod nams kyi phung po de ni yang dag par len pa/ bsod nams kyi stobs de ni yongs su bskyed/ bsod nams kyi shugs de ni rnam par 'phel bar byed pa cing / mthar gyis grong khyer

187a1: seng ge'i gzugs gangan ba der phyin te/ chos kyi tshong dpon rin po chen gtsug pad yongs su tshol tshol ba las/ tsheng 'dus kyi srang zhig na 'dug pa mthong nas/ des de'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi
187a2: bos phyag 'tshal te/ g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/ mdun du 'dug ste thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed/
187a3: na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba ma 'tshal na/ 'phags pa lam gang gis bdag thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'byung
187a4: bar 'gyur ba de lta ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi man ngag legs par mi stsal tam/ / de nas chos kyi tshong dpon rin chen gtsug bud kyis tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyi lag pa nas bzung ste/ rang
187a5: gi khyim gang na ba der khrid de khyim de bstan nas 'di skad ces smras so/ / rigs kyi ba kho bo'i khyim la ltos shig ces nas/ des bltas na khyim de dag cing 'od gsal la 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser
187a6: las byas pa ste/ yangs shing mtho la dngul gyi ra bas bskor ba/ shel gyi rtsigs pas shin tu legs par brtsigs te/ mdzes par byas pa bai dUr+ya'i phung po brgya phrag stong gis rab tu brgyan pa/ mu sa ra
187a7: gal ba'i ka ba bkye ba/ mu tig dmar po las byas pa'i seng ge'i khri shin tu bshams pa/ nor ba rin po che rang bzhin snang ba'i seng ge'i rgyal mtshan sgreng ba/ nor bu rin po che rnam par snang ba'i bla re bres pa/
187a8: gser gyi dra ba yid bzhin gyi nor bus brgyan pas kun nas yog pa/ nor bu rin po che sna tshogs grangs med pas rab tu brgyan pa/ a sma ra gar ba las brtsigs pa'i rdzing bu chu bsil bas gang ba dang ldan pa/

187b1: rin po che thams cad kyi shing gis bskor pa/ rgya che zhid yangs par ma pa bcur brtsegs pa/ shin tu 'tho ba/ sgo brgyad dang ldan par 'dug pa mthong nas/ des khyimado'i nang du phyin te/ kun tu bzlas
187b2: na ri ma khar tha ma'i nang na bza' ba dang btung ba'i rnam pa yongs su gtong ba mthong ngo / / rim khang gnyis pa'i nang na gos kyi rnam pa thams cad yongs su gtong ba mthong ngo // ri ma khar gsum pa'i nang na rin po
187b3: che thams cad kyi rgyan dang / lhab lhub yongs su gtong ba mthong ngo // ri ma khang bzhi pa'i nang na btsun mo'i 'khor dga' ba'i yo byad du bya ba bud med rin po che sa chen po'i steng na bzang du bya ba yongs su gtong ba
187b4: mthong ngo / / ri ma khang lnga pa'i nang nas sa lnga pa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chos yang dag par 'gro ba'i dga' ba la mos pa/ 'jig rten la phan pa dang / bde ba'i sems kyi spyod pa dang ldan pa/
187b5: gtsug lag thams cad mngon par sgrub pa gzungs kyi tshul dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi phyag rgya dang / ting nge 'dzin la rnam par ldang ba dang / ting nge 'dzin la rnam par spyad pa dang / ye shes kyi snang ba mngon par
187b6: bsgrub pa 'dus shing 'khor bar mthong ngo / / ri ma khang drug pa'i nang na byang chub sems dpa' shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rnam par spyod pa rab tu thob pa shes rab shin tu zab pa/ rab tu zhi ba'i chos thams
187b7: cad mngon par shes pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang / gzungs kyi sgo dang / snying po mang pos sgo kun nas byung ba/ bsgribs pa med pa'i spyod yul can mi gnyis pa la yang dag par spyod pa// chos yang dag par 'gro ba la rnam
187b8: par 'phral pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'brang zhing rnam par dbye ba dang / rab tu gsal bar byed pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo mang po yang dag par 'gro ba byang pa rnams kun nas

188a1: 'dus shing 'khod pa mthong ste/ 'di ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo zhi ba'i snying po zhes bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo 'gro ba thams cad du ye shes rnam par phye ba zhes bya ba dang /
188a2: shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo mi g.yo ba'i glong zhes bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo rdul dang bral ba'i 'od ces bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo thub par dka' ba zhes bya ba dang /
188a3: shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo 'gro ba thams cad mos par byed cing rjes su 'brang ba'i dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo phyi bzhin 'brang ba'i dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba dang / shes
188a4: rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo rgya mtsho snying po zhes bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo kun nas lta ba'i btang snyoms thob pa zhes bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo mi zad pa'i mdzod dang
188a5: ldan pa zhes bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo chos thams cad kyi tshul rgya mtsho zhes bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo 'gro ba thams cad kyi rgya mtsho rjes su song ba zhes bya ba dang / shes
188a6: rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo thogs pa med pa'i spobs pa zhes bya ba dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo chos kyi sprin la dmigs pas rim pas mi dmigs pa'i gnas shes bya ba dang / de ltar shes rab
188a7: kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo de dag la sogs pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo grangs med pa brgya stong phrag bcu tshang bar yang dag par 'gro ba byed cing / rgyan brjod du med pa shin tu rnam par phye ba'i 'khor/
188a8: gyi dkyil 'khor na 'khod pa mthong bar gyur to// rim khang bdun pa'i nang na byang chub sems dpa' sgra brnyan lta bu'i bzod pa rab tu thob pa thabs dang ye shes rnam par gdon mi za ba la shin tu byung ba/ de

188b1: bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi sprin yang dag par 'dzin pa sha stag 'dus shing 'khod pa mthong ngo / / ri ma khang brgyad pa'i nang na byang chub sems dpa'i mnyams par 'gro ba'i mngon par shes parab
188b2: tu thob pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par rgyu ba/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du gzugs brnyan rab tu 'byung ba/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du las shin tu rnam par phye ba/ de bzhin
188b3: gshegs pa thams cad kyi zhabs kyi drung nas gud du mi 'phags pa'i yul dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku la yang dag par gzhol ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor du
188b4: sngon du brjod pa'i gtam gyi skyes bur gyur pa/ sha stag kun nas 'dus shing 'khod pa mthong ngo // rim khang dgu pa'i nang na/ byang chub sems dpa' tshe gcig gis thogs pa sha stag 'dus shing 'khod pa mthong
188b5: ngo / / rim khang bcu pa'i nang na de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad thog ma byang chub tu thugs bskyed pa dang / spyod pa dang / 'byung ba dang / smon lam rgya mtsho dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i yul dang /
188b6: sangs rgyas kyi zhing dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du bcas pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu sgrog pa dang / bcas pa dang / sems can 'dul bar mdzad pa'i byin gyis rlabs dang bcas
188b7: par mthong ngo / / mthong nas kyang chos kyi tshong dpon rin chen gtsug pud la 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa khyod la 'di lta bu'i phun sum tshogs pa mnga' na/ phun sum tshogs pa'i rnam pa de ji lta ba
188b8: zhig du spyad pa mdzad dge ba'i rtsa ba ni su zhig la yongs su bskyang bskur / / des smras pa/ rigs kyi bu kho bos dran te/ 'das pa'i dus kyi bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das

189a1: ba'i yang pha rol gcig na/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'khor lo sna tshogs shes bya bar/ de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbyings 'od gzer mtha' yas pas yongs su brgyan pa'i chos kyi rgyal bzhes
189a2: byab mkhyen pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gzugs pa/ 'jig rten maldan pa/ blan med pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba/ kha lo snu ba/ lha dang ni rnams kyi ston pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
189a3: 'jig rten dbyung ba ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa de ye shes rnam par spad pa la stsogs pa nyan thos bye ba phrag brgya dang / ye shes kyi nyi ma'i gzi brjid la stsogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' zlab brgya
189a4: phrag stong dang / thabs gcig du rgyal po'i chos kyi dbang phyug rgyal pos spyan drangs nas/ bza' shing gi ra ba chen po rin po che rin chen brgyal ma chen rgyan gyis mdzes pa zhes bya bar gshegs te/ de bzhin
189a5: gshegs pa de grong khyer du gshegs nas/ tshod 'dus kyi srang nas chung bzhud pa'i tshe/ kho bos de bzhin gshegs pa de dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos kyi dge 'dun dang bcas pa la mchod pa bya ba'i
189a6: phyir/ sil snyan dang / rol mo'i sgra zhig kyang phyung / spos kyi ri lu zhig kyang bsregs te/ bdug spos kyis dasang po bo// spos kyi ri lu gcig po de/ de ltar bsregs pas zhag bdun du 'dzam bu'i gling thams
189a7: cad kyang spos kyi na bun gyi sprin kha dog sna tshogs dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi lus dang 'dra bas yongs su khebs par gyur te// spos kyi na bun gyi sprin de dag las kyang sgra 'di skad du brjod de/ de bzhin
189a8: gshegs pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ dus gsum du dri ma med pa'i ye shes kyi phung po dang ldan pa'o// thams cad mkhyen pa ste/ sgrib pa thams cad mi mda' ba'o// nyon mongs pa'i bag chags thams cad

189b1: yongs su byang ba ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa la yon phul ba thams cad kyang thams cad mkhyen pa'i don chen po tshad med pa bsgrubs par 'gyur ro// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yang dag par gzhol bar
189b2: 'gyur ro zhes/ de skad du kho bo'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su smin par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad dge ba'i rtsa ba las shugs yang dag par bskyed pa'i phyir/ spos kyi nabun gyi sprin de las/ sangs rgyas
189b3: kyi byed kyis rlabs kyis sgra'i rnam pa de lta bu byung ngo / / rigs kyi bu de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyis/ bstan pa'i tshe 'phrul gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba de yang kho bos gnas gsum du yongs su bsngos te/
189b4: gsum gang zhe na 'di ltar phongs pa thams cad shin tu rgyun gcad pa dang / dam pa'i chos mnyan pa dang mi 'bral ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mthong ba
189b5: yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsti'o/ / rigs kyi bu kho bas ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sngon lam gyi dkyil 'khor thogs pa mang pa'i rgyan ces bya ba 'di shes par zad na/
189b6: kho bos byang chub sems dpa' yon tan rin po che tshad myed pa'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sku rgya mtsho dang / tha mi dad pa la zhugs pa/ tha mi dad pa'i chos kyi sprin gyi char yang dag par 'dzin pa/
189b7: tha ming dpal yon tan rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/ kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i dra ba rnam par rgyas par gyur pa/ ting nge 'dzin tha mi dad pa'i yul la zhugs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad tha mi dang pa
189b8: dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rgyun gcig tu gyur pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang tha mi dad cing rnam par mi rtog par spyod pa/ dus gsum tha mi dad pas mnyam pa nyid la zhugs pa/ bskal pa thams cad pa mi da

190a1: bar yongs su gnas par myi skye ba/ kun tu lta ba tha mi dad pa'i yul gyi sa la gnas pa de dag gi spyod pa shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan// drang srong rigs kyi bu
190a2: lha phyogs kyi rgud 'di nyid na yul spa'i rtsa ba zhes bya ba yod de/ de'i grong khyer kun nas sgo zhes bya ba na/ tshed dpon spos 'tshod kun tu lta ba zhes bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la ji
190a3: ltar byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig/ de nas tshod dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis chos kyi tshod dpon rin chen
190a4: gtsug phud kyi rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ chos kyi tshod dpon rin chen gtsug pud la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas yang dang yang ltas te/ chos kyi tshed dpon
190a5: rin chen gtsug phud kyi drung nas song ngo / / sangs rgyas zad ga cad ces bya ba shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// bam po bcu bzhi pa// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs sangs rgyas mtha'
190a6: yas pa mthong ba la zhugs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' mtha' yas pa dang 'grogs pa rab tu thob pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i lam mtha' yas pa'i tshul gyis snang bar gyur pa/ chos kyi tshul mtha'
190a7: yas pas mngon par brlan pas shin du rtogs pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa' mos pa mtha' yas pa'i lam gyis rnam par dag pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i dbang po'i mtha' yas
190a8: pa'i snang ba rab tu thob pa/ byang chub sems dpa' bsam pa mtha' yas pa'i stobs la gnas pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mtha' yas pa'i rjes su song ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ byad

190b1: chub sems dpa'i smon 'am mtha' yas pa'i stobs yongs su skyes pa/ byang chub sems dpa' gzhan gyis thub pa med pa'i mtha' yas pa'i rgyal mtshan can/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes snang ba//
190b2: mtha' yas pa'i klud dang ldan pa// byang chub sems dpa'i chos mtha' yas pa'i snang ba rab tu thob pa de mthar gyis yul spa'i rtsa ba gang na der byin nas/ grong khyer kun gnas sgo yongs su tshol zhing
190b3: phyogs dang / phyogs mtshams dang / yul phyogs nyen kor kun dang / skad dang gshod dang / mnyam pa dang mi mnyam pa thams cad du yongs su skyo ba med pa'i bsam pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa'i
190b4: sems dang / ldog pa med pa'i brtson 'grus dang / thub pa med pa'i sems kyis/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi gdams dag ma brjod pa dang / rtag tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi spyod pa ma nor pas sems
190b5: rab tu bsgos pa dang / sgo kun nas rnam par dmigs pa'i dbang po dang ldan pa dang / bag med pa thams cad dang bral ba dang / mig dang rna ba g.yeng ba med par kun tu tshel tshol nas yul pa'i rtsa ba'i
190b6: dbus shig na/ grong khyer kun nas sgo tshong 'dus kyi rdal stong phrag bcu'i gnas su gyur pa/ de shin tu bzang por grub pa/ ra ba brtan pas bskor ba/ shin tu mtho ba bzhi mdo brgyad kyis brgyan pa
190b7: 'dug par mthong ste/ 'di'i nang na spos 'tshod kun tu lta ba yang spos 'tshod gi 'khyams shig na 'dug pa mthong nas/ spos 'tshod kun nas lwa ba gang na ba dar byin te/ spos 'tshod kun tu la ba'i rkang
190b8: pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ mdun du 'dug ste/ thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na/ ji

191a1: ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba ma 'tshal to// smras pa rigs kyi bu de ltar khyod kyis bla na med pa yang dag
191a2: par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa legs so legs so/ / rigs kyi bu kho bos ni sems can thams cad kyi nad shes te/ rlung las gyur pa dang / mkhris pa las gyur pa dang / bad kan las
191a3: gyur pa dang / cha mnyam par 'khrugs pa dang / gzhan gyis gnod par byas pa dang / ma yin pa las gyur pa dang / dug 'thungs pa dang / sngags dang / mtshon dang / ro langs pa'i sbyor ba sna tshogs dang /
191a4: me las gyur pa dang / chus bskod pa las gyur pa dang / bsngags pa dang 'jigs pa sna tshogs las gyur pa thams cad kyang shes so// nad de dag thams cad shes par bya ba yang shes te/ 'di ltar stan
191a5: par bye ba yang rab tu shes so/ / skyug par bye ba dang / bkru ba dang brtar ba dang gtar ba dang / sna'i mchog dang nyar dang gdugs dang / lums dang / byug pa dang / dug gso ba dang / 'byung po'i gdon med par
191a6: bya ba dang / bcud dang khrus dang / gzhig pa dang / bskyed pa dang / kha dog spyad pa dang / nyam bstod pa'ang rab tu shes te/ rigs kyi bu phyogs bcu nas sems can gang ji snyed cig lo ba'i drung du 'ong ba de dag
191a7: thams cad kyi nang thams cad kyang rab tu zhi bar byed dade/ nad sos nas kyang legs par bkru ba dang / lus la byug pas drug pa byas nas/ ci'i tshul gyi rgyan gyis yan lag shin tu brgyan te/ ci rigs
191a8: ba'i gos lus la bskon nas/ kha zas bro ba'i mchog dang ldan pa sna tshogs kyis yongs su tshim byas te/ nor dpag tu med pas kyang phun sum tshogs par byed do// de'i 'og tu yang de dag la mi gtsang ba

191b1: bstan cing / 'dod chags spang ba'i phyir chos ston to// byams pa chen po yongs su bsngags shing zhe sdang spang ba'i phyir chos ston to// chos rnam par dbye ba'i bye brag bstan cing gti mug spang ba'i phyi ngos smon to//
191b2: khyad par 'ong du chud pa'i tshul gyi sgo yang dag par bstan cing cha mnyam pa'i spyod pa dang / nyon mongs pa srung ba'i phyir chos son ka/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan gyi chos dang ldan pa'i gtam thams cad yongs
191b3: su brjod cing byang chub kyi sems 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su ston to/ / tshad gzung du med pa yongs su ston to// snying rje chen po'i 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su ston to// bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs rgya
191b4: chen po brtsegs pa yang dag par bsngags shing yon tan tshad med pa 'thob pa dang / 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su ston to// sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba yongs su
191b5: bstan cing theg pa chen po'i smon lam 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su ston to/ / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad dang / bskal pa thams cad du gnas par bya ba'i spyod pa'i dra ba shin tu rgyas par bshad cing byang
191b6: chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa 'thob pa dang / 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su ston to// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su bsngags shing mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos brgyan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sa
191b7: 'thob pa dang 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su ston to/ / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su brjod cing de bzhin gshegs pa'i yongs su dag pa thams cad du 'gro ba 'thob pa dang / 'byung ba'i rgyu yongs su
191b8: ston to/ / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su brjod cing de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs dang / sku mdog rnam par dag pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyu yongs su ston to// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol du phyin

192a1: pa yongs su brjod cing de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa thob par dga' ba yongs su ston to/ / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i yongs su brjod ngang bzhin gshegs pa'i skuzil gyis mnan pa/
192a2: zil gyis gnon pa rnam par dag pa yongs su ston to// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su brjod cing chos kyi sku yongs su dag pa yongs su ston to// thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su brjod
192a3: cing 'gro ba thams cad la mngon du gyur pa'i sku gtsang zhing rnam par dag pa yongs su ston to/ / smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su brjod cing bskal pa thams cad kyi dus su 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems
192a4: dang 'grogs pa'i sku rnam par dag pa yongs su ston to/ / stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su brjod cing sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du mngon par 'byung ba'i sku rnam par dag pa yongs su ston to//
192a5: shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su brjod cing 'gro ba thams cad bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du tshim par mdzad pa'i sku rnam par dag pa yongs su ston to// mi dge ba'i chos thams cad las rnam par ldog
192a6: pa yongs su brjod cing blta na phul du bzang ba'i sku rnam par dag pa yongs su ston to/ / de ltar de dag chos kyi sbyin pas yongs su bsdud de/ nor dang rin po che mtha' yas pa'i tshogs kyis nye bar brten
192a7: pa byes shing so sor 'gyed do/ / yang rigs kyi bu kho bos ni spos dang / bdug spos dang / bsgo ba dang / bsku ba sgor shes te/ 'di ltar spos kyi rgyal po gzhal du med pa la stsogs pa dang / spos kyi rgyal po sa 'du
192a8: ra la sogs pa dang / spos gyi rgyal po mi 'phags pa la sogs pa dang / spos kyi rgyal po rnam par gsal byed la sogs pa dang / spos kyi rgyal po nyi ma yod pa la sogs pa dang / spos kyi rgyal po dus dang 'thun pa/

192b1: la sogs pa dang / spos kyi rgyal ba sngal gyi steng pa'i tsan dan las sngags pa dang / spos kyi rgyal po sprin gyi a ga ru la sogs pa dang / spos kyi rgyal po dbang po mi 'khrugs pa la sogs pa/ spos spar ba
192b2: thams cad kyang rab tu shes sa/ / yang rigs kyi bral ba ni sems can thams cad yongs su tshim par byed pa dang / sgo thams cad nas sangs rgyas blta zhing mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur ba'i smom
192b3: kyi gzugs shes te/ rigs kyi ba kho bo ni sems can thams cad yongs su tshim par byed pa dang / sgo thams cad nas sangs rgyas blta zhing mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur ba'i spos kyi gzugs 'dis
192b4: kho bo'i bsam pa thams cad kyang yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur te/ de'i mthus kho bos sems can thams cad yongs su skyob pa'i rgyan gyi sprin byin gyis rlob pa byed de/ 'di ltar spos kyi khang brtags
192b5: pa'i sprin gyi rgyan nas rnam pa thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa mchod cing re mgror bya ba'i rgyan gyi sprin gyi bar du byin gyis rlob pa byed do/ / rigs kyi bu kho bo ni nam de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod
192b6: pa bya bar 'dod pa de'i tshe/ kho bos sems can thams cad yongs su tshim par byed pa dang / sgo thams cad nas sangs rgyas blta zhing mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur ba'i spos kyi gzugs 'di las spos
192b7: kyi mdzod kyi khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin tshad gzung du mod pa brten cing / phyogs bcu'i chos kyi dbyings thams cad na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi dkyil 'khor chos kyi dbyings thams cad du
192b8: spos thams cad kyi mdzod kyi khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin gyi rgyan byin gyis rlob pa byed do/ / chos kyi dbyings thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi khang pa'i

193a1: sprin gyi char dang / spos kyi ra ba'i sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi bgam gyi sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi rta babs kyi sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi skar khung gi sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi bu shu'i sprin gyi
193a2: rgyan dang / spos kyi zla gam gyi sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi gdugs sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi rgyal mtshan sgreng ba'i sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi lha'i ba dan gyi sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi bla re'i sprin gyi rgyan dang
193a3: spos kyi gzugs kyi dra ba'i sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi 'od kyi sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos kyi snang ba'i dri ma med pa'i sprin gyi rgyan dang / spos thams cad kyi sprin gyi char rab tu 'bab pa'i rgyun byin gyis rlob ste/ rigs
193a4: kyi bu kho bos ni sems can thams cad yongs su tshim par byed pa dang / sgo thams cad nas sangs rgyas blta zhing mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur ba'i spos kyi gzugs kyi chos kyi sgo 'di shes par zad na/ kho bos
193a5: byang chub sems dpa' sman gyi rgyal po lta bur gyur pa/ blta na don yod pa/ 'grogs na don yod pa/ rjes su dran na yod pa/ brtul zhugs rjes su byas na don yod pa/ ming thos na don yod pa/
193a6: mthong ba tsam gyis sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa zhi par 'gyur ba/ mthong ba tsam gyis sems can rnams ngan song gi rgyud las ldog par 'gyur ba/ mthong ba tsam gyis sems can thams
193a7: cad sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi chos la skabs phye ba thob par gyur pa/ mthong ba tsam gyis sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po thams cad zhi bar 'gyur ba/ mthong ba tsam gyis sems can rnams
193a8: 'jigs pa dang / 'khor ba'i lam gyi rgyud thams cad kyi 'jigs pa dang bral bar 'gyur ba/ mthong ba tsam gyis sems can rnams thams cad mkhyen pa'i phyogs la rten par 'gyur ba'i phyir

193b1: mi 'jigs pa thob par 'gyur ba/ mthong ba tsam gyis sems can rnams rga shi'i grog po dang g.yang sar ma ltung ba/ mthong ba tsam gyis sems can rnams chos kyi dbyangs mnyam pa nyid la gnas pas mya ngan
193b2: las 'das pa'i bde ba 'thob par 'gyur ba de dag gi spyod pa shes pa'am yon tan brjod par nus re skan/ / drang srong rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na grong khyer ta la'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba yod de/
193b3: dan rgyal po me zhes bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig/ de nas tshong dpon gyi
193b4: bu nor bzangs/ tshong dpon spos 'tshong kun tu lta ba'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ tshong dpon spos 'tshong kun tu blta ba la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas yang dang
193b5: yang bltas te/ tshong dpon spos 'tshong kun tu blta ba'i drung nas song ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs dge ba'i bshes gnyen gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa de dag rjes su dran par byed cing / dge ba'i
193b6: bshes gnyen gyi gdams ngag gi sgo de dag rjes su dran par bya ba dang / bdag gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su bzung ngo // zhes bya ba'i sems yongs su tshim par bya ba dang / bdag ni dge ba'i bshes
193b7: gnyen gyis yongs su bsrungs pas/ de ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir ldog par yang mi 'gyur ro// snyam du rnam par sems shing / sems dga' ba ni rab tu thob/ sems dang
193b8: ba dang sems rab tu dga' ba dang / sems rab tu dga' ba dang / sems rangs pa dang / sems mgu ba dang / sems mos pa dang / sems kyi shugs dang / sems rnam par zhi ba dang / sems rgya

194a1: can pa dang / sems pa can dang / sems la gas pa mad pa dang sems la gams med pa dang / sems rnam par bya dang / sems yang dag par nanal pa dang / sems kyi dang dang / sems kyidapa
194a2: sgru ba dang / sems kyi ma khong chad pa dang / sems kyi nang nyas par dgod pa dang / sems sangs rgyas mame pas can pa dang / sems stobs bcu'i mid la byu ba dang mi 'bral ba'ang thos nas// de mthar
194a3: sa ldangs nas stong sa dang / song nas thong dang mal nas yul du tshol zhing / grong gyer ta Sha'i rgyal mtshan ga na pa dar byin te/ rgyal po ma gangan bzugs pas rnas na// de 'bri bgazhan dag gis 'di skad sa
194a4: bstan te/ rigs kyi bu 'dir rgyal po mo ni rgyal po'i don bsgrub pa'i phyir seng ge'i gdan la bzhugs shing / rgyal ba'i phrin las mdzad do// khams rab tu stod do// chad pas gcad par 'os pa ni chad pas
194a5: gcad do/ / dgas su par 'os pa ni bya dgas srad do// g.yon yod pa rnams la rtsod med do// rtsod pa rnams kyi nal tsan yongs su gcod de// dma' pa rnams ni dbugs 'byin to// dregs pa rnams ni
194a6: bar mdzad do/ / srog gcod pa las ni rnam par zlog go/ ma byin par len pa dang ni rnam par dbyed pa mdzad do// gzhan gyis yongs su bzung ba la mngon par zhen pa ni rnam par zhi bar mdzad do// rdzun du smra ba
194a7: las phyir zlog pa mdzad do/ / phra ma'i tshig dang ni rnam par 'bral bar mdzad do// zhe gcod pa'i ngag ni rgyun gcod pa mdzad do// tshig khyal pa las ni yongs su glon no// chags sems dang ni mi 'dre ba mdzad
194a8: ro/ / gnod sems dang ni rgyang ring ngo // log par lta ba dang ni 'dre ba med par mdzad do// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs rgyal po me gang na ba der phyin te/ des mthong ba rgyal po me ni de rin po che'i seng ge'i khri chen

194b1: bo rdo rje mthu bo che'i nor bu sna tshogs kyis smras pa/ rin po che'i 'od gsal ba rnam pa sna tshogs grangs med pa las byas pa'i rkang pa bkye ba/ rin po che gcig ma yin pas legs par smras shing brgyan pas/
194b2: yid du 'ong ba'i lhun dang ldan pa/ gser gyi lug 'od kyi dra bas legs par blangs shing chub par btags pa/ nor bu rin po che du ma'i sgron mas shin tu snang bar byas pa/ nor bu rin po che dbang gi rgyal po las
194b3: byas pa'i pad mo'i snying po can/ lha rngus rin po che'i san rim pa du mar bting ba/ gam yo nas lha rdzas kyi spos sna tshogs kyi bdug spos kyis shin tu gdugs pa/ rin po che'i rgyal mtshan sbeng ba/ brgya phras
194b4: stong gis mdzes par byas pa/ rin po che'i ba dan brgya phrag stong rnam par bres pas brgyan pa/ rin po che'i me tog gi chun po sna tshogs kyi lda ldi bkye bas shin tu mdzes par byas pa/ snying nas lha rdzas
194b5: kyi rin po che'i bla re sna tshogs bres pa zhig la 'dug cing / de ni gzhon zhing dar la bab pa/ gzugs mdzes shing blta na yid du 'ong ba/ skra mthon ting g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pa dang ldan pa/ mgo
194b6: gdugs ltar 'dug pa gtsug tor spyi bo can/ 'bral ba yangs pa/ mig dkar nag 'byes shing ring la/ rdzi ma'i ba'i rdzi ma ltar 'dug pa/ sna'i dbyibs lags shing bzang la ran par mdzes pa dang ldan
194b7: pa/ / mchu mtshal ltar 'dog bzang zhing shin tu legs pa dang ldan pa/ so mnyam zhing thags bzang la shin tu dkar ba bzhi bcu tshang ba dang ldan pa/ 'gram pa'i ltar seng ge'i 'gram pa ltar 'dug pa/
194b8: khur bshas rgyas pa/ smin tsugs gzhu ltar 'dug cing ring la shin tu mdzes pa/ mdzod spu zla ba'i kha dog ltar 'dug pa'i thig le can/ rna ba'i shal ring zhing lhod par 'byang ba/ zla ba nya ba ltar bzhin

195a1: madrangs dang ldan zhing shin tu bzang ba/ mgul zlum zhing rung ltar mdzes pa/ snying ka dpal gyis be'us brgyan pa/ ro stod seng ge'i ro stod ltar 'dug pa/ thal gong shin tu rgyas pa/ dpung ma
195a2: lhun legs shing zlum pa/ lag pa ring ba dra bar 'brel bar sor mo can/ rka lag 'khor los brgyan pa/ rka lag 'jam zhing gzhon la sha rgyas pa/ bdun shin tu mtho ba// rked pa rdo rje ltar 'dug pa/
195a3: lus che zhing drang ba/ brla zlum pa/ po mtshan gsang ba'i sbubs na 'dug pa/ byin pa ri dgas e ne ya'i byin pa ltar 'dug pa/ sor mo ring ba/ rkang pa'i rting pa yangs pa/ 'od 'dom gang ba dang ldan pa
195a4: mdog gser gyi kha dog ltar 'dug pa/ ba s+phu re re nas g.yas phyogs su gyen du 'khyil pa/ shing na gro da'i rgyal po ltar chu zheng gab pa/ lus mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos shin tu brgyan pa/ mgo
195a5: la nor bu rin po che yid bzhin gyi cod pan thogs pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser las byas pa'i pha phral ba'i ban phra gam gyis mdzes par brgyan pa/ rna ba las rin po che i na tra ni la'i rna cha dri ma med
195a6: pa 'phyang ba/ nor bu rin po che rin btang med pa'i se mo de'i 'od kyis snang bar byas pas/ dri ma med pa'i ro stod rgyas pa dang ldan pa/ lha rdzas kyi nor bu dam pa'i rin po che'i dpung brgyan dang / gdu bus
195a7: lag pa mdzes par brgyan pa zhig ste/ rin po che'i gdugs chen po rin po che bai dUr+ya'i dri ma med pa'i yu ba can/ rin po che'i shar bu brgya phrag bcus rnam par phye ba/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser gyi bla ga ma can/
195a8: nor bu rin po che sgra snang ba rnam par dag pa'i snying po can/ rin po che'i dril bu'i phreng ba las sgra snyan cing / yid du 'ong ba 'byung ba/ nor bu rin po che'i 'od phyogs kun tu 'phro ba can drung nas bzung zhing

195b1: bsdang ba/ rgyal ba'ig brjod dang dbang chen po la gnas pa/ srad la gzhan gyi 'khor gyis gtsab med/ dgra'i 'jigs pa dang bral ba'i dbang phyug dang ldan par 'dug pa mthong ba// de'i 'khar kun nas
195b2: kyang blon po song phrag bcu tshogs shing rgyal po'i dgos pa bsgrub pa la btsan pa mthong ngo / / de'i mdun na chad pas bcod pa'i mi sems can dmyal ba'i srungs ma lta bu/ gshin rdzo g.yog 'khor lta bu 'dzi
195b3: 'jigs lngar gos gyon pa/ gtum zhing mi zad pa 'jigs pa chen po skyed pa mig dmar bso gtsigs pa/ gdong gi gnyer ma gsum khro gnyer du bsdus pa/ ral gri dang star dang / lcags kyi chang mdung dang /
195b4: mnga' dang be rga dang / mdung la sogs pa'i mtshon cha dang / lag cha thogs pa'i lus dang / bzhin gyi dbyibs mi sdug cing 'jigs su rung ba/ sprin nag po ltar 'dug pa/ mi snyan cing brlang la sdang ba'i sgo drag
195b5: bo 'byin pa/ gzi ltar bar dka' ba/ 'jigs pa chen po bskyed pa/ srog chags brgya phrag stong gi snying 'gam par byed pa/ de lta bu dag chad pas gcad par 'os pa'i sems can chad pas gtsang ba la btson pa
195b6: mthong ngo / / de na srog chags rga ba gzhan gyi nor la 'phrog pa/ sems can gyi longs spad chung sdud pa/ lam skugs shing 'phrog pa/ grong dang grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / lha sa la mas gtor ba/ grong du
195b7: chem po byed pa/ khyim phugs 'dabs pa/ sdig sdig ltar byed pa/ dug ldang ba/ dkrugs ma byed pa/ thod mi byed pa/ byi ba byed pa/ log par zhugs pa/ gnod par sems dpa'/ 'dod chen chab/
195b8: sdig pa sna tshogs kyi las mi bzad pa byed pa/ brgya stong mang po bcing ba dam po lngas bcings shing rgyal po me'i drung du khrid bdag kyang mthong ngo // de dag la'ang rgyal po mes ci rigs par chad pas gcad par

196a1: gyur pa mthong ngo / / des na rgyal po mes sgo zhing la la ni rka lag bcad/ la la ni rna ba dang sna bcad/ la la ni mig phyung / la la ni yan lag dang nying lag dang / mgo gcod/ la la ni lus thams cad mes
196a2: patang / la la ni brtsa'i chu khol bas lus la gtor cing bags pa bsnyil ba la sogs pa/ de lta ba'i chad pa sna tshogs du ma mi bzang ba drag pa brlang ba yid du mi 'ong ba srog 'phrog pa dag kyang byed par mthong ngo //
196a3: gsad pa'i sa den 'ang bsad pa'i rga lag dang / rnamag dang sna dang / mgo dang yan lag dang nyid lag gi phrang po ri rab tsam du spangs pa mthong ngo // khrag gi mtshe dpag tshad gsum tsam du zab la chu zheng du dpag
196a4: tshad du ma yod pa/ yang mthong ngo // de na shi ba'i rkeng rus yan lag dang nying lag dang / mgo dang bral ba brgya stong du ma la/ spyad khi dang wa dang / khyi dang bya rog dang / bya rgod dang / khra dang bya ku ru ra mang pos gang
196a5: ste/ 'drad cing 'thog pa mthong ngo // de la 'dal la ni kha dog du gyur te/ sngon por gyur pa tsam/ la la ni rnams pa tsam/ la la ni bam pa tsam/ la la ni 'bu zhugs pa tsam du gyur te/ shin tu smyig ya
196a6: zhing 'jigs 'jigs ltar 'dug pa mthong ngo / / gsad pa de dag gis bsod pa'i tshe/ mi sdug pa tshe dgur byas pas na 'jigs 'jigs skad dang / snying rje rje skad du sgra 'byin cing cho nges 'debs pa'i sgra chen po
196a7: thos na/ skyi g.ya' zhing mi dga' ba chen po skyed pa sems can dmyal ba chen po'i ris gzhom pa'i sgra lta bu'ang thos so// des de ltar kha btags ste brdungs pa dang / shin tu 'jigs pa'i drag shul mthong
196a8: nas/ 'di snyam du gyur te// bdag ni sems can thams cad la phan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon du zhugs te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su

196b1: tshol zhing 'bad de/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams la dge ba'i ni ci zhig bgyi// mi dge ba ni gang zhig spang zhes 'drin/ rgyal po ma 'di la ni dge ba'i chos kyang med de/ kha na ma tho ba chen po'i las la spyod pa yid kyi
196b2: yongs su rtog pa shin tu gtum pa dang ldan pa/ sems can pha rol gyi srog gcod pa la zhugs pa/ sems can pha rol shin tu mnar ba la brtson pa/ tshe phyi ma la lta ba med pa/ ngan song gi g.yang sa'i
196b3: gang ka na 'dug pa/ zhig na 'di las ji ga zhig byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa'ang thos par 'gyur ram snyam ste/ de de ltar sems shing yid la byed de/ sems can thams cad yongs su bskyab pa dang / mngon
196b4: par brtson pa/ snying rje chen po skyes pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ de la steng gi nam mkha'i dbyings las lha mang pos bos pa/ rigs kyi bu drang srong rgyal ba drod kyi skye mched kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi gdams
196b5: ngag du bya ba mi dran nam/ des gyen dra nam mkha'i dbyings la bltas nas/ dran no zhes brjod do// lha rnams kyis smras pa/ rigs kyi bu khyod dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi gdams ngag la de ltar the tsom ma
196b6: skyed cig/ rigs kyi bu dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams ni yang dag pa ma nor bar ston gyi log pa ma yin no// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi thabs mkhas pas spyod pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis
196b7: mi khyab bo/ / sems can yongs su sdud pa'i ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sems can la phan 'dogs pa'i ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab po// sems can tshar gcod pa'i ye shes bsam gyis
196b8: mi khyab po/ / sems can gzing stod pa'i ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab po// sems can yongs su spyod pa'i ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab po// sems can yongs su spyod pa'i ye shes bsam gyis mi

197a1: khyab po/ / sems can 'jud pa'i ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa// sems can yongs su smin par byed pa'i ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab po// sems can 'dul ba'i ye shes bsam gyi mi khyab po// drang
197a2: srod rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dris shig ces nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis lha'i dag mnyan ta/ rgyal po ma gang na ba der song ste phyin nas/ rgyal po mi'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos
197a3: phyag 'tshal te/ rgyal po me la lan brgya song du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas mdun du 'dug ste/ thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par
197a4: rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed na/ de ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba ma 'tshal te/ 'phags pa'i byang chub sems
197a5: dpa' rnams la gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa mdzad do zhes bdag gis thos na/ 'phags pa ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bgyid
197a6: bdag la bka' stsal du gsol/ / de nas rgyal po mes rgyal po'i bya ba byas te/ seng ge'i khri las langs nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyi lag ba g.yas pa nas bzung ste/ rgyal po'i pho brang tu
197a7: la'i rgyal mtshan du khrid do/ / de mthar gyis rang gi gnas su phyin nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang du khrid de khri la bzhag nas 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu di'i khyim
197a8: dang longs spyod la ltos shes nas/ des bltas na khyim de rgya che zhing yangs la rin po che bdun gyi ra bas yongs su bskor ba/ nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi khang pas shin tu mdzes par byas pa/ rin po

197b1: tshe'i khang pa brtsegs pa brgya'i stong du mas rab tu brgyan pa/ ner bu rin po che bas ma gyis mi khyab pa'i 'od shin tu 'bar bas gze brjid rab tu 'bar bar byas pa/ ner bur na pa ches tshogs kyis rnam par tha
197b2: par rnam par phye 'ang bris pas rnam par mdzes par byas pa/ mu tig dmar po'i kab bkye ba/ nad du seng ge'i khri mus ragal ba las byas pa/ nor bu rin pa cha brgya stong du mas rnam pasna tshogs su brgyan pa/ shi
197b3: bshams pa/ nor bu rin po che'i skar ma sdang ba'i seng ge'i rgyal mtshan shin tu bsgred pa/ steng nas nor bu rin po che rnam par snang ba'i bla re bres pa/ yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po ches tshogs kyi dra bas kun nas
197b4: nor bu rin po che sna tshogs grangs med pas rab tu brgyan pa/ bgam gyi rgyan dang ldan pa/ a sma gar ba las byas pa'i rdzing bu bsil bas gang ba dang ldan pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi shing gis 'khor bar 'du
197b5: pa mthong ngo / / de'i 'khor bud med bzang zhing mdzes la lta na sdug pa/ kha dog rgyas pa/ bzang ba'i phul du byung ba dang ldan pa/ sku tsal thams cad kyi tshul la mkhas pa sngon du ldang ba/ phyi nas nyal ba
197b6: byams pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ ci bsgo ba bzhin du byed cing / dag nyan pa/ bye ba phrag bcu yang 'khod par mthong ngo // de nas rgyal po mes tshod dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smras so//
197b7: rigs kyi bu ji snyam du sems/ cig sdig pa byed pa rnams la las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par grub pa 'di lta bu yod dam// lus phun sum tshogs pa 'di lta bu yod dam/ 'khor phun sum tshogs pa
197b8: 'di lta bu yod dam/ / sbrid pa chen po phun sum tshogs pa 'di lta bu yod dam// dbang phyug dang dbang chen po thob pa phun sum tshogs pa 'di lta bu yod dam/ smras pa 'phags pa de lta bu ni ma mchis so// des

198a1: smras pa/ / rigs kyi bu ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa/ sgyu ma'i rnam pa thob pa ste/ rigs kyi bu ra'i yul ni gnas pa'i sems can 'di dag kya pal cher srog gcod pa byed pa/ mabyin
198a2: par len pa/ 'dod pas log par g.yem pa/ rdzun du smra ba/ phra ma can/ tshig brlad por smra ba/ byung rgyal du brjod pa/ chags sems dang ldan pa/ gnod sems can/ log par blta ba/ sdig pa'i las
198a3: byed pa/ bri zhing gtum pa/ bab rgyal can/ mi dge ba'i las kyi bya ba sna tshogs dang ldan pa dag ste/ de dag ni rnam pa gzhan gyis sdig pa'i spyod pa las bzlog pa dang / dgag pa dang / bstan par mi nus te/ de ltar
198a4: rigs kyi bu nga ni sems can 'di dag gdul ba dang / yongs su smin par bya ba dang / shin tu dul bar bya ba dang / phan pa la gdod par bya ba'i phyir/ snying rje chen po mdun byas te/ bsod pa'i gshed ma sprul pa
198a5: rnams/ / sadang pa'i myir sprul pa rnams la'ang / gsod du gzung ba dang / chad pas gcod pa'i mi sprul pa rnams mi dge ba'i las kyi lam la spyod par sprul pa'i mi rnams la chad pa sna tshogs kyis gcod du
198a6: gzung ba dang / rga lag dang sna dang rna ba dang / yan lag dang nying lag dang / mgo bcad pa las byung ba'i sdug bsngal mi bzad pa nyams su tshor bar gyur pa lta bu dag kyang yongs su ston pa byed de/ de mthong nas
198a7: nga'i khams na gnas pa'i sems can de dag nyes pa gtong zhing skyo ba'i shugs thob par 'gyur ro/ / 'jigs pa skye zhing bag tsha ba skye bar 'gyur ro// de dag sdig pa'i las byed pa rnams gtong zhing bag byed par
198a8: 'gyur ro/ / rigs kyi bu de ltar nga ni sems can 'di dag thabs des nyes pa stong zhing 'jigs pa'i sems dang ldan pa dang / skyo ba'i yid dang ldan par shes nas/ mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam las bzlog ste/

198b1: dge ba'i bcu'i las kyi lam dang ldan par byas nas dga' zhing bde ba'i mthar phyin pa/ sdug bsngal thams cad rgyun chad pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bde ba la gdod pa byed kyi/ rigs kyi bu nga ni lus dang ngag
198b2: gam/ yid kyis kyang sems can su la'ang co mi 'dri/ bro mi 'tsham mo rigs kyi bu nga ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal gyis bkrid shes pa ste/ byol song gi skye gnas glen pa'i khams su gtogs pa'i
198b3: las kyang chung ngu na/ rtswa'i rtse mos blta ba'i sog chags bre'u 'ga' la yang sems bskyed pa cig tsam du yang sdug bsngal bar bya bar mi dga' na/ zhing du gyur cing dge ba'i las kyi lam bskyed par nus pa'i mi
198b4: lta zhig la cig spos/ / rigs kyi bu da ni rmi lam na yang mi dge ba'i chos yongs su rgyu ba mi skyed na/ ched du bsams te lta smos re skan// rigs kyi bu de ltar ngas ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgru ba'o/
198b5: rnam pa 'di shes par zad na/ ngas ni byang chub sems dpa'i mi skye ba'i chos kyi bzod pa thob pa/ srid pa dang lam gyi rgyud thams cad sgyu ma'i rnam pa khong du chud pa sprul pa lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa' spyod pas
198b6: 'byung ba/ gzugs brnyan lta bu'i 'jig rten thams cad rnam par rig pa/ rmi lam lta bu'i chos nyid khong du chud pa/ thogs pa med pa'i sgo'i chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul la rjes su zhugs pa/ mig 'phrul la bu
198b7: spyod pa'i dra ba rtogs par gyur pa/ ye shes bsgribs pa med pa'i spyod yul gyi yul dang ldan pa/ kun tu yang dag par gzhol ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi lam gyis byung ba/ glong kun tu 'khyil ba'i rgyud kyi gzugs la
198b8: dbang sgyur ba/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul gyi yul khong du chud pa rnams kyi spyod yul shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan// drang srong rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid na/ grong khyer 'od bzang

199a1: po zhes bya ba yod de/ de na rgyal po 'od chen po zhes bya ba 'dug gis/ de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang / ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig/
199a2: de nas tshong dpon kyi bu nor bzangs kyis rgyal po me'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ rgyal po me la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas te/ yang dang yang bltas te rgyal po me'i drud nas song
199a3: do/ / de nas tshod dpodan gyi bu nor bzangs ye shes sgyu ma de rjes su dran par byed cing / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa/ sgyu ma'i rnam pa de la bsam pa dang / chos nyid sgyu ma'i rnam pa de la rab tu brtag pa dang /
199a4: las kyi rgyu ma mnyam pa de kho na khong du chud par bya ba dang / chos kyi sgyu ma mnyam par de la rjes su bsam pa dang / chos kyis yongs su smin par bya ba'i sprul pa mnyam pa de khong du khong du chud par bya ba dang / ye shes

199b1: na bzhugs shes dris na/ de la 'gro ba mang pos bstan pa/ rigs kyi bu de re re 'di ni grong khyer 'od bzang po zhes bya ba yin te/ 'di ni rgyal po 'od chen po bzhugs so zhes nas/ de nas tshong dpon gyi ba nor bzangs

239a1: shes par zad na/ khems byung chub sems dpa'i chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa la zhugs pa/ chos thams cad la rlob sems med pa dag nas kyang skyil mo drung cig gis dbyings thams cad
239a2: rgyas par 'gengs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rang gi lus su 'dus par ston kyang / skad cig gcig gis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi drang du 'dod pa/ lus la sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul thams cad
239a3: 'byung shing d+hA/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du led pa'i yang brjod du med pa ba spu'i nyag ma gcig gis skams shing mngon par 'phen pa/ rang gi ba spu'i bu gar 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
239a4: po'i 'dra ba dang / 'jigs pa'i skal ba yongs su ston pa/ skad gcig cig laM bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par gnas pa/ mnyam pa nyid kyis yang dag par 'dzud pa/ skad cig gcig gis brjod
239a5: du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bskul par 'khor ba de dag gi spyod pa shes pa'am/ yon tan brjod par nus re skan/ song rigs kyi bu lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di nyid kyi yul bgrod dka' ba na/ grong khyer rin po
239a6: che rgyan ces bya ba yod de/ den bcom pa ma lha'i bshes gnyen ma zhes bya ba 'dug gis de'i gan du song la ji ltar byang chub sems dang / sa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang /
239a7: slang nan tan du bya ba dris shig/ de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor b.rangs kyis dge slong ma seng ge rnam par bsgyings pa'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ dge slong mas gi rnab par bsgru pa
239a8: la lan brgya stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas yang dang yang bltas te/ dge slong ma sing ge rnam par bsgyings pi'i drung nas song ngo // de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs shes ra

239b1: kyisnang ba chen po des sems snang bar gyur pa de thams cad mkhyen pa nyid shes rab sna ba ldan sems ma nyid kyi rang gzhin gyi stobs snang ba dal nA yang dag par rjes sun/ sems cad /
239b2: cad kyi skad rnam par dmigs pa'i mdzod kyi gzungs kyi tshul de ni brtan par byed/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo yang dag par 'dzin pa'i gzungs kyi tshul de ni shin tu rgya
239b3: byed snying rje chen po 'gro ba thams cad kyi skyabs su gyur pa'i stobs de ni nye bar ston chos thams cad kyi tshul snang ba'i sgo nas/ yang dag par 'byung ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shugs de la ni ba
239b4: tu rtog/ chos kyi dbyings rgya chen po'i dkyil 'khor rgyas par 'gengs pa'i smon lam yongs su dag pa de'i rjes su ni 'brang / chos thams cad kyi phyogs snang bar byed pa'i ye shes kyi 'od de ni shin tu gsal
239b5: bar byed/ chos thams cad kyis phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par phye ba rgyas par 'gengs pa'i mngon par shes pa'i stobs de ni mngon par sgrub/ byang chub sems dpa'i lam dang / dran pa
239b6: thams cad nye bar blangs pas brtsams pa mthar dbyung ba'i smon lam de ni yongs su rdzogs par byed cing / mthar gyis yul bgrod dka' ba'i grong khyer rin po che rgyan gang na pa drir phyin te/ bcomam
239b7: b+ha ba shes gnyen ma yongs su tshol tshol ba dang / de la bcom pa ma lha'i bshes gnyen gyi yon tan mngon par mi shes la ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi tshu la la mkhas pa'i mi ji snyed par dag 'dasar
239b8: drisams te/ mi 'di de ltar zhi zhing rdul ba'i dbang po dang / ldan pa de ltar shes bzhin dang ldan te/ de ltar 'khrul pa med cing de ltar yid 'khrug pa med la de ltar gnya' shing gang tsam du la ste/ de sa

240a1: gnod pas mi tshugs shing de ltar mtshan mar mi 'dzin la/ gzugs kyi rnam pa thams cad la g.yeng ba med pa'i mig dang ldan te/ yid la 'brel ba med cing / bsam pazab la mngon par mdzes te/ rgya mtsho ltar
240a2: 'dug cing sems mi nyam me 'khrug pa de la bcom pa ma lha'i bshes gnyen mas ko ci zhig bya/ 'di lta bu dag ni 'dod chags la dga' ba med de/ sems phyen ci log dang ldan yang mi srid do// 'di lta bu dag
240a3: nisdug cing gtsang ba'i 'du shes yongs su rbA med de/ 'di lta bu dag ni 'dod pas 'khol kyang ma srid do// 'di lta bu dag ni bud med kyi dbang du 'gyur ba med de/ 'di lta bu dag ni bdud kyi spyod yul la spyod kyang mi sring ngo //
240a4: 'di lta bu dag ni bdud kyi spyod yul la chags pa med de/ 'di lta bu dag ni 'dod pa'i 'dam du bying ba yang mi srid do// 'di lta bu dag ni bdud kyi zhags pas bcings par 'gyur ba med do/ dgos po byed kyang mi srid do//
240a5: snyam mo// gang yang bcom pa ma lha'i bshes gnyen pa'i yon tan gyi khyad par mngon par shes shing / ye shes kyi spyod de yul mngon du gyur pa de dag ni 'di skad ces 'dzer te/ rigs kyi bu de ltar khyod bcom pa ma
240a6: bshes gnyen ma la yongs su dri bar sems pa ni khyod kyang 'thob par bya bar legs par thob pa ste/ legs so legs so// khyod ni nges par sangs rgyas su smon pa'o// khyod ni bdag nges par sems can thams cad
240a7: kyis gnas su 'gyur bar 'dod pa'o/ / khyod ni nges par sems can thams cad kyi 'dod chags kyi zug rngu dbyung bar 'dod pa'o// khyod ni nges par sdug cing gtsang ba'i 'du shes rnam par gtor bar 'dod pa'o// rigs

240b1: nyams bde la tshim zhing yid bde ba skyes nas/ bcom pa ma'i lha'i bshes gnyen ma'i khyim gang na ba der byin nas/ de'i khyimache zhing yangs la rin po che'i rab rim pa bcus bskor ba/ rin po cheta pa'i phreng ba rim pa bcus
240b2: kun nas bsko ga 'bas skyes chus gang ba/ lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i pad me dang / a pal dang / kA mra dang / me tog pan da rigs chu yongs su khebs pa yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i rgyas yongs sug gar gzhigs
240b3: gyi bye ma bdal pa/ spos yid du 'ong ba dang / 'dres pa'i dri zhim pas gang pa/ rin po che sil ma mang pos shin tu brgyan pa/ rim pa bcus kun nas bskor ba/ rin po che thams cad las bya'i khang pa dang / gzhal med khang dang
240b4: khang pa brtsegs pas rnam par dkrigs shing ba gam dang rta babs dang / skar khung gi shar bu dang / zla gam seng ge'i shi tog dang / snang ba'i rgyal mtshan la stsogs pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyis 'od kyis 'bar ba rin po
240b5: che rnam pa sna tshogs grangs med pa'i 'byung gnas kyis brgyan pa/ rin po che dag bai dUr+yas smras pa'i gzhi dang ldan pa/ lha rdzas kyi spos zhim po thams cad kyis 'khor thams cid nas/ gdugs shing bsangs pa/
240b6: a ga ru nag po mchog gis bdug spos kyis dri zhim par bdug pa/ spos kyi byug pas 'khor kun nas byugs pas/ rin po che sna tshogs kyi lan kun gyis rtsig ngos kun tu bres pa/ steng 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser
240b7: gyi dra ba rin po che sna tshogs kyis rab tu brgyan pa/ kun nas bkab pa/ gser gyi dril bu dra ba brgya stong rlung gis bskod cing / 'khrol ba'i sgra 'ong zhing snyan pa 'byung ba rin po che thams cad kyi me tog gi sman sil ma
240b8: kun tu bkram pas/ rin po che'i me tog gi rgyan dang ldan pa rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi rgyal mtshan bsgreng bas/ sgo shin tu brgyani pa/ ner bu rin pa che sna tshogs kyi 'od kyi dra ba sdang ba/ mu med par brjod

241a1: yod pa/ rin po che bai dUr+ya'i sdong po dang / rdo rje man shel la sogs pa'i gter brgya stong kun gyis shes pa/ phan sam tshogs pa'i mdzod mi zad pa dang ldan pa/ bza' shing gi rab chen pos bcas brgyan
241a2: pa mthong ste/ de na bcom pa ma lha'i bshes gnyen ma gzugs mdzes shing bzang la bltan sdug pa/ gnom pa'i kha dog dam pas rgyas pa dang ldan pa/ gser gyi kha dog ljang 'dug pa 'i mdog can sku mthon ting
241a3: 'dug pa/ lus kyi yan lag dang nying lag dang / tshul dang 'dra bar rnam par grub pa/ 'dod pa'i khams kyi lha dang mi thams cad las 'phags pa'i kha dog dang gzugs dang dbyibs mdzes pa dang ldan pa/ tshangs pa
241a4: las kyang 'das pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad kyi sgra skad kyi tshul la mkhas pa brgyan thams cad dang ldan zhing yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs can rnam par thar pa yi ge 'khor la
241a5: rgyan la mkhas pa dang ldan pa/ bzo dang gtsug lag thams cad la mkhas par byung ba/ chos kyi ye shes sgyu ma la mkhas par bslab pa// byang chub sems dpa'i thabs dang / tshul rnam pa thams cad thob

241a7: po che'i rgyan dang / lha ba lnga bzangs med pas rab tu brgyan pa/ las shin ta 'bar ba/ nor bu rin po che dam pa yid bzhin gyi rgyal ba'i cod pan thogs pa/ rin po che ba dUr+ya'i phreng ba mdo zangs rdo rje

241b1: cing yid du 'ong ba dang ldan pa/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs chen po'i gter ma zad pa'i mdzod dang ldan pa 'jug mthong ste/ de khyim de dag thams cad dang / rin po che'i gnas dang / gzhal med
241b2: khar kyi rgyan de dag thams cad kyang rang gi las las byung ba'i 'od dga' bar byed pa/ lus bde bas dang sems bskyed pa/ sems khong du sa dga' bar byed pas gsal bar sdang bar byas pa mthong ngo /
241b3: de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis bcom pa ma lha'i bshes gnyen ma'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ mdun du 'dug nas thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags ma bdag gis

241b5: ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams la gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa mdzad do zhes bdag gis thos na/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar nan

241b7: de ltar kho mo na lha rnams la lha mo'i gzugs dang kha dog dang / dbyibs dang chu zheng las kyang lhag par kha dog gsal ba dang / rnam par dag pa ci la mos pa bzhin du snang bar byed do// de bzhin du klu dang gnod

242a1: zhing rnam par dag pas ci la mos pa bzhin du snang bar byed ngo / / sems can gang 'dod chags kyis kun nas 'khor ba'i sems dang ldan pa dag/ kho ma'i drung du 'ongs na'ang de dag thams cad la kho ma ni 'dod chags

243a1: dpon gyi chung ma zhig ru gyur te/ blo gros bzang mo zhes bya'o// de nas kho mo cho 'phrul gyis yang dag par sprul nas khyim thab dang / lhan cig du 'dod dong ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa grong bar gyi srad du gshegs pa la

243a4: sems dpa' thabs dang ye shes mtha' yas pa gnas pa/ bsod nams rgya che zhing yangs pa'i mdzod dang ldan pa/ ye shes kyi yul la thub pa med pa de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ yon tan brjod par nas re skad/

243b6: 'da' bar 'gyur ba med do/ / rigs kyi bu de ltar kho bo ni de bzhir gshegs pa'i mchod rten tsan dan gyi khri 'phang gi sgo 'byed pa ste/ kho bo ni mchod rten gyi sgo 'byed pas byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sangs
243b7: rgyas kyi rigs mi zad pa'i brgyan ces bya ba thob po/ / rigs kyi bu kho bo ni ting nge 'dzin 'di la sems kyi skad skad cig du mnyam par gzhag ste/ sems kyi skad cig thams cad la'ang khyad par gyi rnab

244a1: 'di sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyad pa bsod bskyabs la stsogs pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / gser thub dang log par dang sel dang / thams cad mngar ba dang / gtsug tor dang rnam par gzigs dang
244a2: rgyal ba dang / rdzogs mdzad dang / grags mchog dang / pad mo'i blo la stsogs pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyang sangs rgyas mthong ba'i mtshams 'brel bas/ sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu bachud pa rgun mi 'chang
244a3: pa'i tshul gyis mngon sum du mthong ste/ sems kyi skad cig cig la sangs rgyas brgya yang mthong ngo // de'i 'og ma'i sems kyis sangs rgyas stong yang mthong ngo // de'i 'og ma'i sems kyis sangs rgyas brgya phrag stong
244a4: yang mthong ngo / / de bzhin du sangs rgyas bye ba dang / sangs rgyas bye ba phrag brgya dang / sangs rgyas bye ba phrag stong dang / sangs rgyas bye ba brgya phrag stong dang / sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig dang / sangs rgyas bye ba dung phyur
244a5: dang / sangs rgyas bye ba thams cad dang / sangs rgyas bye ba khrags khrigs dang / de'i 'og ma'i sems kyis sangs rgyas 'byung ba gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag kyang mthong
244a6: de'i 'og mi'i sems kyis de bzhin gshegs pa 'dzam bu'i gling gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang mthong ngo / / de'i 'og ma'i sems kyis de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du
244a7: med pa'i bar gyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang mthong ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa dag gis thugs dang po bskyed pa'i tshogs gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa la'ang 'jug go/ thugs dang po bskyed pas
244a8: 'thob pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa la'ang 'jug go/ smon lam rnam pa tha dad pa mngon par bsgrub pa rnam par dag pa la'ang 'jug go// spyod pa rnam par dag pa la'ang 'jug go// pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su

244b1: rdzogs par mdzad pa la'ang 'jug go/ / byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams cad yongs su bsgrubs pa la'ang 'jug go// bzod pa brnyes pa rnam par dag pa la'ang 'jug go// bdud kyi daklags mas rnam par 'thor/
244b2: ba khrumachog gi mthu byung ba la 'jug go// mngon par rdzogs par 'chang rgya ba'i rnam par 'brel ba'i rgyan la 'jug go// sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag par mdzad pa rnam par tha dad pala'ang 'jug go// sems

255b1: sa'i lhamo brtan mas cho dan kyi nor bzangs la 'disad ces smras so/ / rags kyi pa khyod 'dir 'ongs pa legs so// sa'i phyogs 'den sngon khyod kyi gnas su gyur te/ kho mo'i mngon sum du dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa yin na
